01M-MATT-01-01 BIBLOV GENESEWV IHSOU CRISTOU UIOU DAUID UIOU ABRAAM
01M-MATT-01-02 ABRAAM EGENNHSEN TON ISAAK ISAAK DE EGENNHSEN TON IAKWB IAKWB DE EGENNHSEN TON IOUDAN KAI TOUV ADELFOUV AUTOU
01M-MATT-01-03 IOUDAV DE EGENNHSEN TON FAREV KAI TON ZARA EK THV YAMAR FAREV DE EGENNHSEN TON ESRWM ESRWM DE EGENNHSEN TON ARAM
01M-MATT-01-04 ARAM DE EGENNHSEN TON AMINADAB AMINADAB DE EGENNHSEN TON NAASSWN NAASSWN DE EGENNHSEN TON SALMWN
01M-MATT-01-05 SALMWN DE EGENNHSEN TON BOOZ EK THV RACAB BOOZ DE EGENNHSEN TON WBHD EK THV ROUY WBHD DE EGENNHSEN TON IESSAI

01M-MATT-01-16 IAKWB DE EGENNHSEN TON IWSHF TON ANDRA MARIAV EX HV EGENNHYH IHSOUV O LEGOMENOV CRISTOV
01M-MATT-01-17 PASAI OUN AI GENEAI APO ABRAAM EWV DAUID GENEAI DEKATESSAREV KAI APO DAUID EWV THV METOIKESIAV BABULWNOV GENEAI DEKATESSAREV KAI APO THV METOIKESIAV BABULWNOV EWV TOU CRISTOU GENEAI DEKATESSAREV
01M-MATT-01-18 TOU DE IHSOU CRISTOU H GENNHSIV OUTWV HN MNHSTEUYEISHV GAR THV MHTROV AUTOU MARIAV TW IWSHF PRIN H SUNELYEIN AUTOUV EUREYH EN GASTRI ECOUSA EK PNEUMATOV AGIOU
01M-MATT-01-19 IWSHF DE O ANHR AUTHV DIKAIOV WN KAI MH YELWN AUTHN PARADEIGMATISAI EBOULHYH LAYRA APOLUSAI AUTHN
01M-MATT-01-20 TAUTA DE AUTOU ENYUMHYENTOV IDOU AGGELOV KURIOU KAT ONAR EFANH AUTW LEGWN IWSHF UIOV DAUID MH FOBHYHV PARALABEIN MARIAM THN GUNAIKA SOU TO GAR EN AUTH GENNHYEN EK PNEUMATOV ESTIN AGIOU
01M-MATT-01-21 TEXETAI DE UION KAI KALESEIV TO ONOMA AUTOU IHSOUN AUTOV GAR SWSEI TON LAON AUTOU APO TWN AMARTIWN AUTWN
01M-MATT-01-22 TOUTO DE OLON GEGONEN INA PLHRWYH TO RHYEN UPO TOU KURIOU DIA TOU PROFHTOU LEGONTOV
01M-MATT-01-23 IDOU H PARYENOV EN GASTRI EXEI KAI TEXETAI UION KAI KALESOUSIN TO ONOMA AUTOU EMMANOUHL O ESTIN MEYERMHNEUOMENON MEY HMWN O YEOV
01M-MATT-01-24 DIEGERYEIV DE O IWSHF APO TOU UPNOU EPOIHSEN WV PROSETAXEN AUTW O AGGELOV KURIOU KAI PARELABEN THN GUNAIKA AUTOU
01M-MATT-01-25 KAI OUK EGINWSKEN AUTHN EWV OU ETEKEN TON UION AUTHV TON PRWTOTOKON KAI EKALESEN TO ONOMA AUTOU IHSOUN
01M-MATT-02-01 TOU DE IHSOU GENNHYENTOV EN BHYLEEM THV IOUDAIAV EN HMERAIV HRWDOU TOU BASILEWV IDOU MAGOI APO ANATOLWN PAREGENONTO EIV IEROSOLUMA
01M-MATT-02-02 LEGONTEV POU ESTIN O TECYEIV BASILEUV TWN IOUDAIWN EIDOMEN GAR AUTOU TON ASTERA EN TH ANATOLH KAI HLYOMEN PROSKUNHSAI AUTW
01M-MATT-02-03 AKOUSAV DE HRWDHV O BASILEUV ETARACYH KAI PASA IEROSOLUMA MET AUTOU
01M-MATT-02-04 KAI SUNAGAGWN PANTAV TOUV ARCIEREIV KAI GRAMMATEIV TOU LAOU EPUNYANETO PAR AUTWN POU O CRISTOV GENNATAI
01M-MATT-02-05 OI DE EIPON AUTW EN BHYLEEM THV IOUDAIAV OUTWV GAR GEGRAPTAI DIA TOU PROFHTOU
01M-MATT-02-06 KAI SU BHYLEEM GH IOUDA OUDAMWV ELACISTH EI EN TOIV HGEMOSIN IOUDA EK SOU GAR EXELEUSETAI HGOUMENOV OSTIV POIMANEI TON LAON MOU TON ISRAHL
01M-MATT-02-07 TOTE HRWDHV LAYRA KALESAV TOUV MAGOUV HKRIBWSEN PAR AUTWN TON CRONON TOU FAINOMENOU ASTEROV
01M-MATT-02-08 KAI PEMQAV AUTOUV EIV BHYLEEM EIPEN POREUYENTEV AKRIBWV EXETASATE PERI TOU PAIDIOU EPAN DE EURHTE APAGGEILATE MOI OPWV KAGW ELYWN PROSKUNHSW AUTW
01M-MATT-02-09 OI DE AKOUSANTEV TOU BASILEWV EPOREUYHSAN KAI IDOU O ASTHR ON EIDON EN TH ANATOLH PROHGEN AUTOUV EWV ELYWN ESTH EPANW OU HN TO PAIDION
01M-MATT-02-10 IDONTEV DE TON ASTERA ECARHSAN CARAN MEGALHN SFODRA
01M-MATT-02-11 KAI ELYONTEV EIV THN OIKIAN EIDON TO PAIDION META MARIAV THV MHTROV AUTOU KAI PESONTEV PROSEKUNHSAN AUTW KAI ANOIXANTEV TOUV YHSAUROUV AUTWN PROSHNEGKAN AUTW DWRA CRUSON KAI LIBANON KAI SMURNAN
01M-MATT-02-12 KAI CRHMATISYENTEV KAT ONAR MH ANAKAMQAI PROV HRWDHN DI ALLHV ODOU ANECWRHSAN EIV THN CWRAN AUTWN
01M-MATT-02-13 ANACWRHSANTWN DE AUTWN IDOU AGGELOV KURIOU FAINETAI KAT ONAR TW IWSHF LEGWN EGERYEIV PARALABE TO PAIDION KAI THN MHTERA AUTOU KAI FEUGE EIV AIGUPTON KAI ISYI EKEI EWV AN EIPW SOI MELLEI GAR HRWDHV ZHTEIN TO PAIDION TOU APOLESAI AUTO
01M-MATT-02-14 O DE EGERYEIV PARELABEN TO PAIDION KAI THN MHTERA AUTOU NUKTOV KAI ANECWRHSEN EIV AIGUPTON
01M-MATT-02-15 KAI HN EKEI EWV THV TELEUTHV HRWDOU INA PLHRWYH TO RHYEN UPO TOU KURIOU DIA TOU PROFHTOU LEGONTOV EX AIGUPTOU EKALESA TON UION MOU
01M-MATT-02-16 TOTE HRWDHV IDWN OTI ENEPAICYH UPO TWN MAGWN EYUMWYH LIAN KAI APOSTEILAV ANEILEN PANTAV TOUV PAIDAV TOUV EN BHYLEEM KAI EN PASIN TOIV ORIOIV AUTHV APO DIETOUV KAI KATWTERW KATA TON CRONON ON HKRIBWSEN PARA TWN MAGWN
01M-MATT-02-17 TOTE EPLHRWYH TO RHYEN UPO IEREMIOU TOU PROFHTOU LEGONTOV
01M-MATT-02-18 FWNH EN RAMA HKOUSYH YRHNOV KAI KLAUYMOV KAI ODURMOV POLUV RACHL KLAIOUSA TA TEKNA AUTHV KAI OUK HYELEN PARAKLHYHNAI OTI OUK EISIN
01M-MATT-02-19 TELEUTHSANTOV DE TOU HRWDOU IDOU AGGELOV KURIOU KAT ONAR FAINETAI TW IWSHF EN AIGUPTW
01M-MATT-02-20 LEGWN EGERYEIV PARALABE TO PAIDION KAI THN MHTERA AUTOU KAI POREUOU EIV GHN ISRAHL TEYNHKASIN GAR OI ZHTOUNTEV THN QUCHN TOU PAIDIOU
01M-MATT-02-21 O DE EGERYEIV PARELABEN TO PAIDION KAI THN MHTERA AUTOU KAI HLYEN EIV GHN ISRAHL
01M-MATT-02-22 AKOUSAV DE OTI ARCELAOV BASILEUEI EPI THV IOUDAIAV ANTI HRWDOU TOU PATROV AUTOU EFOBHYH EKEI APELYEIN CRHMATISYEIV DE KAT ONAR ANECWRHSEN EIV TA MERH THV GALILAIAV
01M-MATT-02-23 KAI ELYWN KATWKHSEN EIV POLIN LEGOMENHN NAZARET OPWV PLHRWYH TO RHYEN DIA TWN PROFHTWN OTI NAZWRAIOV KLHYHSETAI
01M-MATT-03-01 EN DE TAIV HMERAIV EKEINAIV PARAGINETAI IWANNHV O BAPTISTHV KHRUSSWN EN TH ERHMW THV IOUDAIAV
01M-MATT-03-02 KAI LEGWN METANOEITE HGGIKEN GAR H BASILEIA TWN OURANWN
01M-MATT-03-03 OUTOV GAR ESTIN O RHYEIV UPO HSAIOU TOU PROFHTOU LEGONTOV FWNH BOWNTOV EN TH ERHMW ETOIMASATE THN ODON KURIOU EUYEIAV POIEITE TAV TRIBOUV AUTOU
01M-MATT-03-04 AUTOV DE O IWANNHV EICEN TO ENDUMA AUTOU APO TRICWN KAMHLOU KAI ZWNHN DERMATINHN PERI THN OSFUN AUTOU H DE TROFH AUTOU HN AKRIDEV KAI MELI AGRION
01M-MATT-03-05 TOTE EXEPOREUETO PROV AUTON IEROSOLUMA KAI PASA H IOUDAIA KAI PASA H PERICWROV TOU IORDANOU
01M-MATT-03-06 KAI EBAPTIZONTO EN TW IORDANH UP AUTOU EXOMOLOGOUMENOI TAV AMARTIAV AUTWN
01M-MATT-03-07 IDWN DE POLLOUV TWN FARISAIWN KAI SADDOUKAIWN ERCOMENOUV EPI TO BAPTISMA AUTOU EIPEN AUTOIV GENNHMATA ECIDNWN TIV UPEDEIXEN UMIN FUGEIN APO THV MELLOUSHV ORGHV
01M-MATT-03-08 POIHSATE OUN KARPON AXION THV METANOIAV
01M-MATT-03-09 KAI MH DOXHTE LEGEIN EN EAUTOIV PATERA ECOMEN TON ABRAAM LEGW GAR UMIN OTI DUNATAI O YEOV EK TWN LIYWN TOUTWN EGEIRAI TEKNA TW ABRAAM
01M-MATT-03-10 HDH DE KAI H AXINH PROV THN RIZAN TWN DENDRWN KEITAI PAN OUN DENDRON MH POIOUN KARPON KALON EKKOPTETAI KAI EIV PUR BALLETAI
01M-MATT-03-11 EGW MEN BAPTIZW UMAV EN UDATI EIV METANOIAN O DE OPISW MOU ERCOMENOV ISCUROTEROV MOU ESTIN OU OUK EIMI IKANOV TA UPODHMATA BASTASAI AUTOV UMAV BAPTISEI EN PNEUMATI AGIW
01M-MATT-03-12 OU TO PTUON EN TH CEIRI AUTOU KAI DIAKAYARIEI THN ALWNA AUTOU KAI SUNAXEI TON SITON AUTOU EIV THN APOYHKHN TO DE ACURON KATAKAUSEI PURI ASBESTW
01M-MATT-03-13 TOTE PARAGINETAI O IHSOUV APO THV GALILAIAV EPI TON IORDANHN PROV TON IWANNHN TOU BAPTISYHNAI UP AUTOU
01M-MATT-03-14 O DE IWANNHV DIEKWLUEN AUTON LEGWN EGW CREIAN ECW UPO SOU BAPTISYHNAI KAI SU ERCH PROV ME
01M-MATT-03-15 APOKRIYEIV DE O IHSOUV EIPEN PROV AUTON AFEV ARTI OUTWV GAR PREPON ESTIN HMIN PLHRWSAI PASAN DIKAIOSUNHN TOTE AFIHSIN AUTON
01M-MATT-03-16 KAI BAPTISYEIV O IHSOUV ANEBH EUYUV APO TOU UDATOV KAI IDOU ANEWCYHSAN AUTW OI OURANOI KAI EIDEN TO PNEUMA TOU YEOU KATABAINON WSEI PERISTERAN KAI ERCOMENON EP AUTON
01M-MATT-03-17 KAI IDOU FWNH EK TWN OURANWN LEGOUSA OUTOV ESTIN O UIOV MOU O AGAPHTOV EN W EUDOKHSA
01M-MATT-04-01 TOTE O IHSOUV ANHCYH EIV THN ERHMON UPO TOU PNEUMATOV PEIRASYHNAI UPO TOU DIABOLOU

01M-MATT-04-04 O DE APOKRIYEIV EIPEN GEGRAPTAI OUK EP ARTW MONW ZHSETAI ANYRWPOV ALL EPI PANTI RHMATI EKPOREUOMENW DIA STOMATOV YEOU
01M-MATT-04-05 TOTE PARALAMBANEI AUTON O DIABOLOV EIV THN AGIAN POLIN KAI ISTHSIN AUTON EPI TO PTERUGION TOU IEROU
01M-MATT-04-06 KAI LEGEI AUTW EI UIOV EI TOU YEOU BALE SEAUTON KATW GEGRAPTAI GAR OTI TOIV AGGELOIV AUTOU ENTELEITAI PERI SOU KAI EPI CEIRWN AROUSIN SE MHPOTE PROSKOQHV PROV LIYON TON PODA SOU

01M-MATT-04-19 KAI LEGEI AUTOIV DEUTE OPISW MOU KAI POIHSW UMAV ALIEIV ANYRWPWN
01M-MATT-04-20 OI DE EUYEWV AFENTEV TA DIKTUA HKOLOUYHSAN AUTW
01M-MATT-04-21 KAI PROBAV EKEIYEN EIDEN ALLOUV DUO ADELFOUV IAKWBON TON TOU ZEBEDAIOU KAI IWANNHN TON ADELFON AUTOU EN TW PLOIW META ZEBEDAIOU TOU PATROV AUTWN KATARTIZONTAV TA DIKTUA AUTWN KAI EKALESEN AUTOUV
01M-MATT-04-22 OI DE EUYEWV AFENTEV TO PLOION KAI TON PATERA AUTWN HKOLOUYHSAN AUTW
01M-MATT-04-23 KAI PERIHGEN OLHN THN GALILAIAN O IHSOUV DIDASKWN EN TAIV SUNAGWGAIV AUTWN KAI KHRUSSWN TO EUAGGELION THV BASILEIAV KAI YERAPEUWN PASAN NOSON KAI PASAN MALAKIAN EN TW LAW
01M-MATT-04-24 KAI APHLYEN H AKOH AUTOU EIV OLHN THN SURIAN KAI PROSHNEGKAN AUTW PANTAV TOUV KAKWV ECONTAV POIKILAIV NOSOIV KAI BASANOIV SUNECOMENOUV KAI DAIMONIZOMENOUV KAI SELHNIAZOMENOUV KAI PARALUTIKOUV KAI EYERAPEUSEN AUTOUV

02K-MARK-14-42 EGEIRESYE AGWMEN IDOU O PARADIDOUV ME HGGIKEN

02K-MARK-16-01 KAI DIAGENOMENOU TOU SABBATOU MARIA H MAGDALHNH KAI MARIA IAKWBOU KAI SALWMH HGORASAN ARWMATA INA ELYOUSAI ALEIQWSIN AUTON

03L-LUKE-01-05 EGENETO EN TAIV HMERAIV HRWDOU TOU BASILEWV THV IOUDAIAV IEREUV TIV ONOMATI ZACARIAV EX EFHMERIAV ABIA KAI H GUNH AUTOU EK TWN YUGATERWN AARWN KAI TO ONOMA AUTHV ELISABET

03L-LUKE-01-20 KAI IDOU ESH SIWPWN KAI MH DUNAMENOV LALHSAI ACRI HV HMERAV GENHTAI TAUTA ANY WN OUK EPISTEUSAV TOIV LOGOIV MOU OITINEV PLHRWYHSONTAI EIV TON KAIRON AUTWN

03L-LUKE-01-37 OTI OUK ADUNATHSEI PARA TW YEW PAN RHMA

03L-LUKE-07-20 PARAGENOMENOI DE PROV AUTON OI ANDREV EIPON IWANNHV O BAPTISTHV APESTALKEN HMAV PROV SE LEGWN SU EI O ERCOMENOV H ALLON PROSDOKWMEN

03L-LUKE-08-01 KAI EGENETO EN TW KAYEXHV KAI AUTOV DIWDEUEN KATA POLIN KAI KWMHN KHRUSSWN KAI EUAGGELIZOMENOV THN BASILEIAN TOU YEOU KAI OI DWDEKA SUN AUTW

03L-LUKE-09-34 TAUTA DE AUTOU LEGONTOV EGENETO NEFELH KAI EPESKIASEN AUTOUV EFOBHYHSAN DE EN TW EKEINOUV EISELYEIN EIV THN NEFELHN

03L-LUKE-09-36 KAI EN TW GENESYAI THN FWNHN EUREYH O IHSOUV MONOV KAI AUTOI ESIGHSAN KAI OUDENI APHGGEILAN EN EKEINAIV TAIV HMERAIV OUDEN WN EWRAKASIN
03L-LUKE-09-37 EGENETO DE EN TH EXHV HMERA KATELYONTWN AUTWN APO TOU OROUV SUNHNTHSEN AUTW OCLOV POLUV

03L-LUKE-09-40 KAI EDEHYHN TWN MAYHTWN SOU INA EKBALWSIN AUTO KAI OUK HDUNHYHSAN
03L-LUKE-09-41 APOKRIYEIV DE O IHSOUV EIPEN W GENEA APISTOV KAI DIESTRAMMENH EWV POTE ESOMAI PROV UMAV KAI ANEXOMAI UMWN PROSAGAGE TON UION SOU WDE
03L-LUKE-09-42 ETI DE PROSERCOMENOU AUTOU ERRHXEN AUTON TO DAIMONION KAI SUNESPARAXEN EPETIMHSEN DE O IHSOUV TW PNEUMATI TW AKAYARTW KAI IASATO TON PAIDA KAI APEDWKEN AUTON TW PATRI AUTOU
03L-LUKE-09-43 EXEPLHSSONTO DE PANTEV EPI TH MEGALEIOTHTI TOU YEOU PANTWN DE YAUMAZONTWN EPI PASIN OIV EPOIHSEN O IHSOUV EIPEN PROV TOUV MAYHTAV AUTOU
03L-LUKE-09-44 YESYE UMEIV EIV TA WTA UMWN TOUV LOGOUV TOUTOUV O GAR UIOV TOU ANYRWPOU MELLEI PARADIDOSYAI EIV CEIRAV ANYRWPWN
03L-LUKE-09-45 OI DE HGNOOUN TO RHMA TOUTO KAI HN PARAKEKALUMMENON AP AUTWN INA MH AISYWNTAI AUTO KAI EFOBOUNTO ERWTHSAI AUTON PERI TOU RHMATOV TOUTOU
03L-LUKE-09-46 EISHLYEN DE DIALOGISMOV EN AUTOIV TO TIV AN EIH MEIZWN AUTWN
03L-LUKE-09-47 O DE IHSOUV IDWN TON DIALOGISMON THV KARDIAV AUTWN EPILABOMENOV PAIDIOU ESTHSEN AUTO PAR EAUTW
03L-LUKE-09-48 KAI EIPEN AUTOIV OV EAN DEXHTAI TOUTO TO PAIDION EPI TW ONOMATI MOU EME DECETAI KAI OV EAN EME DEXHTAI DECETAI TON APOSTEILANTA ME O GAR MIKROTEROV EN PASIN UMIN UPARCWN OUTOV ESTAI MEGAV
03L-LUKE-09-49 APOKRIYEIV DE O IWANNHV EIPEN EPISTATA EIDOMEN TINA EPI TW ONOMATI SOU EKBALLONTA DAIMONIA KAI EKWLUSAMEN AUTON OTI OUK AKOLOUYEI MEY HMWN
03L-LUKE-09-50 KAI EIPEN PROV AUTON O IHSOUV MH KWLUETE OV GAR OUK ESTIN KAY HMWN UPER HMWN ESTIN
03L-LUKE-09-51 EGENETO DE EN TW SUMPLHROUSYAI TAV HMERAV THV ANALHQEWV AUTOU KAI AUTOV TO PROSWPON AUTOU ESTHRIXEN TOU POREUESYAI EIV IEROUSALHM
03L-LUKE-09-52 KAI APESTEILEN AGGELOUV PRO PROSWPOU AUTOU KAI POREUYENTEV EISHLYON EIV KWMHN SAMAREITWN WSTE ETOIMASAI AUTW
03L-LUKE-09-53 KAI OUK EDEXANTO AUTON OTI TO PROSWPON AUTOU HN POREUOMENON EIV IEROUSALHM
03L-LUKE-09-54 IDONTEV DE OI MAYHTAI AUTOU IAKWBOV KAI IWANNHV EIPON KURIE YELEIV EIPWMEN PUR KATABHNAI APO TOU OURANOU KAI ANALWSAI AUTOUV WV KAI HLIAV EPOIHSEN
03L-LUKE-09-55 STRAFEIV DE EPETIMHSEN AUTOIV KAI EIPEN OUK OIDATE OIOU PNEUMATOV ESTE UMEIV
03L-LUKE-09-56 O GAR UIOV TOU ANYRWPOU OUK HLYEN QUCAV ANYRWPWN APOLESAI ALLA SWSAI KAI EPOREUYHSAN EIV ETERAN KWMHN
03L-LUKE-09-57 EGENETO DE POREUOMENWN AUTWN EN TH ODW EIPEN TIV PROV AUTON AKOLOUYHSW SOI OPOU AN APERCH KURIE
03L-LUKE-09-58 KAI EIPEN AUTW O IHSOUV AI ALWPEKEV FWLEOUV ECOUSIN KAI TA PETEINA TOU OURANOU KATASKHNWSEIV O DE UIOV TOU ANYRWPOU OUK ECEI POU THN KEFALHN KLINH
03L-LUKE-09-59 EIPEN DE PROV ETERON AKOLOUYEI MOI O DE EIPEN KURIE EPITREQON MOI APELYONTI PRWTON YAQAI TON PATERA MOU
03L-LUKE-09-60 EIPEN DE AUTW O IHSOUV AFEV TOUV NEKROUV YAQAI TOUV EAUTWN NEKROUV SU DE APELYWN DIAGGELLE THN BASILEIAN TOU YEOU

03L-LUKE-09-62 EIPEN DE O IHSOUV PROV AUTON OUDEIV EPIBALWN THN CEIRA AUTOU EP AROTRON KAI BLEPWN EIV TA OPISW EUYETOV ESTIN EIV THN BASILEIAN TOU YEOU
03L-LUKE-10-01 META DE TAUTA ANEDEIXEN O KURIOV KAI ETEROUV EBDOMHKONTA KAI APESTEILEN AUTOUV ANA DUO PRO PROSWPOU AUTOU EIV PASAN POLIN KAI TOPON OU EMELLEN AUTOV ERCESYAI
03L-LUKE-10-02 ELEGEN OUN PROV AUTOUV O MEN YERISMOV POLUV OI DE ERGATAI OLIGOI DEHYHTE OUN TOU KURIOU TOU YERISMOU OPWV EKBALH ERGATAV EIV TON YERISMON AUTOU
03L-LUKE-10-03 UPAGETE IDOU EGW APOSTELLW UMAV WV ARNAV EN MESW LUKWN
03L-LUKE-10-04 MH BASTAZETE BALANTION MH PHRAN MHDE UPODHMATA KAI MHDENA KATA THN ODON ASPASHSYE
03L-LUKE-10-05 EIV HN D AN OIKIAN EISERCHSYE PRWTON LEGETE EIRHNH TW OIKW TOUTW
03L-LUKE-10-06 KAI EAN H EKEI UIOV EIRHNHV EPANAPAUSETAI EP AUTON H EIRHNH UMWN EI DE MHGE EF UMAV ANAKAMQEI
03L-LUKE-10-07 EN AUTH DE TH OIKIA MENETE ESYIONTEV KAI PINONTEV TA PAR AUTWN AXIOV GAR O ERGATHV TOU MISYOU AUTOU ESTIN MH METABAINETE EX OIKIAV EIV OIKIAN
03L-LUKE-10-08 KAI EIV HN AN POLIN EISERCHSYE KAI DECWNTAI UMAV ESYIETE TA PARATIYEMENA UMIN

03L-LUKE-10-11 KAI TON KONIORTON TON KOLLHYENTA HMIN EK THV POLEWV UMWN APOMASSOMEYA UMIN PLHN TOUTO GINWSKETE OTI HGGIKEN EF UMAV H BASILEIA TOU YEOU

03L-LUKE-10-15 KAI SU KAPERNAOUM H EWV TOU OURANOU UQWYEISA EWV ADOU KATABIBASYHSH
03L-LUKE-10-16 O AKOUWN UMWN EMOU AKOUEI KAI O AYETWN UMAV EME AYETEI O DE EME AYETWN AYETEI TON APOSTEILANTA ME

03L-LUKE-10-18 EIPEN DE AUTOIV EYEWROUN TON SATANAN WV ASTRAPHN EK TOU OURANOU PESONTA
03L-LUKE-10-19 IDOU DIDWMI UMIN THN EXOUSIAN TOU PATEIN EPANW OFEWN KAI SKORPIWN KAI EPI PASAN THN DUNAMIN TOU ECYROU KAI OUDEN UMAV OU MH ADIKHSH
03L-LUKE-10-20 PLHN EN TOUTW MH CAIRETE OTI TA PNEUMATA UMIN UPOTASSETAI CAIRETE DE OTI TA ONOMATA UMWN EGRAFH EN TOIV OURANOIV
03L-LUKE-10-21 EN AUTH TH WRA HGALLIASATO TW PNEUMATI O IHSOUV KAI EIPEN EXOMOLOGOUMAI SOI PATER KURIE TOU OURANOU KAI THV GHV OTI APEKRUQAV TAUTA APO SOFWN KAI SUNETWN KAI APEKALUQAV AUTA NHPIOIV NAI O PATHR OTI OUTWV EGENETO EUDOKIA EMPROSYEN SOU
03L-LUKE-10-22 KAI STRAFEIV PROV TOUV MAYHTAV EIPEN PANTA MOI PAREDOYH UPO TOU PATROV MOU KAI OUDEIV GINWSKEI TIV ESTIN O UIOV EI MH O PATHR KAI TIV ESTIN O PATHR EI MH O UIOV KAI W EAN BOULHTAI O UIOV APOKALUQAI
03L-LUKE-10-23 KAI STRAFEIV PROV TOUV MAYHTAV KAT IDIAN EIPEN MAKARIOI OI OFYALMOI OI BLEPONTEV A BLEPETE
03L-LUKE-10-24 LEGW GAR UMIN OTI POLLOI PROFHTAI KAI BASILEIV HYELHSAN IDEIN A UMEIV BLEPETE KAI OUK EIDON KAI AKOUSAI A AKOUETE KAI OUK HKOUSAN
03L-LUKE-10-25 KAI IDOU NOMIKOV TIV ANESTH EKPEIRAZWN AUTON KAI LEGWN DIDASKALE TI POIHSAV ZWHN AIWNION KLHRONOMHSW

03L-LUKE-10-28 EIPEN DE AUTW ORYWV APEKRIYHV TOUTO POIEI KAI ZHSH

03L-LUKE-10-30 UPOLABWN DE O IHSOUV EIPEN ANYRWPOV TIV KATEBAINEN APO IEROUSALHM EIV IERICW KAI LHSTAIV PERIEPESEN OI KAI EKDUSANTEV AUTON KAI PLHGAV EPIYENTEV APHLYON AFENTEV HMIYANH TUGCANONTA

03L-LUKE-10-35 KAI EPI THN AURION EXELYWN EKBALWN DUO DHNARIA EDWKEN TW PANDOCEI KAI EIPEN AUTW EPIMELHYHTI AUTOU KAI O TI AN PROSDAPANHSHV EGW EN TW EPANERCESYAI ME APODWSW SOI

03L-LUKE-11-01 KAI EGENETO EN TW EINAI AUTON EN TOPW TINI PROSEUCOMENON WV EPAUSATO EIPEN TIV TWN MAYHTWN AUTOU PROV AUTON KURIE DIDAXON HMAV PROSEUCESYAI KAYWV KAI IWANNHV EDIDAXEN TOUV MAYHTAV AUTOU
03L-LUKE-11-02 EIPEN DE AUTOIV OTAN PROSEUCHSYE LEGETE PATER HMWN O EN TOIV OURANOIV AGIASYHTW TO ONOMA SOU ELYETW H BASILEIA SOU GENHYHTW TO YELHMA SOU WV EN OURANW KAI EPI THV GHV
03L-LUKE-11-03 TON ARTON HMWN TON EPIOUSION DIDOU HMIN TO KAY HMERAN
03L-LUKE-11-04 KAI AFEV HMIN TAV AMARTIAV HMWN KAI GAR AUTOI AFIEMEN PANTI OFEILONTI HMIN KAI MH EISENEGKHV HMAV EIV PEIRASMON ALLA RUSAI HMAV APO TOU PONHROU
03L-LUKE-11-05 KAI EIPEN PROV AUTOUV TIV EX UMWN EXEI FILON KAI POREUSETAI PROV AUTON MESONUKTIOU KAI EIPH AUTW FILE CRHSON MOI TREIV ARTOUV

03L-LUKE-11-13 EI OUN UMEIV PONHROI UPARCONTEV OIDATE DOMATA AGAYA DIDONAI TOIV TEKNOIV UMWN POSW MALLON O PATHR O EX OURANOU DWSEI PNEUMA AGION TOIV AITOUSIN AUTON
03L-LUKE-11-14 KAI HN EKBALLWN DAIMONION KAI AUTO HN KWFON EGENETO DE TOU DAIMONIOU EXELYONTOV ELALHSEN O KWFOV KAI EYAUMASAN OI OCLOI

03L-LUKE-11-18 EI DE KAI O SATANAV EF EAUTON DIEMERISYH PWV STAYHSETAI H BASILEIA AUTOU OTI LEGETE EN BEELZEBOUL EKBALLEIN ME TA DAIMONIA

03L-LUKE-11-23 O MH WN MET EMOU KAT EMOU ESTIN KAI O MH SUNAGWN MET EMOU SKORPIZEI

03L-LUKE-11-54 ENEDREUONTEV AUTON ZHTOUNTEV YHREUSAI TI EK TOU STOMATOV AUTOU INA KATHGORHSWSIN AUTOU
03L-LUKE-12-01 EN OIV EPISUNACYEISWN TWN MURIADWN TOU OCLOU WSTE KATAPATEIN ALLHLOUV HRXATO LEGEIN PROV TOUV MAYHTAV AUTOU PRWTON PROSECETE EAUTOIV APO THV ZUMHV TWN FARISAIWN HTIV ESTIN UPOKRISIV

03L-LUKE-13-01 PARHSAN DE TINEV EN AUTW TW KAIRW APAGGELLONTEV AUTW PERI TWN GALILAIWN WN TO AIMA PILATOV EMIXEN META TWN YUSIWN AUTWN

03L-LUKE-24-45 TOTE DIHNOIXEN AUTWN TON NOUN TOU SUNIENAI TAV GRAFAV

03L-LUKE-24-47 KAI KHRUCYHNAI EPI TW ONOMATI AUTOU METANOIAN KAI AFESIN AMARTIWN EIV PANTA TA EYNH ARXAMENON APO IEROUSALHM
03L-LUKE-24-48 UMEIV DE ESTE MARTUREV TOUTWN
03L-LUKE-24-49 KAI IDOU EGW APOSTELLW THN EPAGGELIAN TOU PATROV MOU EF UMAV UMEIV DE KAYISATE EN TH POLEI IEROUSALHM EWV OU ENDUSHSYE DUNAMIN EX UQOUV
03L-LUKE-24-50 EXHGAGEN DE AUTOUV EXW EWV EIV BHYANIAN KAI EPARAV TAV CEIRAV AUTOU EULOGHSEN AUTOUV
03L-LUKE-24-51 KAI EGENETO EN TW EULOGEIN AUTON AUTOUV DIESTH AP AUTWN KAI ANEFERETO EIV TON OURANON
03L-LUKE-24-52 KAI AUTOI PROSKUNHSANTEV AUTON UPESTREQAN EIV IEROUSALHM META CARAV MEGALHV
03L-LUKE-24-53 KAI HSAN DIA PANTOV EN TW IERW AINOUNTEV KAI EULOGOUNTEV TON YEON AMHN
04J-JOHN-01-01 EN ARCH HN O LOGOV KAI O LOGOV HN PROV TON YEON KAI YEOV HN O LOGOV
04J-JOHN-01-02 OUTOV HN EN ARCH PROV TON YEON
04J-JOHN-01-03 PANTA DI AUTOU EGENETO KAI CWRIV AUTOU EGENETO OUDE EN O GEGONEN
04J-JOHN-01-04 EN AUTW ZWH HN KAI H ZWH HN TO FWV TWN ANYRWPWN
04J-JOHN-01-05 KAI TO FWV EN TH SKOTIA FAINEI KAI H SKOTIA AUTO OU KATELABEN
04J-JOHN-01-06 EGENETO ANYRWPOV APESTALMENOV PARA YEOU ONOMA AUTW IWANNHV
04J-JOHN-01-07 OUTOV HLYEN EIV MARTURIAN INA MARTURHSH PERI TOU FWTOV INA PANTEV PISTEUSWSIN DI AUTOU
04J-JOHN-01-08 OUK HN EKEINOV TO FWV ALL INA MARTURHSH PERI TOU FWTOV
04J-JOHN-01-09 HN TO FWV TO ALHYINON O FWTIZEI PANTA ANYRWPON ERCOMENON EIV TON KOSMON
04J-JOHN-01-10 EN TW KOSMW HN KAI O KOSMOV DI AUTOU EGENETO KAI O KOSMOV AUTON OUK EGNW
04J-JOHN-01-11 EIV TA IDIA HLYEN KAI OI IDIOI AUTON OU PARELABON
04J-JOHN-01-12 OSOI DE ELABON AUTON EDWKEN AUTOIV EXOUSIAN TEKNA YEOU GENESYAI TOIV PISTEUOUSIN EIV TO ONOMA AUTOU
04J-JOHN-01-13 OI OUK EX AIMATWN OUDE EK YELHMATOV SARKOV OUDE EK YELHMATOV ANDROV ALL EK YEOU EGENNHYHSAN
04J-JOHN-01-14 KAI O LOGOV SARX EGENETO KAI ESKHNWSEN EN HMIN KAI EYEASAMEYA THN DOXAN AUTOU DOXAN WV MONOGENOUV PARA PATROV PLHRHV CARITOV KAI ALHYEIAV
04J-JOHN-01-15 IWANNHV MARTUREI PERI AUTOU KAI KEKRAGEN LEGWN OUTOV HN ON EIPON O OPISW MOU ERCOMENOV EMPROSYEN MOU GEGONEN OTI PRWTOV MOU HN
04J-JOHN-01-16 KAI EK TOU PLHRWMATOV AUTOU HMEIV PANTEV ELABOMEN KAI CARIN ANTI CARITOV
04J-JOHN-01-17 OTI O NOMOV DIA MWSEWV EDOYH H CARIV KAI H ALHYEIA DIA IHSOU CRISTOU EGENETO
04J-JOHN-01-18 YEON OUDEIV EWRAKEN PWPOTE O MONOGENHV UIOV O WN EIV TON KOLPON TOU PATROV EKEINOV EXHGHSATO
04J-JOHN-01-19 KAI AUTH ESTIN H MARTURIA TOU IWANNOU OTE APESTEILAN OI IOUDAIOI EX IEROSOLUMWN IEREIV KAI LEUITAV INA ERWTHSWSIN AUTON SU TIV EI
04J-JOHN-01-20 KAI WMOLOGHSEN KAI OUK HRNHSATO KAI WMOLOGHSEN OTI OUK EIMI EGW O CRISTOV
04J-JOHN-01-21 KAI HRWTHSAN AUTON TI OUN HLIAV EI SU KAI LEGEI OUK EIMI O PROFHTHV EI SU KAI APEKRIYH OU
04J-JOHN-01-22 EIPON OUN AUTW TIV EI INA APOKRISIN DWMEN TOIV PEMQASIN HMAV TI LEGEIV PERI SEAUTOU
04J-JOHN-01-23 EFH EGW FWNH BOWNTOV EN TH ERHMW EUYUNATE THN ODON KURIOU KAYWV EIPEN HSAIAV O PROFHTHV
04J-JOHN-01-24 KAI OI APESTALMENOI HSAN EK TWN FARISAIWN
04J-JOHN-01-25 KAI HRWTHSAN AUTON KAI EIPON AUTW TI OUN BAPTIZEIV EI SU OUK EI O CRISTOV OUTE HLIAV OUTE O PROFHTHV
04J-JOHN-01-26 APEKRIYH AUTOIV O IWANNHV LEGWN EGW BAPTIZW EN UDATI MESOV DE UMWN ESTHKEN ON UMEIV OUK OIDATE
04J-JOHN-01-27 AUTOV ESTIN O OPISW MOU ERCOMENOV OV EMPROSYEN MOU GEGONEN OU EGW OUK EIMI AXIOV INA LUSW AUTOU TON IMANTA TOU UPODHMATOV
04J-JOHN-01-28 TAUTA EN BHYANIA EGENETO PERAN TOU IORDANOU OPOU HN IWANNHV BAPTIZWN
04J-JOHN-01-29 TH EPAURION BLEPEI TON IHSOUN ERCOMENON PROV AUTON KAI LEGEI IDE O AMNOV TOU YEOU O AIRWN THN AMARTIAN TOU KOSMOU
04J-JOHN-01-30 OUTOV ESTIN PERI OU EGW EIPON OPISW MOU ERCETAI ANHR OV EMPROSYEN MOU GEGONEN OTI PRWTOV MOU HN
04J-JOHN-01-31 KAGW OUK HDEIN AUTON ALL INA FANERWYH TW ISRAHL DIA TOUTO HLYON EGW EN TW UDATI BAPTIZWN
04J-JOHN-01-32 KAI EMARTURHSEN IWANNHV LEGWN OTI TEYEAMAI TO PNEUMA KATABAINON WSEI PERISTERAN EX OURANOU KAI EMEINEN EP AUTON
04J-JOHN-01-33 KAGW OUK HDEIN AUTON ALL O PEMQAV ME BAPTIZEIN EN UDATI EKEINOV MOI EIPEN EF ON AN IDHV TO PNEUMA KATABAINON KAI MENON EP AUTON OUTOV ESTIN O BAPTIZWN EN PNEUMATI AGIW
04J-JOHN-01-34 KAGW EWRAKA KAI MEMARTURHKA OTI OUTOV ESTIN O UIOV TOU YEOU
04J-JOHN-01-35 TH EPAURION PALIN EISTHKEI O IWANNHV KAI EK TWN MAYHTWN AUTOU DUO
04J-JOHN-01-36 KAI EMBLEQAV TW IHSOU PERIPATOUNTI LEGEI IDE O AMNOV TOU YEOU
04J-JOHN-01-37 KAI HKOUSAN AUTOU OI DUO MAYHTAI LALOUNTOV KAI HKOLOUYHSAN TW IHSOU
04J-JOHN-01-38 STRAFEIV DE O IHSOUV KAI YEASAMENOV AUTOUV AKOLOUYOUNTAV LEGEI AUTOIV TI ZHTEITE OI DE EIPON AUTW RABBI O LEGETAI ERMHNEUOMENON DIDASKALE POU MENEIV
04J-JOHN-01-39 LEGEI AUTOIV ERCESYE KAI IDETE HLYON KAI EIDON POU MENEI KAI PAR AUTW EMEINAN THN HMERAN EKEINHN WRA HN WV DEKATH
04J-JOHN-01-40 HN ANDREAV O ADELFOV SIMWNOV PETROU EIV EK TWN DUO TWN AKOUSANTWN PARA IWANNOU KAI AKOLOUYHSANTWN AUTW
04J-JOHN-01-41 EURISKEI OUTOV PRWTOV TON ADELFON TON IDION SIMWNA KAI LEGEI AUTW EURHKAMEN TON MESIAN O ESTIN MEYERMHNEUOMENON CRISTOV
04J-JOHN-01-42 KAI HGAGEN AUTON PROV TON IHSOUN EMBLEQAV AUTW O IHSOUV EIPEN SU EI SIMWN O UIOV IWNA SU KLHYHSH KHFAV O ERMHNEUETAI PETROV
04J-JOHN-01-43 TH EPAURION HYELHSEN EXELYEIN EIV THN GALILAIAN KAI EURISKEI FILIPPON KAI LEGEI AUTW O IHSOUV AKOLOUYEI MOI
04J-JOHN-01-44 HN DE O FILIPPOV APO BHYSAIDA EK THV POLEWV ANDREOU KAI PETROU
04J-JOHN-01-45 EURISKEI FILIPPOV TON NAYANAHL KAI LEGEI AUTW ON EGRAQEN MWSHV EN TW NOMW KAI OI PROFHTAI EURHKAMEN IHSOUN TON UION TOU IWSHF TON APO NAZARET
04J-JOHN-01-46 KAI EIPEN AUTW NAYANAHL EK NAZARET DUNATAI TI AGAYON EINAI LEGEI AUTW FILIPPOV ERCOU KAI IDE
04J-JOHN-01-47 EIDEN O IHSOUV TON NAYANAHL ERCOMENON PROV AUTON KAI LEGEI PERI AUTOU IDE ALHYWV ISRAHLITHV EN W DOLOV OUK ESTIN
04J-JOHN-01-48 LEGEI AUTW NAYANAHL POYEN ME GINWSKEIV APEKRIYH IHSOUV KAI EIPEN AUTW PRO TOU SE FILIPPON FWNHSAI ONTA UPO THN SUKHN EIDON SE
04J-JOHN-01-49 APEKRIYH NAYANAHL KAI LEGEI AUTW RABBI SU EI O UIOV TOU YEOU SU EI O BASILEUV TOU ISRAHL
04J-JOHN-01-50 APEKRIYH IHSOUV KAI EIPEN AUTW OTI EIPON SOI EIDON SE UPOKATW THV SUKHV PISTEUEIV MEIZW TOUTWN OQEI
04J-JOHN-01-51 KAI LEGEI AUTW AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN AP ARTI OQESYE TON OURANON ANEWGOTA KAI TOUV AGGELOUV TOU YEOU ANABAINONTAV KAI KATABAINONTAV EPI TON UION TOU ANYRWPOU
04J-JOHN-02-01 KAI TH HMERA TH TRITH GAMOV EGENETO EN KANA THV GALILAIAV KAI HN H MHTHR TOU IHSOU EKEI
04J-JOHN-02-02 EKLHYH DE KAI O IHSOUV KAI OI MAYHTAI AUTOU EIV TON GAMON
04J-JOHN-02-03 KAI USTERHSANTOV OINOU LEGEI H MHTHR TOU IHSOU PROV AUTON OINON OUK ECOUSIN
04J-JOHN-02-04 LEGEI AUTH O IHSOUV TI EMOI KAI SOI GUNAI OUPW HKEI H WRA MOU
04J-JOHN-02-05 LEGEI H MHTHR AUTOU TOIV DIAKONOIV O TI AN LEGH UMIN POIHSATE
04J-JOHN-02-06 HSAN DE EKEI UDRIAI LIYINAI EX KEIMENAI KATA TON KAYARISMON TWN IOUDAIWN CWROUSAI ANA METRHTAV DUO H TREIV
04J-JOHN-02-07 LEGEI AUTOIV O IHSOUV GEMISATE TAV UDRIAV UDATOV KAI EGEMISAN AUTAV EWV ANW
04J-JOHN-02-08 KAI LEGEI AUTOIV ANTLHSATE NUN KAI FERETE TW ARCITRIKLINW KAI HNEGKAN
04J-JOHN-02-09 WV DE EGEUSATO O ARCITRIKLINOV TO UDWR OINON GEGENHMENON KAI OUK HDEI POYEN ESTIN OI DE DIAKONOI HDEISAN OI HNTLHKOTEV TO UDWR FWNEI TON NUMFION O ARCITRIKLINOV
04J-JOHN-02-10 KAI LEGEI AUTW PAV ANYRWPOV PRWTON TON KALON OINON TIYHSIN KAI OTAN MEYUSYWSIN TOTE TON ELASSW SU TETHRHKAV TON KALON OINON EWV ARTI
04J-JOHN-02-11 TAUTHN EPOIHSEN THN ARCHN TWN SHMEIWN O IHSOUV EN KANA THV GALILAIAV KAI EFANERWSEN THN DOXAN AUTOU KAI EPISTEUSAN EIV AUTON OI MAYHTAI AUTOU
04J-JOHN-02-12 META TOUTO KATEBH EIV KAPERNAOUM AUTOV KAI H MHTHR AUTOU KAI OI ADELFOI AUTOU KAI OI MAYHTAI AUTOU KAI EKEI EMEINAN OU POLLAV HMERAV
04J-JOHN-02-13 KAI EGGUV HN TO PASCA TWN IOUDAIWN KAI ANEBH EIV IEROSOLUMA O IHSOUV
04J-JOHN-02-14 KAI EUREN EN TW IERW TOUV PWLOUNTAV BOAV KAI PROBATA KAI PERISTERAV KAI TOUV KERMATISTAV KAYHMENOUV
04J-JOHN-02-15 KAI POIHSAV FRAGELLION EK SCOINIWN PANTAV EXEBALEN EK TOU IEROU TA TE PROBATA KAI TOUV BOAV KAI TWN KOLLUBISTWN EXECEEN TO KERMA KAI TAV TRAPEZAV ANESTREQEN
04J-JOHN-02-16 KAI TOIV TAV PERISTERAV PWLOUSIN EIPEN ARATE TAUTA ENTEUYEN MH POIEITE TON OIKON TOU PATROV MOU OIKON EMPORIOU
04J-JOHN-02-17 EMNHSYHSAN DE OI MAYHTAI AUTOU OTI GEGRAMMENON ESTIN O ZHLOV TOU OIKOU SOU KATAFAGETAI ME
04J-JOHN-02-18 APEKRIYHSAN OUN OI IOUDAIOI KAI EIPON AUTW TI SHMEION DEIKNUEIV HMIN OTI TAUTA POIEIV
04J-JOHN-02-19 APEKRIYH IHSOUV KAI EIPEN AUTOIV LUSATE TON NAON TOUTON KAI EN TRISIN HMERAIV EGERW AUTON
04J-JOHN-02-20 EIPON OUN OI IOUDAIOI TESSARAKONTA KAI EX ETESIN WKODOMHYH O NAOV OUTOV KAI SU EN TRISIN HMERAIV EGEREIV AUTON
04J-JOHN-02-21 EKEINOV DE ELEGEN PERI TOU NAOU TOU SWMATOV AUTOU
04J-JOHN-02-22 OTE OUN HGERYH EK NEKRWN EMNHSYHSAN OI MAYHTAI AUTOU OTI TOUTO ELEGEN KAI EPISTEUSAN TH GRAFH KAI TW LOGW W EIPEN O IHSOUV
04J-JOHN-02-23 WV DE HN EN TOIV IEROSOLUMOIV EN TW PASCA EN TH EORTH POLLOI EPISTEUSAN EIV TO ONOMA AUTOU YEWROUNTEV AUTOU TA SHMEIA A EPOIEI
04J-JOHN-02-24 AUTOV DE O IHSOUV OUK EPISTEUEN EAUTON AUTOIV DIA TO AUTON GINWSKEIN PANTAV
04J-JOHN-02-25 KAI OTI OU CREIAN EICEN INA TIV MARTURHSH PERI TOU ANYRWPOU AUTOV GAR EGINWSKEN TI HN EN TW ANYRWPW
04J-JOHN-03-01 HN DE ANYRWPOV EK TWN FARISAIWN NIKODHMOV ONOMA AUTW ARCWN TWN IOUDAIWN
04J-JOHN-03-02 OUTOV HLYEN PROV AUTON NUKTOV KAI EIPEN AUTW RABBI OIDAMEN OTI APO YEOU ELHLUYAV DIDASKALOV OUDEIV GAR TAUTA TA SHMEIA DUNATAI POIEIN A SU POIEIV EAN MH H O YEOV MET AUTOU
04J-JOHN-03-03 APEKRIYH O IHSOUV KAI EIPEN AUTW AMHN AMHN LEGW SOI EAN MH TIV GENNHYH ANWYEN OU DUNATAI IDEIN THN BASILEIAN TOU YEOU
04J-JOHN-03-04 LEGEI PROV AUTON O NIKODHMOV PWV DUNATAI ANYRWPOV GENNHYHNAI GERWN WN MH DUNATAI EIV THN KOILIAN THV MHTROV AUTOU DEUTERON EISELYEIN KAI GENNHYHNAI
04J-JOHN-03-05 APEKRIYH IHSOUV AMHN AMHN LEGW SOI EAN MH TIV GENNHYH EX UDATOV KAI PNEUMATOV OU DUNATAI EISELYEIN EIV THN BASILEIAN TOU YEOU
04J-JOHN-03-06 TO GEGENNHMENON EK THV SARKOV SARX ESTIN KAI TO GEGENNHMENON EK TOU PNEUMATOV PNEUMA ESTIN
04J-JOHN-03-07 MH YAUMASHV OTI EIPON SOI DEI UMAV GENNHYHNAI ANWYEN
04J-JOHN-03-08 TO PNEUMA OPOU YELEI PNEI KAI THN FWNHN AUTOU AKOUEIV ALL OUK OIDAV POYEN ERCETAI KAI POU UPAGEI OUTWV ESTIN PAV O GEGENNHMENOV EK TOU PNEUMATOV
04J-JOHN-03-09 APEKRIYH NIKODHMOV KAI EIPEN AUTW PWV DUNATAI TAUTA GENESYAI
04J-JOHN-03-10 APEKRIYH IHSOUV KAI EIPEN AUTW SU EI O DIDASKALOV TOU ISRAHL KAI TAUTA OU GINWSKEIV
04J-JOHN-03-11 AMHN AMHN LEGW SOI OTI O OIDAMEN LALOUMEN KAI O EWRAKAMEN MARTUROUMEN KAI THN MARTURIAN HMWN OU LAMBANETE
04J-JOHN-03-12 EI TA EPIGEIA EIPON UMIN KAI OU PISTEUETE PWV EAN EIPW UMIN TA EPOURANIA PISTEUSETE
04J-JOHN-03-13 KAI OUDEIV ANABEBHKEN EIV TON OURANON EI MH O EK TOU OURANOU KATABAV O UIOV TOU ANYRWPOU O WN EN TW OURANW
04J-JOHN-03-14 KAI KAYWV MWSHV UQWSEN TON OFIN EN TH ERHMW OUTWV UQWYHNAI DEI TON UION TOU ANYRWPOU
04J-JOHN-03-15 INA PAV O PISTEUWN EIV AUTON MH APOLHTAI ALL ECH ZWHN AIWNION
04J-JOHN-03-16 OUTWV GAR HGAPHSEN O YEOV TON KOSMON WSTE TON UION AUTOU TON MONOGENH EDWKEN INA PAV O PISTEUWN EIV AUTON MH APOLHTAI ALL ECH ZWHN AIWNION
04J-JOHN-03-17 OU GAR APESTEILEN O YEOV TON UION AUTOU EIV TON KOSMON INA KRINH TON KOSMON ALL INA SWYH O KOSMOV DI AUTOU
04J-JOHN-03-18 O PISTEUWN EIV AUTON OU KRINETAI O DE MH PISTEUWN HDH KEKRITAI OTI MH PEPISTEUKEN EIV TO ONOMA TOU MONOGENOUV UIOU TOU YEOU
04J-JOHN-03-19 AUTH DE ESTIN H KRISIV OTI TO FWV ELHLUYEN EIV TON KOSMON KAI HGAPHSAN OI ANYRWPOI MALLON TO SKOTOV H TO FWV HN GAR PONHRA AUTWN TA ERGA
04J-JOHN-03-20 PAV GAR O FAULA PRASSWN MISEI TO FWV KAI OUK ERCETAI PROV TO FWV INA MH ELEGCYH TA ERGA AUTOU
04J-JOHN-03-21 O DE POIWN THN ALHYEIAN ERCETAI PROV TO FWV INA FANERWYH AUTOU TA ERGA OTI EN YEW ESTIN EIRGASMENA
04J-JOHN-03-22 META TAUTA HLYEN O IHSOUV KAI OI MAYHTAI AUTOU EIV THN IOUDAIAN GHN KAI EKEI DIETRIBEN MET AUTWN KAI EBAPTIZEN
04J-JOHN-03-23 HN DE KAI IWANNHV BAPTIZWN EN AINWN EGGUV TOU SALHM OTI UDATA POLLA HN EKEI KAI PAREGINONTO KAI EBAPTIZONTO
04J-JOHN-03-24 OUPW GAR HN BEBLHMENOV EIV THN FULAKHN O IWANNHV
04J-JOHN-03-25 EGENETO OUN ZHTHSIV EK TWN MAYHTWN IWANNOU META IOUDAIOU PERI KAYARISMOU
04J-JOHN-03-26 KAI HLYON PROV TON IWANNHN KAI EIPON AUTW RABBI OV HN META SOU PERAN TOU IORDANOU W SU MEMARTURHKAV IDE OUTOV BAPTIZEI KAI PANTEV ERCONTAI PROV AUTON
04J-JOHN-03-27 APEKRIYH IWANNHV KAI EIPEN OU DUNATAI ANYRWPOV LAMBANEIN OUDEN EAN MH H DEDOMENON AUTW EK TOU OURANOU

04J-JOHN-03-29 O ECWN THN NUMFHN NUMFIOV ESTIN O DE FILOV TOU NUMFIOU O ESTHKWV KAI AKOUWN AUTOU CARA CAIREI DIA THN FWNHN TOU NUMFIOU AUTH OUN H CARA H EMH PEPLHRWTAI
04J-JOHN-03-30 EKEINON DEI AUXANEIN EME DE ELATTOUSYAI
04J-JOHN-03-31 O ANWYEN ERCOMENOV EPANW PANTWN ESTIN O WN EK THV GHV EK THV GHV ESTIN KAI EK THV GHV LALEI O EK TOU OURANOU ERCOMENOV EPANW PANTWN ESTIN
04J-JOHN-03-32 KAI O EWRAKEN KAI HKOUSEN TOUTO MARTUREI KAI THN MARTURIAN AUTOU OUDEIV LAMBANEI
04J-JOHN-03-33 O LABWN AUTOU THN MARTURIAN ESFRAGISEN OTI O YEOV ALHYHV ESTIN
04J-JOHN-03-34 ON GAR APESTEILEN O YEOV TA RHMATA TOU YEOU LALEI OU GAR EK METROU DIDWSIN O YEOV TO PNEUMA

04J-JOHN-04-01 WV OUN EGNW O KURIOV OTI HKOUSAN OI FARISAIOI OTI IHSOUV PLEIONAV MAYHTAV POIEI KAI BAPTIZEI H IWANNHV
04J-JOHN-04-02 KAITOIGE IHSOUV AUTOV OUK EBAPTIZEN ALL OI MAYHTAI AUTOU
04J-JOHN-04-03 AFHKEN THN IOUDAIAN KAI APHLYEN EIV THN GALILAIAN
04J-JOHN-04-04 EDEI DE AUTON DIERCESYAI DIA THV SAMAREIAV
04J-JOHN-04-05 ERCETAI OUN EIV POLIN THV SAMAREIAV LEGOMENHN SUCAR PLHSION TOU CWRIOU O EDWKEN IAKWB IWSHF TW UIW AUTOU
04J-JOHN-04-06 HN DE EKEI PHGH TOU IAKWB O OUN IHSOUV KEKOPIAKWV EK THV ODOIPORIAV EKAYEZETO OUTWV EPI TH PHGH WRA HN WSEI EKTH
04J-JOHN-04-07 ERCETAI GUNH EK THV SAMAREIAV ANTLHSAI UDWR LEGEI AUTH O IHSOUV DOV MOI PIEIN
04J-JOHN-04-08 OI GAR MAYHTAI AUTOU APELHLUYEISAN EIV THN POLIN INA TROFAV AGORASWSIN
04J-JOHN-04-09 LEGEI OUN AUTW H GUNH H SAMAREITIV PWV SU IOUDAIOV WN PAR EMOU PIEIN AITEIV OUSHV GUNAIKOV SAMAREITIDOV OU GAR SUGCRWNTAI IOUDAIOI SAMAREITAIV
04J-JOHN-04-10 APEKRIYH IHSOUV KAI EIPEN AUTH EI HDEIV THN DWREAN TOU YEOU KAI TIV ESTIN O LEGWN SOI DOV MOI PIEIN SU AN HTHSAV AUTON KAI EDWKEN AN SOI UDWR ZWN
04J-JOHN-04-11 LEGEI AUTW H GUNH KURIE OUTE ANTLHMA ECEIV KAI TO FREAR ESTIN BAYU POYEN OUN ECEIV TO UDWR TO ZWN
04J-JOHN-04-12 MH SU MEIZWN EI TOU PATROV HMWN IAKWB OV EDWKEN HMIN TO FREAR KAI AUTOV EX AUTOU EPIEN KAI OI UIOI AUTOU KAI TA YREMMATA AUTOU
04J-JOHN-04-13 APEKRIYH IHSOUV KAI EIPEN AUTH PAV O PINWN EK TOU UDATOV TOUTOU DIQHSEI PALIN
04J-JOHN-04-14 OV D AN PIH EK TOU UDATOV OU EGW DWSW AUTW OU MH DIQHSH EIV TON AIWNA ALLA TO UDWR O DWSW AUTW GENHSETAI EN AUTW PHGH UDATOV ALLOMENOU EIV ZWHN AIWNION
04J-JOHN-04-15 LEGEI PROV AUTON H GUNH KURIE DOV MOI TOUTO TO UDWR INA MH DIQW MHDE ERCOMAI ENYADE ANTLEIN
04J-JOHN-04-16 LEGEI AUTH O IHSOUV UPAGE FWNHSON TON ANDRA SOU KAI ELYE ENYADE
04J-JOHN-04-17 APEKRIYH H GUNH KAI EIPEN OUK ECW ANDRA LEGEI AUTH O IHSOUV KALWV EIPAV OTI ANDRA OUK ECW
04J-JOHN-04-18 PENTE GAR ANDRAV ESCEV KAI NUN ON ECEIV OUK ESTIN SOU ANHR TOUTO ALHYEV EIRHKAV
04J-JOHN-04-19 LEGEI AUTW H GUNH KURIE YEWRW OTI PROFHTHV EI SU
04J-JOHN-04-20 OI PATEREV HMWN EN TW OREI TOUTW PROSEKUNHSAN KAI UMEIV LEGETE OTI EN IEROSOLUMOIV ESTIN O TOPOV OPOU DEI PROSKUNEIN
04J-JOHN-04-21 LEGEI AUTH O IHSOUV GUNAI PISTEUSON MOI OTI ERCETAI WRA OTE OUTE EN TW OREI TOUTW OUTE EN IEROSOLUMOIV PROSKUNHSETE TW PATRI
04J-JOHN-04-22 UMEIV PROSKUNEITE O OUK OIDATE HMEIV PROSKUNOUMEN O OIDAMEN OTI H SWTHRIA EK TWN IOUDAIWN ESTIN
04J-JOHN-04-23 ALL ERCETAI WRA KAI NUN ESTIN OTE OI ALHYINOI PROSKUNHTAI PROSKUNHSOUSIN TW PATRI EN PNEUMATI KAI ALHYEIA KAI GAR O PATHR TOIOUTOUV ZHTEI TOUV PROSKUNOUNTAV AUTON
04J-JOHN-04-24 PNEUMA O YEOV KAI TOUV PROSKUNOUNTAV AUTON EN PNEUMATI KAI ALHYEIA DEI PROSKUNEIN
04J-JOHN-04-25 LEGEI AUTW H GUNH OIDA OTI MESIAV ERCETAI O LEGOMENOV CRISTOV OTAN ELYH EKEINOV ANAGGELEI HMIN PANTA
04J-JOHN-04-26 LEGEI AUTH O IHSOUV EGW EIMI O LALWN SOI
04J-JOHN-04-27 KAI EPI TOUTW HLYON OI MAYHTAI AUTOU KAI EYAUMASAN OTI META GUNAIKOV ELALEI OUDEIV MENTOI EIPEN TI ZHTEIV H TI LALEIV MET AUTHV
04J-JOHN-04-28 AFHKEN OUN THN UDRIAN AUTHV H GUNH KAI APHLYEN EIV THN POLIN KAI LEGEI TOIV ANYRWPOIV
04J-JOHN-04-29 DEUTE IDETE ANYRWPON OV EIPEN MOI PANTA OSA EPOIHSA MHTI OUTOV ESTIN O CRISTOV
04J-JOHN-04-30 EXHLYON EK THV POLEWV KAI HRCONTO PROV AUTON
04J-JOHN-04-31 EN DE TW METAXU HRWTWN AUTON OI MAYHTAI LEGONTEV RABBI FAGE
04J-JOHN-04-32 O DE EIPEN AUTOIV EGW BRWSIN ECW FAGEIN HN UMEIV OUK OIDATE
04J-JOHN-04-33 ELEGON OUN OI MAYHTAI PROV ALLHLOUV MH TIV HNEGKEN AUTW FAGEIN
04J-JOHN-04-34 LEGEI AUTOIV O IHSOUV EMON BRWMA ESTIN INA POIW TO YELHMA TOU PEMQANTOV ME KAI TELEIWSW AUTOU TO ERGON
04J-JOHN-04-35 OUC UMEIV LEGETE OTI ETI TETRAMHNOV ESTIN KAI O YERISMOV ERCETAI IDOU LEGW UMIN EPARATE TOUV OFYALMOUV UMWN KAI YEASASYE TAV CWRAV OTI LEUKAI EISIN PROV YERISMON HDH
04J-JOHN-04-36 KAI O YERIZWN MISYON LAMBANEI KAI SUNAGEI KARPON EIV ZWHN AIWNION INA KAI O SPEIRWN OMOU CAIRH KAI O YERIZWN
04J-JOHN-04-37 EN GAR TOUTW O LOGOV ESTIN O ALHYINOV OTI ALLOV ESTIN O SPEIRWN KAI ALLOV O YERIZWN
04J-JOHN-04-38 EGW APESTEILA UMAV YERIZEIN O OUC UMEIV KEKOPIAKATE ALLOI KEKOPIAKASIN KAI UMEIV EIV TON KOPON AUTWN EISELHLUYATE
04J-JOHN-04-39 EK DE THV POLEWV EKEINHV POLLOI EPISTEUSAN EIV AUTON TWN SAMAREITWN DIA TON LOGON THV GUNAIKOV MARTUROUSHV OTI EIPEN MOI PANTA OSA EPOIHSA
04J-JOHN-04-40 WV OUN HLYON PROV AUTON OI SAMAREITAI HRWTWN AUTON MEINAI PAR AUTOIV KAI EMEINEN EKEI DUO HMERAV
04J-JOHN-04-41 KAI POLLW PLEIOUV EPISTEUSAN DIA TON LOGON AUTOU
04J-JOHN-04-42 TH TE GUNAIKI ELEGON OTI OUKETI DIA THN SHN LALIAN PISTEUOMEN AUTOI GAR AKHKOAMEN KAI OIDAMEN OTI OUTOV ESTIN ALHYWV O SWTHR TOU KOSMOU O CRISTOV
04J-JOHN-04-43 META DE TAV DUO HMERAV EXHLYEN EKEIYEN KAI APHLYEN EIV THN GALILAIAN
04J-JOHN-04-44 AUTOV GAR O IHSOUV EMARTURHSEN OTI PROFHTHV EN TH IDIA PATRIDI TIMHN OUK ECEI
04J-JOHN-04-45 OTE OUN HLYEN EIV THN GALILAIAN EDEXANTO AUTON OI GALILAIOI PANTA EWRAKOTEV A EPOIHSEN EN IEROSOLUMOIV EN TH EORTH KAI AUTOI GAR HLYON EIV THN EORTHN
04J-JOHN-04-46 HLYEN OUN PALIN O IHSOUV EIV THN KANA THV GALILAIAV OPOU EPOIHSEN TO UDWR OINON KAI HN TIV BASILIKOV OU O UIOV HSYENEI EN KAPERNAOUM
04J-JOHN-04-47 OUTOV AKOUSAV OTI IHSOUV HKEI EK THV IOUDAIAV EIV THN GALILAIAN APHLYEN PROV AUTON KAI HRWTA AUTON INA KATABH KAI IASHTAI AUTOU TON UION EMELLEN GAR APOYNHSKEIN
04J-JOHN-04-48 EIPEN OUN O IHSOUV PROV AUTON EAN MH SHMEIA KAI TERATA IDHTE OU MH PISTEUSHTE
04J-JOHN-04-49 LEGEI PROV AUTON O BASILIKOV KURIE KATABHYI PRIN APOYANEIN TO PAIDION MOU
04J-JOHN-04-50 LEGEI AUTW O IHSOUV POREUOU O UIOV SOU ZH KAI EPISTEUSEN O ANYRWPOV TW LOGW W EIPEN AUTW O IHSOUV KAI EPOREUETO
04J-JOHN-04-51 HDH DE AUTOU KATABAINONTOV OI DOULOI AUTOU APHNTHSAN AUTW KAI APHGGEILAN LEGONTEV OTI O PAIV SOU ZH
04J-JOHN-04-52 EPUYETO OUN PAR AUTWN THN WRAN EN H KOMQOTERON ESCEN KAI EIPON AUTW OTI CYEV WRAN EBDOMHN AFHKEN AUTON O PURETOV
04J-JOHN-04-53 EGNW OUN O PATHR OTI EN EKEINH TH WRA EN H EIPEN AUTW O IHSOUV OTI O UIOV SOU ZH KAI EPISTEUSEN AUTOV KAI H OIKIA AUTOU OLH
04J-JOHN-04-54 TOUTO PALIN DEUTERON SHMEION EPOIHSEN O IHSOUV ELYWN EK THV IOUDAIAV EIV THN GALILAIAN
04J-JOHN-05-01 META TAUTA HN H EORTH TWN IOUDAIWN KAI ANEBH O IHSOUV EIV IEROSOLUMA
04J-JOHN-05-02 ESTIN DE EN TOIV IEROSOLUMOIV EPI TH PROBATIKH KOLUMBHYRA H EPILEGOMENH EBRAISTI BHYESDA PENTE STOAV ECOUSA
04J-JOHN-05-03 EN TAUTAIV KATEKEITO PLHYOV POLU TWN ASYENOUNTWN TUFLWN CWLWN XHRWN EKDECOMENWN THN TOU UDATOV KINHSIN
04J-JOHN-05-04 AGGELOV GAR KATA KAIRON KATEBAINEN EN TH KOLUMBHYRA KAI ETARASSEN TO UDWR O OUN PRWTOV EMBAV META THN TARACHN TOU UDATOV UGIHV EGINETO W DHPOTE KATEICETO NOSHMATI
04J-JOHN-05-05 HN DE TIV ANYRWPOV EKEI TRIAKONTA OKTW ETH ECWN EN TH ASYENEIA
04J-JOHN-05-06 TOUTON IDWN O IHSOUV KATAKEIMENON KAI GNOUV OTI POLUN HDH CRONON ECEI LEGEI AUTW YELEIV UGIHV GENESYAI
04J-JOHN-05-07 APEKRIYH AUTW O ASYENWN KURIE ANYRWPON OUK ECW INA OTAN TARACYH TO UDWR BALH ME EIV THN KOLUMBHYRAN EN W DE ERCOMAI EGW ALLOV PRO EMOU KATABAINEI
04J-JOHN-05-08 LEGEI AUTW O IHSOUV EGEIRAI ARON TON KRABBATON SOU KAI PERIPATEI
04J-JOHN-05-09 KAI EUYEWV EGENETO UGIHV O ANYRWPOV KAI HREN TON KRABBATON AUTOU KAI PERIEPATEI HN DE SABBATON EN EKEINH TH HMERA
04J-JOHN-05-10 ELEGON OUN OI IOUDAIOI TW TEYERAPEUMENW SABBATON ESTIN OUK EXESTIN SOI ARAI TON KRABBATON
04J-JOHN-05-11 APEKRIYH AUTOIV O POIHSAV ME UGIH EKEINOV MOI EIPEN ARON TON KRABBATON SOU KAI PERIPATEI
04J-JOHN-05-12 HRWTHSAN OUN AUTON TIV ESTIN O ANYRWPOV O EIPWN SOI ARON TON KRABBATON SOU KAI PERIPATEI
04J-JOHN-05-13 O DE IAYEIV OUK HDEI TIV ESTIN O GAR IHSOUV EXENEUSEN OCLOU ONTOV EN TW TOPW
04J-JOHN-05-14 META TAUTA EURISKEI AUTON O IHSOUV EN TW IERW KAI EIPEN AUTW IDE UGIHV GEGONAV MHKETI AMARTANE INA MH CEIRON TI SOI GENHTAI
04J-JOHN-05-15 APHLYEN O ANYRWPOV KAI ANHGGEILEN TOIV IOUDAIOIV OTI IHSOUV ESTIN O POIHSAV AUTON UGIH
04J-JOHN-05-16 KAI DIA TOUTO EDIWKON TON IHSOUN OI IOUDAIOI KAI EZHTOUN AUTON APOKTEINAI OTI TAUTA EPOIEI EN SABBATW
04J-JOHN-05-17 O DE IHSOUV APEKRINATO AUTOIV O PATHR MOU EWV ARTI ERGAZETAI KAGW ERGAZOMAI
04J-JOHN-05-18 DIA TOUTO OUN MALLON EZHTOUN AUTON OI IOUDAIOI APOKTEINAI OTI OU MONON ELUEN TO SABBATON ALLA KAI PATERA IDION ELEGEN TON YEON ISON EAUTON POIWN TW YEW
04J-JOHN-05-19 APEKRINATO OUN O IHSOUV KAI EIPEN AUTOIV AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN OU DUNATAI O UIOV POIEIN AF EAUTOU OUDEN EAN MH TI BLEPH TON PATERA POIOUNTA A GAR AN EKEINOV POIH TAUTA KAI O UIOV OMOIWV POIEI
04J-JOHN-05-20 O GAR PATHR FILEI TON UION KAI PANTA DEIKNUSIN AUTW A AUTOV POIEI KAI MEIZONA TOUTWN DEIXEI AUTW ERGA INA UMEIV YAUMAZHTE
04J-JOHN-05-21 WSPER GAR O PATHR EGEIREI TOUV NEKROUV KAI ZWOPOIEI OUTWV KAI O UIOV OUV YELEI ZWOPOIEI
04J-JOHN-05-22 OUDE GAR O PATHR KRINEI OUDENA ALLA THN KRISIN PASAN DEDWKEN TW UIW
04J-JOHN-05-23 INA PANTEV TIMWSIN TON UION KAYWV TIMWSIN TON PATERA O MH TIMWN TON UION OU TIMA TON PATERA TON PEMQANTA AUTON
04J-JOHN-05-24 AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN OTI O TON LOGON MOU AKOUWN KAI PISTEUWN TW PEMQANTI ME ECEI ZWHN AIWNION KAI EIV KRISIN OUK ERCETAI ALLA METABEBHKEN EK TOU YANATOU EIV THN ZWHN
04J-JOHN-05-25 AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN OTI ERCETAI WRA KAI NUN ESTIN OTE OI NEKROI AKOUSONTAI THV FWNHV TOU UIOU TOU YEOU KAI OI AKOUSANTEV ZHSONTAI
04J-JOHN-05-26 WSPER GAR O PATHR ECEI ZWHN EN EAUTW OUTWV EDWKEN KAI TW UIW ZWHN ECEIN EN EAUTW
04J-JOHN-05-27 KAI EXOUSIAN EDWKEN AUTW KAI KRISIN POIEIN OTI UIOV ANYRWPOU ESTIN
04J-JOHN-05-28 MH YAUMAZETE TOUTO OTI ERCETAI WRA EN H PANTEV OI EN TOIV MNHMEIOIV AKOUSONTAI THV FWNHV AUTOU
04J-JOHN-05-29 KAI EKPOREUSONTAI OI TA AGAYA POIHSANTEV EIV ANASTASIN ZWHV OI DE TA FAULA PRAXANTEV EIV ANASTASIN KRISEWV
04J-JOHN-05-30 OU DUNAMAI EGW POIEIN AP EMAUTOU OUDEN KAYWV AKOUW KRINW KAI H KRISIV H EMH DIKAIA ESTIN OTI OU ZHTW TO YELHMA TO EMON ALLA TO YELHMA TOU PEMQANTOV ME PATROV
04J-JOHN-05-31 EAN EGW MARTURW PERI EMAUTOU H MARTURIA MOU OUK ESTIN ALHYHV
04J-JOHN-05-32 ALLOV ESTIN O MARTURWN PERI EMOU KAI OIDA OTI ALHYHV ESTIN H MARTURIA HN MARTUREI PERI EMOU
04J-JOHN-05-33 UMEIV APESTALKATE PROV IWANNHN KAI MEMARTURHKEN TH ALHYEIA
04J-JOHN-05-34 EGW DE OU PARA ANYRWPOU THN MARTURIAN LAMBANW ALLA TAUTA LEGW INA UMEIV SWYHTE
04J-JOHN-05-35 EKEINOV HN O LUCNOV O KAIOMENOV KAI FAINWN UMEIV DE HYELHSATE AGALLIAYHNAI PROV WRAN EN TW FWTI AUTOU
04J-JOHN-05-36 EGW DE ECW THN MARTURIAN MEIZW TOU IWANNOU TA GAR ERGA A EDWKEN MOI O PATHR INA TELEIWSW AUTA AUTA TA ERGA A EGW POIW MARTUREI PERI EMOU OTI O PATHR ME APESTALKEN
04J-JOHN-05-37 KAI O PEMQAV ME PATHR AUTOV MEMARTURHKEN PERI EMOU OUTE FWNHN AUTOU AKHKOATE PWPOTE OUTE EIDOV AUTOU EWRAKATE
04J-JOHN-05-38 KAI TON LOGON AUTOU OUK ECETE MENONTA EN UMIN OTI ON APESTEILEN EKEINOV TOUTW UMEIV OU PISTEUETE
04J-JOHN-05-39 EREUNATE TAV GRAFAV OTI UMEIV DOKEITE EN AUTAIV ZWHN AIWNION ECEIN KAI EKEINAI EISIN AI MARTUROUSAI PERI EMOU
04J-JOHN-05-40 KAI OU YELETE ELYEIN PROV ME INA ZWHN ECHTE
04J-JOHN-05-41 DOXAN PARA ANYRWPWN OU LAMBANW
04J-JOHN-05-42 ALL EGNWKA UMAV OTI THN AGAPHN TOU YEOU OUK ECETE EN EAUTOIV
04J-JOHN-05-43 EGW ELHLUYA EN TW ONOMATI TOU PATROV MOU KAI OU LAMBANETE ME EAN ALLOV ELYH EN TW ONOMATI TW IDIW EKEINON LHQESYE
04J-JOHN-05-44 PWV DUNASYE UMEIV PISTEUSAI DOXAN PARA ALLHLWN LAMBANONTEV KAI THN DOXAN THN PARA TOU MONOU YEOU OU ZHTEITE
04J-JOHN-05-45 MH DOKEITE OTI EGW KATHGORHSW UMWN PROV TON PATERA ESTIN O KATHGORWN UMWN MWSHV EIV ON UMEIV HLPIKATE
04J-JOHN-05-46 EI GAR EPISTEUETE MWSH EPISTEUETE AN EMOI PERI GAR EMOU EKEINOV EGRAQEN
04J-JOHN-05-47 EI DE TOIV EKEINOU GRAMMASIN OU PISTEUETE PWV TOIV EMOIV RHMASIN PISTEUSETE
04J-JOHN-06-01 META TAUTA APHLYEN O IHSOUV PERAN THV YALASSHV THV GALILAIAV THV TIBERIADOV
04J-JOHN-06-02 KAI HKOLOUYEI AUTW OCLOV POLUV OTI EWRWN AUTOU TA SHMEIA A EPOIEI EPI TWN ASYENOUNTWN
04J-JOHN-06-03 ANHLYEN DE EIV TO OROV O IHSOUV KAI EKEI EKAYHTO META TWN MAYHTWN AUTOU
04J-JOHN-06-04 HN DE EGGUV TO PASCA H EORTH TWN IOUDAIWN
04J-JOHN-06-05 EPARAV OUN O IHSOUV TOUV OFYALMOUV KAI YEASAMENOV OTI POLUV OCLOV ERCETAI PROV AUTON LEGEI PROV TON FILIPPON POYEN AGORASOMEN ARTOUV INA FAGWSIN OUTOI
04J-JOHN-06-06 TOUTO DE ELEGEN PEIRAZWN AUTON AUTOV GAR HDEI TI EMELLEN POIEIN
04J-JOHN-06-07 APEKRIYH AUTW FILIPPOV DIAKOSIWN DHNARIWN ARTOI OUK ARKOUSIN AUTOIV INA EKASTOV AUTWN BRACU TI LABH
04J-JOHN-06-08 LEGEI AUTW EIV EK TWN MAYHTWN AUTOU ANDREAV O ADELFOV SIMWNOV PETROU
04J-JOHN-06-09 ESTIN PAIDARION EN WDE O ECEI PENTE ARTOUV KRIYINOUV KAI DUO OQARIA ALLA TAUTA TI ESTIN EIV TOSOUTOUV
04J-JOHN-06-10 EIPEN DE O IHSOUV POIHSATE TOUV ANYRWPOUV ANAPESEIN HN DE CORTOV POLUV EN TW TOPW ANEPESON OUN OI ANDREV TON ARIYMON WSEI PENTAKISCILIOI
04J-JOHN-06-11 ELABEN DE TOUV ARTOUV O IHSOUV KAI EUCARISTHSAV DIEDWKEN TOIV MAYHTAIV OI DE MAYHTAI TOIV ANAKEIMENOIV OMOIWV KAI EK TWN OQARIWN OSON HYELON
04J-JOHN-06-12 WV DE ENEPLHSYHSAN LEGEI TOIV MAYHTAIV AUTOU SUNAGAGETE TA PERISSEUSANTA KLASMATA INA MH TI APOLHTAI
04J-JOHN-06-13 SUNHGAGON OUN KAI EGEMISAN DWDEKA KOFINOUV KLASMATWN EK TWN PENTE ARTWN TWN KRIYINWN A EPERISSEUSEN TOIV BEBRWKOSIN
04J-JOHN-06-14 OI OUN ANYRWPOI IDONTEV O EPOIHSEN SHMEION O IHSOUV ELEGON OTI OUTOV ESTIN ALHYWV O PROFHTHV O ERCOMENOV EIV TON KOSMON
04J-JOHN-06-15 IHSOUV OUN GNOUV OTI MELLOUSIN ERCESYAI KAI ARPAZEIN AUTON INA POIHSWSIN AUTON BASILEA ANECWRHSEN EIV TO OROV AUTOV MONOV
04J-JOHN-06-16 WV DE OQIA EGENETO KATEBHSAN OI MAYHTAI AUTOU EPI THN YALASSAN
04J-JOHN-06-17 KAI EMBANTEV EIV TO PLOION HRCONTO PERAN THV YALASSHV EIV KAPERNAOUM KAI SKOTIA HDH EGEGONEI KAI OUK ELHLUYEI PROV AUTOUV O IHSOUV
04J-JOHN-06-18 H TE YALASSA ANEMOU MEGALOU PNEONTOV DIHGEIRETO
04J-JOHN-06-19 ELHLAKOTEV OUN WV STADIOUV EIKOSI PENTE H TRIAKONTA YEWROUSIN TON IHSOUN PERIPATOUNTA EPI THV YALASSHV KAI EGGUV TOU PLOIOU GINOMENON KAI EFOBHYHSAN
04J-JOHN-06-20 O DE LEGEI AUTOIV EGW EIMI MH FOBEISYE
04J-JOHN-06-21 HYELON OUN LABEIN AUTON EIV TO PLOION KAI EUYEWV TO PLOION EGENETO EPI THV GHV EIV HN UPHGON
04J-JOHN-06-22 TH EPAURION O OCLOV O ESTHKWV PERAN THV YALASSHV IDWN OTI PLOIARION ALLO OUK HN EKEI EI MH EN EKEINO EIV O ENEBHSAN OI MAYHTAI AUTOU KAI OTI OU SUNEISHLYEN TOIV MAYHTAIV AUTOU O IHSOUV EIV TO PLOIARION ALLA MONOI OI MAYHTAI AUTOU APHLYON
04J-JOHN-06-23 ALLA DE HLYEN PLOIARIA EK TIBERIADOV EGGUV TOU TOPOU OPOU EFAGON TON ARTON EUCARISTHSANTOV TOU KURIOU
04J-JOHN-06-24 OTE OUN EIDEN O OCLOV OTI IHSOUV OUK ESTIN EKEI OUDE OI MAYHTAI AUTOU ENEBHSAN AUTOI EIV TA PLOIA KAI HLYON EIV KAPERNAOUM ZHTOUNTEV TON IHSOUN
04J-JOHN-06-25 KAI EURONTEV AUTON PERAN THV YALASSHV EIPON AUTW RABBI POTE WDE GEGONAV
04J-JOHN-06-26 APEKRIYH AUTOIV O IHSOUV KAI EIPEN AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN ZHTEITE ME OUC OTI EIDETE SHMEIA ALL OTI EFAGETE EK TWN ARTWN KAI ECORTASYHTE
04J-JOHN-06-27 ERGAZESYE MH THN BRWSIN THN APOLLUMENHN ALLA THN BRWSIN THN MENOUSAN EIV ZWHN AIWNION HN O UIOV TOU ANYRWPOU UMIN DWSEI TOUTON GAR O PATHR ESFRAGISEN O YEOV
04J-JOHN-06-28 EIPON OUN PROV AUTON TI POIWMEN INA ERGAZWMEYA TA ERGA TOU YEOU
04J-JOHN-06-29 APEKRIYH IHSOUV KAI EIPEN AUTOIV TOUTO ESTIN TO ERGON TOU YEOU INA PISTEUSHTE EIV ON APESTEILEN EKEINOV
04J-JOHN-06-30 EIPON OUN AUTW TI OUN POIEIV SU SHMEION INA IDWMEN KAI PISTEUSWMEN SOI TI ERGAZH
04J-JOHN-06-31 OI PATEREV HMWN TO MANNA EFAGON EN TH ERHMW KAYWV ESTIN GEGRAMMENON ARTON EK TOU OURANOU EDWKEN AUTOIV FAGEIN
04J-JOHN-06-32 EIPEN OUN AUTOIV O IHSOUV AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN OU MWSHV DEDWKEN UMIN TON ARTON EK TOU OURANOU ALL O PATHR MOU DIDWSIN UMIN TON ARTON EK TOU OURANOU TON ALHYINON
04J-JOHN-06-33 O GAR ARTOV TOU YEOU ESTIN O KATABAINWN EK TOU OURANOU KAI ZWHN DIDOUV TW KOSMW
04J-JOHN-06-34 EIPON OUN PROV AUTON KURIE PANTOTE DOV HMIN TON ARTON TOUTON
04J-JOHN-06-35 EIPEN DE AUTOIV O IHSOUV EGW EIMI O ARTOV THV ZWHV O ERCOMENOV PROV ME OU MH PEINASH KAI O PISTEUWN EIV EME OU MH DIQHSH PWPOTE
04J-JOHN-06-36 ALL EIPON UMIN OTI KAI EWRAKATE ME KAI OU PISTEUETE
04J-JOHN-06-37 PAN O DIDWSIN MOI O PATHR PROV EME HXEI KAI TON ERCOMENON PROV ME OU MH EKBALW EXW
04J-JOHN-06-38 OTI KATABEBHKA EK TOU OURANOU OUC INA POIW TO YELHMA TO EMON ALLA TO YELHMA TOU PEMQANTOV ME
04J-JOHN-06-39 TOUTO DE ESTIN TO YELHMA TOU PEMQANTOV ME PATROV INA PAN O DEDWKEN MOI MH APOLESW EX AUTOU ALLA ANASTHSW AUTO TH ESCATH HMERA
04J-JOHN-06-40 TOUTO DE ESTIN TO YELHMA TOU PEMQANTOV ME INA PAV O YEWRWN TON UION KAI PISTEUWN EIV AUTON ECH ZWHN AIWNION KAI ANASTHSW AUTON EGW TH ESCATH HMERA
04J-JOHN-06-41 EGOGGUZON OUN OI IOUDAIOI PERI AUTOU OTI EIPEN EGW EIMI O ARTOV O KATABAV EK TOU OURANOU
04J-JOHN-06-42 KAI ELEGON OUC OUTOV ESTIN IHSOUV O UIOV IWSHF OU HMEIV OIDAMEN TON PATERA KAI THN MHTERA PWV OUN LEGEI OUTOV OTI EK TOU OURANOU KATABEBHKA
04J-JOHN-06-43 APEKRIYH OUN O IHSOUV KAI EIPEN AUTOIV MH GOGGUZETE MET ALLHLWN
04J-JOHN-06-44 OUDEIV DUNATAI ELYEIN PROV ME EAN MH O PATHR O PEMQAV ME ELKUSH AUTON KAI EGW ANASTHSW AUTON EN TH ESCATH HMERA
04J-JOHN-06-45 ESTIN GEGRAMMENON EN TOIV PROFHTAIV KAI ESONTAI PANTEV DIDAKTOI YEOU PAV OUN O AKOUWN PARA TOU PATROV KAI MAYWN ERCETAI PROV ME
04J-JOHN-06-46 OUC OTI TON PATERA TIV EWRAKEN EI MH O WN PARA TOU YEOU OUTOV EWRAKEN TON PATERA
04J-JOHN-06-47 AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN O PISTEUWN EIV EME ECEI ZWHN AIWNION
04J-JOHN-06-48 EGW EIMI O ARTOV THV ZWHV
04J-JOHN-06-49 OI PATEREV UMWN EFAGON TO MANNA EN TH ERHMW KAI APEYANON
04J-JOHN-06-50 OUTOV ESTIN O ARTOV O EK TOU OURANOU KATABAINWN INA TIV EX AUTOU FAGH KAI MH APOYANH
04J-JOHN-06-51 EGW EIMI O ARTOV O ZWN O EK TOU OURANOU KATABAV EAN TIV FAGH EK TOUTOU TOU ARTOU ZHSETAI EIV TON AIWNA KAI O ARTOV DE ON EGW DWSW H SARX MOU ESTIN HN EGW DWSW UPER THV TOU KOSMOU ZWHV
04J-JOHN-06-52 EMACONTO OUN PROV ALLHLOUV OI IOUDAIOI LEGONTEV PWV DUNATAI OUTOV HMIN DOUNAI THN SARKA FAGEIN
04J-JOHN-06-53 EIPEN OUN AUTOIV O IHSOUV AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN EAN MH FAGHTE THN SARKA TOU UIOU TOU ANYRWPOU KAI PIHTE AUTOU TO AIMA OUK ECETE ZWHN EN EAUTOIV
04J-JOHN-06-54 O TRWGWN MOU THN SARKA KAI PINWN MOU TO AIMA ECEI ZWHN AIWNION KAI EGW ANASTHSW AUTON TH ESCATH HMERA
04J-JOHN-06-55 H GAR SARX MOU ALHYWV ESTIN BRWSIV KAI TO AIMA MOU ALHYWV ESTIN POSIV
04J-JOHN-06-56 O TRWGWN MOU THN SARKA KAI PINWN MOU TO AIMA EN EMOI MENEI KAGW EN AUTW
04J-JOHN-06-57 KAYWV APESTEILEN ME O ZWN PATHR KAGW ZW DIA TON PATERA KAI O TRWGWN ME KAKEINOV ZHSETAI DI EME
04J-JOHN-06-58 OUTOV ESTIN O ARTOV O EK TOU OURANOU KATABAV OU KAYWV EFAGON OI PATEREV UMWN TO MANNA KAI APEYANON O TRWGWN TOUTON TON ARTON ZHSETAI EIV TON AIWNA
04J-JOHN-06-59 TAUTA EIPEN EN SUNAGWGH DIDASKWN EN KAPERNAOUM
04J-JOHN-06-60 POLLOI OUN AKOUSANTEV EK TWN MAYHTWN AUTOU EIPON SKLHROV ESTIN OUTOV O LOGOV TIV DUNATAI AUTOU AKOUEIN
04J-JOHN-06-61 EIDWV DE O IHSOUV EN EAUTW OTI GOGGUZOUSIN PERI TOUTOU OI MAYHTAI AUTOU EIPEN AUTOIV TOUTO UMAV SKANDALIZEI
04J-JOHN-06-62 EAN OUN YEWRHTE TON UION TOU ANYRWPOU ANABAINONTA OPOU HN TO PROTERON
04J-JOHN-06-63 TO PNEUMA ESTIN TO ZWOPOIOUN H SARX OUK WFELEI OUDEN TA RHMATA A EGW LALW UMIN PNEUMA ESTIN KAI ZWH ESTIN
04J-JOHN-06-64 ALL EISIN EX UMWN TINEV OI OU PISTEUOUSIN HDEI GAR EX ARCHV O IHSOUV TINEV EISIN OI MH PISTEUONTEV KAI TIV ESTIN O PARADWSWN AUTON
04J-JOHN-06-65 KAI ELEGEN DIA TOUTO EIRHKA UMIN OTI OUDEIV DUNATAI ELYEIN PROV ME EAN MH H DEDOMENON AUTW EK TOU PATROV MOU
04J-JOHN-06-66 EK TOUTOU POLLOI APHLYON TWN MAYHTWN AUTOU EIV TA OPISW KAI OUKETI MET AUTOU PERIEPATOUN
04J-JOHN-06-67 EIPEN OUN O IHSOUV TOIV DWDEKA MH KAI UMEIV YELETE UPAGEIN

04J-JOHN-06-71 ELEGEN DE TON IOUDAN SIMWNOV ISKARIWTHN OUTOV GAR EMELLEN AUTON PARADIDONAI EIV WN EK TWN DWDEKA
04J-JOHN-07-01 KAI PERIEPATEI O IHSOUV META TAUTA EN TH GALILAIA OU GAR HYELEN EN TH IOUDAIA PERIPATEIN OTI EZHTOUN AUTON OI IOUDAIOI APOKTEINAI
04J-JOHN-07-02 HN DE EGGUV H EORTH TWN IOUDAIWN H SKHNOPHGIA
04J-JOHN-07-03 EIPON OUN PROV AUTON OI ADELFOI AUTOU METABHYI ENTEUYEN KAI UPAGE EIV THN IOUDAIAN INA KAI OI MAYHTAI SOU YEWRHSWSIN TA ERGA SOU A POIEIV
04J-JOHN-07-04 OUDEIV GAR EN KRUPTW TI POIEI KAI ZHTEI AUTOV EN PARRHSIA EINAI EI TAUTA POIEIV FANERWSON SEAUTON TW KOSMW
04J-JOHN-07-05 OUDE GAR OI ADELFOI AUTOU EPISTEUON EIV AUTON
04J-JOHN-07-06 LEGEI OUN AUTOIV O IHSOUV O KAIROV O EMOV OUPW PARESTIN O DE KAIROV O UMETEROV PANTOTE ESTIN ETOIMOV
04J-JOHN-07-07 OU DUNATAI O KOSMOV MISEIN UMAV EME DE MISEI OTI EGW MARTURW PERI AUTOU OTI TA ERGA AUTOU PONHRA ESTIN
04J-JOHN-07-08 UMEIV ANABHTE EIV THN EORTHN TAUTHN EGW OUPW ANABAINW EIV THN EORTHN TAUTHN OTI O KAIROV O EMOV OUPW PEPLHRWTAI
04J-JOHN-07-09 TAUTA DE EIPWN AUTOIV EMEINEN EN TH GALILAIA
04J-JOHN-07-10 WV DE ANEBHSAN OI ADELFOI AUTOU TOTE KAI AUTOV ANEBH EIV THN EORTHN OU FANERWV ALL WV EN KRUPTW
04J-JOHN-07-11 OI OUN IOUDAIOI EZHTOUN AUTON EN TH EORTH KAI ELEGON POU ESTIN EKEINOV
04J-JOHN-07-12 KAI GOGGUSMOV POLUV PERI AUTOU HN EN TOIV OCLOIV OI MEN ELEGON OTI AGAYOV ESTIN ALLOI ELEGON OU ALLA PLANA TON OCLON
04J-JOHN-07-13 OUDEIV MENTOI PARRHSIA ELALEI PERI AUTOU DIA TON FOBON TWN IOUDAIWN
04J-JOHN-07-14 HDH DE THV EORTHV MESOUSHV ANEBH O IHSOUV EIV TO IERON KAI EDIDASKEN
04J-JOHN-07-15 KAI EYAUMAZON OI IOUDAIOI LEGONTEV PWV OUTOV GRAMMATA OIDEN MH MEMAYHKWV
04J-JOHN-07-16 APEKRIYH OUN AUTOIV O IHSOUV KAI EIPEN H EMH DIDACH OUK ESTIN EMH ALLA TOU PEMQANTOV ME
04J-JOHN-07-17 EAN TIV YELH TO YELHMA AUTOU POIEIN GNWSETAI PERI THV DIDACHV POTERON EK TOU YEOU ESTIN H EGW AP EMAUTOU LALW
04J-JOHN-07-18 O AF EAUTOU LALWN THN DOXAN THN IDIAN ZHTEI O DE ZHTWN THN DOXAN TOU PEMQANTOV AUTON OUTOV ALHYHV ESTIN KAI ADIKIA EN AUTW OUK ESTIN
04J-JOHN-07-19 OU MWSHV DEDWKEN UMIN TON NOMON KAI OUDEIV EX UMWN POIEI TON NOMON TI ME ZHTEITE APOKTEINAI
04J-JOHN-07-20 APEKRIYH O OCLOV KAI EIPEN DAIMONION ECEIV TIV SE ZHTEI APOKTEINAI
04J-JOHN-07-21 APEKRIYH IHSOUV KAI EIPEN AUTOIV EN ERGON EPOIHSA KAI PANTEV YAUMAZETE
04J-JOHN-07-22 DIA TOUTO MWSHV DEDWKEN UMIN THN PERITOMHN OUC OTI EK TOU MWSEWV ESTIN ALL EK TWN PATERWN KAI EN SABBATW PERITEMNETE ANYRWPON
04J-JOHN-07-23 EI PERITOMHN LAMBANEI ANYRWPOV EN SABBATW INA MH LUYH O NOMOV MWSEWV EMOI COLATE OTI OLON ANYRWPON UGIH EPOIHSA EN SABBATW
04J-JOHN-07-24 MH KRINETE KAT OQIN ALLA THN DIKAIAN KRISIN KRINATE
04J-JOHN-07-25 ELEGON OUN TINEV EK TWN IEROSOLUMITWN OUC OUTOV ESTIN ON ZHTOUSIN APOKTEINAI
04J-JOHN-07-26 KAI IDE PARRHSIA LALEI KAI OUDEN AUTW LEGOUSIN MHPOTE ALHYWV EGNWSAN OI ARCONTEV OTI OUTOV ESTIN ALHYWV O CRISTOV
04J-JOHN-07-27 ALLA TOUTON OIDAMEN POYEN ESTIN O DE CRISTOV OTAN ERCHTAI OUDEIV GINWSKEI POYEN ESTIN
04J-JOHN-07-28 EKRAXEN OUN EN TW IERW DIDASKWN O IHSOUV KAI LEGWN KAME OIDATE KAI OIDATE POYEN EIMI KAI AP EMAUTOU OUK ELHLUYA ALL ESTIN ALHYINOV O PEMQAV ME ON UMEIV OUK OIDATE
04J-JOHN-07-29 EGW OIDA AUTON OTI PAR AUTOU EIMI KAKEINOV ME APESTEILEN
04J-JOHN-07-30 EZHTOUN OUN AUTON PIASAI KAI OUDEIV EPEBALEN EP AUTON THN CEIRA OTI OUPW ELHLUYEI H WRA AUTOU
04J-JOHN-07-31 POLLOI DE EK TOU OCLOU EPISTEUSAN EIV AUTON KAI ELEGON OTI O CRISTOV OTAN ELYH MHTI PLEIONA SHMEIA TOUTWN POIHSEI WN OUTOV EPOIHSEN
04J-JOHN-07-32 HKOUSAN OI FARISAIOI TOU OCLOU GOGGUZONTOV PERI AUTOU TAUTA KAI APESTEILAN UPHRETAV OI FARISAIOI KAI OI ARCIEREIV INA PIASWSIN AUTON
04J-JOHN-07-33 EIPEN OUN O IHSOUV ETI MIKRON CRONON MEY UMWN EIMI KAI UPAGW PROV TON PEMQANTA ME
04J-JOHN-07-34 ZHTHSETE ME KAI OUC EURHSETE KAI OPOU EIMI EGW UMEIV OU DUNASYE ELYEIN
04J-JOHN-07-35 EIPON OUN OI IOUDAIOI PROV EAUTOUV POU OUTOV MELLEI POREUESYAI OTI HMEIV OUC EURHSOMEN AUTON MH EIV THN DIASPORAN TWN ELLHNWN MELLEI POREUESYAI KAI DIDASKEIN TOUV ELLHNAV
04J-JOHN-07-36 TIV ESTIN OUTOV O LOGOV ON EIPEN ZHTHSETE ME KAI OUC EURHSETE KAI OPOU EIMI EGW UMEIV OU DUNASYE ELYEIN
04J-JOHN-07-37 EN DE TH ESCATH HMERA TH MEGALH THV EORTHV EISTHKEI O IHSOUV KAI EKRAXEN LEGWN EAN TIV DIQA ERCESYW PROV ME KAI PINETW
04J-JOHN-07-38 O PISTEUWN EIV EME KAYWV EIPEN H GRAFH POTAMOI EK THV KOILIAV AUTOU REUSOUSIN UDATOV ZWNTOV
04J-JOHN-07-39 TOUTO DE EIPEN PERI TOU PNEUMATOV OU EMELLON LAMBANEIN OI PISTEUONTEV EIV AUTON OUPW GAR HN PNEUMA AGION OTI IHSOUV OUDEPW EDOXASYH
04J-JOHN-07-40 POLLOI OUN EK TOU OCLOU AKOUSANTEV TON LOGON ELEGON OUTOV ESTIN ALHYWV O PROFHTHV

04J-JOHN-07-43 SCISMA OUN EN TW OCLW EGENETO DI AUTON

04J-JOHN-07-49 ALL O OCLOV OUTOV O MH GINWSKWN TON NOMON EPIKATARATOI EISIN

04J-JOHN-07-52 APEKRIYHSAN KAI EIPON AUTW MH KAI SU EK THV GALILAIAV EI EREUNHSON KAI IDE OTI PROFHTHV EK THV GALILAIAV OUK EGHGERTAI
04J-JOHN-07-53 KAI EPOREUYH EKASTOV EIV TON OIKON AUTOU

04J-JOHN-08-02 ORYROU DE PALIN PAREGENETO EIV TO IERON KAI PAV O LAOV HRCETO KAI KAYISAV EDIDASKEN AUTOUV
04J-JOHN-08-03 AGOUSIN DE OI GRAMMATEIV KAI OI FARISAIOI PROV AUTON GUNAIKA EN MOICEIA KATALHFYEISAN KAI STHSANTEV AUTHN EN MESW
04J-JOHN-08-04 LEGOUSIN AUTW PEIRAZONTEV DIDASKALE AUTH H GUNH KATELHFYH EP AUTOFORW MOICEUOMENH
04J-JOHN-08-05 EN DE TW NOMW MWSHV HMIN ENETEILATO TAV TOIAUTAV LIYOBOLEISYAI SU OUN TI LEGEIV
04J-JOHN-08-06 TOUTO DE ELEGON PEIRAZONTEV AUTON INA ECWSIN KATHGOREIN AUTOU O DE IHSOUV KATW KUQAV TW DAKTULW EGRAFEN EIV THN GHN MH PROSPOIOUMENOV
04J-JOHN-08-07 WV DE EPEMENON ERWTWNTEV AUTON ANAKUQAV EIPEN PROV AUTOUV O ANAMARTHTOV UMWN PRWTON EP AUTHN TON LIYON BALETW
04J-JOHN-08-08 KAI PALIN KATW KUQAV EGRAFEN EIV THN GHN

04J-JOHN-08-10 ANAKUQAV DE O IHSOUV KAI MHDENA YEASAMENOV PLHN THV GUNAIKOV EIPEN AUTH POU EISIN EKEINOI OI KATHGOROI SOU OUDEIV SE KATEKRINEN
04J-JOHN-08-11 H DE EIPEN OUDEIV KURIE EIPEN DE O IHSOUV OUDE EGW SE KRINW POREUOU KAI MHKETI AMARTANE
04J-JOHN-08-12 PALIN OUN AUTOIV O IHSOUV ELALHSEN LEGWN EGW EIMI TO FWV TOU KOSMOU O AKOLOUYWN EMOI OU MH PERIPATHSH EN TH SKOTIA ALL EXEI TO FWV THV ZWHV

04J-JOHN-08-14 APEKRIYH IHSOUV KAI EIPEN AUTOIV KAN EGW MARTURW PERI EMAUTOU ALHYHV ESTIN H MARTURIA MOU OTI OIDA POYEN HLYON KAI POU UPAGW UMEIV DE OUK OIDATE POYEN ERCOMAI KAI POU UPAGW

04J-JOHN-08-21 EIPEN OUN PALIN AUTOIV O IHSOUV EGW UPAGW KAI ZHTHSETE ME KAI EN TH AMARTIA UMWN APOYANEISYE OPOU EGW UPAGW UMEIV OU DUNASYE ELYEIN

04J-JOHN-08-24 EIPON OUN UMIN OTI APOYANEISYE EN TAIV AMARTIAIV UMWN EAN GAR MH PISTEUSHTE OTI EGW EIMI APOYANEISYE EN TAIV AMARTIAIV UMWN
