04J-JOHN-09-21 PWV DE NUN BLEPEI OUK OIDAMEN H TIV HNOIXEN AUTOU TOUV OFYALMOUV HMEIV OUK OIDAMEN AUTOV HLIKIAN ECEI AUTON ERWTHSATE AUTOV PERI EAUTOU LALHSEI
04J-JOHN-09-22 TAUTA EIPON OI GONEIV AUTOU OTI EFOBOUNTO TOUV IOUDAIOUV HDH GAR SUNETEYEINTO OI IOUDAIOI INA EAN TIV AUTON OMOLOGHSH CRISTON APOSUNAGWGOV GENHTAI
04J-JOHN-09-23 DIA TOUTO OI GONEIV AUTOU EIPON OTI HLIKIAN ECEI AUTON ERWTHSATE
04J-JOHN-09-24 EFWNHSAN OUN EK DEUTEROU TON ANYRWPON OV HN TUFLOV KAI EIPON AUTW DOV DOXAN TW YEW HMEIV OIDAMEN OTI O ANYRWPOV OUTOV AMARTWLOV ESTIN
04J-JOHN-09-25 APEKRIYH OUN EKEINOV KAI EIPEN EI AMARTWLOV ESTIN OUK OIDA EN OIDA OTI TUFLOV WN ARTI BLEPW
04J-JOHN-09-26 EIPON DE AUTW PALIN TI EPOIHSEN SOI PWV HNOIXEN SOU TOUV OFYALMOUV
04J-JOHN-09-27 APEKRIYH AUTOIV EIPON UMIN HDH KAI OUK HKOUSATE TI PALIN YELETE AKOUEIN MH KAI UMEIV YELETE AUTOU MAYHTAI GENESYAI
04J-JOHN-09-28 ELOIDORHSAN AUTON KAI EIPON SU EI MAYHTHV EKEINOU HMEIV DE TOU MWSEWV ESMEN MAYHTAI
04J-JOHN-09-29 HMEIV OIDAMEN OTI MWSH LELALHKEN O YEOV TOUTON DE OUK OIDAMEN POYEN ESTIN
04J-JOHN-09-30 APEKRIYH O ANYRWPOV KAI EIPEN AUTOIV EN GAR TOUTW YAUMASTON ESTIN OTI UMEIV OUK OIDATE POYEN ESTIN KAI ANEWXEN MOU TOUV OFYALMOUV
04J-JOHN-09-31 OIDAMEN DE OTI AMARTWLWN O YEOV OUK AKOUEI ALL EAN TIV YEOSEBHV H KAI TO YELHMA AUTOU POIH TOUTOU AKOUEI
04J-JOHN-09-32 EK TOU AIWNOV OUK HKOUSYH OTI HNOIXEN TIV OFYALMOUV TUFLOU GEGENNHMENOU
04J-JOHN-09-33 EI MH HN OUTOV PARA YEOU OUK HDUNATO POIEIN OUDEN
04J-JOHN-09-34 APEKRIYHSAN KAI EIPON AUTW EN AMARTIAIV SU EGENNHYHV OLOV KAI SU DIDASKEIV HMAV KAI EXEBALON AUTON EXW
04J-JOHN-09-35 HKOUSEN O IHSOUV OTI EXEBALON AUTON EXW KAI EURWN AUTON EIPEN AUTW SU PISTEUEIV EIV TON UION TOU YEOU
04J-JOHN-09-36 APEKRIYH EKEINOV KAI EIPEN KAI TIV ESTIN KURIE INA PISTEUSW EIV AUTON
04J-JOHN-09-37 EIPEN DE AUTW O IHSOUV KAI EWRAKAV AUTON KAI O LALWN META SOU EKEINOV ESTIN
04J-JOHN-09-38 O DE EFH PISTEUW KURIE KAI PROSEKUNHSEN AUTW
04J-JOHN-09-39 KAI EIPEN O IHSOUV EIV KRIMA EGW EIV TON KOSMON TOUTON HLYON INA OI MH BLEPONTEV BLEPWSIN KAI OI BLEPONTEV TUFLOI GENWNTAI
04J-JOHN-09-40 KAI HKOUSAN EK TWN FARISAIWN TAUTA OI ONTEV MET AUTOU KAI EIPON AUTW MH KAI HMEIV TUFLOI ESMEN
04J-JOHN-09-41 EIPEN AUTOIV O IHSOUV EI TUFLOI HTE OUK AN EICETE AMARTIAN NUN DE LEGETE OTI BLEPOMEN H OUN AMARTIA UMWN MENEI
04J-JOHN-10-01 AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN O MH EISERCOMENOV DIA THV YURAV EIV THN AULHN TWN PROBATWN ALLA ANABAINWN ALLACOYEN EKEINOV KLEPTHV ESTIN KAI LHSTHV
04J-JOHN-10-02 O DE EISERCOMENOV DIA THV YURAV POIMHN ESTIN TWN PROBATWN
04J-JOHN-10-03 TOUTW O YURWROV ANOIGEI KAI TA PROBATA THV FWNHV AUTOU AKOUEI KAI TA IDIA PROBATA KALEI KAT ONOMA KAI EXAGEI AUTA
04J-JOHN-10-04 KAI OTAN TA IDIA PROBATA EKBALH EMPROSYEN AUTWN POREUETAI KAI TA PROBATA AUTW AKOLOUYEI OTI OIDASIN THN FWNHN AUTOU
04J-JOHN-10-05 ALLOTRIW DE OU MH AKOLOUYHSWSIN ALLA FEUXONTAI AP AUTOU OTI OUK OIDASIN TWN ALLOTRIWN THN FWNHN
04J-JOHN-10-06 TAUTHN THN PAROIMIAN EIPEN AUTOIV O IHSOUV EKEINOI DE OUK EGNWSAN TINA HN A ELALEI AUTOIV
04J-JOHN-10-07 EIPEN OUN PALIN AUTOIV O IHSOUV AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN OTI EGW EIMI H YURA TWN PROBATWN
04J-JOHN-10-08 PANTEV OSOI HLYON KLEPTAI EISIN KAI LHSTAI ALL OUK HKOUSAN AUTWN TA PROBATA
04J-JOHN-10-09 EGW EIMI H YURA DI EMOU EAN TIV EISELYH SWYHSETAI KAI EISELEUSETAI KAI EXELEUSETAI KAI NOMHN EURHSEI
04J-JOHN-10-10 O KLEPTHV OUK ERCETAI EI MH INA KLEQH KAI YUSH KAI APOLESH EGW HLYON INA ZWHN ECWSIN KAI PERISSON ECWSIN
04J-JOHN-10-11 EGW EIMI O POIMHN O KALOV O POIMHN O KALOV THN QUCHN AUTOU TIYHSIN UPER TWN PROBATWN
04J-JOHN-10-12 O MISYWTOV DE KAI OUK WN POIMHN OU OUK EISIN TA PROBATA IDIA YEWREI TON LUKON ERCOMENON KAI AFIHSIN TA PROBATA KAI FEUGEI KAI O LUKOV ARPAZEI AUTA KAI SKORPIZEI TA PROBATA
04J-JOHN-10-13 O DE MISYWTOV FEUGEI OTI MISYWTOV ESTIN KAI OU MELEI AUTW PERI TWN PROBATWN
04J-JOHN-10-14 EGW EIMI O POIMHN O KALOV KAI GINWSKW TA EMA KAI GINWSKOMAI UPO TWN EMWN
04J-JOHN-10-15 KAYWV GINWSKEI ME O PATHR KAGW GINWSKW TON PATERA KAI THN QUCHN MOU TIYHMI UPER TWN PROBATWN
04J-JOHN-10-16 KAI ALLA PROBATA ECW A OUK ESTIN EK THV AULHV TAUTHV KAKEINA ME DEI AGAGEIN KAI THV FWNHV MOU AKOUSOUSIN KAI GENHSETAI MIA POIMNH EIV POIMHN
04J-JOHN-10-17 DIA TOUTO O PATHR ME AGAPA OTI EGW TIYHMI THN QUCHN MOU INA PALIN LABW AUTHN
04J-JOHN-10-18 OUDEIV AIREI AUTHN AP EMOU ALL EGW TIYHMI AUTHN AP EMAUTOU EXOUSIAN ECW YEINAI AUTHN KAI EXOUSIAN ECW PALIN LABEIN AUTHN TAUTHN THN ENTOLHN ELABON PARA TOU PATROV MOU
04J-JOHN-10-19 SCISMA OUN PALIN EGENETO EN TOIV IOUDAIOIV DIA TOUV LOGOUV TOUTOUV
04J-JOHN-10-20 ELEGON DE POLLOI EX AUTWN DAIMONION ECEI KAI MAINETAI TI AUTOU AKOUETE
04J-JOHN-10-21 ALLOI ELEGON TAUTA TA RHMATA OUK ESTIN DAIMONIZOMENOU MH DAIMONION DUNATAI TUFLWN OFYALMOUV ANOIGEIN
04J-JOHN-10-22 EGENETO DE TA EGKAINIA EN IEROSOLUMOIV KAI CEIMWN HN
04J-JOHN-10-23 KAI PERIEPATEI O IHSOUV EN TW IERW EN TH STOA SOLOMWNOV
04J-JOHN-10-24 EKUKLWSAN OUN AUTON OI IOUDAIOI KAI ELEGON AUTW EWV POTE THN QUCHN HMWN AIREIV EI SU EI O CRISTOV EIPE HMIN PARRHSIA
04J-JOHN-10-25 APEKRIYH AUTOIV O IHSOUV EIPON UMIN KAI OU PISTEUETE TA ERGA A EGW POIW EN TW ONOMATI TOU PATROV MOU TAUTA MARTUREI PERI EMOU
04J-JOHN-10-26 ALL UMEIV OU PISTEUETE OU GAR ESTE EK TWN PROBATWN TWN EMWN KAYWV EIPON UMIN
04J-JOHN-10-27 TA PROBATA TA EMA THV FWNHV MOU AKOUEI KAGW GINWSKW AUTA KAI AKOLOUYOUSIN MOI
04J-JOHN-10-28 KAGW ZWHN AIWNION DIDWMI AUTOIV KAI OU MH APOLWNTAI EIV TON AIWNA KAI OUC ARPASEI TIV AUTA EK THV CEIROV MOU
04J-JOHN-10-29 O PATHR MOU OV DEDWKEN MOI MEIZWN PANTWN ESTIN KAI OUDEIV DUNATAI ARPAZEIN EK THV CEIROV TOU PATROV MOU
04J-JOHN-10-30 EGW KAI O PATHR EN ESMEN
04J-JOHN-10-31 EBASTASAN OUN PALIN LIYOUV OI IOUDAIOI INA LIYASWSIN AUTON
04J-JOHN-10-32 APEKRIYH AUTOIV O IHSOUV POLLA KALA ERGA EDEIXA UMIN EK TOU PATROV MOU DIA POION AUTWN ERGON LIYAZETE ME
04J-JOHN-10-33 APEKRIYHSAN AUTW OI IOUDAIOI LEGONTEV PERI KALOU ERGOU OU LIYAZOMEN SE ALLA PERI BLASFHMIAV KAI OTI SU ANYRWPOV WN POIEIV SEAUTON YEON
04J-JOHN-10-34 APEKRIYH AUTOIV O IHSOUV OUK ESTIN GEGRAMMENON EN TW NOMW UMWN EGW EIPA YEOI ESTE
04J-JOHN-10-35 EI EKEINOUV EIPEN YEOUV PROV OUV O LOGOV TOU YEOU EGENETO KAI OU DUNATAI LUYHNAI H GRAFH
04J-JOHN-10-36 ON O PATHR HGIASEN KAI APESTEILEN EIV TON KOSMON UMEIV LEGETE OTI BLASFHMEIV OTI EIPON UIOV TOU YEOU EIMI
04J-JOHN-10-37 EI OU POIW TA ERGA TOU PATROV MOU MH PISTEUETE MOI
04J-JOHN-10-38 EI DE POIW KAN EMOI MH PISTEUHTE TOIV ERGOIV PISTEUSATE INA GNWTE KAI PISTEUSHTE OTI EN EMOI O PATHR KAGW EN AUTW
04J-JOHN-10-39 EZHTOUN OUN PALIN AUTON PIASAI KAI EXHLYEN EK THV CEIROV AUTWN
04J-JOHN-10-40 KAI APHLYEN PALIN PERAN TOU IORDANOU EIV TON TOPON OPOU HN IWANNHV TO PRWTON BAPTIZWN KAI EMEINEN EKEI
04J-JOHN-10-41 KAI POLLOI HLYON PROV AUTON KAI ELEGON OTI IWANNHV MEN SHMEION EPOIHSEN OUDEN PANTA DE OSA EIPEN IWANNHV PERI TOUTOU ALHYH HN
04J-JOHN-10-42 KAI EPISTEUSAN POLLOI EKEI EIV AUTON
04J-JOHN-11-01 HN DE TIV ASYENWN LAZAROV APO BHYANIAV EK THV KWMHV MARIAV KAI MARYAV THV ADELFHV AUTHV
04J-JOHN-11-02 HN DE MARIA H ALEIQASA TON KURION MURW KAI EKMAXASA TOUV PODAV AUTOU TAIV YRIXIN AUTHV HV O ADELFOV LAZAROV HSYENEI
04J-JOHN-11-03 APESTEILAN OUN AI ADELFAI PROV AUTON LEGOUSAI KURIE IDE ON FILEIV ASYENEI
04J-JOHN-11-04 AKOUSAV DE O IHSOUV EIPEN AUTH H ASYENEIA OUK ESTIN PROV YANATON ALL UPER THV DOXHV TOU YEOU INA DOXASYH O UIOV TOU YEOU DI AUTHV
04J-JOHN-11-05 HGAPA DE O IHSOUV THN MARYAN KAI THN ADELFHN AUTHV KAI TON LAZARON
04J-JOHN-11-06 WV OUN HKOUSEN OTI ASYENEI TOTE MEN EMEINEN EN W HN TOPW DUO HMERAV
04J-JOHN-11-07 EPEITA META TOUTO LEGEI TOIV MAYHTAIV AGWMEN EIV THN IOUDAIAN PALIN
04J-JOHN-11-08 LEGOUSIN AUTW OI MAYHTAI RABBI NUN EZHTOUN SE LIYASAI OI IOUDAIOI KAI PALIN UPAGEIV EKEI
04J-JOHN-11-09 APEKRIYH IHSOUV OUCI DWDEKA EISIN WRAI THV HMERAV EAN TIV PERIPATH EN TH HMERA OU PROSKOPTEI OTI TO FWV TOU KOSMOU TOUTOU BLEPEI
04J-JOHN-11-10 EAN DE TIV PERIPATH EN TH NUKTI PROSKOPTEI OTI TO FWV OUK ESTIN EN AUTW
04J-JOHN-11-11 TAUTA EIPEN KAI META TOUTO LEGEI AUTOIV LAZAROV O FILOV HMWN KEKOIMHTAI ALLA POREUOMAI INA EXUPNISW AUTON
04J-JOHN-11-12 EIPON OUN OI MAYHTAI AUTOU KURIE EI KEKOIMHTAI SWYHSETAI
04J-JOHN-11-13 EIRHKEI DE O IHSOUV PERI TOU YANATOU AUTOU EKEINOI DE EDOXAN OTI PERI THV KOIMHSEWV TOU UPNOU LEGEI
04J-JOHN-11-14 TOTE OUN EIPEN AUTOIV O IHSOUV PARRHSIA LAZAROV APEYANEN
04J-JOHN-11-15 KAI CAIRW DI UMAV INA PISTEUSHTE OTI OUK HMHN EKEI ALLA AGWMEN PROV AUTON
04J-JOHN-11-16 EIPEN OUN YWMAV O LEGOMENOV DIDUMOV TOIV SUMMAYHTAIV AGWMEN KAI HMEIV INA APOYANWMEN MET AUTOU
04J-JOHN-11-17 ELYWN OUN O IHSOUV EUREN AUTON TESSARAV HMERAV HDH ECONTA EN TW MNHMEIW
04J-JOHN-11-18 HN DE H BHYANIA EGGUV TWN IEROSOLUMWN WV APO STADIWN DEKAPENTE
04J-JOHN-11-19 KAI POLLOI EK TWN IOUDAIWN ELHLUYEISAN PROV TAV PERI MARYAN KAI MARIAN INA PARAMUYHSWNTAI AUTAV PERI TOU ADELFOU AUTWN
04J-JOHN-11-20 H OUN MARYA WV HKOUSEN OTI IHSOUV ERCETAI UPHNTHSEN AUTW MARIA DE EN TW OIKW EKAYEZETO
04J-JOHN-11-21 EIPEN OUN MARYA PROV TON IHSOUN KURIE EI HV WDE O ADELFOV MOU OUK AN ETEYNHKEI
04J-JOHN-11-22 ALLA KAI NUN OIDA OTI OSA AN AITHSH TON YEON DWSEI SOI O YEOV
04J-JOHN-11-23 LEGEI AUTH O IHSOUV ANASTHSETAI O ADELFOV SOU
04J-JOHN-11-24 LEGEI AUTW MARYA OIDA OTI ANASTHSETAI EN TH ANASTASEI EN TH ESCATH HMERA
04J-JOHN-11-25 EIPEN AUTH O IHSOUV EGW EIMI H ANASTASIV KAI H ZWH O PISTEUWN EIV EME KAN APOYANH ZHSETAI
04J-JOHN-11-26 KAI PAV O ZWN KAI PISTEUWN EIV EME OU MH APOYANH EIV TON AIWNA PISTEUEIV TOUTO
04J-JOHN-11-27 LEGEI AUTW NAI KURIE EGW PEPISTEUKA OTI SU EI O CRISTOV O UIOV TOU YEOU O EIV TON KOSMON ERCOMENOV
04J-JOHN-11-28 KAI TAUTA EIPOUSA APHLYEN KAI EFWNHSEN MARIAN THN ADELFHN AUTHV LAYRA EIPOUSA O DIDASKALOV PARESTIN KAI FWNEI SE
04J-JOHN-11-29 EKEINH WV HKOUSEN EGEIRETAI TACU KAI ERCETAI PROV AUTON
04J-JOHN-11-30 OUPW DE ELHLUYEI O IHSOUV EIV THN KWMHN ALL HN EN TW TOPW OPOU UPHNTHSEN AUTW H MARYA
04J-JOHN-11-31 OI OUN IOUDAIOI OI ONTEV MET AUTHV EN TH OIKIA KAI PARAMUYOUMENOI AUTHN IDONTEV THN MARIAN OTI TACEWV ANESTH KAI EXHLYEN HKOLOUYHSAN AUTH LEGONTEV OTI UPAGEI EIV TO MNHMEION INA KLAUSH EKEI
04J-JOHN-11-32 H OUN MARIA WV HLYEN OPOU HN O IHSOUV IDOUSA AUTON EPESEN AUTOU EIV TOUV PODAV LEGOUSA AUTW KURIE EI HV WDE OUK AN APEYANEN MOU O ADELFOV
04J-JOHN-11-33 IHSOUV OUN WV EIDEN AUTHN KLAIOUSAN KAI TOUV SUNELYONTAV AUTH IOUDAIOUV KLAIONTAV ENEBRIMHSATO TW PNEUMATI KAI ETARAXEN EAUTON
04J-JOHN-11-34 KAI EIPEN POU TEYEIKATE AUTON LEGOUSIN AUTW KURIE ERCOU KAI IDE
04J-JOHN-11-35 EDAKRUSEN O IHSOUV
04J-JOHN-11-36 ELEGON OUN OI IOUDAIOI IDE PWV EFILEI AUTON
04J-JOHN-11-37 TINEV DE EX AUTWN EIPON OUK HDUNATO OUTOV O ANOIXAV TOUV OFYALMOUV TOU TUFLOU POIHSAI INA KAI OUTOV MH APOYANH
04J-JOHN-11-38 IHSOUV OUN PALIN EMBRIMWMENOV EN EAUTW ERCETAI EIV TO MNHMEION HN DE SPHLAION KAI LIYOV EPEKEITO EP AUTW
04J-JOHN-11-39 LEGEI O IHSOUV ARATE TON LIYON LEGEI AUTW H ADELFH TOU TEYNHKOTOV MARYA KURIE HDH OZEI TETARTAIOV GAR ESTIN
04J-JOHN-11-40 LEGEI AUTH O IHSOUV OUK EIPON SOI OTI EAN PISTEUSHV OQEI THN DOXAN TOU YEOU
04J-JOHN-11-41 HRAN OUN TON LIYON OU HN O TEYNHKWV KEIMENOV O DE IHSOUV HREN TOUV OFYALMOUV ANW KAI EIPEN PATER EUCARISTW SOI OTI HKOUSAV MOU
04J-JOHN-11-42 EGW DE HDEIN OTI PANTOTE MOU AKOUEIV ALLA DIA TON OCLON TON PERIESTWTA EIPON INA PISTEUSWSIN OTI SU ME APESTEILAV
04J-JOHN-11-43 KAI TAUTA EIPWN FWNH MEGALH EKRAUGASEN LAZARE DEURO EXW
04J-JOHN-11-44 KAI EXHLYEN O TEYNHKWV DEDEMENOV TOUV PODAV KAI TAV CEIRAV KEIRIAIV KAI H OQIV AUTOU SOUDARIW PERIEDEDETO LEGEI AUTOIV O IHSOUV LUSATE AUTON KAI AFETE UPAGEIN
04J-JOHN-11-45 POLLOI OUN EK TWN IOUDAIWN OI ELYONTEV PROV THN MARIAN KAI YEASAMENOI A EPOIHSEN O IHSOUV EPISTEUSAN EIV AUTON
04J-JOHN-11-46 TINEV DE EX AUTWN APHLYON PROV TOUV FARISAIOUV KAI EIPON AUTOIV A EPOIHSEN O IHSOUV
04J-JOHN-11-47 SUNHGAGON OUN OI ARCIEREIV KAI OI FARISAIOI SUNEDRION KAI ELEGON TI POIOUMEN OTI OUTOV O ANYRWPOV POLLA SHMEIA POIEI
04J-JOHN-11-48 EAN AFWMEN AUTON OUTWV PANTEV PISTEUSOUSIN EIV AUTON KAI ELEUSONTAI OI RWMAIOI KAI AROUSIN HMWN KAI TON TOPON KAI TO EYNOV
04J-JOHN-11-49 EIV DE TIV EX AUTWN KAIAFAV ARCIEREUV WN TOU ENIAUTOU EKEINOU EIPEN AUTOIV UMEIV OUK OIDATE OUDEN
04J-JOHN-11-50 OUDE DIALOGIZESYE OTI SUMFEREI HMIN INA EIV ANYRWPOV APOYANH UPER TOU LAOU KAI MH OLON TO EYNOV APOLHTAI
04J-JOHN-11-51 TOUTO DE AF EAUTOU OUK EIPEN ALLA ARCIEREUV WN TOU ENIAUTOU EKEINOU PROEFHTEUSEN OTI EMELLEN IHSOUV APOYNHSKEIN UPER TOU EYNOUV
04J-JOHN-11-52 KAI OUC UPER TOU EYNOUV MONON ALL INA KAI TA TEKNA TOU YEOU TA DIESKORPISMENA SUNAGAGH EIV EN
04J-JOHN-11-53 AP EKEINHV OUN THV HMERAV SUNEBOULEUSANTO INA APOKTEINWSIN AUTON
04J-JOHN-11-54 IHSOUV OUN OUKETI PARRHSIA PERIEPATEI EN TOIV IOUDAIOIV ALLA APHLYEN EKEIYEN EIV THN CWRAN EGGUV THV ERHMOU EIV EFRAIM LEGOMENHN POLIN KAKEI DIETRIBEN META TWN MAYHTWN AUTOU
04J-JOHN-11-55 HN DE EGGUV TO PASCA TWN IOUDAIWN KAI ANEBHSAN POLLOI EIV IEROSOLUMA EK THV CWRAV PRO TOU PASCA INA AGNISWSIN EAUTOUV
04J-JOHN-11-56 EZHTOUN OUN TON IHSOUN KAI ELEGON MET ALLHLWN EN TW IERW ESTHKOTEV TI DOKEI UMIN OTI OU MH ELYH EIV THN EORTHN
04J-JOHN-11-57 DEDWKEISAN DE KAI OI ARCIEREIV KAI OI FARISAIOI ENTOLHN INA EAN TIV GNW POU ESTIN MHNUSH OPWV PIASWSIN AUTON
04J-JOHN-12-01 O OUN IHSOUV PRO EX HMERWN TOU PASCA HLYEN EIV BHYANIAN OPOU HN LAZAROV O TEYNHKWV ON HGEIREN EK NEKRWN
04J-JOHN-12-02 EPOIHSAN OUN AUTW DEIPNON EKEI KAI H MARYA DIHKONEI O DE LAZAROV EIV HN TWN ANAKEIMENWN SUN AUTW
04J-JOHN-12-03 H OUN MARIA LABOUSA LITRAN MUROU NARDOU PISTIKHV POLUTIMOU HLEIQEN TOUV PODAV TOU IHSOU KAI EXEMAXEN TAIV YRIXIN AUTHV TOUV PODAV AUTOU H DE OIKIA EPLHRWYH EK THV OSMHV TOU MUROU
04J-JOHN-12-04 LEGEI OUN EIV EK TWN MAYHTWN AUTOU IOUDAV SIMWNOV ISKARIWTHV O MELLWN AUTON PARADIDONAI
04J-JOHN-12-05 DIA TI TOUTO TO MURON OUK EPRAYH TRIAKOSIWN DHNARIWN KAI EDOYH PTWCOIV
04J-JOHN-12-06 EIPEN DE TOUTO OUC OTI PERI TWN PTWCWN EMELEN AUTW ALL OTI KLEPTHV HN KAI TO GLWSSOKOMON EICEN KAI TA BALLOMENA EBASTAZEN
04J-JOHN-12-07 EIPEN OUN O IHSOUV AFEV AUTHN EIV THN HMERAN TOU ENTAFIASMOU MOU TETHRHKEN AUTO
04J-JOHN-12-08 TOUV PTWCOUV GAR PANTOTE ECETE MEY EAUTWN EME DE OU PANTOTE ECETE
04J-JOHN-12-09 EGNW OUN OCLOV POLUV EK TWN IOUDAIWN OTI EKEI ESTIN KAI HLYON OU DIA TON IHSOUN MONON ALL INA KAI TON LAZARON IDWSIN ON HGEIREN EK NEKRWN
04J-JOHN-12-10 EBOULEUSANTO DE OI ARCIEREIV INA KAI TON LAZARON APOKTEINWSIN
04J-JOHN-12-11 OTI POLLOI DI AUTON UPHGON TWN IOUDAIWN KAI EPISTEUON EIV TON IHSOUN
04J-JOHN-12-12 TH EPAURION OCLOV POLUV O ELYWN EIV THN EORTHN AKOUSANTEV OTI ERCETAI IHSOUV EIV IEROSOLUMA
04J-JOHN-12-13 ELABON TA BAIA TWN FOINIKWN KAI EXHLYON EIV UPANTHSIN AUTW KAI EKRAZON WSANNA EULOGHMENOV O ERCOMENOV EN ONOMATI KURIOU BASILEUV TOU ISRAHL
04J-JOHN-12-14 EURWN DE O IHSOUV ONARION EKAYISEN EP AUTO KAYWV ESTIN GEGRAMMENON
04J-JOHN-12-15 MH FOBOU YUGATER SIWN IDOU O BASILEUV SOU ERCETAI KAYHMENOV EPI PWLON ONOU
04J-JOHN-12-16 TAUTA DE OUK EGNWSAN OI MAYHTAI AUTOU TO PRWTON ALL OTE EDOXASYH IHSOUV TOTE EMNHSYHSAN OTI TAUTA HN EP AUTW GEGRAMMENA KAI TAUTA EPOIHSAN AUTW
04J-JOHN-12-17 EMARTUREI OUN O OCLOV O WN MET AUTOU OTE TON LAZARON EFWNHSEN EK TOU MNHMEIOU KAI HGEIREN AUTON EK NEKRWN
04J-JOHN-12-18 DIA TOUTO KAI UPHNTHSEN AUTW O OCLOV OTI HKOUSEN TOUTO AUTON PEPOIHKENAI TO SHMEION
04J-JOHN-12-19 OI OUN FARISAIOI EIPON PROV EAUTOUV YEWREITE OTI OUK WFELEITE OUDEN IDE O KOSMOV OPISW AUTOU APHLYEN
04J-JOHN-12-20 HSAN DE TINEV ELLHNEV EK TWN ANABAINONTWN INA PROSKUNHSWSIN EN TH EORTH
04J-JOHN-12-21 OUTOI OUN PROSHLYON FILIPPW TW APO BHYSAIDA THV GALILAIAV KAI HRWTWN AUTON LEGONTEV KURIE YELOMEN TON IHSOUN IDEIN
04J-JOHN-12-22 ERCETAI FILIPPOV KAI LEGEI TW ANDREA KAI PALIN ANDREAV KAI FILIPPOV LEGOUSIN TW IHSOU
04J-JOHN-12-23 O DE IHSOUV APEKRINATO AUTOIV LEGWN ELHLUYEN H WRA INA DOXASYH O UIOV TOU ANYRWPOU
04J-JOHN-12-24 AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN EAN MH O KOKKOV TOU SITOU PESWN EIV THN GHN APOYANH AUTOV MONOV MENEI EAN DE APOYANH POLUN KARPON FEREI
04J-JOHN-12-25 O FILWN THN QUCHN AUTOU APOLESEI AUTHN KAI O MISWN THN QUCHN AUTOU EN TW KOSMW TOUTW EIV ZWHN AIWNION FULAXEI AUTHN
04J-JOHN-12-26 EAN EMOI DIAKONH TIV EMOI AKOLOUYEITW KAI OPOU EIMI EGW EKEI KAI O DIAKONOV O EMOV ESTAI KAI EAN TIV EMOI DIAKONH TIMHSEI AUTON O PATHR
04J-JOHN-12-27 NUN H QUCH MOU TETARAKTAI KAI TI EIPW PATER SWSON ME EK THV WRAV TAUTHV ALLA DIA TOUTO HLYON EIV THN WRAN TAUTHN
04J-JOHN-12-28 PATER DOXASON SOU TO ONOMA HLYEN OUN FWNH EK TOU OURANOU KAI EDOXASA KAI PALIN DOXASW
04J-JOHN-12-29 O OUN OCLOV O ESTWV KAI AKOUSAV ELEGEN BRONTHN GEGONENAI ALLOI ELEGON AGGELOV AUTW LELALHKEN
04J-JOHN-12-30 APEKRIYH IHSOUV KAI EIPEN OU DI EME AUTH H FWNH GEGONEN ALLA DI UMAV
04J-JOHN-12-31 NUN KRISIV ESTIN TOU KOSMOU TOUTOU NUN O ARCWN TOU KOSMOU TOUTOU EKBLHYHSETAI EXW
04J-JOHN-12-32 KAGW EAN UQWYW EK THV GHV PANTAV ELKUSW PROV EMAUTON
04J-JOHN-12-33 TOUTO DE ELEGEN SHMAINWN POIW YANATW EMELLEN APOYNHSKEIN
04J-JOHN-12-34 APEKRIYH AUTW O OCLOV HMEIV HKOUSAMEN EK TOU NOMOU OTI O CRISTOV MENEI EIV TON AIWNA KAI PWV SU LEGEIV DEI UQWYHNAI TON UION TOU ANYRWPOU TIV ESTIN OUTOV O UIOV TOU ANYRWPOU
04J-JOHN-12-35 EIPEN OUN AUTOIV O IHSOUV ETI MIKRON CRONON TO FWV MEY UMWN ESTIN PERIPATEITE EWV TO FWV ECETE INA MH SKOTIA UMAV KATALABH KAI O PERIPATWN EN TH SKOTIA OUK OIDEN POU UPAGEI
04J-JOHN-12-36 EWV TO FWV ECETE PISTEUETE EIV TO FWV INA UIOI FWTOV GENHSYE TAUTA ELALHSEN O IHSOUV KAI APELYWN EKRUBH AP AUTWN
04J-JOHN-12-37 TOSAUTA DE AUTOU SHMEIA PEPOIHKOTOV EMPROSYEN AUTWN OUK EPISTEUON EIV AUTON
04J-JOHN-12-38 INA O LOGOV HSAIOU TOU PROFHTOU PLHRWYH ON EIPEN KURIE TIV EPISTEUSEN TH AKOH HMWN KAI O BRACIWN KURIOU TINI APEKALUFYH
04J-JOHN-12-39 DIA TOUTO OUK HDUNANTO PISTEUEIN OTI PALIN EIPEN HSAIAV
04J-JOHN-12-40 TETUFLWKEN AUTWN TOUV OFYALMOUV KAI PEPWRWKEN AUTWN THN KARDIAN INA MH IDWSIN TOIV OFYALMOIV KAI NOHSWSIN TH KARDIA KAI EPISTRAFWSIN KAI IASWMAI AUTOUV
04J-JOHN-12-41 TAUTA EIPEN HSAIAV OTE EIDEN THN DOXAN AUTOU KAI ELALHSEN PERI AUTOU
04J-JOHN-12-42 OMWV MENTOI KAI EK TWN ARCONTWN POLLOI EPISTEUSAN EIV AUTON ALLA DIA TOUV FARISAIOUV OUC WMOLOGOUN INA MH APOSUNAGWGOI GENWNTAI
04J-JOHN-12-43 HGAPHSAN GAR THN DOXAN TWN ANYRWPWN MALLON HPER THN DOXAN TOU YEOU
04J-JOHN-12-44 IHSOUV DE EKRAXEN KAI EIPEN O PISTEUWN EIV EME OU PISTEUEI EIV EME ALL EIV TON PEMQANTA ME
04J-JOHN-12-45 KAI O YEWRWN EME YEWREI TON PEMQANTA ME
04J-JOHN-12-46 EGW FWV EIV TON KOSMON ELHLUYA INA PAV O PISTEUWN EIV EME EN TH SKOTIA MH MEINH
04J-JOHN-12-47 KAI EAN TIV MOU AKOUSH TWN RHMATWN KAI MH PISTEUSH EGW OU KRINW AUTON OU GAR HLYON INA KRINW TON KOSMON ALL INA SWSW TON KOSMON
04J-JOHN-12-48 O AYETWN EME KAI MH LAMBANWN TA RHMATA MOU ECEI TON KRINONTA AUTON O LOGOV ON ELALHSA EKEINOV KRINEI AUTON EN TH ESCATH HMERA
04J-JOHN-12-49 OTI EGW EX EMAUTOU OUK ELALHSA ALL O PEMQAV ME PATHR AUTOV MOI ENTOLHN EDWKEN TI EIPW KAI TI LALHSW
04J-JOHN-12-50 KAI OIDA OTI H ENTOLH AUTOU ZWH AIWNIOV ESTIN A OUN LALW EGW KAYWV EIRHKEN MOI O PATHR OUTWV LALW
04J-JOHN-13-01 PRO DE THV EORTHV TOU PASCA EIDWV O IHSOUV OTI ELHLUYEN AUTOU H WRA INA METABH EK TOU KOSMOU TOUTOU PROV TON PATERA AGAPHSAV TOUV IDIOUV TOUV EN TW KOSMW EIV TELOV HGAPHSEN AUTOUV
04J-JOHN-13-02 KAI DEIPNOU GENOMENOU TOU DIABOLOU HDH BEBLHKOTOV EIV THN KARDIAN IOUDA SIMWNOV ISKARIWTOU INA AUTON PARADW
04J-JOHN-13-03 EIDWV O IHSOUV OTI PANTA DEDWKEN AUTW O PATHR EIV TAV CEIRAV KAI OTI APO YEOU EXHLYEN KAI PROV TON YEON UPAGEI
04J-JOHN-13-04 EGEIRETAI EK TOU DEIPNOU KAI TIYHSIN TA IMATIA KAI LABWN LENTION DIEZWSEN EAUTON
04J-JOHN-13-05 EITA BALLEI UDWR EIV TON NIPTHRA KAI HRXATO NIPTEIN TOUV PODAV TWN MAYHTWN KAI EKMASSEIN TW LENTIW W HN DIEZWSMENOV
04J-JOHN-13-06 ERCETAI OUN PROV SIMWNA PETRON KAI LEGEI AUTW EKEINOV KURIE SU MOU NIPTEIV TOUV PODAV
04J-JOHN-13-07 APEKRIYH IHSOUV KAI EIPEN AUTW O EGW POIW SU OUK OIDAV ARTI GNWSH DE META TAUTA
04J-JOHN-13-08 LEGEI AUTW PETROV OU MH NIQHV TOUV PODAV MOU EIV TON AIWNA APEKRIYH AUTW O IHSOUV EAN MH NIQW SE OUK ECEIV MEROV MET EMOU
04J-JOHN-13-09 LEGEI AUTW SIMWN PETROV KURIE MH TOUV PODAV MOU MONON ALLA KAI TAV CEIRAV KAI THN KEFALHN
04J-JOHN-13-10 LEGEI AUTW O IHSOUV O LELOUMENOV OU CREIAN ECEI H TOUV PODAV NIQASYAI ALL ESTIN KAYAROV OLOV KAI UMEIV KAYAROI ESTE ALL OUCI PANTEV
04J-JOHN-13-11 HDEI GAR TON PARADIDONTA AUTON DIA TOUTO EIPEN OUCI PANTEV KAYAROI ESTE
04J-JOHN-13-12 OTE OUN ENIQEN TOUV PODAV AUTWN KAI ELABEN TA IMATIA AUTOU ANAPESWN PALIN EIPEN AUTOIV GINWSKETE TI PEPOIHKA UMIN
04J-JOHN-13-13 UMEIV FWNEITE ME O DIDASKALOV KAI O KURIOV KAI KALWV LEGETE EIMI GAR
04J-JOHN-13-14 EI OUN EGW ENIQA UMWN TOUV PODAV O KURIOV KAI O DIDASKALOV KAI UMEIV OFEILETE ALLHLWN NIPTEIN TOUV PODAV
04J-JOHN-13-15 UPODEIGMA GAR EDWKA UMIN INA KAYWV EGW EPOIHSA UMIN KAI UMEIV POIHTE
04J-JOHN-13-16 AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN OUK ESTIN DOULOV MEIZWN TOU KURIOU AUTOU OUDE APOSTOLOV MEIZWN TOU PEMQANTOV AUTON
04J-JOHN-13-17 EI TAUTA OIDATE MAKARIOI ESTE EAN POIHTE AUTA
04J-JOHN-13-18 OU PERI PANTWN UMWN LEGW EGW OIDA OUV EXELEXAMHN ALL INA H GRAFH PLHRWYH O TRWGWN MET EMOU TON ARTON EPHREN EP EME THN PTERNAN AUTOU
04J-JOHN-13-19 AP ARTI LEGW UMIN PRO TOU GENESYAI INA OTAN GENHTAI PISTEUSHTE OTI EGW EIMI
04J-JOHN-13-20 AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN O LAMBANWN EAN TINA PEMQW EME LAMBANEI O DE EME LAMBANWN LAMBANEI TON PEMQANTA ME
04J-JOHN-13-21 TAUTA EIPWN O IHSOUV ETARACYH TW PNEUMATI KAI EMARTURHSEN KAI EIPEN AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN OTI EIV EX UMWN PARADWSEI ME
04J-JOHN-13-22 EBLEPON OUN EIV ALLHLOUV OI MAYHTAI APOROUMENOI PERI TINOV LEGEI
04J-JOHN-13-23 HN DE ANAKEIMENOV EIV TWN MAYHTWN AUTOU EN TW KOLPW TOU IHSOU ON HGAPA O IHSOUV
04J-JOHN-13-24 NEUEI OUN TOUTW SIMWN PETROV PUYESYAI TIV AN EIH PERI OU LEGEI
04J-JOHN-13-25 EPIPESWN DE EKEINOV OUTWV EPI TO STHYOV TOU IHSOU LEGEI AUTW KURIE TIV ESTIN
04J-JOHN-13-26 APOKRINETAI O IHSOUV EKEINOV ESTIN W EGW BAQAV TO QWMION EPIDWSW KAI EMBAQAV TO QWMION DIDWSIN IOUDA SIMWNOV ISKARIWTH
04J-JOHN-13-27 KAI META TO QWMION TOTE EISHLYEN EIV EKEINON O SATANAV LEGEI OUN AUTW O IHSOUV O POIEIV POIHSON TACION
04J-JOHN-13-28 TOUTO DE OUDEIV EGNW TWN ANAKEIMENWN PROV TI EIPEN AUTW
04J-JOHN-13-29 TINEV GAR EDOKOUN EPEI TO GLWSSOKOMON EICEN O IOUDAV OTI LEGEI AUTW O IHSOUV AGORASON WN CREIAN ECOMEN EIV THN EORTHN H TOIV PTWCOIV INA TI DW
04J-JOHN-13-30 LABWN OUN TO QWMION EKEINOV EUYEWV EXHLYEN HN DE NUX
04J-JOHN-13-31 OTE EXHLYEN LEGEI O IHSOUV NUN EDOXASYH O UIOV TOU ANYRWPOU KAI O YEOV EDOXASYH EN AUTW
04J-JOHN-13-32 EI O YEOV EDOXASYH EN AUTW KAI O YEOV DOXASEI AUTON EN EAUTW KAI EUYUV DOXASEI AUTON
04J-JOHN-13-33 TEKNIA ETI MIKRON MEY UMWN EIMI ZHTHSETE ME KAI KAYWV EIPON TOIV IOUDAIOIV OTI OPOU UPAGW EGW UMEIV OU DUNASYE ELYEIN KAI UMIN LEGW ARTI
04J-JOHN-13-34 ENTOLHN KAINHN DIDWMI UMIN INA AGAPATE ALLHLOUV KAYWV HGAPHSA UMAV INA KAI UMEIV AGAPATE ALLHLOUV
04J-JOHN-13-35 EN TOUTW GNWSONTAI PANTEV OTI EMOI MAYHTAI ESTE EAN AGAPHN ECHTE EN ALLHLOIV
04J-JOHN-13-36 LEGEI AUTW SIMWN PETROV KURIE POU UPAGEIV APEKRIYH AUTW O IHSOUV OPOU UPAGW OU DUNASAI MOI NUN AKOLOUYHSAI USTERON DE AKOLOUYHSEIV MOI
04J-JOHN-13-37 LEGEI AUTW PETROV KURIE DIA TI OU DUNAMAI SOI AKOLOUYHSAI ARTI THN QUCHN MOU UPER SOU YHSW
04J-JOHN-13-38 APEKRIYH AUTW O IHSOUV THN QUCHN SOU UPER EMOU YHSEIV AMHN AMHN LEGW SOI OU MH ALEKTWR FWNHSH EWV OU APARNHSH ME TRIV
04J-JOHN-14-01 MH TARASSESYW UMWN H KARDIA PISTEUETE EIV TON YEON KAI EIV EME PISTEUETE
04J-JOHN-14-02 EN TH OIKIA TOU PATROV MOU MONAI POLLAI EISIN EI DE MH EIPON AN UMIN POREUOMAI ETOIMASAI TOPON UMIN
04J-JOHN-14-03 KAI EAN POREUYW ETOIMASW UMIN TOPON PALIN ERCOMAI KAI PARALHQOMAI UMAV PROV EMAUTON INA OPOU EIMI EGW KAI UMEIV HTE
04J-JOHN-14-04 KAI OPOU EGW UPAGW OIDATE KAI THN ODON OIDATE
04J-JOHN-14-05 LEGEI AUTW YWMAV KURIE OUK OIDAMEN POU UPAGEIV KAI PWV DUNAMEYA THN ODON EIDENAI
04J-JOHN-14-06 LEGEI AUTW O IHSOUV EGW EIMI H ODOV KAI H ALHYEIA KAI H ZWH OUDEIV ERCETAI PROV TON PATERA EI MH DI EMOU
04J-JOHN-14-07 EI EGNWKEITE ME KAI TON PATERA MOU EGNWKEITE AN KAI AP ARTI GINWSKETE AUTON KAI EWRAKATE AUTON
04J-JOHN-14-08 LEGEI AUTW FILIPPOV KURIE DEIXON HMIN TON PATERA KAI ARKEI HMIN
04J-JOHN-14-09 LEGEI AUTW O IHSOUV TOSOUTON CRONON MEY UMWN EIMI KAI OUK EGNWKAV ME FILIPPE O EWRAKWV EME EWRAKEN TON PATERA KAI PWV SU LEGEIV DEIXON HMIN TON PATERA
04J-JOHN-14-10 OU PISTEUEIV OTI EGW EN TW PATRI KAI O PATHR EN EMOI ESTIN TA RHMATA A EGW LALW UMIN AP EMAUTOU OU LALW O DE PATHR O EN EMOI MENWN AUTOV POIEI TA ERGA
04J-JOHN-14-11 PISTEUETE MOI OTI EGW EN TW PATRI KAI O PATHR EN EMOI EI DE MH DIA TA ERGA AUTA PISTEUETE MOI
04J-JOHN-14-12 AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN O PISTEUWN EIV EME TA ERGA A EGW POIW KAKEINOV POIHSEI KAI MEIZONA TOUTWN POIHSEI OTI EGW PROV TON PATERA MOU POREUOMAI
04J-JOHN-14-13 KAI O TI AN AITHSHTE EN TW ONOMATI MOU TOUTO POIHSW INA DOXASYH O PATHR EN TW UIW
04J-JOHN-14-14 EAN TI AITHSHTE ME EN TW ONOMATI MOU EGW POIHSW
04J-JOHN-14-15 EAN AGAPATE ME TAV ENTOLAV TAV EMAV THRHSATE
04J-JOHN-14-16 KAI EGW ERWTHSW TON PATERA KAI ALLON PARAKLHTON DWSEI UMIN INA MENH MEY UMWN EIV TON AIWNA
04J-JOHN-14-17 TO PNEUMA THV ALHYEIAV O O KOSMOV OU DUNATAI LABEIN OTI OU YEWREI AUTO OUDE GINWSKEI AUTO UMEIV DE GINWSKETE AUTO OTI PAR UMIN MENEI KAI EN UMIN ESTAI
04J-JOHN-14-18 OUK AFHSW UMAV ORFANOUV ERCOMAI PROV UMAV
04J-JOHN-14-19 ETI MIKRON KAI O KOSMOV ME OUKETI YEWREI UMEIV DE YEWREITE ME OTI EGW ZW KAI UMEIV ZHSESYE
04J-JOHN-14-20 EN EKEINH TH HMERA GNWSESYE UMEIV OTI EGW EN TW PATRI MOU KAI UMEIV EN EMOI KAI EGW EN UMIN
04J-JOHN-14-21 O ECWN TAV ENTOLAV MOU KAI THRWN AUTAV EKEINOV ESTIN O AGAPWN ME O DE AGAPWN ME AGAPHYHSETAI UPO TOU PATROV MOU KAI EGW AGAPHSW AUTON KAI EMFANISW AUTW EMAUTON
04J-JOHN-14-22 LEGEI AUTW IOUDAV OUC O ISKARIWTHV KURIE KAI TI GEGONEN OTI HMIN MELLEIV EMFANIZEIN SEAUTON KAI OUCI TW KOSMW
04J-JOHN-14-23 APEKRIYH IHSOUV KAI EIPEN AUTW EAN TIV AGAPA ME TON LOGON MOU THRHSEI KAI O PATHR MOU AGAPHSEI AUTON KAI PROV AUTON ELEUSOMEYA KAI MONHN PAR AUTW POIHSOMEN
04J-JOHN-14-24 O MH AGAPWN ME TOUV LOGOUV MOU OU THREI KAI O LOGOV ON AKOUETE OUK ESTIN EMOV ALLA TOU PEMQANTOV ME PATROV
04J-JOHN-14-25 TAUTA LELALHKA UMIN PAR UMIN MENWN
04J-JOHN-14-26 O DE PARAKLHTOV TO PNEUMA TO AGION O PEMQEI O PATHR EN TW ONOMATI MOU EKEINOV UMAV DIDAXEI PANTA KAI UPOMNHSEI UMAV PANTA A EIPON UMIN
04J-JOHN-14-27 EIRHNHN AFIHMI UMIN EIRHNHN THN EMHN DIDWMI UMIN OU KAYWV O KOSMOV DIDWSIN EGW DIDWMI UMIN MH TARASSESYW UMWN H KARDIA MHDE DEILIATW
04J-JOHN-14-28 HKOUSATE OTI EGW EIPON UMIN UPAGW KAI ERCOMAI PROV UMAV EI HGAPATE ME ECARHTE AN OTI EIPON POREUOMAI PROV TON PATERA OTI O PATHR MOU MEIZWN MOU ESTIN
04J-JOHN-14-29 KAI NUN EIRHKA UMIN PRIN GENESYAI INA OTAN GENHTAI PISTEUSHTE
04J-JOHN-14-30 OUKETI POLLA LALHSW MEY UMWN ERCETAI GAR O TOU KOSMOU ARCWN KAI EN EMOI OUK ECEI OUDEN
04J-JOHN-14-31 ALL INA GNW O KOSMOV OTI AGAPW TON PATERA KAI KAYWV ENETEILATO MOI O PATHR OUTWV POIW EGEIRESYE AGWMEN ENTEUYEN
04J-JOHN-15-01 EGW EIMI H AMPELOV H ALHYINH KAI O PATHR MOU O GEWRGOV ESTIN
04J-JOHN-15-02 PAN KLHMA EN EMOI MH FERON KARPON AIREI AUTO KAI PAN TO KARPON FERON KAYAIREI AUTO INA PLEIONA KARPON FERH
04J-JOHN-15-03 HDH UMEIV KAYAROI ESTE DIA TON LOGON ON LELALHKA UMIN
04J-JOHN-15-04 MEINATE EN EMOI KAGW EN UMIN KAYWV TO KLHMA OU DUNATAI KARPON FEREIN AF EAUTOU EAN MH MEINH EN TH AMPELW OUTWV OUDE UMEIV EAN MH EN EMOI MEINHTE
04J-JOHN-15-05 EGW EIMI H AMPELOV UMEIV TA KLHMATA O MENWN EN EMOI KAGW EN AUTW OUTOV FEREI KARPON POLUN OTI CWRIV EMOU OU DUNASYE POIEIN OUDEN
04J-JOHN-15-06 EAN MH TIV MEINH EN EMOI EBLHYH EXW WV TO KLHMA KAI EXHRANYH KAI SUNAGOUSIN AUTA KAI EIV TO PUR BALLOUSIN KAI KAIETAI
04J-JOHN-15-07 EAN MEINHTE EN EMOI KAI TA RHMATA MOU EN UMIN MEINH O EAN YELHTE AITHSESYE KAI GENHSETAI UMIN
04J-JOHN-15-08 EN TOUTW EDOXASYH O PATHR MOU INA KARPON POLUN FERHTE KAI GENHSESYE EMOI MAYHTAI
04J-JOHN-15-09 KAYWV HGAPHSEN ME O PATHR KAGW HGAPHSA UMAV MEINATE EN TH AGAPH TH EMH
04J-JOHN-15-10 EAN TAV ENTOLAV MOU THRHSHTE MENEITE EN TH AGAPH MOU KAYWV EGW TAV ENTOLAV TOU PATROV MOU TETHRHKA KAI MENW AUTOU EN TH AGAPH
04J-JOHN-15-11 TAUTA LELALHKA UMIN INA H CARA H EMH EN UMIN MEINH KAI H CARA UMWN PLHRWYH
04J-JOHN-15-12 AUTH ESTIN H ENTOLH H EMH INA AGAPATE ALLHLOUV KAYWV HGAPHSA UMAV
04J-JOHN-15-13 MEIZONA TAUTHV AGAPHN OUDEIV ECEI INA TIV THN QUCHN AUTOU YH UPER TWN FILWN AUTOU
04J-JOHN-15-14 UMEIV FILOI MOU ESTE EAN POIHTE OSA EGW ENTELLOMAI UMIN
04J-JOHN-15-15 OUKETI UMAV LEGW DOULOUV OTI O DOULOV OUK OIDEN TI POIEI AUTOU O KURIOV UMAV DE EIRHKA FILOUV OTI PANTA A HKOUSA PARA TOU PATROV MOU EGNWRISA UMIN
04J-JOHN-15-16 OUC UMEIV ME EXELEXASYE ALL EGW EXELEXAMHN UMAV KAI EYHKA UMAV INA UMEIV UPAGHTE KAI KARPON FERHTE KAI O KARPOV UMWN MENH INA O TI AN AITHSHTE TON PATERA EN TW ONOMATI MOU DW UMIN
04J-JOHN-15-17 TAUTA ENTELLOMAI UMIN INA AGAPATE ALLHLOUV
04J-JOHN-15-18 EI O KOSMOV UMAV MISEI GINWSKETE OTI EME PRWTON UMWN MEMISHKEN
04J-JOHN-15-19 EI EK TOU KOSMOU HTE O KOSMOV AN TO IDION EFILEI OTI DE EK TOU KOSMOU OUK ESTE ALL EGW EXELEXAMHN UMAV EK TOU KOSMOU DIA TOUTO MISEI UMAV O KOSMOV
04J-JOHN-15-20 MNHMONEUETE TOU LOGOU OU EGW EIPON UMIN OUK ESTIN DOULOV MEIZWN TOU KURIOU AUTOU EI EME EDIWXAN KAI UMAV DIWXOUSIN EI TON LOGON MOU ETHRHSAN KAI TON UMETERON THRHSOUSIN
04J-JOHN-15-21 ALLA TAUTA PANTA POIHSOUSIN UMIN DIA TO ONOMA MOU OTI OUK OIDASIN TON PEMQANTA ME
04J-JOHN-15-22 EI MH HLYON KAI ELALHSA AUTOIV AMARTIAN OUK EICON NUN DE PROFASIN OUK ECOUSIN PERI THV AMARTIAV AUTWN
04J-JOHN-15-23 O EME MISWN KAI TON PATERA MOU MISEI
04J-JOHN-15-24 EI TA ERGA MH EPOIHSA EN AUTOIV A OUDEIV ALLOV PEPOIHKEN AMARTIAN OUK EICON NUN DE KAI EWRAKASIN KAI MEMISHKASIN KAI EME KAI TON PATERA MOU
04J-JOHN-15-25 ALL INA PLHRWYH O LOGOV O GEGRAMMENOV EN TW NOMW AUTWN OTI EMISHSAN ME DWREAN
04J-JOHN-15-26 OTAN DE ELYH O PARAKLHTOV ON EGW PEMQW UMIN PARA TOU PATROV TO PNEUMA THV ALHYEIAV O PARA TOU PATROV EKPOREUETAI EKEINOV MARTURHSEI PERI EMOU
04J-JOHN-15-27 KAI UMEIV DE MARTUREITE OTI AP ARCHV MET EMOU ESTE
04J-JOHN-16-01 TAUTA LELALHKA UMIN INA MH SKANDALISYHTE
04J-JOHN-16-02 APOSUNAGWGOUV POIHSOUSIN UMAV ALL ERCETAI WRA INA PAV O APOKTEINAV UMAV DOXH LATREIAN PROSFEREIN TW YEW
04J-JOHN-16-03 KAI TAUTA POIHSOUSIN OTI OUK EGNWSAN TON PATERA OUDE EME
04J-JOHN-16-04 ALLA TAUTA LELALHKA UMIN INA OTAN ELYH H WRA MNHMONEUHTE AUTWN OTI EGW EIPON UMIN TAUTA DE UMIN EX ARCHV OUK EIPON OTI MEY UMWN HMHN
04J-JOHN-16-05 NUN DE UPAGW PROV TON PEMQANTA ME KAI OUDEIV EX UMWN ERWTA ME POU UPAGEIV
04J-JOHN-16-06 ALL OTI TAUTA LELALHKA UMIN H LUPH PEPLHRWKEN UMWN THN KARDIAN
04J-JOHN-16-07 ALL EGW THN ALHYEIAN LEGW UMIN SUMFEREI UMIN INA EGW APELYW EAN GAR EGW MH APELYW O PARAKLHTOV OUK ELEUSETAI PROV UMAV EAN DE POREUYW PEMQW AUTON PROV UMAV
04J-JOHN-16-08 KAI ELYWN EKEINOV ELEGXEI TON KOSMON PERI AMARTIAV KAI PERI DIKAIOSUNHV KAI PERI KRISEWV

04J-JOHN-16-10 PERI DIKAIOSUNHV DE OTI PROV TON PATERA MOU UPAGW KAI OUKETI YEWREITE ME
04J-JOHN-16-11 PERI DE KRISEWV OTI O ARCWN TOU KOSMOU TOUTOU KEKRITAI
04J-JOHN-16-12 ETI POLLA ECW LEGEIN UMIN ALL OU DUNASYE BASTAZEIN ARTI
04J-JOHN-16-13 OTAN DE ELYH EKEINOV TO PNEUMA THV ALHYEIAV ODHGHSEI UMAV EIV PASAN THN ALHYEIAN OU GAR LALHSEI AF EAUTOU ALL OSA AN AKOUSH LALHSEI KAI TA ERCOMENA ANAGGELEI UMIN
04J-JOHN-16-14 EKEINOV EME DOXASEI OTI EK TOU EMOU LHQETAI KAI ANAGGELEI UMIN
04J-JOHN-16-15 PANTA OSA ECEI O PATHR EMA ESTIN DIA TOUTO EIPON OTI EK TOU EMOU LAMBANEI KAI ANAGGELEI UMIN
04J-JOHN-16-16 MIKRON KAI OU YEWREITE ME KAI PALIN MIKRON KAI OQESYE ME OTI UPAGW PROV TON PATERA
04J-JOHN-16-17 EIPON OUN EK TWN MAYHTWN AUTOU PROV ALLHLOUV TI ESTIN TOUTO O LEGEI HMIN MIKRON KAI OU YEWREITE ME KAI PALIN MIKRON KAI OQESYE ME KAI OTI EGW UPAGW PROV TON PATERA
04J-JOHN-16-18 ELEGON OUN TOUTO TI ESTIN O LEGEI TO MIKRON OUK OIDAMEN TI LALEI
04J-JOHN-16-19 EGNW OUN O IHSOUV OTI HYELON AUTON ERWTAN KAI EIPEN AUTOIV PERI TOUTOU ZHTEITE MET ALLHLWN OTI EIPON MIKRON KAI OU YEWREITE ME KAI PALIN MIKRON KAI OQESYE ME
04J-JOHN-16-20 AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN OTI KLAUSETE KAI YRHNHSETE UMEIV O DE KOSMOV CARHSETAI UMEIV DE LUPHYHSESYE ALL H LUPH UMWN EIV CARAN GENHSETAI
04J-JOHN-16-21 H GUNH OTAN TIKTH LUPHN ECEI OTI HLYEN H WRA AUTHV OTAN DE GENNHSH TO PAIDION OUKETI MNHMONEUEI THV YLIQEWV DIA THN CARAN OTI EGENNHYH ANYRWPOV EIV TON KOSMON
04J-JOHN-16-22 KAI UMEIV OUN LUPHN MEN NUN ECETE PALIN DE OQOMAI UMAV KAI CARHSETAI UMWN H KARDIA KAI THN CARAN UMWN OUDEIV AIREI AF UMWN
04J-JOHN-16-23 KAI EN EKEINH TH HMERA EME OUK ERWTHSETE OUDEN AMHN AMHN LEGW UMIN OTI OSA AN AITHSHTE TON PATERA EN TW ONOMATI MOU DWSEI UMIN
04J-JOHN-16-24 EWV ARTI OUK HTHSATE OUDEN EN TW ONOMATI MOU AITEITE KAI LHQESYE INA H CARA UMWN H PEPLHRWMENH
04J-JOHN-16-25 TAUTA EN PAROIMIAIV LELALHKA UMIN ALL ERCETAI WRA OTE OUKETI EN PAROIMIAIV LALHSW UMIN ALLA PARRHSIA PERI TOU PATROV ANAGGELW UMIN
04J-JOHN-16-26 EN EKEINH TH HMERA EN TW ONOMATI MOU AITHSESYE KAI OU LEGW UMIN OTI EGW ERWTHSW TON PATERA PERI UMWN
04J-JOHN-16-27 AUTOV GAR O PATHR FILEI UMAV OTI UMEIV EME PEFILHKATE KAI PEPISTEUKATE OTI EGW PARA TOU YEOU EXHLYON
04J-JOHN-16-28 EXHLYON PARA TOU PATROV KAI ELHLUYA EIV TON KOSMON PALIN AFIHMI TON KOSMON KAI POREUOMAI PROV TON PATERA
04J-JOHN-16-29 LEGOUSIN AUTW OI MAYHTAI AUTOU IDE NUN PARRHSIA LALEIV KAI PAROIMIAN OUDEMIAN LEGEIV
04J-JOHN-16-30 NUN OIDAMEN OTI OIDAV PANTA KAI OU CREIAN ECEIV INA TIV SE ERWTA EN TOUTW PISTEUOMEN OTI APO YEOU EXHLYEV
04J-JOHN-16-31 APEKRIYH AUTOIV O IHSOUV ARTI PISTEUETE
04J-JOHN-16-32 IDOU ERCETAI WRA KAI NUN ELHLUYEN INA SKORPISYHTE EKASTOV EIV TA IDIA KAI EME MONON AFHTE KAI OUK EIMI MONOV OTI O PATHR MET EMOU ESTIN
04J-JOHN-16-33 TAUTA LELALHKA UMIN INA EN EMOI EIRHNHN ECHTE EN TW KOSMW YLIQIN ECETE ALLA YARSEITE EGW NENIKHKA TON KOSMON
04J-JOHN-17-01 TAUTA ELALHSEN O IHSOUV KAI EPHREN TOUV OFYALMOUV AUTOU EIV TON OURANON KAI EIPEN PATER ELHLUYEN H WRA DOXASON SOU TON UION INA KAI O UIOV SOU DOXASH SE
04J-JOHN-17-02 KAYWV EDWKAV AUTW EXOUSIAN PASHV SARKOV INA PAN O DEDWKAV AUTW DWSEI AUTOIV ZWHN AIWNION
04J-JOHN-17-03 AUTH DE ESTIN H AIWNIOV ZWH INA GINWSKWSIN SE TON MONON ALHYINON YEON KAI ON APESTEILAV IHSOUN CRISTON
04J-JOHN-17-04 EGW SE EDOXASA EPI THV GHV TO ERGON ETELEIWSA O DEDWKAV MOI INA POIHSW
04J-JOHN-17-05 KAI NUN DOXASON ME SU PATER PARA SEAUTW TH DOXH H EICON PRO TOU TON KOSMON EINAI PARA SOI
04J-JOHN-17-06 EFANERWSA SOU TO ONOMA TOIV ANYRWPOIV OUV DEDWKAV MOI EK TOU KOSMOU SOI HSAN KAI EMOI AUTOUV DEDWKAV KAI TON LOGON SOU TETHRHKASIN
04J-JOHN-17-07 NUN EGNWKAN OTI PANTA OSA DEDWKAV MOI PARA SOU ESTIN
04J-JOHN-17-08 OTI TA RHMATA A DEDWKAV MOI DEDWKA AUTOIV KAI AUTOI ELABON KAI EGNWSAN ALHYWV OTI PARA SOU EXHLYON KAI EPISTEUSAN OTI SU ME APESTEILAV
04J-JOHN-17-09 EGW PERI AUTWN ERWTW OU PERI TOU KOSMOU ERWTW ALLA PERI WN DEDWKAV MOI OTI SOI EISIN
04J-JOHN-17-10 KAI TA EMA PANTA SA ESTIN KAI TA SA EMA KAI DEDOXASMAI EN AUTOIV
04J-JOHN-17-11 KAI OUKETI EIMI EN TW KOSMW KAI OUTOI EN TW KOSMW EISIN KAI EGW PROV SE ERCOMAI PATER AGIE THRHSON AUTOUV EN TW ONOMATI SOU W DEDWKAV MOI INA WSIN EN KAYWV HMEIV
04J-JOHN-17-12 OTE HMHN MET AUTWN EN TW KOSMW EGW ETHROUN AUTOUV EN TW ONOMATI SOU OUV DEDWKAV MOI EFULAXA KAI OUDEIV EX AUTWN APWLETO EI MH O UIOV THV APWLEIAV INA H GRAFH PLHRWYH
04J-JOHN-17-13 NUN DE PROV SE ERCOMAI KAI TAUTA LALW EN TW KOSMW INA ECWSIN THN CARAN THN EMHN PEPLHRWMENHN EN AUTOIV
04J-JOHN-17-14 EGW DEDWKA AUTOIV TON LOGON SOU KAI O KOSMOV EMISHSEN AUTOUV OTI OUK EISIN EK TOU KOSMOU KAYWV EGW OUK EIMI EK TOU KOSMOU
04J-JOHN-17-15 OUK ERWTW INA ARHV AUTOUV EK TOU KOSMOU ALL INA THRHSHV AUTOUV EK TOU PONHROU
04J-JOHN-17-16 EK TOU KOSMOU OUK EISIN KAYWV EGW EK TOU KOSMOU OUK EIMI
04J-JOHN-17-17 AGIASON AUTOUV EN TH ALHYEIA SOU O LOGOV O SOV ALHYEIA ESTIN
04J-JOHN-17-18 KAYWV EME APESTEILAV EIV TON KOSMON KAGW APESTEILA AUTOUV EIV TON KOSMON
04J-JOHN-17-19 KAI UPER AUTWN EGW AGIAZW EMAUTON INA KAI AUTOI WSIN HGIASMENOI EN ALHYEIA
04J-JOHN-17-20 OU PERI TOUTWN DE ERWTW MONON ALLA KAI PERI TWN PISTEUONTWN DIA TOU LOGOU AUTWN EIV EME
04J-JOHN-17-21 INA PANTEV EN WSIN KAYWV SU PATER EN EMOI KAGW EN SOI INA KAI AUTOI EN HMIN EN WSIN INA O KOSMOV PISTEUSH OTI SU ME APESTEILAV
04J-JOHN-17-22 KAI EGW THN DOXAN HN DEDWKAV MOI DEDWKA AUTOIV INA WSIN EN KAYWV HMEIV EN ESMEN
04J-JOHN-17-23 EGW EN AUTOIV KAI SU EN EMOI INA WSIN TETELEIWMENOI EIV EN KAI INA GINWSKH O KOSMOV OTI SU ME APESTEILAV KAI HGAPHSAV AUTOUV KAYWV EME HGAPHSAV
04J-JOHN-17-24 PATER OUV DEDWKAV MOI YELW INA OPOU EIMI EGW KAKEINOI WSIN MET EMOU INA YEWRWSIN THN DOXAN THN EMHN HN EDWKAV MOI OTI HGAPHSAV ME PRO KATABOLHV KOSMOU
04J-JOHN-17-25 PATER DIKAIE KAI O KOSMOV SE OUK EGNW EGW DE SE EGNWN KAI OUTOI EGNWSAN OTI SU ME APESTEILAV
04J-JOHN-17-26 KAI EGNWRISA AUTOIV TO ONOMA SOU KAI GNWRISW INA H AGAPH HN HGAPHSAV ME EN AUTOIV H KAGW EN AUTOIV
04J-JOHN-18-01 TAUTA EIPWN O IHSOUV EXHLYEN SUN TOIV MAYHTAIV AUTOU PERAN TOU CEIMARROU TWN KEDRWN OPOU HN KHPOV EIV ON EISHLYEN AUTOV KAI OI MAYHTAI AUTOU
04J-JOHN-18-02 HDEI DE KAI IOUDAV O PARADIDOUV AUTON TON TOPON OTI POLLAKIV SUNHCYH O IHSOUV EKEI META TWN MAYHTWN AUTOU
04J-JOHN-18-03 O OUN IOUDAV LABWN THN SPEIRAN KAI EK TWN ARCIEREWN KAI FARISAIWN UPHRETAV ERCETAI EKEI META FANWN KAI LAMPADWN KAI OPLWN
04J-JOHN-18-04 IHSOUV OUN EIDWV PANTA TA ERCOMENA EP AUTON EXELYWN EIPEN AUTOIV TINA ZHTEITE
04J-JOHN-18-05 APEKRIYHSAN AUTW IHSOUN TON NAZWRAION LEGEI AUTOIV O IHSOUV EGW EIMI EISTHKEI DE KAI IOUDAV O PARADIDOUV AUTON MET AUTWN
04J-JOHN-18-06 WV OUN EIPEN AUTOIV OTI EGW EIMI APHLYON EIV TA OPISW KAI EPESON CAMAI
04J-JOHN-18-07 PALIN OUN AUTOUV EPHRWTHSEN TINA ZHTEITE OI DE EIPON IHSOUN TON NAZWRAION
04J-JOHN-18-08 APEKRIYH IHSOUV EIPON UMIN OTI EGW EIMI EI OUN EME ZHTEITE AFETE TOUTOUV UPAGEIN
04J-JOHN-18-09 INA PLHRWYH O LOGOV ON EIPEN OTI OUV DEDWKAV MOI OUK APWLESA EX AUTWN OUDENA
04J-JOHN-18-10 SIMWN OUN PETROV ECWN MACAIRAN EILKUSEN AUTHN KAI EPAISEN TON TOU ARCIEREWV DOULON KAI APEKOQEN AUTOU TO WTION TO DEXION HN DE ONOMA TW DOULW MALCOV
04J-JOHN-18-11 EIPEN OUN O IHSOUV TW PETRW BALE THN MACAIRAN SOU EIV THN YHKHN TO POTHRION O DEDWKEN MOI O PATHR OU MH PIW AUTO
04J-JOHN-18-12 H OUN SPEIRA KAI O CILIARCOV KAI OI UPHRETAI TWN IOUDAIWN SUNELABON TON IHSOUN KAI EDHSAN AUTON
04J-JOHN-18-13 KAI APHGAGON AUTON PROV ANNAN PRWTON HN GAR PENYEROV TOU KAIAFA OV HN ARCIEREUV TOU ENIAUTOU EKEINOU
04J-JOHN-18-14 HN DE KAIAFAV O SUMBOULEUSAV TOIV IOUDAIOIV OTI SUMFEREI ENA ANYRWPON APOLESYAI UPER TOU LAOU
04J-JOHN-18-15 HKOLOUYEI DE TW IHSOU SIMWN PETROV KAI O ALLOV MAYHTHV O DE MAYHTHV EKEINOV HN GNWSTOV TW ARCIEREI KAI SUNEISHLYEN TW IHSOU EIV THN AULHN TOU ARCIEREWV
04J-JOHN-18-16 O DE PETROV EISTHKEI PROV TH YURA EXW EXHLYEN OUN O MAYHTHV O ALLOV OV HN GNWSTOV TW ARCIEREI KAI EIPEN TH YURWRW KAI EISHGAGEN TON PETRON
04J-JOHN-18-17 LEGEI OUN H PAIDISKH H YURWROV TW PETRW MH KAI SU EK TWN MAYHTWN EI TOU ANYRWPOU TOUTOU LEGEI EKEINOV OUK EIMI
04J-JOHN-18-18 EISTHKEISAN DE OI DOULOI KAI OI UPHRETAI ANYRAKIAN PEPOIHKOTEV OTI QUCOV HN KAI EYERMAINONTO HN DE MET AUTWN O PETROV ESTWV KAI YERMAINOMENOV
04J-JOHN-18-19 O OUN ARCIEREUV HRWTHSEN TON IHSOUN PERI TWN MAYHTWN AUTOU KAI PERI THV DIDACHV AUTOU
04J-JOHN-18-20 APEKRIYH AUTW O IHSOUV EGW PARRHSIA ELALHSA TW KOSMW EGW PANTOTE EDIDAXA EN SUNAGWGH KAI EN TW IERW OPOU PANTOTE OI IOUDAIOI SUNERCONTAI KAI EN KRUPTW ELALHSA OUDEN
04J-JOHN-18-21 TI ME EPERWTAV EPERWTHSON TOUV AKHKOOTAV TI ELALHSA AUTOIV IDE OUTOI OIDASIN A EIPON EGW
04J-JOHN-18-22 TAUTA DE AUTOU EIPONTOV EIV TWN UPHRETWN PARESTHKWV EDWKEN RAPISMA TW IHSOU EIPWN OUTWV APOKRINH TW ARCIEREI
04J-JOHN-18-23 APEKRIYH AUTW O IHSOUV EI KAKWV ELALHSA MARTURHSON PERI TOU KAKOU EI DE KALWV TI ME DEREIV
04J-JOHN-18-24 APESTEILEN AUTON O ANNAV DEDEMENON PROV KAIAFAN TON ARCIEREA
04J-JOHN-18-25 HN DE SIMWN PETROV ESTWV KAI YERMAINOMENOV EIPON OUN AUTW MH KAI SU EK TWN MAYHTWN AUTOU EI HRNHSATO OUN EKEINOV KAI EIPEN OUK EIMI
04J-JOHN-18-26 LEGEI EIV EK TWN DOULWN TOU ARCIEREWV SUGGENHV WN OU APEKOQEN PETROV TO WTION OUK EGW SE EIDON EN TW KHPW MET AUTOU
04J-JOHN-18-27 PALIN OUN HRNHSATO O PETROV KAI EUYEWV ALEKTWR EFWNHSEN
04J-JOHN-18-28 AGOUSIN OUN TON IHSOUN APO TOU KAIAFA EIV TO PRAITWRION HN DE PRWI KAI AUTOI OUK EISHLYON EIV TO PRAITWRION INA MH MIANYWSIN ALL INA FAGWSIN TO PASCA
04J-JOHN-18-29 EXHLYEN OUN O PILATOV PROV AUTOUV KAI EIPEN TINA KATHGORIAN FERETE KATA TOU ANYRWPOU TOUTOU
04J-JOHN-18-30 APEKRIYHSAN KAI EIPON AUTW EI MH HN OUTOV KAKOPOIOV OUK AN SOI PAREDWKAMEN AUTON
04J-JOHN-18-31 EIPEN OUN AUTOIV O PILATOV LABETE AUTON UMEIV KAI KATA TON NOMON UMWN KRINATE AUTON EIPON OUN AUTW OI IOUDAIOI HMIN OUK EXESTIN APOKTEINAI OUDENA
04J-JOHN-18-32 INA O LOGOV TOU IHSOU PLHRWYH ON EIPEN SHMAINWN POIW YANATW HMELLEN APOYNHSKEIN
04J-JOHN-18-33 EISHLYEN OUN EIV TO PRAITWRION PALIN O PILATOV KAI EFWNHSEN TON IHSOUN KAI EIPEN AUTW SU EI O BASILEUV TWN IOUDAIWN
04J-JOHN-18-34 APEKRIYH AUTW O IHSOUV AF EAUTOU SU TOUTO LEGEIV H ALLOI SOI EIPON PERI EMOU
04J-JOHN-18-35 APEKRIYH O PILATOV MHTI EGW IOUDAIOV EIMI TO EYNOV TO SON KAI OI ARCIEREIV PAREDWKAN SE EMOI TI EPOIHSAV
04J-JOHN-18-36 APEKRIYH IHSOUV H BASILEIA H EMH OUK ESTIN EK TOU KOSMOU TOUTOU EI EK TOU KOSMOU TOUTOU HN H BASILEIA H EMH OI UPHRETAI AN OI EMOI HGWNIZONTO INA MH PARADOYW TOIV IOUDAIOIV NUN DE H BASILEIA H EMH OUK ESTIN ENTEUYEN
04J-JOHN-18-37 EIPEN OUN AUTW O PILATOV OUKOUN BASILEUV EI SU APEKRIYH IHSOUV SU LEGEIV OTI BASILEUV EIMI EGW EGW EIV TOUTO GEGENNHMAI KAI EIV TOUTO ELHLUYA EIV TON KOSMON INA MARTURHSW TH ALHYEIA PAV O WN EK THV ALHYEIAV AKOUEI MOU THV FWNHV
04J-JOHN-18-38 LEGEI AUTW O PILATOV TI ESTIN ALHYEIA KAI TOUTO EIPWN PALIN EXHLYEN PROV TOUV IOUDAIOUV KAI LEGEI AUTOIV EGW OUDEMIAN AITIAN EURISKW EN AUTW
04J-JOHN-18-39 ESTIN DE SUNHYEIA UMIN INA ENA UMIN APOLUSW EN TW PASCA BOULESYE OUN UMIN APOLUSW TON BASILEA TWN IOUDAIWN
04J-JOHN-18-40 EKRAUGASAN OUN PALIN PANTEV LEGONTEV MH TOUTON ALLA TON BARABBAN HN DE O BARABBAV LHSTHV
04J-JOHN-19-01 TOTE OUN ELABEN O PILATOV TON IHSOUN KAI EMASTIGWSEN
04J-JOHN-19-02 KAI OI STRATIWTAI PLEXANTEV STEFANON EX AKANYWN EPEYHKAN AUTOU TH KEFALH KAI IMATION PORFUROUN PERIEBALON AUTON
04J-JOHN-19-03 KAI ELEGON CAIRE O BASILEUV TWN IOUDAIWN KAI EDIDOUN AUTW RAPISMATA
04J-JOHN-19-04 EXHLYEN OUN PALIN EXW O PILATOV KAI LEGEI AUTOIV IDE AGW UMIN AUTON EXW INA GNWTE OTI EN AUTW OUDEMIAN AITIAN EURISKW
04J-JOHN-19-05 EXHLYEN OUN O IHSOUV EXW FORWN TON AKANYINON STEFANON KAI TO PORFUROUN IMATION KAI LEGEI AUTOIV IDE O ANYRWPOV
04J-JOHN-19-06 OTE OUN EIDON AUTON OI ARCIEREIV KAI OI UPHRETAI EKRAUGASAN LEGONTEV STAURWSON STAURWSON AUTON LEGEI AUTOIV O PILATOV LABETE AUTON UMEIV KAI STAURWSATE EGW GAR OUC EURISKW EN AUTW AITIAN
04J-JOHN-19-07 APEKRIYHSAN AUTW OI IOUDAIOI HMEIV NOMON ECOMEN KAI KATA TON NOMON HMWN OFEILEI APOYANEIN OTI EAUTON UION YEOU EPOIHSEN
04J-JOHN-19-08 OTE OUN HKOUSEN O PILATOV TOUTON TON LOGON MALLON EFOBHYH
04J-JOHN-19-09 KAI EISHLYEN EIV TO PRAITWRION PALIN KAI LEGEI TW IHSOU POYEN EI SU O DE IHSOUV APOKRISIN OUK EDWKEN AUTW
04J-JOHN-19-10 LEGEI OUN AUTW O PILATOV EMOI OU LALEIV OUK OIDAV OTI EXOUSIAN ECW STAURWSAI SE KAI EXOUSIAN ECW APOLUSAI SE
04J-JOHN-19-11 APEKRIYH IHSOUV OUK EICEV EXOUSIAN OUDEMIAN KAT EMOU EI MH HN SOI DEDOMENON ANWYEN DIA TOUTO O PARADIDOUV ME SOI MEIZONA AMARTIAN ECEI
04J-JOHN-19-12 EK TOUTOU EZHTEI O PILATOV APOLUSAI AUTON OI DE IOUDAIOI EKRAZON LEGONTEV EAN TOUTON APOLUSHV OUK EI FILOV TOU KAISAROV PAV O BASILEA EAUTON POIWN ANTILEGEI TW KAISARI
04J-JOHN-19-13 O OUN PILATOV AKOUSAV TOUTON TON LOGON HGAGEN EXW TON IHSOUN KAI EKAYISEN EPI TOU BHMATOV EIV TOPON LEGOMENON LIYOSTRWTON EBRAISTI DE GABBAYA
04J-JOHN-19-14 HN DE PARASKEUH TOU PASCA WRA DE WSEI EKTH KAI LEGEI TOIV IOUDAIOIV IDE O BASILEUV UMWN
04J-JOHN-19-15 OI DE EKRAUGASAN ARON ARON STAURWSON AUTON LEGEI AUTOIV O PILATOV TON BASILEA UMWN STAURWSW APEKRIYHSAN OI ARCIEREIV OUK ECOMEN BASILEA EI MH KAISARA
04J-JOHN-19-16 TOTE OUN PAREDWKEN AUTON AUTOIV INA STAURWYH PARELABON DE TON IHSOUN KAI HGAGON
04J-JOHN-19-17 KAI BASTAZWN TON STAURON AUTOU EXHLYEN EIV TOPON LEGOMENON KRANIOU TOPON OV LEGETAI EBRAISTI GOLGOYA
04J-JOHN-19-18 OPOU AUTON ESTAURWSAN KAI MET AUTOU ALLOUV DUO ENTEUYEN KAI ENTEUYEN MESON DE TON IHSOUN
04J-JOHN-19-19 EGRAQEN DE KAI TITLON O PILATOV KAI EYHKEN EPI TOU STAUROU HN DE GEGRAMMENON IHSOUV O NAZWRAIOV O BASILEUV TWN IOUDAIWN
04J-JOHN-19-20 TOUTON OUN TON TITLON POLLOI ANEGNWSAN TWN IOUDAIWN OTI EGGUV HN O TOPOV THV POLEWV OPOU ESTAURWYH O IHSOUV KAI HN GEGRAMMENON EBRAISTI ELLHNISTI RWMAISTI
04J-JOHN-19-21 ELEGON OUN TW PILATW OI ARCIEREIV TWN IOUDAIWN MH GRAFE O BASILEUV TWN IOUDAIWN ALL OTI EKEINOV EIPEN BASILEUV EIMI TWN IOUDAIWN
04J-JOHN-19-22 APEKRIYH O PILATOV O GEGRAFA GEGRAFA
04J-JOHN-19-23 OI OUN STRATIWTAI OTE ESTAURWSAN TON IHSOUN ELABON TA IMATIA AUTOU KAI EPOIHSAN TESSARA MERH EKASTW STRATIWTH MEROV KAI TON CITWNA HN DE O CITWN ARAFOV EK TWN ANWYEN UFANTOV DI OLOU
04J-JOHN-19-24 EIPON OUN PROV ALLHLOUV MH SCISWMEN AUTON ALLA LACWMEN PERI AUTOU TINOV ESTAI INA H GRAFH PLHRWYH H LEGOUSA DIEMERISANTO TA IMATIA MOU EAUTOIV KAI EPI TON IMATISMON MOU EBALON KLHRON OI MEN OUN STRATIWTAI TAUTA EPOIHSAN
04J-JOHN-19-25 EISTHKEISAN DE PARA TW STAURW TOU IHSOU H MHTHR AUTOU KAI H ADELFH THV MHTROV AUTOU MARIA H TOU KLWPA KAI MARIA H MAGDALHNH
04J-JOHN-19-26 IHSOUV OUN IDWN THN MHTERA KAI TON MAYHTHN PARESTWTA ON HGAPA LEGEI TH MHTRI AUTOU GUNAI IDOU O UIOV SOU
04J-JOHN-19-27 EITA LEGEI TW MAYHTH IDOU H MHTHR SOU KAI AP EKEINHV THV WRAV ELABEN O MAYHTHV AUTHN EIV TA IDIA
04J-JOHN-19-28 META TOUTO IDWN O IHSOUV OTI PANTA HDH TETELESTAI INA TELEIWYH H GRAFH LEGEI DIQW
04J-JOHN-19-29 SKEUOV OUN EKEITO OXOUV MESTON OI DE PLHSANTEV SPOGGON OXOUV KAI USSWPW PERIYENTEV PROSHNEGKAN AUTOU TW STOMATI
04J-JOHN-19-30 OTE OUN ELABEN TO OXOV O IHSOUV EIPEN TETELESTAI KAI KLINAV THN KEFALHN PAREDWKEN TO PNEUMA
04J-JOHN-19-31 OI OUN IOUDAIOI INA MH MEINH EPI TOU STAUROU TA SWMATA EN TW SABBATW EPEI PARASKEUH HN HN GAR MEGALH H HMERA EKEINOU TOU SABBATOU HRWTHSAN TON PILATON INA KATEAGWSIN AUTWN TA SKELH KAI ARYWSIN
04J-JOHN-19-32 HLYON OUN OI STRATIWTAI KAI TOU MEN PRWTOU KATEAXAN TA SKELH KAI TOU ALLOU TOU SUSTAURWYENTOV AUTW
04J-JOHN-19-33 EPI DE TON IHSOUN ELYONTEV WV EIDON AUTON HDH TEYNHKOTA OU KATEAXAN AUTOU TA SKELH
04J-JOHN-19-34 ALL EIV TWN STRATIWTWN LOGCH AUTOU THN PLEURAN ENUXEN KAI EUYEWV EXHLYEN AIMA KAI UDWR
04J-JOHN-19-35 KAI O EWRAKWV MEMARTURHKEN KAI ALHYINH ESTIN AUTOU H MARTURIA KAKEINOV OIDEN OTI ALHYH LEGEI INA UMEIV PISTEUSHTE
04J-JOHN-19-36 EGENETO GAR TAUTA INA H GRAFH PLHRWYH OSTOUN OU SUNTRIBHSETAI AP AUTOU
04J-JOHN-19-37 KAI PALIN ETERA GRAFH LEGEI OQONTAI EIV ON EXEKENTHSAN
04J-JOHN-19-38 META TAUTA HRWTHSEN TON PILATON IWSHF O APO ARIMAYAIAV WN MAYHTHV TOU IHSOU KEKRUMMENOV DE DIA TON FOBON TWN IOUDAIWN INA ARH TO SWMA TOU IHSOU KAI EPETREQEN O PILATOV HLYEN OUN KAI HREN TO SWMA TOU IHSOU
04J-JOHN-19-39 HLYEN DE KAI NIKODHMOV O ELYWN PROV TON IHSOUN NUKTOV TO PRWTON FERWN MIGMA SMURNHV KAI ALOHV WV LITRAV EKATON
04J-JOHN-19-40 ELABON OUN TO SWMA TOU IHSOU KAI EDHSAN AUTO EN OYONIOIV META TWN ARWMATWN KAYWV EYOV ESTIN TOIV IOUDAIOIV ENTAFIAZEIN
04J-JOHN-19-41 HN DE EN TW TOPW OPOU ESTAURWYH KHPOV KAI EN TW KHPW MNHMEION KAINON EN W OUDEPW OUDEIV ETEYH
04J-JOHN-19-42 EKEI OUN DIA THN PARASKEUHN TWN IOUDAIWN OTI EGGUV HN TO MNHMEION EYHKAN TON IHSOUN
04J-JOHN-20-01 TH DE MIA TWN SABBATWN MARIA H MAGDALHNH ERCETAI PRWI SKOTIAV ETI OUSHV EIV TO MNHMEION KAI BLEPEI TON LIYON HRMENON EK TOU MNHMEIOU
04J-JOHN-20-02 TRECEI OUN KAI ERCETAI PROV SIMWNA PETRON KAI PROV TON ALLON MAYHTHN ON EFILEI O IHSOUV KAI LEGEI AUTOIV HRAN TON KURION EK TOU MNHMEIOU KAI OUK OIDAMEN POU EYHKAN AUTON
04J-JOHN-20-03 EXHLYEN OUN O PETROV KAI O ALLOV MAYHTHV KAI HRCONTO EIV TO MNHMEION
04J-JOHN-20-04 ETRECON DE OI DUO OMOU KAI O ALLOV MAYHTHV PROEDRAMEN TACION TOU PETROU KAI HLYEN PRWTOV EIV TO MNHMEION
04J-JOHN-20-05 KAI PARAKUQAV BLEPEI KEIMENA TA OYONIA OU MENTOI EISHLYEN
04J-JOHN-20-06 ERCETAI OUN SIMWN PETROV AKOLOUYWN AUTW KAI EISHLYEN EIV TO MNHMEION KAI YEWREI TA OYONIA KEIMENA
04J-JOHN-20-07 KAI TO SOUDARION O HN EPI THV KEFALHV AUTOU OU META TWN OYONIWN KEIMENON ALLA CWRIV ENTETULIGMENON EIV ENA TOPON
04J-JOHN-20-08 TOTE OUN EISHLYEN KAI O ALLOV MAYHTHV O ELYWN PRWTOV EIV TO MNHMEION KAI EIDEN KAI EPISTEUSEN
04J-JOHN-20-09 OUDEPW GAR HDEISAN THN GRAFHN OTI DEI AUTON EK NEKRWN ANASTHNAI
04J-JOHN-20-10 APHLYON OUN PALIN PROV EAUTOUV OI MAYHTAI
04J-JOHN-20-11 MARIA DE EISTHKEI PROV TO MNHMEION KLAIOUSA EXW WV OUN EKLAIEN PAREKUQEN EIV TO MNHMEION
04J-JOHN-20-12 KAI YEWREI DUO AGGELOUV EN LEUKOIV KAYEZOMENOUV ENA PROV TH KEFALH KAI ENA PROV TOIV POSIN OPOU EKEITO TO SWMA TOU IHSOU
04J-JOHN-20-13 KAI LEGOUSIN AUTH EKEINOI GUNAI TI KLAIEIV LEGEI AUTOIV OTI HRAN TON KURION MOU KAI OUK OIDA POU EYHKAN AUTON
04J-JOHN-20-14 KAI TAUTA EIPOUSA ESTRAFH EIV TA OPISW KAI YEWREI TON IHSOUN ESTWTA KAI OUK HDEI OTI IHSOUV ESTIN
04J-JOHN-20-15 LEGEI AUTH O IHSOUV GUNAI TI KLAIEIV TINA ZHTEIV EKEINH DOKOUSA OTI O KHPOUROV ESTIN LEGEI AUTW KURIE EI SU EBASTASAV AUTON EIPE MOI POU EYHKAV AUTON KAGW AUTON ARW
04J-JOHN-20-16 LEGEI AUTH O IHSOUV MARIA STRAFEISA EKEINH LEGEI AUTW RABBOUNI O LEGETAI DIDASKALE
04J-JOHN-20-17 LEGEI AUTH O IHSOUV MH MOU APTOU OUPW GAR ANABEBHKA PROV TON PATERA MOU POREUOU DE PROV TOUV ADELFOUV MOU KAI EIPE AUTOIV ANABAINW PROV TON PATERA MOU KAI PATERA UMWN KAI YEON MOU KAI YEON UMWN
04J-JOHN-20-18 ERCETAI MARIA H MAGDALHNH APAGGELLOUSA TOIV MAYHTAIV OTI EWRAKEN TON KURION KAI TAUTA EIPEN AUTH
04J-JOHN-20-19 OUSHV OUN OQIAV TH HMERA EKEINH TH MIA TWN SABBATWN KAI TWN YURWN KEKLEISMENWN OPOU HSAN OI MAYHTAI SUNHGMENOI DIA TON FOBON TWN IOUDAIWN HLYEN O IHSOUV KAI ESTH EIV TO MESON KAI LEGEI AUTOIV EIRHNH UMIN
04J-JOHN-20-20 KAI TOUTO EIPWN EDEIXEN AUTOIV TAV CEIRAV KAI THN PLEURAN AUTOU ECARHSAN OUN OI MAYHTAI IDONTEV TON KURION
04J-JOHN-20-21 EIPEN OUN AUTOIV O IHSOUV PALIN EIRHNH UMIN KAYWV APESTALKEN ME O PATHR KAGW PEMPW UMAV
04J-JOHN-20-22 KAI TOUTO EIPWN ENEFUSHSEN KAI LEGEI AUTOIV LABETE PNEUMA AGION
04J-JOHN-20-23 AN TINWN AFHTE TAV AMARTIAV AFIENTAI AUTOIV AN TINWN KRATHTE KEKRATHNTAI
04J-JOHN-20-24 YWMAV DE EIV EK TWN DWDEKA O LEGOMENOV DIDUMOV OUK HN MET AUTWN OTE HLYEN O IHSOUV
04J-JOHN-20-25 ELEGON OUN AUTW OI ALLOI MAYHTAI EWRAKAMEN TON KURION O DE EIPEN AUTOIV EAN MH IDW EN TAIV CERSIN AUTOU TON TUPON TWN HLWN KAI BALW TON DAKTULON MOU EIV TON TUPON TWN HLWN KAI BALW THN CEIRA MOU EIV THN PLEURAN AUTOU OU MH PISTEUSW
04J-JOHN-20-26 KAI MEY HMERAV OKTW PALIN HSAN ESW OI MAYHTAI AUTOU KAI YWMAV MET AUTWN ERCETAI O IHSOUV TWN YURWN KEKLEISMENWN KAI ESTH EIV TO MESON KAI EIPEN EIRHNH UMIN
04J-JOHN-20-27 EITA LEGEI TW YWMA FERE TON DAKTULON SOU WDE KAI IDE TAV CEIRAV MOU KAI FERE THN CEIRA SOU KAI BALE EIV THN PLEURAN MOU KAI MH GINOU APISTOV ALLA PISTOV
04J-JOHN-20-28 KAI APEKRIYH YWMAV KAI EIPEN AUTW O KURIOV MOU KAI O YEOV MOU
04J-JOHN-20-29 LEGEI AUTW O IHSOUV OTI EWRAKAV ME PEPISTEUKAV MAKARIOI OI MH IDONTEV KAI PISTEUSANTEV
04J-JOHN-20-30 POLLA MEN OUN KAI ALLA SHMEIA EPOIHSEN O IHSOUV ENWPION TWN MAYHTWN AUTOU A OUK ESTIN GEGRAMMENA EN TW BIBLIW TOUTW
04J-JOHN-20-31 TAUTA DE GEGRAPTAI INA PISTEUSHTE OTI IHSOUV ESTIN O CRISTOV O UIOV TOU YEOU KAI INA PISTEUONTEV ZWHN ECHTE EN TW ONOMATI AUTOU
04J-JOHN-21-01 META TAUTA EFANERWSEN EAUTON PALIN O IHSOUV TOIV MAYHTAIV EPI THV YALASSHV THV TIBERIADOV EFANERWSEN DE OUTWV
04J-JOHN-21-02 HSAN OMOU SIMWN PETROV KAI YWMAV O LEGOMENOV DIDUMOV KAI NAYANAHL O APO KANA THV GALILAIAV KAI OI TOU ZEBEDAIOU KAI ALLOI EK TWN MAYHTWN AUTOU DUO
04J-JOHN-21-03 LEGEI AUTOIV SIMWN PETROV UPAGW ALIEUEIN LEGOUSIN AUTW ERCOMEYA KAI HMEIV SUN SOI EXHLYON KAI ENEBHSAN EIV TO PLOION EUYUV KAI EN EKEINH TH NUKTI EPIASAN OUDEN
04J-JOHN-21-04 PRWIAV DE HDH GENOMENHV ESTH O IHSOUV EIV TON AIGIALON OU MENTOI HDEISAN OI MAYHTAI OTI IHSOUV ESTIN
04J-JOHN-21-05 LEGEI OUN AUTOIV O IHSOUV PAIDIA MH TI PROSFAGION ECETE APEKRIYHSAN AUTW OU
04J-JOHN-21-06 O DE EIPEN AUTOIV BALETE EIV TA DEXIA MERH TOU PLOIOU TO DIKTUON KAI EURHSETE EBALON OUN KAI OUKETI AUTO ELKUSAI ISCUSAN APO TOU PLHYOUV TWN ICYUWN
04J-JOHN-21-07 LEGEI OUN O MAYHTHV EKEINOV ON HGAPA O IHSOUV TW PETRW O KURIOV ESTIN SIMWN OUN PETROV AKOUSAV OTI O KURIOV ESTIN TON EPENDUTHN DIEZWSATO HN GAR GUMNOV KAI EBALEN EAUTON EIV THN YALASSAN
04J-JOHN-21-08 OI DE ALLOI MAYHTAI TW PLOIARIW HLYON OU GAR HSAN MAKRAN APO THV GHV ALL WV APO PHCWN DIAKOSIWN SURONTEV TO DIKTUON TWN ICYUWN
04J-JOHN-21-09 WV OUN APEBHSAN EIV THN GHN BLEPOUSIN ANYRAKIAN KEIMENHN KAI OQARION EPIKEIMENON KAI ARTON
04J-JOHN-21-10 LEGEI AUTOIV O IHSOUV ENEGKATE APO TWN OQARIWN WN EPIASATE NUN
04J-JOHN-21-11 ANEBH SIMWN PETROV KAI EILKUSEN TO DIKTUON EPI THV GHV MESTON ICYUWN MEGALWN EKATON PENTHKONTA TRIWN KAI TOSOUTWN ONTWN OUK ESCISYH TO DIKTUON
04J-JOHN-21-12 LEGEI AUTOIV O IHSOUV DEUTE ARISTHSATE OUDEIV DE ETOLMA TWN MAYHTWN EXETASAI AUTON SU TIV EI EIDOTEV OTI O KURIOV ESTIN
04J-JOHN-21-13 ERCETAI OUN O IHSOUV KAI LAMBANEI TON ARTON KAI DIDWSIN AUTOIV KAI TO OQARION OMOIWV
04J-JOHN-21-14 TOUTO HDH TRITON EFANERWYH O IHSOUV TOIV MAYHTAIV AUTOU EGERYEIV EK NEKRWN
04J-JOHN-21-15 OTE OUN HRISTHSAN LEGEI TW SIMWNI PETRW O IHSOUV SIMWN IWNA AGAPAV ME PLEION TOUTWN LEGEI AUTW NAI KURIE SU OIDAV OTI FILW SE LEGEI AUTW BOSKE TA ARNIA MOU
04J-JOHN-21-16 LEGEI AUTW PALIN DEUTERON SIMWN IWNA AGAPAV ME LEGEI AUTW NAI KURIE SU OIDAV OTI FILW SE LEGEI AUTW POIMAINE TA PROBATA MOU
04J-JOHN-21-17 LEGEI AUTW TO TRITON SIMWN IWNA FILEIV ME ELUPHYH O PETROV OTI EIPEN AUTW TO TRITON FILEIV ME KAI EIPEN AUTW KURIE SU PANTA OIDAV SU GINWSKEIV OTI FILW SE LEGEI AUTW O IHSOUV BOSKE TA PROBATA MOU
04J-JOHN-21-18 AMHN AMHN LEGW SOI OTE HV NEWTEROV EZWNNUEV SEAUTON KAI PERIEPATEIV OPOU HYELEV OTAN DE GHRASHV EKTENEIV TAV CEIRAV SOU KAI ALLOV SE ZWSEI KAI OISEI OPOU OU YELEIV
04J-JOHN-21-19 TOUTO DE EIPEN SHMAINWN POIW YANATW DOXASEI TON YEON KAI TOUTO EIPWN LEGEI AUTW AKOLOUYEI MOI
04J-JOHN-21-20 EPISTRAFEIV DE O PETROV BLEPEI TON MAYHTHN ON HGAPA O IHSOUV AKOLOUYOUNTA OV KAI ANEPESEN EN TW DEIPNW EPI TO STHYOV AUTOU KAI EIPEN KURIE TIV ESTIN O PARADIDOUV SE
04J-JOHN-21-21 TOUTON IDWN O PETROV LEGEI TW IHSOU KURIE OUTOV DE TI
04J-JOHN-21-22 LEGEI AUTW O IHSOUV EAN AUTON YELW MENEIN EWV ERCOMAI TI PROV SE SU AKOLOUYEI MOI
04J-JOHN-21-23 EXHLYEN OUN O LOGOV OUTOV EIV TOUV ADELFOUV OTI O MAYHTHV EKEINOV OUK APOYNHSKEI KAI OUK EIPEN AUTW O IHSOUV OTI OUK APOYNHSKEI ALL EAN AUTON YELW MENEIN EWV ERCOMAI TI PROV SE
04J-JOHN-21-24 OUTOV ESTIN O MAYHTHV O MARTURWN PERI TOUTWN KAI GRAQAV TAUTA KAI OIDAMEN OTI ALHYHV ESTIN H MARTURIA AUTOU
04J-JOHN-21-25 ESTIN DE KAI ALLA POLLA OSA EPOIHSEN O IHSOUV ATINA EAN GRAFHTAI KAY EN OUDE AUTON OIMAI TON KOSMON CWRHSAI TA GRAFOMENA BIBLIA AMHN
05L-ACTS-01-01 TON MEN PRWTON LOGON EPOIHSAMHN PERI PANTWN W YEOFILE WN HRXATO O IHSOUV POIEIN TE KAI DIDASKEIN
05L-ACTS-01-02 ACRI HV HMERAV ENTEILAMENOV TOIV APOSTOLOIV DIA PNEUMATOV AGIOU OUV EXELEXATO ANELHFYH
05L-ACTS-01-03 OIV KAI PARESTHSEN EAUTON ZWNTA META TO PAYEIN AUTON EN POLLOIV TEKMHRIOIV DI HMERWN TESSARAKONTA OPTANOMENOV AUTOIV KAI LEGWN TA PERI THV BASILEIAV TOU YEOU
05L-ACTS-01-04 KAI SUNALIZOMENOV PARHGGEILEN AUTOIV APO IEROSOLUMWN MH CWRIZESYAI ALLA PERIMENEIN THN EPAGGELIAN TOU PATROV HN HKOUSATE MOU
05L-ACTS-01-05 OTI IWANNHV MEN EBAPTISEN UDATI UMEIV DE BAPTISYHSESYE EN PNEUMATI AGIW OU META POLLAV TAUTAV HMERAV
05L-ACTS-01-06 OI MEN OUN SUNELYONTEV EPHRWTWN AUTON LEGONTEV KURIE EI EN TW CRONW TOUTW APOKAYISTANEIV THN BASILEIAN TW ISRAHL
05L-ACTS-01-07 EIPEN DE PROV AUTOUV OUC UMWN ESTIN GNWNAI CRONOUV H KAIROUV OUV O PATHR EYETO EN TH IDIA EXOUSIA
05L-ACTS-01-08 ALLA LHQESYE DUNAMIN EPELYONTOV TOU AGIOU PNEUMATOV EF UMAV KAI ESESYE MOI MARTUREV EN TE IEROUSALHM KAI EN PASH TH IOUDAIA KAI SAMAREIA KAI EWV ESCATOU THV GHV
05L-ACTS-01-09 KAI TAUTA EIPWN BLEPONTWN AUTWN EPHRYH KAI NEFELH UPELABEN AUTON APO TWN OFYALMWN AUTWN
05L-ACTS-01-10 KAI WV ATENIZONTEV HSAN EIV TON OURANON POREUOMENOU AUTOU KAI IDOU ANDREV DUO PAREISTHKEISAN AUTOIV EN ESYHTI LEUKH
05L-ACTS-01-11 OI KAI EIPON ANDREV GALILAIOI TI ESTHKATE EMBLEPONTEV EIV TON OURANON OUTOV O IHSOUV O ANALHFYEIV AF UMWN EIV TON OURANON OUTWV ELEUSETAI ON TROPON EYEASASYE AUTON POREUOMENON EIV TON OURANON
05L-ACTS-01-12 TOTE UPESTREQAN EIV IEROUSALHM APO OROUV TOU KALOUMENOU ELAIWNOV O ESTIN EGGUV IEROUSALHM SABBATOU ECON ODON
05L-ACTS-01-13 KAI OTE EISHLYON ANEBHSAN EIV TO UPERWON OU HSAN KATAMENONTEV O TE PETROV KAI IAKWBOV KAI IWANNHV KAI ANDREAV FILIPPOV KAI YWMAV BARYOLOMAIOV KAI MATYAIOV IAKWBOV ALFAIOU KAI SIMWN O ZHLWTHV KAI IOUDAV IAKWBOU
05L-ACTS-01-14 OUTOI PANTEV HSAN PROSKARTEROUNTEV OMOYUMADON TH PROSEUCH KAI TH DEHSEI SUN GUNAIXIN KAI MARIA TH MHTRI TOU IHSOU KAI SUN TOIV ADELFOIV AUTOU
05L-ACTS-01-15 KAI EN TAIV HMERAIV TAUTAIV ANASTAV PETROV EN MESW TWN MAYHTWN EIPEN HN TE OCLOV ONOMATWN EPI TO AUTO WV EKATON EIKOSI
05L-ACTS-01-16 ANDREV ADELFOI EDEI PLHRWYHNAI THN GRAFHN TAUTHN HN PROEIPEN TO PNEUMA TO AGION DIA STOMATOV DAUID PERI IOUDA TOU GENOMENOU ODHGOU TOIV SULLABOUSIN TON IHSOUN
05L-ACTS-01-17 OTI KATHRIYMHMENOV HN SUN HMIN KAI ELACEN TON KLHRON THV DIAKONIAV TAUTHV
05L-ACTS-01-18 OUTOV MEN OUN EKTHSATO CWRION EK MISYOU THV ADIKIAV KAI PRHNHV GENOMENOV ELAKHSEN MESOV KAI EXECUYH PANTA TA SPLAGCNA AUTOU
05L-ACTS-01-19 KAI GNWSTON EGENETO PASIN TOIV KATOIKOUSIN IEROUSALHM WSTE KLHYHNAI TO CWRION EKEINO TH IDIA DIALEKTW AUTWN AKELDAMA TOUT ESTIN CWRION AIMATOV
05L-ACTS-01-20 GEGRAPTAI GAR EN BIBLW QALMWN GENHYHTW H EPAULIV AUTOU ERHMOV KAI MH ESTW O KATOIKWN EN AUTH KAI THN EPISKOPHN AUTOU LABOI ETEROV
05L-ACTS-01-21 DEI OUN TWN SUNELYONTWN HMIN ANDRWN EN PANTI CRONW EN W EISHLYEN KAI EXHLYEN EF HMAV O KURIOV IHSOUV
05L-ACTS-01-22 ARXAMENOV APO TOU BAPTISMATOV IWANNOU EWV THV HMERAV HV ANELHFYH AF HMWN MARTURA THV ANASTASEWV AUTOU GENESYAI SUN HMIN ENA TOUTWN
05L-ACTS-01-23 KAI ESTHSAN DUO IWSHF TON KALOUMENON BARSABAN OV EPEKLHYH IOUSTOV KAI MATYIAN
05L-ACTS-01-24 KAI PROSEUXAMENOI EIPON SU KURIE KARDIOGNWSTA PANTWN ANADEIXON ON EXELEXW EK TOUTWN TWN DUO ENA
05L-ACTS-01-25 LABEIN TON KLHRON THV DIAKONIAV TAUTHV KAI APOSTOLHV EX HV PAREBH IOUDAV POREUYHNAI EIV TON TOPON TON IDION
05L-ACTS-01-26 KAI EDWKAN KLHROUV AUTWN KAI EPESEN O KLHROV EPI MATYIAN KAI SUGKATEQHFISYH META TWN ENDEKA APOSTOLWN
05L-ACTS-02-01 KAI EN TW SUMPLHROUSYAI THN HMERAN THV PENTHKOSTHV HSAN APANTEV OMOYUMADON EPI TO AUTO
05L-ACTS-02-02 KAI EGENETO AFNW EK TOU OURANOU HCOV WSPER FEROMENHV PNOHV BIAIAV KAI EPLHRWSEN OLON TON OIKON OU HSAN KAYHMENOI
05L-ACTS-02-03 KAI WFYHSAN AUTOIV DIAMERIZOMENAI GLWSSAI WSEI PUROV EKAYISEN TE EF ENA EKASTON AUTWN
05L-ACTS-02-04 KAI EPLHSYHSAN APANTEV PNEUMATOV AGIOU KAI HRXANTO LALEIN ETERAIV GLWSSAIV KAYWV TO PNEUMA EDIDOU AUTOIV APOFYEGGESYAI
05L-ACTS-02-05 HSAN DE EN IEROUSALHM KATOIKOUNTEV IOUDAIOI ANDREV EULABEIV APO PANTOV EYNOUV TWN UPO TON OURANON
05L-ACTS-02-06 GENOMENHV DE THV FWNHV TAUTHV SUNHLYEN TO PLHYOV KAI SUNECUYH OTI HKOUON EIV EKASTOV TH IDIA DIALEKTW LALOUNTWN AUTWN
05L-ACTS-02-07 EXISTANTO DE PANTEV KAI EYAUMAZON LEGONTEV PROV ALLHLOUV OUK IDOU PANTEV OUTOI EISIN OI LALOUNTEV GALILAIOI
05L-ACTS-02-08 KAI PWV HMEIV AKOUOMEN EKASTOV TH IDIA DIALEKTW HMWN EN H EGENNHYHMEN
05L-ACTS-02-09 PARYOI KAI MHDOI KAI ELAMITAI KAI OI KATOIKOUNTEV THN MESOPOTAMIAN IOUDAIAN TE KAI KAPPADOKIAN PONTON KAI THN ASIAN
05L-ACTS-02-10 FRUGIAN TE KAI PAMFULIAN AIGUPTON KAI TA MERH THV LIBUHV THV KATA KURHNHN KAI OI EPIDHMOUNTEV RWMAIOI IOUDAIOI TE KAI PROSHLUTOI
05L-ACTS-02-11 KRHTEV KAI ARABEV AKOUOMEN LALOUNTWN AUTWN TAIV HMETERAIV GLWSSAIV TA MEGALEIA TOU YEOU
05L-ACTS-02-12 EXISTANTO DE PANTEV KAI DIHPOROUN ALLOV PROV ALLON LEGONTEV TI AN YELOI TOUTO EINAI
05L-ACTS-02-13 ETEROI DE CLEUAZONTEV ELEGON OTI GLEUKOUV MEMESTWMENOI EISIN
05L-ACTS-02-14 STAYEIV DE PETROV SUN TOIV ENDEKA EPHREN THN FWNHN AUTOU KAI APEFYEGXATO AUTOIV ANDREV IOUDAIOI KAI OI KATOIKOUNTEV IEROUSALHM APANTEV TOUTO UMIN GNWSTON ESTW KAI ENWTISASYE TA RHMATA MOU
05L-ACTS-02-15 OU GAR WV UMEIV UPOLAMBANETE OUTOI MEYUOUSIN ESTIN GAR WRA TRITH THV HMERAV
05L-ACTS-02-16 ALLA TOUTO ESTIN TO EIRHMENON DIA TOU PROFHTOU IWHL
05L-ACTS-02-17 KAI ESTAI EN TAIV ESCATAIV HMERAIV LEGEI O YEOV EKCEW APO TOU PNEUMATOV MOU EPI PASAN SARKA KAI PROFHTEUSOUSIN OI UIOI UMWN KAI AI YUGATEREV UMWN KAI OI NEANISKOI UMWN ORASEIV OQONTAI KAI OI PRESBUTEROI UMWN ENUPNIA ENUPNIASYHSONTAI
05L-ACTS-02-18 KAI GE EPI TOUV DOULOUV MOU KAI EPI TAV DOULAV MOU EN TAIV HMERAIV EKEINAIV EKCEW APO TOU PNEUMATOV MOU KAI PROFHTEUSOUSIN
05L-ACTS-02-19 KAI DWSW TERATA EN TW OURANW ANW KAI SHMEIA EPI THV GHV KATW AIMA KAI PUR KAI ATMIDA KAPNOU
05L-ACTS-02-20 O HLIOV METASTRAFHSETAI EIV SKOTOV KAI H SELHNH EIV AIMA PRIN H ELYEIN THN HMERAN KURIOU THN MEGALHN KAI EPIFANH
05L-ACTS-02-21 KAI ESTAI PAV OV AN EPIKALESHTAI TO ONOMA KURIOU SWYHSETAI
05L-ACTS-02-22 ANDREV ISRAHLITAI AKOUSATE TOUV LOGOUV TOUTOUV IHSOUN TON NAZWRAION ANDRA APO TOU YEOU APODEDEIGMENON EIV UMAV DUNAMESIN KAI TERASIN KAI SHMEIOIV OIV EPOIHSEN DI AUTOU O YEOV EN MESW UMWN KAYWV KAI AUTOI OIDATE
05L-ACTS-02-23 TOUTON TH WRISMENH BOULH KAI PROGNWSEI TOU YEOU EKDOTON LABONTEV DIA CEIRWN ANOMWN PROSPHXANTEV ANEILETE
05L-ACTS-02-24 ON O YEOV ANESTHSEN LUSAV TAV WDINAV TOU YANATOU KAYOTI OUK HN DUNATON KRATEISYAI AUTON UP AUTOU
05L-ACTS-02-25 DAUID GAR LEGEI EIV AUTON PROWRWMHN TON KURION ENWPION MOU DIA PANTOV OTI EK DEXIWN MOU ESTIN INA MH SALEUYW
05L-ACTS-02-26 DIA TOUTO EUFRANYH H KARDIA MOU KAI HGALLIASATO H GLWSSA MOU ETI DE KAI H SARX MOU KATASKHNWSEI EP ELPIDI
05L-ACTS-02-27 OTI OUK EGKATALEIQEIV THN QUCHN MOU EIV ADOU OUDE DWSEIV TON OSION SOU IDEIN DIAFYORAN
05L-ACTS-02-28 EGNWRISAV MOI ODOUV ZWHV PLHRWSEIV ME EUFROSUNHV META TOU PROSWPOU SOU
05L-ACTS-02-29 ANDREV ADELFOI EXON EIPEIN META PARRHSIAV PROV UMAV PERI TOU PATRIARCOU DAUID OTI KAI ETELEUTHSEN KAI ETAFH KAI TO MNHMA AUTOU ESTIN EN HMIN ACRI THV HMERAV TAUTHV
05L-ACTS-02-30 PROFHTHV OUN UPARCWN KAI EIDWV OTI ORKW WMOSEN AUTW O YEOV EK KARPOU THV OSFUOV AUTOU TO KATA SARKA ANASTHSEIN TON CRISTON KAYISAI EPI TOU YRONOU AUTOU
05L-ACTS-02-31 PROIDWN ELALHSEN PERI THV ANASTASEWV TOU CRISTOU OTI OU KATELEIFYH H QUCH AUTOU EIV ADOU OUDE H SARX AUTOU EIDEN DIAFYORAN
05L-ACTS-02-32 TOUTON TON IHSOUN ANESTHSEN O YEOV OU PANTEV HMEIV ESMEN MARTUREV
05L-ACTS-02-33 TH DEXIA OUN TOU YEOU UQWYEIV THN TE EPAGGELIAN TOU AGIOU PNEUMATOV LABWN PARA TOU PATROV EXECEEN TOUTO O NUN UMEIV BLEPETE KAI AKOUETE
05L-ACTS-02-34 OU GAR DAUID ANEBH EIV TOUV OURANOUV LEGEI DE AUTOV EIPEN O KURIOV TW KURIW MOU KAYOU EK DEXIWN MOU
05L-ACTS-02-35 EWV AN YW TOUV ECYROUV SOU UPOPODION TWN PODWN SOU
05L-ACTS-02-36 ASFALWV OUN GINWSKETW PAV OIKOV ISRAHL OTI KAI KURION KAI CRISTON AUTON O YEOV EPOIHSEN TOUTON TON IHSOUN ON UMEIV ESTAURWSATE
05L-ACTS-02-37 AKOUSANTEV DE KATENUGHSAN TH KARDIA EIPON TE PROV TON PETRON KAI TOUV LOIPOUV APOSTOLOUV TI POIHSOMEN ANDREV ADELFOI
05L-ACTS-02-38 PETROV DE EFH PROV AUTOUV METANOHSATE KAI BAPTISYHTW EKASTOV UMWN EPI TW ONOMATI IHSOU CRISTOU EIV AFESIN AMARTIWN KAI LHQESYE THN DWREAN TOU AGIOU PNEUMATOV
05L-ACTS-02-39 UMIN GAR ESTIN H EPAGGELIA KAI TOIV TEKNOIV UMWN KAI PASIN TOIV EIV MAKRAN OSOUV AN PROSKALESHTAI KURIOV O YEOV HMWN
05L-ACTS-02-40 ETEROIV TE LOGOIV PLEIOSIN DIEMARTURETO KAI PAREKALEI LEGWN SWYHTE APO THV GENEAV THV SKOLIAV TAUTHV
05L-ACTS-02-41 OI MEN OUN ASMENWV APODEXAMENOI TON LOGON AUTOU EBAPTISYHSAN KAI PROSETEYHSAN TH HMERA EKEINH QUCAI WSEI TRISCILIAI
05L-ACTS-02-42 HSAN DE PROSKARTEROUNTEV TH DIDACH TWN APOSTOLWN KAI TH KOINWNIA KAI TH KLASEI TOU ARTOU KAI TAIV PROSEUCAIV
05L-ACTS-02-43 EGENETO DE PASH QUCH FOBOV POLLA TE TERATA KAI SHMEIA DIA TWN APOSTOLWN EGINETO
05L-ACTS-02-44 PANTEV DE OI PISTEUONTEV HSAN EPI TO AUTO KAI EICON APANTA KOINA
05L-ACTS-02-45 KAI TA KTHMATA KAI TAV UPARXEIV EPIPRASKON KAI DIEMERIZON AUTA PASIN KAYOTI AN TIV CREIAN EICEN
05L-ACTS-02-46 KAY HMERAN TE PROSKARTEROUNTEV OMOYUMADON EN TW IERW KLWNTEV TE KAT OIKON ARTON METELAMBANON TROFHV EN AGALLIASEI KAI AFELOTHTI KARDIAV
05L-ACTS-02-47 AINOUNTEV TON YEON KAI ECONTEV CARIN PROV OLON TON LAON O DE KURIOV PROSETIYEI TOUV SWZOMENOUV KAY HMERAN TH EKKLHSIA
05L-ACTS-03-01 EPI TO AUTO DE PETROV KAI IWANNHV ANEBAINON EIV TO IERON EPI THN WRAN THV PROSEUCHV THN ENATHN
05L-ACTS-03-02 KAI TIV ANHR CWLOV EK KOILIAV MHTROV AUTOU UPARCWN EBASTAZETO ON ETIYOUN KAY HMERAN PROV THN YURAN TOU IEROU THN LEGOMENHN WRAIAN TOU AITEIN ELEHMOSUNHN PARA TWN EISPOREUOMENWN EIV TO IERON
05L-ACTS-03-03 OV IDWN PETRON KAI IWANNHN MELLONTAV EISIENAI EIV TO IERON HRWTA ELEHMOSUNHN
05L-ACTS-03-04 ATENISAV DE PETROV EIV AUTON SUN TW IWANNH EIPEN BLEQON EIV HMAV
05L-ACTS-03-05 O DE EPEICEN AUTOIV PROSDOKWN TI PAR AUTWN LABEIN
05L-ACTS-03-06 EIPEN DE PETROV ARGURION KAI CRUSION OUC UPARCEI MOI O DE ECW TOUTO SOI DIDWMI EN TW ONOMATI IHSOU CRISTOU TOU NAZWRAIOU EGEIRAI KAI PERIPATEI
05L-ACTS-03-07 KAI PIASAV AUTON THV DEXIAV CEIROV HGEIREN PARACRHMA DE ESTEREWYHSAN AUTOU AI BASEIV KAI TA SFURA
05L-ACTS-03-08 KAI EXALLOMENOV ESTH KAI PERIEPATEI KAI EISHLYEN SUN AUTOIV EIV TO IERON PERIPATWN KAI ALLOMENOV KAI AINWN TON YEON
05L-ACTS-03-09 KAI EIDEN AUTON PAV O LAOV PERIPATOUNTA KAI AINOUNTA TON YEON
05L-ACTS-03-10 EPEGINWSKON TE AUTON OTI OUTOV HN O PROV THN ELEHMOSUNHN KAYHMENOV EPI TH WRAIA PULH TOU IEROU KAI EPLHSYHSAN YAMBOUV KAI EKSTASEWV EPI TW SUMBEBHKOTI AUTW
05L-ACTS-03-11 KRATOUNTOV DE TOU IAYENTOV CWLOU TON PETRON KAI IWANNHN SUNEDRAMEN PROV AUTOUV PAV O LAOV EPI TH STOA TH KALOUMENH SOLOMWNTOV EKYAMBOI
05L-ACTS-03-12 IDWN DE PETROV APEKRINATO PROV TON LAON ANDREV ISRAHLITAI TI YAUMAZETE EPI TOUTW H HMIN TI ATENIZETE WV IDIA DUNAMEI H EUSEBEIA PEPOIHKOSIN TOU PERIPATEIN AUTON
05L-ACTS-03-13 O YEOV ABRAAM KAI ISAAK KAI IAKWB O YEOV TWN PATERWN HMWN EDOXASEN TON PAIDA AUTOU IHSOUN ON UMEIV MEN PAREDWKATE KAI HRNHSASYE AUTON KATA PROSWPON PILATOU KRINANTOV EKEINOU APOLUEIN
05L-ACTS-03-14 UMEIV DE TON AGION KAI DIKAION HRNHSASYE KAI HTHSASYE ANDRA FONEA CARISYHNAI UMIN
05L-ACTS-03-15 TON DE ARCHGON THV ZWHV APEKTEINATE ON O YEOV HGEIREN EK NEKRWN OU HMEIV MARTUREV ESMEN
05L-ACTS-03-16 KAI EPI TH PISTEI TOU ONOMATOV AUTOU TOUTON ON YEWREITE KAI OIDATE ESTEREWSEN TO ONOMA AUTOU KAI H PISTIV H DI AUTOU EDWKEN AUTW THN OLOKLHRIAN TAUTHN APENANTI PANTWN UMWN
05L-ACTS-03-17 KAI NUN ADELFOI OIDA OTI KATA AGNOIAN EPRAXATE WSPER KAI OI ARCONTEV UMWN
05L-ACTS-03-18 O DE YEOV A PROKATHGGEILEN DIA STOMATOV PANTWN TWN PROFHTWN AUTOU PAYEIN TON CRISTON EPLHRWSEN OUTWV
05L-ACTS-03-19 METANOHSATE OUN KAI EPISTREQATE EIV TO EXALEIFYHNAI UMWN TAV AMARTIAV OPWV AN ELYWSIN KAIROI ANAQUXEWV APO PROSWPOU TOU KURIOU
05L-ACTS-03-20 KAI APOSTEILH TON PROKECEIRISMENON UMIN CRISTON IHSOUN
05L-ACTS-03-21 ON DEI OURANON MEN DEXASYAI ACRI CRONWN APOKATASTASEWV PANTWN WN ELALHSEN O YEOV DIA STOMATOV PANTWN TWN AGIWN AUTOU PROFHTWN AP AIWNOV
05L-ACTS-03-22 MWSHV MEN GAR PROV TOUV PATERAV EIPEN OTI PROFHTHN UMIN ANASTHSEI KURIOV O YEOV HMWN EK TWN ADELFWN UMWN WV EME AUTOU AKOUSESYE KATA PANTA OSA AN LALHSH PROV UMAV
05L-ACTS-03-23 ESTAI DE PASA QUCH HTIV EAN MH AKOUSH TOU PROFHTOU EKEINOU EXOLOYREUYHSETAI EK TOU LAOU
05L-ACTS-03-24 KAI PANTEV DE OI PROFHTAI APO SAMOUHL KAI TWN KAYEXHV OSOI ELALHSAN KAI KATHGGEILAN TAV HMERAV TAUTAV
05L-ACTS-03-25 UMEIV ESTE UIOI TWN PROFHTWN KAI THV DIAYHKHV HV DIEYETO O YEOV PROV TOUV PATERAV HMWN LEGWN PROV ABRAAM KAI EN TW SPERMATI SOU ENEULOGHYHSONTAI PASAI AI PATRIAI THV GHV
05L-ACTS-03-26 UMIN PRWTON O YEOV ANASTHSAV TON PAIDA AUTOU IHSOUN APESTEILEN AUTON EULOGOUNTA UMAV EN TW APOSTREFEIN EKASTON APO TWN PONHRIWN UMWN
05L-ACTS-04-01 LALOUNTWN DE AUTWN PROV TON LAON EPESTHSAN AUTOIV OI IEREIV KAI O STRATHGOV TOU IEROU KAI OI SADDOUKAIOI
05L-ACTS-04-02 DIAPONOUMENOI DIA TO DIDASKEIN AUTOUV TON LAON KAI KATAGGELLEIN EN TW IHSOU THN ANASTASIN TWN NEKRWN
05L-ACTS-04-03 KAI EPEBALON AUTOIV TAV CEIRAV KAI EYENTO EIV THRHSIN EIV THN AURION HN GAR ESPERA HDH
05L-ACTS-04-04 POLLOI DE TWN AKOUSANTWN TON LOGON EPISTEUSAN KAI EGENHYH O ARIYMOV TWN ANDRWN WSEI CILIADEV PENTE
05L-ACTS-04-05 EGENETO DE EPI THN AURION SUNACYHNAI AUTWN TOUV ARCONTAV KAI PRESBUTEROUV KAI GRAMMATEIV EIV IEROUSALHM
05L-ACTS-04-06 KAI ANNAN TON ARCIEREA KAI KAIAFAN KAI IWANNHN KAI ALEXANDRON KAI OSOI HSAN EK GENOUV ARCIERATIKOU
05L-ACTS-04-07 KAI STHSANTEV AUTOUV EN MESW EPUNYANONTO EN POIA DUNAMEI H EN POIW ONOMATI EPOIHSATE TOUTO UMEIV
05L-ACTS-04-08 TOTE PETROV PLHSYEIV PNEUMATOV AGIOU EIPEN PROV AUTOUV ARCONTEV TOU LAOU KAI PRESBUTEROI TOU ISRAHL
05L-ACTS-04-09 EI HMEIV SHMERON ANAKRINOMEYA EPI EUERGESIA ANYRWPOU ASYENOUV EN TINI OUTOV SESWSTAI
05L-ACTS-04-10 GNWSTON ESTW PASIN UMIN KAI PANTI TW LAW ISRAHL OTI EN TW ONOMATI IHSOU CRISTOU TOU NAZWRAIOU ON UMEIV ESTAURWSATE ON O YEOV HGEIREN EK NEKRWN EN TOUTW OUTOV PARESTHKEN ENWPION UMWN UGIHV
05L-ACTS-04-11 OUTOV ESTIN O LIYOV O EXOUYENHYEIV UF UMWN TWN OIKODOMOUNTWN O GENOMENOV EIV KEFALHN GWNIAV
05L-ACTS-04-12 KAI OUK ESTIN EN ALLW OUDENI H SWTHRIA OUTE GAR ONOMA ESTIN ETERON TO DEDOMENON EN ANYRWPOIV EN W DEI SWYHNAI HMAV
05L-ACTS-04-13 YEWROUNTEV DE THN TOU PETROU PARRHSIAN KAI IWANNOU KAI KATALABOMENOI OTI ANYRWPOI AGRAMMATOI EISIN KAI IDIWTAI EYAUMAZON EPEGINWSKON TE AUTOUV OTI SUN TW IHSOU HSAN
05L-ACTS-04-14 TON DE ANYRWPON BLEPONTEV SUN AUTOIV ESTWTA TON TEYERAPEUMENON OUDEN EICON ANTEIPEIN
05L-ACTS-04-15 KELEUSANTEV DE AUTOUV EXW TOU SUNEDRIOU APELYEIN SUNEBALLON PROV ALLHLOUV
05L-ACTS-04-16 LEGONTEV TI POIHSOMEN TOIV ANYRWPOIV TOUTOIV OTI MEN GAR GNWSTON SHMEION GEGONEN DI AUTWN PASIN TOIV KATOIKOUSIN IEROUSALHM FANERON KAI OU DUNAMEYA ARNHSASYAI
05L-ACTS-04-17 ALL INA MH EPI PLEION DIANEMHYH EIV TON LAON APEILH APEILHSOMEYA AUTOIV MHKETI LALEIN EPI TW ONOMATI TOUTW MHDENI ANYRWPWN
05L-ACTS-04-18 KAI KALESANTEV AUTOUV PARHGGEILAN AUTOIV TO KAYOLOU MH FYEGGESYAI MHDE DIDASKEIN EPI TW ONOMATI TOU IHSOU
05L-ACTS-04-19 O DE PETROV KAI IWANNHV APOKRIYENTEV PROV AUTOUV EIPON EI DIKAION ESTIN ENWPION TOU YEOU UMWN AKOUEIN MALLON H TOU YEOU KRINATE
05L-ACTS-04-20 OU DUNAMEYA GAR HMEIV A EIDOMEN KAI HKOUSAMEN MH LALEIN
05L-ACTS-04-21 OI DE PROSAPEILHSAMENOI APELUSAN AUTOUV MHDEN EURISKONTEV TO PWV KOLASONTAI AUTOUV DIA TON LAON OTI PANTEV EDOXAZON TON YEON EPI TW GEGONOTI
05L-ACTS-04-22 ETWN GAR HN PLEIONWN TESSARAKONTA O ANYRWPOV EF ON EGEGONEI TO SHMEION TOUTO THV IASEWV
05L-ACTS-04-23 APOLUYENTEV DE HLYON PROV TOUV IDIOUV KAI APHGGEILAN OSA PROV AUTOUV OI ARCIEREIV KAI OI PRESBUTEROI EIPON
05L-ACTS-04-24 OI DE AKOUSANTEV OMOYUMADON HRAN FWNHN PROV TON YEON KAI EIPON DESPOTA SU O YEOV O POIHSAV TON OURANON KAI THN GHN KAI THN YALASSAN KAI PANTA TA EN AUTOIV
05L-ACTS-04-25 O DIA STOMATOV DAUID PAIDOV SOU EIPWN INA TI EFRUAXAN EYNH KAI LAOI EMELETHSAN KENA
05L-ACTS-04-26 PARESTHSAN OI BASILEIV THV GHV KAI OI ARCONTEV SUNHCYHSAN EPI TO AUTO KATA TOU KURIOU KAI KATA TOU CRISTOU AUTOU
05L-ACTS-04-27 SUNHCYHSAN GAR EP ALHYEIAV EPI TON AGION PAIDA SOU IHSOUN ON ECRISAV HRWDHV TE KAI PONTIOV PILATOV SUN EYNESIN KAI LAOIV ISRAHL
05L-ACTS-04-28 POIHSAI OSA H CEIR SOU KAI H BOULH SOU PROWRISEN GENESYAI
05L-ACTS-04-29 KAI TA NUN KURIE EPIDE EPI TAV APEILAV AUTWN KAI DOV TOIV DOULOIV SOU META PARRHSIAV PASHV LALEIN TON LOGON SOU
05L-ACTS-04-30 EN TW THN CEIRA SOU EKTEINEIN SE EIV IASIN KAI SHMEIA KAI TERATA GINESYAI DIA TOU ONOMATOV TOU AGIOU PAIDOV SOU IHSOU
05L-ACTS-04-31 KAI DEHYENTWN AUTWN ESALEUYH O TOPOV EN W HSAN SUNHGMENOI KAI EPLHSYHSAN APANTEV PNEUMATOV AGIOU KAI ELALOUN TON LOGON TOU YEOU META PARRHSIAV
05L-ACTS-04-32 TOU DE PLHYOUV TWN PISTEUSANTWN HN H KARDIA KAI H QUCH MIA KAI OUDE EIV TI TWN UPARCONTWN AUTWN ELEGEN IDION EINAI ALL HN AUTOIV APANTA KOINA
05L-ACTS-04-33 KAI MEGALH DUNAMEI APEDIDOUN TO MARTURION OI APOSTOLOI THV ANASTASEWV TOU KURIOU IHSOU CARIV TE MEGALH HN EPI PANTAV AUTOUV
05L-ACTS-04-34 OUDE GAR ENDEHV TIV UPHRCEN EN AUTOIV OSOI GAR KTHTOREV CWRIWN H OIKIWN UPHRCON PWLOUNTEV EFERON TAV TIMAV TWN PIPRASKOMENWN
05L-ACTS-04-35 KAI ETIYOUN PARA TOUV PODAV TWN APOSTOLWN DIEDIDOTO DE EKASTW KAYOTI AN TIV CREIAN EICEN
05L-ACTS-04-36 IWSHV DE O EPIKLHYEIV BARNABAV APO TWN APOSTOLWN O ESTIN MEYERMHNEUOMENON UIOV PARAKLHSEWV LEUITHV KUPRIOV TW GENEI
05L-ACTS-04-37 UPARCONTOV AUTW AGROU PWLHSAV HNEGKEN TO CRHMA KAI EYHKEN PARA TOUV PODAV TWN APOSTOLWN
05L-ACTS-05-01 ANHR DE TIV ANANIAV ONOMATI SUN SAPFEIRH TH GUNAIKI AUTOU EPWLHSEN KTHMA
05L-ACTS-05-02 KAI ENOSFISATO APO THV TIMHV SUNEIDUIAV KAI THV GUNAIKOV AUTOU KAI ENEGKAV MEROV TI PARA TOUV PODAV TWN APOSTOLWN EYHKEN
05L-ACTS-05-03 EIPEN DE PETROV ANANIA DIA TI EPLHRWSEN O SATANAV THN KARDIAN SOU QEUSASYAI SE TO PNEUMA TO AGION KAI NOSFISASYAI SE APO THV TIMHV TOU CWRIOU
05L-ACTS-05-04 OUCI MENON SOI EMENEN KAI PRAYEN EN TH SH EXOUSIA UPHRCEN TI OTI EYOU EN TH KARDIA SOU TO PRAGMA TOUTO OUK EQEUSW ANYRWPOIV ALLA TW YEW
05L-ACTS-05-05 AKOUWN DE O ANANIAV TOUV LOGOUV TOUTOUV PESWN EXEQUXEN KAI EGENETO FOBOV MEGAV EPI PANTAV TOUV AKOUONTAV TAUTA
05L-ACTS-05-06 ANASTANTEV DE OI NEWTEROI SUNESTEILAN AUTON KAI EXENEGKANTEV EYAQAN
05L-ACTS-05-07 EGENETO DE WV WRWN TRIWN DIASTHMA KAI H GUNH AUTOU MH EIDUIA TO GEGONOV EISHLYEN
05L-ACTS-05-08 APEKRIYH DE AUTH O PETROV EIPE MOI EI TOSOUTOU TO CWRION APEDOSYE H DE EIPEN NAI TOSOUTOU
05L-ACTS-05-09 O DE PETROV EIPEN PROV AUTHN TI OTI SUNEFWNHYH UMIN PEIRASAI TO PNEUMA KURIOU IDOU OI PODEV TWN YAQANTWN TON ANDRA SOU EPI TH YURA KAI EXOISOUSIN SE
05L-ACTS-05-10 EPESEN DE PARACRHMA PARA TOUV PODAV AUTOU KAI EXEQUXEN EISELYONTEV DE OI NEANISKOI EURON AUTHN NEKRAN KAI EXENEGKANTEV EYAQAN PROV TON ANDRA AUTHV
05L-ACTS-05-11 KAI EGENETO FOBOV MEGAV EF OLHN THN EKKLHSIAN KAI EPI PANTAV TOUV AKOUONTAV TAUTA
05L-ACTS-05-12 DIA DE TWN CEIRWN TWN APOSTOLWN EGINETO SHMEIA KAI TERATA EN TW LAW POLLA KAI HSAN OMOYUMADON APANTEV EN TH STOA SOLOMWNTOV
05L-ACTS-05-13 TWN DE LOIPWN OUDEIV ETOLMA KOLLASYAI AUTOIV ALL EMEGALUNEN AUTOUV O LAOV
05L-ACTS-05-14 MALLON DE PROSETIYENTO PISTEUONTEV TW KURIW PLHYH ANDRWN TE KAI GUNAIKWN
05L-ACTS-05-15 WSTE KATA TAV PLATEIAV EKFEREIN TOUV ASYENEIV KAI TIYENAI EPI KLINWN KAI KRABBATWN INA ERCOMENOU PETROU KAN H SKIA EPISKIASH TINI AUTWN
05L-ACTS-05-16 SUNHRCETO DE KAI TO PLHYOV TWN PERIX POLEWN EIV IEROUSALHM FERONTEV ASYENEIV KAI OCLOUMENOUV UPO PNEUMATWN AKAYARTWN OITINEV EYERAPEUONTO APANTEV
05L-ACTS-05-17 ANASTAV DE O ARCIEREUV KAI PANTEV OI SUN AUTW H OUSA AIRESIV TWN SADDOUKAIWN EPLHSYHSAN ZHLOU
05L-ACTS-05-18 KAI EPEBALON TAV CEIRAV AUTWN EPI TOUV APOSTOLOUV KAI EYENTO AUTOUV EN THRHSEI DHMOSIA
05L-ACTS-05-19 AGGELOV DE KURIOU DIA THV NUKTOV HNOIXEN TAV YURAV THV FULAKHV EXAGAGWN TE AUTOUV EIPEN
05L-ACTS-05-20 POREUESYE KAI STAYENTEV LALEITE EN TW IERW TW LAW PANTA TA RHMATA THV ZWHV TAUTHV
05L-ACTS-05-21 AKOUSANTEV DE EISHLYON UPO TON ORYRON EIV TO IERON KAI EDIDASKON PARAGENOMENOV DE O ARCIEREUV KAI OI SUN AUTW SUNEKALESAN TO SUNEDRION KAI PASAN THN GEROUSIAN TWN UIWN ISRAHL KAI APESTEILAN EIV TO DESMWTHRION ACYHNAI AUTOUV
05L-ACTS-05-22 OI DE UPHRETAI PARAGENOMENOI OUC EURON AUTOUV EN TH FULAKH ANASTREQANTEV DE APHGGEILAN
05L-ACTS-05-23 LEGONTEV OTI TO MEN DESMWTHRION EUROMEN KEKLEISMENON EN PASH ASFALEIA KAI TOUV FULAKAV ESTWTAV PRO TWN YURWN ANOIXANTEV DE ESW OUDENA EUROMEN
05L-ACTS-05-24 WV DE HKOUSAN TOUV LOGOUV TOUTOUV O TE IEREUV KAI O STRATHGOV TOU IEROU KAI OI ARCIEREIV DIHPOROUN PERI AUTWN TI AN GENOITO TOUTO
05L-ACTS-05-25 PARAGENOMENOV DE TIV APHGGEILEN AUTOIV OTI IDOU OI ANDREV OUV EYESYE EN TH FULAKH EISIN EN TW IERW ESTWTEV KAI DIDASKONTEV TON LAON
05L-ACTS-05-26 TOTE APELYWN O STRATHGOV SUN TOIV UPHRETAIV HGAGEN AUTOUV OU META BIAV EFOBOUNTO GAR TON LAON INA MH LIYASYWSIN
05L-ACTS-05-27 AGAGONTEV DE AUTOUV ESTHSAN EN TW SUNEDRIW KAI EPHRWTHSEN AUTOUV O ARCIEREUV
05L-ACTS-05-28 LEGWN OU PARAGGELIA PARHGGEILAMEN UMIN MH DIDASKEIN EPI TW ONOMATI TOUTW KAI IDOU PEPLHRWKATE THN IEROUSALHM THV DIDACHV UMWN KAI BOULESYE EPAGAGEIN EF HMAV TO AIMA TOU ANYRWPOU TOUTOU
05L-ACTS-05-29 APOKRIYEIV DE PETROV KAI OI APOSTOLOI EIPON PEIYARCEIN DEI YEW MALLON H ANYRWPOIV
05L-ACTS-05-30 O YEOV TWN PATERWN HMWN HGEIREN IHSOUN ON UMEIV DIECEIRISASYE KREMASANTEV EPI XULOU
05L-ACTS-05-31 TOUTON O YEOV ARCHGON KAI SWTHRA UQWSEN TH DEXIA AUTOU DOUNAI METANOIAN TW ISRAHL KAI AFESIN AMARTIWN
05L-ACTS-05-32 KAI HMEIV ESMEN AUTOU MARTUREV TWN RHMATWN TOUTWN KAI TO PNEUMA DE TO AGION O EDWKEN O YEOV TOIV PEIYARCOUSIN AUTW
05L-ACTS-05-33 OI DE AKOUONTEV DIEPRIONTO KAI EBOULEUONTO ANELEIN AUTOUV
05L-ACTS-05-34 ANASTAV DE TIV EN TW SUNEDRIW FARISAIOV ONOMATI GAMALIHL NOMODIDASKALOV TIMIOV PANTI TW LAW EKELEUSEN EXW BRACU TI TOUV APOSTOLOUV POIHSAI
05L-ACTS-05-35 EIPEN TE PROV AUTOUV ANDREV ISRAHLITAI PROSECETE EAUTOIV EPI TOIV ANYRWPOIV TOUTOIV TI MELLETE PRASSEIN
05L-ACTS-05-36 PRO GAR TOUTWN TWN HMERWN ANESTH YEUDAV LEGWN EINAI TINA EAUTON W PROSEKLHYH ARIYMOV ANDRWN WSEI TETRAKOSIWN OV ANHREYH KAI PANTEV OSOI EPEIYONTO AUTW DIELUYHSAN KAI EGENONTO EIV OUDEN
05L-ACTS-05-37 META TOUTON ANESTH IOUDAV O GALILAIOV EN TAIV HMERAIV THV APOGRAFHV KAI APESTHSEN LAON IKANON OPISW AUTOU KAKEINOV APWLETO KAI PANTEV OSOI EPEIYONTO AUTW DIESKORPISYHSAN
05L-ACTS-05-38 KAI TA NUN LEGW UMIN APOSTHTE APO TWN ANYRWPWN TOUTWN KAI EASATE AUTOUV OTI EAN H EX ANYRWPWN H BOULH H TO ERGON TOUTO KATALUYHSETAI
05L-ACTS-05-39 EI DE EK YEOU ESTIN OU DUNASYE KATALUSAI AUTO MHPOTE KAI YEOMACOI EUREYHTE
05L-ACTS-05-40 EPEISYHSAN DE AUTW KAI PROSKALESAMENOI TOUV APOSTOLOUV DEIRANTEV PARHGGEILAN MH LALEIN EPI TW ONOMATI TOU IHSOU KAI APELUSAN AUTOUV
05L-ACTS-05-41 OI MEN OUN EPOREUONTO CAIRONTEV APO PROSWPOU TOU SUNEDRIOU OTI UPER TOU ONOMATOV TOU IHSOU KATHXIWYHSAN ATIMASYHNAI
05L-ACTS-05-42 PASAN TE HMERAN EN TW IERW KAI KAT OIKON OUK EPAUONTO DIDASKONTEV KAI EUAGGELIZOMENOI IHSOUN TON CRISTON
05L-ACTS-06-01 EN DE TAIV HMERAIV TAUTAIV PLHYUNONTWN TWN MAYHTWN EGENETO GOGGUSMOV TWN ELLHNISTWN PROV TOUV EBRAIOUV OTI PAREYEWROUNTO EN TH DIAKONIA TH KAYHMERINH AI CHRAI AUTWN
05L-ACTS-06-02 PROSKALESAMENOI DE OI DWDEKA TO PLHYOV TWN MAYHTWN EIPON OUK ARESTON ESTIN HMAV KATALEIQANTAV TON LOGON TOU YEOU DIAKONEIN TRAPEZAIV
05L-ACTS-06-03 EPISKEQASYE OUN ADELFOI ANDRAV EX UMWN MARTUROUMENOUV EPTA PLHREIV PNEUMATOV AGIOU KAI SOFIAV OUV KATASTHSWMEN EPI THV CREIAV TAUTHV
05L-ACTS-06-04 HMEIV DE TH PROSEUCH KAI TH DIAKONIA TOU LOGOU PROSKARTERHSOMEN
05L-ACTS-06-05 KAI HRESEN O LOGOV ENWPION PANTOV TOU PLHYOUV KAI EXELEXANTO STEFANON ANDRA PLHRHV PISTEWV KAI PNEUMATOV AGIOU KAI FILIPPON KAI PROCORON KAI NIKANORA KAI TIMWNA KAI PARMENAN KAI NIKOLAON PROSHLUTON ANTIOCEA
05L-ACTS-06-06 OUV ESTHSAN ENWPION TWN APOSTOLWN KAI PROSEUXAMENOI EPEYHKAN AUTOIV TAV CEIRAV
05L-ACTS-06-07 KAI O LOGOV TOU YEOU HUXANEN KAI EPLHYUNETO O ARIYMOV TWN MAYHTWN EN IEROUSALHM SFODRA POLUV TE OCLOV TWN IEREWN UPHKOUON TH PISTEI
05L-ACTS-06-08 STEFANOV DE PLHRHV PISTEWV KAI DUNAMEWV EPOIEI TERATA KAI SHMEIA MEGALA EN TW LAW
05L-ACTS-06-09 ANESTHSAN DE TINEV TWN EK THV SUNAGWGHV THV LEGOMENHV LIBERTINWN KAI KURHNAIWN KAI ALEXANDREWN KAI TWN APO KILIKIAV KAI ASIAV SUZHTOUNTEV TW STEFANW
05L-ACTS-06-10 KAI OUK ISCUON ANTISTHNAI TH SOFIA KAI TW PNEUMATI W ELALEI
05L-ACTS-06-11 TOTE UPEBALON ANDRAV LEGONTAV OTI AKHKOAMEN AUTOU LALOUNTOV RHMATA BLASFHMA EIV MWSHN KAI TON YEON
05L-ACTS-06-12 SUNEKINHSAN TE TON LAON KAI TOUV PRESBUTEROUV KAI TOUV GRAMMATEIV KAI EPISTANTEV SUNHRPASAN AUTON KAI HGAGON EIV TO SUNEDRION
05L-ACTS-06-13 ESTHSAN TE MARTURAV QEUDEIV LEGONTAV O ANYRWPOV OUTOV OU PAUETAI RHMATA BLASFHMA LALWN KATA TOU TOPOU TOU AGIOU KAI TOU NOMOU
05L-ACTS-06-14 AKHKOAMEN GAR AUTOU LEGONTOV OTI IHSOUV O NAZWRAIOV OUTOV KATALUSEI TON TOPON TOUTON KAI ALLAXEI TA EYH A PAREDWKEN HMIN MWSHV
05L-ACTS-06-15 KAI ATENISANTEV EIV AUTON APANTEV OI KAYEZOMENOI EN TW SUNEDRIW EIDON TO PROSWPON AUTOU WSEI PROSWPON AGGELOU
05L-ACTS-07-01 EIPEN DE O ARCIEREUV EI ARA TAUTA OUTWV ECEI
05L-ACTS-07-02 O DE EFH ANDREV ADELFOI KAI PATEREV AKOUSATE O YEOV THV DOXHV WFYH TW PATRI HMWN ABRAAM ONTI EN TH MESOPOTAMIA PRIN H KATOIKHSAI AUTON EN CARRAN
05L-ACTS-07-03 KAI EIPEN PROV AUTON EXELYE EK THV GHV SOU KAI EK THV SUGGENEIAV SOU KAI DEURO EIV GHN HN AN SOI DEIXW
05L-ACTS-07-04 TOTE EXELYWN EK GHV CALDAIWN KATWKHSEN EN CARRAN KAKEIYEN META TO APOYANEIN TON PATERA AUTOU METWKISEN AUTON EIV THN GHN TAUTHN EIV HN UMEIV NUN KATOIKEITE
05L-ACTS-07-05 KAI OUK EDWKEN AUTW KLHRONOMIAN EN AUTH OUDE BHMA PODOV KAI EPHGGEILATO DOUNAI AUTW EIV KATASCESIN AUTHN KAI TW SPERMATI AUTOU MET AUTON OUK ONTOV AUTW TEKNOU
