05L-ACTS-07-06 ELALHSEN DE OUTWV O YEOV OTI ESTAI TO SPERMA AUTOU PAROIKON EN GH ALLOTRIA KAI DOULWSOUSIN AUTO KAI KAKWSOUSIN ETH TETRAKOSIA
05L-ACTS-07-07 KAI TO EYNOV W EAN DOULEUSWSIN KRINW EGW EIPEN O YEOV KAI META TAUTA EXELEUSONTAI KAI LATREUSOUSIN MOI EN TW TOPW TOUTW
05L-ACTS-07-08 KAI EDWKEN AUTW DIAYHKHN PERITOMHV KAI OUTWV EGENNHSEN TON ISAAK KAI PERIETEMEN AUTON TH HMERA TH OGDOH KAI O ISAAK TON IAKWB KAI O IAKWB TOUV DWDEKA PATRIARCAV
05L-ACTS-07-09 KAI OI PATRIARCAI ZHLWSANTEV TON IWSHF APEDONTO EIV AIGUPTON KAI HN O YEOV MET AUTOU
05L-ACTS-07-10 KAI EXEILETO AUTON EK PASWN TWN YLIQEWN AUTOU KAI EDWKEN AUTW CARIN KAI SOFIAN ENANTION FARAW BASILEWV AIGUPTOU KAI KATESTHSEN AUTON HGOUMENON EP AIGUPTON KAI OLON TON OIKON AUTOU
05L-ACTS-07-11 HLYEN DE LIMOV EF OLHN THN GHN AIGUPTOU KAI CANAAN KAI YLIQIV MEGALH KAI OUC EURISKON CORTASMATA OI PATEREV HMWN
05L-ACTS-07-12 AKOUSAV DE IAKWB ONTA SITA EN AIGUPTW EXAPESTEILEN TOUV PATERAV HMWN PRWTON
05L-ACTS-07-13 KAI EN TW DEUTERW ANEGNWRISYH IWSHF TOIV ADELFOIV AUTOU KAI FANERON EGENETO TW FARAW TO GENOV TOU IWSHF
05L-ACTS-07-14 APOSTEILAV DE IWSHF METEKALESATO TON PATERA AUTOU IAKWB KAI PASAN THN SUGGENEIAN EN QUCAIV EBDOMHKONTA PENTE
05L-ACTS-07-15 KATEBH DE IAKWB EIV AIGUPTON KAI ETELEUTHSEN AUTOV KAI OI PATEREV HMWN
05L-ACTS-07-16 KAI METETEYHSAN EIV SUCEM KAI ETEYHSAN EN TW MNHMATI O WNHSATO ABRAAM TIMHV ARGURIOU PARA TWN UIWN EMMOR TOU SUCEM
05L-ACTS-07-17 KAYWV DE HGGIZEN O CRONOV THV EPAGGELIAV HV WMOSEN O YEOV TW ABRAAM HUXHSEN O LAOV KAI EPLHYUNYH EN AIGUPTW
05L-ACTS-07-18 ACRI OU ANESTH BASILEUV ETEROV OV OUK HDEI TON IWSHF
05L-ACTS-07-19 OUTOV KATASOFISAMENOV TO GENOV HMWN EKAKWSEN TOUV PATERAV HMWN TOU POIEIN EKYETA TA BREFH AUTWN EIV TO MH ZWOGONEISYAI
05L-ACTS-07-20 EN W KAIRW EGENNHYH MWSHV KAI HN ASTEIOV TW YEW OV ANETRAFH MHNAV TREIV EN TW OIKW TOU PATROV
05L-ACTS-07-21 EKTEYENTA DE AUTON ANEILETO H YUGATHR FARAW KAI ANEYREQATO AUTON EAUTH EIV UION
05L-ACTS-07-22 KAI EPAIDEUYH MWSHV PASH SOFIA AIGUPTIWN HN DE DUNATOV EN LOGOIV KAI ERGOIV
05L-ACTS-07-23 WV DE EPLHROUTO AUTW TESSARAKONTAETHV CRONOV ANEBH EPI THN KARDIAN AUTOU EPISKEQASYAI TOUV ADELFOUV AUTOU TOUV UIOUV ISRAHL
05L-ACTS-07-24 KAI IDWN TINA ADIKOUMENON HMUNATO KAI EPOIHSEN EKDIKHSIN TW KATAPONOUMENW PATAXAV TON AIGUPTION
05L-ACTS-07-25 ENOMIZEN DE SUNIENAI TOUV ADELFOUV AUTOU OTI O YEOV DIA CEIROV AUTOU DIDWSIN AUTOIV SWTHRIAN OI DE OU SUNHKAN
05L-ACTS-07-26 TH TE EPIOUSH HMERA WFYH AUTOIV MACOMENOIV KAI SUNHLASEN AUTOUV EIV EIRHNHN EIPWN ANDREV ADELFOI ESTE UMEIV INA TI ADIKEITE ALLHLOUV
05L-ACTS-07-27 O DE ADIKWN TON PLHSION APWSATO AUTON EIPWN TIV SE KATESTHSEN ARCONTA KAI DIKASTHN EF HMAV
05L-ACTS-07-28 MH ANELEIN ME SU YELEIV ON TROPON ANEILEV CYEV TON AIGUPTION
05L-ACTS-07-29 EFUGEN DE MWSHV EN TW LOGW TOUTW KAI EGENETO PAROIKOV EN GH MADIAM OU EGENNHSEN UIOUV DUO
05L-ACTS-07-30 KAI PLHRWYENTWN ETWN TESSARAKONTA WFYH AUTW EN TH ERHMW TOU OROUV SINA AGGELOV KURIOU EN FLOGI PUROV BATOU
05L-ACTS-07-31 O DE MWSHV IDWN EYAUMAZEN TO ORAMA PROSERCOMENOU DE AUTOU KATANOHSAI EGENETO FWNH KURIOU PROV AUTON
05L-ACTS-07-32 EGW O YEOV TWN PATERWN SOU O YEOV ABRAAM KAI O YEOV ISAAK KAI O YEOV IAKWB ENTROMOV DE GENOMENOV MWSHV OUK ETOLMA KATANOHSAI
05L-ACTS-07-33 EIPEN DE AUTW O KURIOV LUSON TO UPODHMA TWN PODWN SOU O GAR TOPOV EN W ESTHKAV GH AGIA ESTIN
05L-ACTS-07-34 IDWN EIDON THN KAKWSIN TOU LAOU MOU TOU EN AIGUPTW KAI TOU STENAGMOU AUTWN HKOUSA KAI KATEBHN EXELESYAI AUTOUV KAI NUN DEURO APOSTELW SE EIV AIGUPTON
05L-ACTS-07-35 TOUTON TON MWSHN ON HRNHSANTO EIPONTEV TIV SE KATESTHSEN ARCONTA KAI DIKASTHN TOUTON O YEOV ARCONTA KAI LUTRWTHN APESTEILEN EN CEIRI AGGELOU TOU OFYENTOV AUTW EN TH BATW
05L-ACTS-07-36 OUTOV EXHGAGEN AUTOUV POIHSAV TERATA KAI SHMEIA EN GH AIGUPTW KAI EN ERUYRA YALASSH KAI EN TH ERHMW ETH TESSARAKONTA
05L-ACTS-07-37 OUTOV ESTIN O MWSHV O EIPWN TOIV UIOIV ISRAHL PROFHTHN UMIN ANASTHSEI KURIOV O YEOV HMWN EK TWN ADELFWN UMWN WV EME
05L-ACTS-07-38 OUTOV ESTIN O GENOMENOV EN TH EKKLHSIA EN TH ERHMW META TOU AGGELOU TOU LALOUNTOV AUTW EN TW OREI SINA KAI TWN PATERWN HMWN OV EDEXATO LOGON ZWNTA DOUNAI HMIN
05L-ACTS-07-39 W OUK HYELHSAN UPHKOOI GENESYAI OI PATEREV HMWN ALL APWSANTO KAI ESTRAFHSAN TH KARDIA AUTWN EIV AIGUPTON
05L-ACTS-07-40 EIPONTEV TW AARWN POIHSON HMIN YEOUV OI PROPOREUSONTAI HMWN O GAR MWSHV OUTOV OV EXHGAGEN HMAV EK GHV AIGUPTOU OUK OIDAMEN TI GEGONEN AUTW
05L-ACTS-07-41 KAI EMOSCOPOIHSAN EN TAIV HMERAIV EKEINAIV KAI ANHGAGON YUSIAN TW EIDWLW KAI EUFRAINONTO EN TOIV ERGOIV TWN CEIRWN AUTWN
05L-ACTS-07-42 ESTREQEN DE O YEOV KAI PAREDWKEN AUTOUV LATREUEIN TH STRATIA TOU OURANOU KAYWV GEGRAPTAI EN BIBLW TWN PROFHTWN MH SFAGIA KAI YUSIAV PROSHNEGKATE MOI ETH TESSARAKONTA EN TH ERHMW OIKOV ISRAHL
05L-ACTS-07-43 KAI ANELABETE THN SKHNHN TOU MOLOC KAI TO ASTRON TOU YEOU UMWN REMFAN TOUV TUPOUV OUV EPOIHSATE PROSKUNEIN AUTOIV KAI METOIKIW UMAV EPEKEINA BABULWNOV
05L-ACTS-07-44 H SKHNH TOU MARTURIOU HN TOIV PATRASIN HMWN EN TH ERHMW KAYWV DIETAXATO O LALWN TW MWSH POIHSAI AUTHN KATA TON TUPON ON EWRAKEI
05L-ACTS-07-45 HN KAI EISHGAGON DIADEXAMENOI OI PATEREV HMWN META IHSOU EN TH KATASCESEI TWN EYNWN WN EXWSEN O YEOV APO PROSWPOU TWN PATERWN HMWN EWV TWN HMERWN DAUID
05L-ACTS-07-46 OV EUREN CARIN ENWPION TOU YEOU KAI HTHSATO EUREIN SKHNWMA TW YEW IAKWB
05L-ACTS-07-47 SOLOMWN DE WKODOMHSEN AUTW OIKON
05L-ACTS-07-48 ALL OUC O UQISTOV EN CEIROPOIHTOIV NAOIV KATOIKEI KAYWV O PROFHTHV LEGEI
05L-ACTS-07-49 O OURANOV MOI YRONOV H DE GH UPOPODION TWN PODWN MOU POION OIKON OIKODOMHSETE MOI LEGEI KURIOV H TIV TOPOV THV KATAPAUSEWV MOU
05L-ACTS-07-50 OUCI H CEIR MOU EPOIHSEN TAUTA PANTA
05L-ACTS-07-51 SKLHROTRACHLOI KAI APERITMHTOI TH KARDIA KAI TOIV WSIN UMEIV AEI TW PNEUMATI TW AGIW ANTIPIPTETE WV OI PATEREV UMWN KAI UMEIV
05L-ACTS-07-52 TINA TWN PROFHTWN OUK EDIWXAN OI PATEREV UMWN KAI APEKTEINAN TOUV PROKATAGGEILANTAV PERI THV ELEUSEWV TOU DIKAIOU OU NUN UMEIV PRODOTAI KAI FONEIV GEGENHSYE
05L-ACTS-07-53 OITINEV ELABETE TON NOMON EIV DIATAGAV AGGELWN KAI OUK EFULAXATE
05L-ACTS-07-54 AKOUONTEV DE TAUTA DIEPRIONTO TAIV KARDIAIV AUTWN KAI EBRUCON TOUV ODONTAV EP AUTON
05L-ACTS-07-55 UPARCWN DE PLHRHV PNEUMATOV AGIOU ATENISAV EIV TON OURANON EIDEN DOXAN YEOU KAI IHSOUN ESTWTA EK DEXIWN TOU YEOU
05L-ACTS-07-56 KAI EIPEN IDOU YEWRW TOUV OURANOUV ANEWGMENOUV KAI TON UION TOU ANYRWPOU EK DEXIWN ESTWTA TOU YEOU
05L-ACTS-07-57 KRAXANTEV DE FWNH MEGALH SUNESCON TA WTA AUTWN KAI WRMHSAN OMOYUMADON EP AUTON
05L-ACTS-07-58 KAI EKBALONTEV EXW THV POLEWV ELIYOBOLOUN KAI OI MARTUREV APEYENTO TA IMATIA PARA TOUV PODAV NEANIOU KALOUMENOU SAULOU
05L-ACTS-07-59 KAI ELIYOBOLOUN TON STEFANON EPIKALOUMENON KAI LEGONTA KURIE IHSOU DEXAI TO PNEUMA MOU
05L-ACTS-07-60 YEIV DE TA GONATA EKRAXEN FWNH MEGALH KURIE MH STHSHV AUTOIV THN AMARTIAN TAUTHN KAI TOUTO EIPWN EKOIMHYH
05L-ACTS-08-01 SAULOV DE HN SUNEUDOKWN TH ANAIRESEI AUTOU EGENETO DE EN EKEINH TH HMERA DIWGMOV MEGAV EPI THN EKKLHSIAN THN EN IEROSOLUMOIV PANTEV DE DIESPARHSAN KATA TAV CWRAV THV IOUDAIAV KAI SAMAREIAV PLHN TWN APOSTOLWN
05L-ACTS-08-02 SUNEKOMISAN DE TON STEFANON ANDREV EULABEIV KAI EPOIHSANTO KOPETON MEGAN EP AUTW
05L-ACTS-08-03 SAULOV DE ELUMAINETO THN EKKLHSIAN KATA TOUV OIKOUV EISPOREUOMENOV SURWN TE ANDRAV KAI GUNAIKAV PAREDIDOU EIV FULAKHN
05L-ACTS-08-04 OI MEN OUN DIASPARENTEV DIHLYON EUAGGELIZOMENOI TON LOGON
05L-ACTS-08-05 FILIPPOV DE KATELYWN EIV POLIN THV SAMAREIAV EKHRUSSEN AUTOIV TON CRISTON
05L-ACTS-08-06 PROSEICON TE OI OCLOI TOIV LEGOMENOIV UPO TOU FILIPPOU OMOYUMADON EN TW AKOUEIN AUTOUV KAI BLEPEIN TA SHMEIA A EPOIEI
05L-ACTS-08-07 POLLWN GAR TWN ECONTWN PNEUMATA AKAYARTA BOWNTA FWNH MEGALH EXHRCETO POLLOI DE PARALELUMENOI KAI CWLOI EYERAPEUYHSAN
05L-ACTS-08-08 KAI EGENETO CARA MEGALH EN TH POLEI EKEINH
05L-ACTS-08-09 ANHR DE TIV ONOMATI SIMWN PROUPHRCEN EN TH POLEI MAGEUWN KAI EXISTWN TO EYNOV THV SAMAREIAV LEGWN EINAI TINA EAUTON MEGAN
05L-ACTS-08-10 W PROSEICON APO MIKROU EWV MEGALOU LEGONTEV OUTOV ESTIN H DUNAMIV TOU YEOU H MEGALH
05L-ACTS-08-11 PROSEICON DE AUTW DIA TO IKANW CRONW TAIV MAGEIAIV EXESTAKENAI AUTOUV
05L-ACTS-08-12 OTE DE EPISTEUSAN TW FILIPPW EUAGGELIZOMENW TA PERI THV BASILEIAV TOU YEOU KAI TOU ONOMATOV IHSOU CRISTOU EBAPTIZONTO ANDREV TE KAI GUNAIKEV
05L-ACTS-08-13 O DE SIMWN KAI AUTOV EPISTEUSEN KAI BAPTISYEIV HN PROSKARTERWN TW FILIPPW YEWRWN TE DUNAMEIV KAI SHMEIA GINOMENA EXISTATO
05L-ACTS-08-14 AKOUSANTEV DE OI EN IEROSOLUMOIV APOSTOLOI OTI DEDEKTAI H SAMAREIA TON LOGON TOU YEOU APESTEILAN PROV AUTOUV TON PETRON KAI IWANNHN
05L-ACTS-08-15 OITINEV KATABANTEV PROSHUXANTO PERI AUTWN OPWV LABWSIN PNEUMA AGION
05L-ACTS-08-16 OUPW GAR HN EP OUDENI AUTWN EPIPEPTWKOV MONON DE BEBAPTISMENOI UPHRCON EIV TO ONOMA TOU CRISTOU IHSOU
05L-ACTS-08-17 TOTE EPETIYOUN TAV CEIRAV EP AUTOUV KAI ELAMBANON PNEUMA AGION
05L-ACTS-08-18 YEASAMENOV DE O SIMWN OTI DIA THV EPIYESEWV TWN CEIRWN TWN APOSTOLWN DIDOTAI TO PNEUMA TO AGION PROSHNEGKEN AUTOIV CRHMATA
05L-ACTS-08-19 LEGWN DOTE KAMOI THN EXOUSIAN TAUTHN INA W EAN EPIYW TAV CEIRAV LAMBANH PNEUMA AGION
05L-ACTS-08-20 PETROV DE EIPEN PROV AUTON TO ARGURION SOU SUN SOI EIH EIV APWLEIAN OTI THN DWREAN TOU YEOU ENOMISAV DIA CRHMATWN KTASYAI
05L-ACTS-08-21 OUK ESTIN SOI MERIV OUDE KLHROV EN TW LOGW TOUTW H GAR KARDIA SOU OUK ESTIN EUYEIA ENWPION TOU YEOU
05L-ACTS-08-22 METANOHSON OUN APO THV KAKIAV SOU TAUTHV KAI DEHYHTI TOU YEOU EI ARA AFEYHSETAI SOI H EPINOIA THV KARDIAV SOU
05L-ACTS-08-23 EIV GAR COLHN PIKRIAV KAI SUNDESMON ADIKIAV ORW SE ONTA
05L-ACTS-08-24 APOKRIYEIV DE O SIMWN EIPEN DEHYHTE UMEIV UPER EMOU PROV TON KURION OPWV MHDEN EPELYH EP EME WN EIRHKATE
05L-ACTS-08-25 OI MEN OUN DIAMARTURAMENOI KAI LALHSANTEV TON LOGON TOU KURIOU UPESTREQAN EIV IEROUSALHM POLLAV TE KWMAV TWN SAMAREITWN EUHGGELISANTO
05L-ACTS-08-26 AGGELOV DE KURIOU ELALHSEN PROV FILIPPON LEGWN ANASTHYI KAI POREUOU KATA MESHMBRIAN EPI THN ODON THN KATABAINOUSAN APO IEROUSALHM EIV GAZAN AUTH ESTIN ERHMOV
05L-ACTS-08-27 KAI ANASTAV EPOREUYH KAI IDOU ANHR AIYIOQ EUNOUCOV DUNASTHV KANDAKHV THV BASILISSHV AIYIOPWN OV HN EPI PASHV THV GAZHV AUTHV OV ELHLUYEI PROSKUNHSWN EIV IEROUSALHM
05L-ACTS-08-28 HN TE UPOSTREFWN KAI KAYHMENOV EPI TOU ARMATOV AUTOU KAI ANEGINWSKEN TON PROFHTHN HSAIAN
05L-ACTS-08-29 EIPEN DE TO PNEUMA TW FILIPPW PROSELYE KAI KOLLHYHTI TW ARMATI TOUTW
05L-ACTS-08-30 PROSDRAMWN DE O FILIPPOV HKOUSEN AUTOU ANAGINWSKONTOV TON PROFHTHN HSAIAN KAI EIPEN ARA GE GINWSKEIV A ANAGINWSKEIV
05L-ACTS-08-31 O DE EIPEN PWV GAR AN DUNAIMHN EAN MH TIV ODHGHSH ME PAREKALESEN TE TON FILIPPON ANABANTA KAYISAI SUN AUTW
05L-ACTS-08-32 H DE PERIOCH THV GRAFHV HN ANEGINWSKEN HN AUTH WV PROBATON EPI SFAGHN HCYH KAI WV AMNOV ENANTION TOU KEIRONTOV AUTON AFWNOV OUTWV OUK ANOIGEI TO STOMA AUTOU
05L-ACTS-08-33 EN TH TAPEINWSEI AUTOU H KRISIV AUTOU HRYH THN DE GENEAN AUTOU TIV DIHGHSETAI OTI AIRETAI APO THV GHV H ZWH AUTOU
05L-ACTS-08-34 APOKRIYEIV DE O EUNOUCOV TW FILIPPW EIPEN DEOMAI SOU PERI TINOV O PROFHTHV LEGEI TOUTO PERI EAUTOU H PERI ETEROU TINOV
05L-ACTS-08-35 ANOIXAV DE O FILIPPOV TO STOMA AUTOU KAI ARXAMENOV APO THV GRAFHV TAUTHV EUHGGELISATO AUTW TON IHSOUN
05L-ACTS-08-36 WV DE EPOREUONTO KATA THN ODON HLYON EPI TI UDWR KAI FHSIN O EUNOUCOV IDOU UDWR TI KWLUEI ME BAPTISYHNAI
05L-ACTS-08-37
05L-ACTS-08-38 KAI EKELEUSEN STHNAI TO ARMA KAI KATEBHSAN AMFOTEROI EIV TO UDWR O TE FILIPPOV KAI O EUNOUCOV KAI EBAPTISEN AUTON
05L-ACTS-08-39 OTE DE ANEBHSAN EK TOU UDATOV PNEUMA KURIOU HRPASEN TON FILIPPON KAI OUK EIDEN AUTON OUKETI O EUNOUCOV EPOREUETO GAR THN ODON AUTOU CAIRWN
05L-ACTS-08-40 FILIPPOV DE EUREYH EIV AZWTON KAI DIERCOMENOV EUHGGELIZETO TAV POLEIV PASAV EWV TOU ELYEIN AUTON EIV KAISAREIAN
05L-ACTS-09-01 O DE SAULOV ETI EMPNEWN APEILHV KAI FONOU EIV TOUV MAYHTAV TOU KURIOU PROSELYWN TW ARCIEREI
05L-ACTS-09-02 HTHSATO PAR AUTOU EPISTOLAV EIV DAMASKON PROV TAV SUNAGWGAV OPWV EAN TINAV EURH THV ODOU ONTAV ANDRAV TE KAI GUNAIKAV DEDEMENOUV AGAGH EIV IEROUSALHM
05L-ACTS-09-03 EN DE TW POREUESYAI EGENETO AUTON EGGIZEIN TH DAMASKW KAI EXAIFNHV PERIHSTRAQEN AUTON FWV APO TOU OURANOU
05L-ACTS-09-04 KAI PESWN EPI THN GHN HKOUSEN FWNHN LEGOUSAN AUTW SAOUL SAOUL TI ME DIWKEIV
05L-ACTS-09-05 EIPEN DE TIV EI KURIE O DE KURIOV EIPEN EGW EIMI IHSOUV ON SU DIWKEIV
05L-ACTS-09-06 ALLA ANASTHYI KAI EISELYE EIV THN POLIN KAI LALHYHSETAI SOI TI SE DEI POIEIN
05L-ACTS-09-07 OI DE ANDREV OI SUNODEUONTEV AUTW EISTHKEISAN ENEOI AKOUONTEV MEN THV FWNHV MHDENA DE YEWROUNTEV
05L-ACTS-09-08 HGERYH DE O SAULOV APO THV GHV ANEWGMENWN TE TWN OFYALMWN AUTOU OUDENA EBLEPEN CEIRAGWGOUNTEV DE AUTON EISHGAGON EIV DAMASKON
05L-ACTS-09-09 KAI HN HMERAV TREIV MH BLEPWN KAI OUK EFAGEN OUDE EPIEN
05L-ACTS-09-10 HN DE TIV MAYHTHV EN DAMASKW ONOMATI ANANIAV KAI EIPEN PROV AUTON O KURIOV EN ORAMATI ANANIA O DE EIPEN IDOU EGW KURIE
05L-ACTS-09-11 O DE KURIOV PROV AUTON ANASTAV POREUYHTI EPI THN RUMHN THN KALOUMENHN EUYEIAN KAI ZHTHSON EN OIKIA IOUDA SAULON ONOMATI TARSEA IDOU GAR PROSEUCETAI
05L-ACTS-09-12 KAI EIDEN EN ORAMATI ANDRA ONOMATI ANANIAN EISELYONTA KAI EPIYENTA AUTW CEIRA OPWV ANABLEQH
05L-ACTS-09-13 APEKRIYH DE ANANIAV KURIE AKHKOA APO POLLWN PERI TOU ANDROV TOUTOU OSA KAKA EPOIHSEN TOIV AGIOIV SOU EN IEROUSALHM
05L-ACTS-09-14 KAI WDE ECEI EXOUSIAN PARA TWN ARCIEREWN DHSAI PANTAV TOUV EPIKALOUMENOUV TO ONOMA SOU
05L-ACTS-09-15 EIPEN DE PROV AUTON O KURIOV POREUOU OTI SKEUOV EKLOGHV MOI ESTIN OUTOV TOU BASTASAI TO ONOMA MOU ENWPION EYNWN KAI BASILEWN UIWN TE ISRAHL
05L-ACTS-09-16 EGW GAR UPODEIXW AUTW OSA DEI AUTON UPER TOU ONOMATOV MOU PAYEIN
05L-ACTS-09-17 APHLYEN DE ANANIAV KAI EISHLYEN EIV THN OIKIAN KAI EPIYEIV EP AUTON TAV CEIRAV EIPEN SAOUL ADELFE O KURIOV APESTALKEN ME O OFYEIV SOI EN TH ODW H HRCOU OPWV ANABLEQHV KAI PLHSYHV PNEUMATOV AGIOU
05L-ACTS-09-18 KAI EUYEWV APEPESON APO TWN OFYALMWN AUTOU WSEI LEPIDEV ANEBLEQEN TE KAI ANASTAV EBAPTISYH
05L-ACTS-09-19 KAI LABWN TROFHN ENISCUSEN EGENETO DE O SAULOV META TWN EN DAMASKW MAYHTWN HMERAV TINAV
05L-ACTS-09-20 KAI EUYEWV EN TAIV SUNAGWGAIV EKHRUSSEN TON CRISTON OTI OUTOV ESTIN O UIOV TOU YEOU
05L-ACTS-09-21 EXISTANTO DE PANTEV OI AKOUONTEV KAI ELEGON OUC OUTOV ESTIN O PORYHSAV EN IEROUSALHM TOUV EPIKALOUMENOUV TO ONOMA TOUTO KAI WDE EIV TOUTO ELHLUYEN INA DEDEMENOUV AUTOUV AGAGH EPI TOUV ARCIEREIV
05L-ACTS-09-22 SAULOV DE MALLON ENEDUNAMOUTO KAI SUNECUNEN TOUV IOUDAIOUV TOUV KATOIKOUNTAV EN DAMASKW SUMBIBAZWN OTI OUTOV ESTIN O CRISTOV
05L-ACTS-09-23 WV DE EPLHROUNTO HMERAI IKANAI SUNEBOULEUSANTO OI IOUDAIOI ANELEIN AUTON
05L-ACTS-09-24 EGNWSYH DE TW SAULW H EPIBOULH AUTWN PARETHROUN TE TAV PULAV HMERAV TE KAI NUKTOV OPWV AUTON ANELWSIN
05L-ACTS-09-25 LABONTEV DE AUTON OI MAYHTAI NUKTOV KAYHKAN DIA TOU TEICOUV CALASANTEV EN SPURIDI
05L-ACTS-09-26 PARAGENOMENOV DE O SAULOV EN IEROUSALHM EPEIRATO KOLLASYAI TOIV MAYHTAIV KAI PANTEV EFOBOUNTO AUTON MH PISTEUONTEV OTI ESTIN MAYHTHV
05L-ACTS-09-27 BARNABAV DE EPILABOMENOV AUTON HGAGEN PROV TOUV APOSTOLOUV KAI DIHGHSATO AUTOIV PWV EN TH ODW EIDEN TON KURION KAI OTI ELALHSEN AUTW KAI PWV EN DAMASKW EPARRHSIASATO EN TW ONOMATI TOU IHSOU
05L-ACTS-09-28 KAI HN MET AUTWN EISPOREUOMENOV EIV IEROUSALHM KAI PARRHSIAZOMENOV EN TW ONOMATI TOU KURIOU IHSOU
05L-ACTS-09-29 ELALEI TE KAI SUNEZHTEI PROV TOUV ELLHNISTAV OI DE EPECEIROUN AUTON ANELEIN
05L-ACTS-09-30 EPIGNONTEV DE OI ADELFOI KATHGAGON AUTON EIV KAISAREIAN KAI EXAPESTEILAN AUTON EIV TARSON
05L-ACTS-09-31 AI MEN OUN EKKLHSIAI KAY OLHV THV IOUDAIAV KAI GALILAIAV KAI SAMAREIAV EICON EIRHNHN OIKODOMOUMENAI KAI POREUOMENAI TW FOBW TOU KURIOU KAI TH PARAKLHSEI TOU AGIOU PNEUMATOV EPLHYUNONTO
05L-ACTS-09-32 EGENETO DE PETRON DIERCOMENON DIA PANTWN KATELYEIN KAI PROV TOUV AGIOUV TOUV KATOIKOUNTAV LUDDAN
05L-ACTS-09-33 EUREN DE EKEI ANYRWPON TINA AINEAN ONOMATI EX ETWN OKTW KATAKEIMENON EPI KRABBATW OV HN PARALELUMENOV
05L-ACTS-09-34 KAI EIPEN AUTW O PETROV AINEA IATAI SE IHSOUV O CRISTOV ANASTHYI KAI STRWSON SEAUTW KAI EUYEWV ANESTH
05L-ACTS-09-35 KAI EIDON AUTON PANTEV OI KATOIKOUNTEV LUDDAN KAI TON ASSARWNA OITINEV EPESTREQAN EPI TON KURION
05L-ACTS-09-36 EN IOPPH DE TIV HN MAYHTRIA ONOMATI TABHYA H DIERMHNEUOMENH LEGETAI DORKAV AUTH HN PLHRHV AGAYWN ERGWN KAI ELEHMOSUNWN WN EPOIEI
05L-ACTS-09-37 EGENETO DE EN TAIV HMERAIV EKEINAIV ASYENHSASAN AUTHN APOYANEIN LOUSANTEV DE AUTHN EYHKAN EN UPERWW
05L-ACTS-09-38 EGGUV DE OUSHV LUDDHV TH IOPPH OI MAYHTAI AKOUSANTEV OTI PETROV ESTIN EN AUTH APESTEILAN PROV AUTON PARAKALOUNTEV MH OKNHSAI DIELYEIN EWV AUTWN
05L-ACTS-09-39 ANASTAV DE PETROV SUNHLYEN AUTOIV ON PARAGENOMENON ANHGAGON EIV TO UPERWON KAI PARESTHSAN AUTW PASAI AI CHRAI KLAIOUSAI KAI EPIDEIKNUMENAI CITWNAV KAI IMATIA OSA EPOIEI MET AUTWN OUSA H DORKAV
05L-ACTS-09-40 EKBALWN DE EXW PANTAV O PETROV YEIV TA GONATA PROSHUXATO KAI EPISTREQAV PROV TO SWMA EIPEN TABHYA ANASTHYI H DE HNOIXEN TOUV OFYALMOUV AUTHV KAI IDOUSA TON PETRON ANEKAYISEN
05L-ACTS-09-41 DOUV DE AUTH CEIRA ANESTHSEN AUTHN FWNHSAV DE TOUV AGIOUV KAI TAV CHRAV PARESTHSEN AUTHN ZWSAN
05L-ACTS-09-42 GNWSTON DE EGENETO KAY OLHV THV IOPPHV KAI POLLOI EPISTEUSAN EPI TON KURION
05L-ACTS-09-43 EGENETO DE HMERAV IKANAV MEINAI AUTON EN IOPPH PARA TINI SIMWNI BURSEI
05L-ACTS-10-01 ANHR DE TIV HN EN KAISAREIA ONOMATI KORNHLIOV EKATONTARCHV EK SPEIRHV THV KALOUMENHV ITALIKHV
05L-ACTS-10-02 EUSEBHV KAI FOBOUMENOV TON YEON SUN PANTI TW OIKW AUTOU POIWN TE ELEHMOSUNAV POLLAV TW LAW KAI DEOMENOV TOU YEOU DIA PANTOV
05L-ACTS-10-03 EIDEN EN ORAMATI FANERWV WSEI WRAN ENATHN THV HMERAV AGGELON TOU YEOU EISELYONTA PROV AUTON KAI EIPONTA AUTW KORNHLIE
05L-ACTS-10-04 O DE ATENISAV AUTW KAI EMFOBOV GENOMENOV EIPEN TI ESTIN KURIE EIPEN DE AUTW AI PROSEUCAI SOU KAI AI ELEHMOSUNAI SOU ANEBHSAN EIV MNHMOSUNON ENWPION TOU YEOU
05L-ACTS-10-05 KAI NUN PEMQON EIV IOPPHN ANDRAV KAI METAPEMQAI SIMWNA TON EPIKALOUMENON PETRON
05L-ACTS-10-06 OUTOV XENIZETAI PARA TINI SIMWNI BURSEI W ESTIN OIKIA PARA YALASSAN
05L-ACTS-10-07 WV DE APHLYEN O AGGELOV O LALWN TW KORNHLIW FWNHSAV DUO TWN OIKETWN AUTOU KAI STRATIWTHN EUSEBH TWN PROSKARTEROUNTWN AUTW
05L-ACTS-10-08 KAI EXHGHSAMENOV AUTOIV APANTA APESTEILEN AUTOUV EIV THN IOPPHN
05L-ACTS-10-09 TH DE EPAURION ODOIPOROUNTWN EKEINWN KAI TH POLEI EGGIZONTWN ANEBH PETROV EPI TO DWMA PROSEUXASYAI PERI WRAN EKTHN
05L-ACTS-10-10 EGENETO DE PROSPEINOV KAI HYELEN GEUSASYAI PARASKEUAZONTWN DE EKEINWN EPEPESEN EP AUTON EKSTASIV
05L-ACTS-10-11 KAI YEWREI TON OURANON ANEWGMENON KAI KATABAINON EP AUTON SKEUOV TI WV OYONHN MEGALHN TESSARSIN ARCAIV DEDEMENON KAI KAYIEMENON EPI THV GHV
05L-ACTS-10-12 EN W UPHRCEN PANTA TA TETRAPODA THV GHV KAI TA YHRIA KAI TA ERPETA KAI TA PETEINA TOU OURANOU
05L-ACTS-10-13 KAI EGENETO FWNH PROV AUTON ANASTAV PETRE YUSON KAI FAGE
05L-ACTS-10-14 O DE PETROV EIPEN MHDAMWV KURIE OTI OUDEPOTE EFAGON PAN KOINON H AKAYARTON
05L-ACTS-10-15 KAI FWNH PALIN EK DEUTEROU PROV AUTON A O YEOV EKAYARISEN SU MH KOINOU
05L-ACTS-10-16 TOUTO DE EGENETO EPI TRIV KAI PALIN ANELHFYH TO SKEUOV EIV TON OURANON
05L-ACTS-10-17 WV DE EN EAUTW DIHPOREI O PETROV TI AN EIH TO ORAMA O EIDEN KAI IDOU OI ANDREV OI APESTALMENOI APO TOU KORNHLIOU DIERWTHSANTEV THN OIKIAN SIMWNOV EPESTHSAN EPI TON PULWNA
05L-ACTS-10-18 KAI FWNHSANTEV EPUNYANONTO EI SIMWN O EPIKALOUMENOV PETROV ENYADE XENIZETAI
05L-ACTS-10-19 TOU DE PETROU DIENYUMOUMENOU PERI TOU ORAMATOV EIPEN AUTW TO PNEUMA IDOU ANDREV ZHTOUSIN SE
05L-ACTS-10-20 ALLA ANASTAV KATABHYI KAI POREUOU SUN AUTOIV MHDEN DIAKRINOMENOV DIOTI EGW APESTALKA AUTOUV
05L-ACTS-10-21 KATABAV DE PETROV PROV TOUV ANDRAV EIPEN IDOU EGW EIMI ON ZHTEITE TIV H AITIA DI HN PARESTE
05L-ACTS-10-22 OI DE EIPON KORNHLIOV EKATONTARCHV ANHR DIKAIOV KAI FOBOUMENOV TON YEON MARTUROUMENOV TE UPO OLOU TOU EYNOUV TWN IOUDAIWN ECRHMATISYH UPO AGGELOU AGIOU METAPEMQASYAI SE EIV TON OIKON AUTOU KAI AKOUSAI RHMATA PARA SOU
05L-ACTS-10-23 EISKALESAMENOV OUN AUTOUV EXENISEN TH DE EPAURION O PETROV EXHLYEN SUN AUTOIV KAI TINEV TWN ADELFWN TWN APO IOPPHV SUNHLYON AUTW
05L-ACTS-10-24 KAI TH EPAURION EISHLYON EIV THN KAISAREIAN O DE KORNHLIOV HN PROSDOKWN AUTOUV SUGKALESAMENOV TOUV SUGGENEIV AUTOU KAI TOUV ANAGKAIOUV FILOUV
05L-ACTS-10-25 WV DE EGENETO TOU EISELYEIN TON PETRON SUNANTHSAV AUTW O KORNHLIOV PESWN EPI TOUV PODAV PROSEKUNHSEN
05L-ACTS-10-26 O DE PETROV AUTON HGEIREN LEGWN ANASTHYI KAGW AUTOV ANYRWPOV EIMI
05L-ACTS-10-27 KAI SUNOMILWN AUTW EISHLYEN KAI EURISKEI SUNELHLUYOTAV POLLOUV
05L-ACTS-10-28 EFH TE PROV AUTOUV UMEIV EPISTASYE WV AYEMITON ESTIN ANDRI IOUDAIW KOLLASYAI H PROSERCESYAI ALLOFULW KAI EMOI O YEOV EDEIXEN MHDENA KOINON H AKAYARTON LEGEIN ANYRWPON
05L-ACTS-10-29 DIO KAI ANANTIRRHTWV HLYON METAPEMFYEIV PUNYANOMAI OUN TINI LOGW METEPEMQASYE ME
05L-ACTS-10-30 KAI O KORNHLIOV EFH APO TETARTHV HMERAV MECRI TAUTHV THV WRAV HMHN NHSTEUWN KAI THN ENATHN WRAN PROSEUCOMENOV EN TW OIKW MOU KAI IDOU ANHR ESTH ENWPION MOU EN ESYHTI LAMPRA
05L-ACTS-10-31 KAI FHSIN KORNHLIE EISHKOUSYH SOU H PROSEUCH KAI AI ELEHMOSUNAI SOU EMNHSYHSAN ENWPION TOU YEOU
05L-ACTS-10-32 PEMQON OUN EIV IOPPHN KAI METAKALESAI SIMWNA OV EPIKALEITAI PETROV OUTOV XENIZETAI EN OIKIA SIMWNOV BURSEWV PARA YALASSAN OV PARAGENOMENOV LALHSEI SOI
05L-ACTS-10-33 EXAUTHV OUN EPEMQA PROV SE SU TE KALWV EPOIHSAV PARAGENOMENOV NUN OUN PANTEV HMEIV ENWPION TOU YEOU PARESMEN AKOUSAI PANTA TA PROSTETAGMENA SOI UPO TOU YEOU
05L-ACTS-10-34 ANOIXAV DE PETROV TO STOMA EIPEN EP ALHYEIAV KATALAMBANOMAI OTI OUK ESTIN PROSWPOLHPTHV O YEOV
05L-ACTS-10-35 ALL EN PANTI EYNEI O FOBOUMENOV AUTON KAI ERGAZOMENOV DIKAIOSUNHN DEKTOV AUTW ESTIN
05L-ACTS-10-36 TON LOGON ON APESTEILEN TOIV UIOIV ISRAHL EUAGGELIZOMENOV EIRHNHN DIA IHSOU CRISTOU OUTOV ESTIN PANTWN KURIOV
05L-ACTS-10-37 UMEIV OIDATE TO GENOMENON RHMA KAY OLHV THV IOUDAIAV ARXAMENON APO THV GALILAIAV META TO BAPTISMA O EKHRUXEN IWANNHV
05L-ACTS-10-38 IHSOUN TON APO NAZARET WV ECRISEN AUTON O YEOV PNEUMATI AGIW KAI DUNAMEI OV DIHLYEN EUERGETWN KAI IWMENOV PANTAV TOUV KATADUNASTEUOMENOUV UPO TOU DIABOLOU OTI O YEOV HN MET AUTOU
05L-ACTS-10-39 KAI HMEIV ESMEN MARTUREV PANTWN WN EPOIHSEN EN TE TH CWRA TWN IOUDAIWN KAI EN IEROUSALHM ON KAI ANEILON KREMASANTEV EPI XULOU
05L-ACTS-10-40 TOUTON O YEOV HGEIREN TH TRITH HMERA KAI EDWKEN AUTON EMFANH GENESYAI
05L-ACTS-10-41 OU PANTI TW LAW ALLA MARTUSIN TOIV PROKECEIROTONHMENOIV UPO TOU YEOU HMIN OITINEV SUNEFAGOMEN KAI SUNEPIOMEN AUTW META TO ANASTHNAI AUTON EK NEKRWN
05L-ACTS-10-42 KAI PARHGGEILEN HMIN KHRUXAI TW LAW KAI DIAMARTURASYAI OTI AUTOV ESTIN O WRISMENOV UPO TOU YEOU KRITHV ZWNTWN KAI NEKRWN
05L-ACTS-10-43 TOUTW PANTEV OI PROFHTAI MARTUROUSIN AFESIN AMARTIWN LABEIN DIA TOU ONOMATOV AUTOU PANTA TON PISTEUONTA EIV AUTON
05L-ACTS-10-44 ETI LALOUNTOV TOU PETROU TA RHMATA TAUTA EPEPESEN TO PNEUMA TO AGION EPI PANTAV TOUV AKOUONTAV TON LOGON
05L-ACTS-10-45 KAI EXESTHSAN OI EK PERITOMHV PISTOI OSOI SUNHLYON TW PETRW OTI KAI EPI TA EYNH H DWREA TOU AGIOU PNEUMATOV EKKECUTAI
05L-ACTS-10-46 HKOUON GAR AUTWN LALOUNTWN GLWSSAIV KAI MEGALUNONTWN TON YEON TOTE APEKRIYH O PETROV
05L-ACTS-10-47 MHTI TO UDWR KWLUSAI DUNATAI TIV TOU MH BAPTISYHNAI TOUTOUV OITINEV TO PNEUMA TO AGION ELABON KAYWV KAI HMEIV
05L-ACTS-10-48 PROSETAXEN TE AUTOUV BAPTISYHNAI EN TW ONOMATI TOU KURIOU TOTE HRWTHSAN AUTON EPIMEINAI HMERAV TINAV
05L-ACTS-11-01 HKOUSAN DE OI APOSTOLOI KAI OI ADELFOI OI ONTEV KATA THN IOUDAIAN OTI KAI TA EYNH EDEXANTO TON LOGON TOU YEOU
05L-ACTS-11-02 KAI OTE ANEBH PETROV EIV IEROSOLUMA DIEKRINONTO PROV AUTON OI EK PERITOMHV
05L-ACTS-11-03 LEGONTEV OTI PROV ANDRAV AKROBUSTIAN ECONTAV EISHLYEV KAI SUNEFAGEV AUTOIV
05L-ACTS-11-04 ARXAMENOV DE O PETROV EXETIYETO AUTOIV KAYEXHV LEGWN
05L-ACTS-11-05 EGW HMHN EN POLEI IOPPH PROSEUCOMENOV KAI EIDON EN EKSTASEI ORAMA KATABAINON SKEUOV TI WV OYONHN MEGALHN TESSARSIN ARCAIV KAYIEMENHN EK TOU OURANOU KAI HLYEN ACRI EMOU
05L-ACTS-11-06 EIV HN ATENISAV KATENOOUN KAI EIDON TA TETRAPODA THV GHV KAI TA YHRIA KAI TA ERPETA KAI TA PETEINA TOU OURANOU
05L-ACTS-11-07 HKOUSA DE FWNHV LEGOUSHV MOI ANASTAV PETRE YUSON KAI FAGE
05L-ACTS-11-08 EIPON DE MHDAMWV KURIE OTI PAN KOINON H AKAYARTON OUDEPOTE EISHLYEN EIV TO STOMA MOU
05L-ACTS-11-09 APEKRIYH DE MOI FWNH EK DEUTEROU EK TOU OURANOU A O YEOV EKAYARISEN SU MH KOINOU
05L-ACTS-11-10 TOUTO DE EGENETO EPI TRIV KAI PALIN ANESPASYH APANTA EIV TON OURANON
05L-ACTS-11-11 KAI IDOU EXAUTHV TREIV ANDREV EPESTHSAN EPI THN OIKIAN EN H HMHN APESTALMENOI APO KAISAREIAV PROV ME
05L-ACTS-11-12 EIPEN DE MOI TO PNEUMA SUNELYEIN AUTOIV MHDEN DIAKRINOMENON HLYON DE SUN EMOI KAI OI EX ADELFOI OUTOI KAI EISHLYOMEN EIV TON OIKON TOU ANDROV
05L-ACTS-11-13 APHGGEILEN TE HMIN PWV EIDEN TON AGGELON EN TW OIKW AUTOU STAYENTA KAI EIPONTA AUTW APOSTEILON EIV IOPPHN ANDRAV KAI METAPEMQAI SIMWNA TON EPIKALOUMENON PETRON
05L-ACTS-11-14 OV LALHSEI RHMATA PROV SE EN OIV SWYHSH SU KAI PAV O OIKOV SOU
05L-ACTS-11-15 EN DE TW ARXASYAI ME LALEIN EPEPESEN TO PNEUMA TO AGION EP AUTOUV WSPER KAI EF HMAV EN ARCH
05L-ACTS-11-16 EMNHSYHN DE TOU RHMATOV KURIOU WV ELEGEN IWANNHV MEN EBAPTISEN UDATI UMEIV DE BAPTISYHSESYE EN PNEUMATI AGIW
05L-ACTS-11-17 EI OUN THN ISHN DWREAN EDWKEN AUTOIV O YEOV WV KAI HMIN PISTEUSASIN EPI TON KURION IHSOUN CRISTON EGW DE TIV HMHN DUNATOV KWLUSAI TON YEON
05L-ACTS-11-18 AKOUSANTEV DE TAUTA HSUCASAN KAI EDOXAZON TON YEON LEGONTEV ARA GE KAI TOIV EYNESIN O YEOV THN METANOIAN EDWKEN EIV ZWHN
05L-ACTS-11-19 OI MEN OUN DIASPARENTEV APO THV YLIQEWV THV GENOMENHV EPI STEFANW DIHLYON EWV FOINIKHV KAI KUPROU KAI ANTIOCEIAV MHDENI LALOUNTEV TON LOGON EI MH MONON IOUDAIOIV
05L-ACTS-11-20 HSAN DE TINEV EX AUTWN ANDREV KUPRIOI KAI KURHNAIOI OITINEV EISELYONTEV EIV ANTIOCEIAN ELALOUN PROV TOUV ELLHNISTAV EUAGGELIZOMENOI TON KURION IHSOUN
05L-ACTS-11-21 KAI HN CEIR KURIOU MET AUTWN POLUV TE ARIYMOV PISTEUSAV EPESTREQEN EPI TON KURION
05L-ACTS-11-22 HKOUSYH DE O LOGOV EIV TA WTA THV EKKLHSIAV THV EN IEROSOLUMOIV PERI AUTWN KAI EXAPESTEILAN BARNABAN DIELYEIN EWV ANTIOCEIAV
05L-ACTS-11-23 OV PARAGENOMENOV KAI IDWN THN CARIN TOU YEOU ECARH KAI PAREKALEI PANTAV TH PROYESEI THV KARDIAV PROSMENEIN TW KURIW
05L-ACTS-11-24 OTI HN ANHR AGAYOV KAI PLHRHV PNEUMATOV AGIOU KAI PISTEWV KAI PROSETEYH OCLOV IKANOV TW KURIW
05L-ACTS-11-25 EXHLYEN DE EIV TARSON O BARNABAV ANAZHTHSAI SAULON
05L-ACTS-11-26 KAI EURWN HGAGEN AUTON EIV ANTIOCEIAN EGENETO DE AUTOUV ENIAUTON OLON SUNACYHNAI TH EKKLHSIA KAI DIDAXAI OCLON IKANON CRHMATISAI TE PRWTON EN ANTIOCEIA TOUV MAYHTAV CRISTIANOUV
05L-ACTS-11-27 EN TAUTAIV DE TAIV HMERAIV KATHLYON APO IEROSOLUMWN PROFHTAI EIV ANTIOCEIAN
05L-ACTS-11-28 ANASTAV DE EIV EX AUTWN ONOMATI AGABOV ESHMANEN DIA TOU PNEUMATOV LIMON MEGAN MELLEIN ESESYAI EF OLHN THN OIKOUMENHN OSTIV KAI EGENETO EPI KLAUDIOU KAISAROV
05L-ACTS-11-29 TWN DE MAYHTWN KAYWV EUPOREITO TIV WRISAN EKASTOV AUTWN EIV DIAKONIAN PEMQAI TOIV KATOIKOUSIN EN TH IOUDAIA ADELFOIV
05L-ACTS-11-30 O KAI EPOIHSAN APOSTEILANTEV PROV TOUV PRESBUTEROUV DIA CEIROV BARNABA KAI SAULOU
05L-ACTS-12-01 KAT EKEINON DE TON KAIRON EPEBALEN HRWDHV O BASILEUV TAV CEIRAV KAKWSAI TINAV TWN APO THV EKKLHSIAV
05L-ACTS-12-02 ANEILEN DE IAKWBON TON ADELFON IWANNOU MACAIRA
05L-ACTS-12-03 KAI IDWN OTI ARESTON ESTIN TOIV IOUDAIOIV PROSEYETO SULLABEIN KAI PETRON HSAN DE AI HMERAI TWN AZUMWN
05L-ACTS-12-04 ON KAI PIASAV EYETO EIV FULAKHN PARADOUV TESSARSIN TETRADIOIV STRATIWTWN FULASSEIN AUTON BOULOMENOV META TO PASCA ANAGAGEIN AUTON TW LAW
05L-ACTS-12-05 O MEN OUN PETROV ETHREITO EN TH FULAKH PROSEUCH DE HN EKTENHV GINOMENH UPO THV EKKLHSIAV PROV TON YEON UPER AUTOU
05L-ACTS-12-06 OTE DE EMELLEN AUTON PROAGEIN O HRWDHV TH NUKTI EKEINH HN O PETROV KOIMWMENOV METAXU DUO STRATIWTWN DEDEMENOV ALUSESIN DUSIN FULAKEV TE PRO THV YURAV ETHROUN THN FULAKHN
05L-ACTS-12-07 KAI IDOU AGGELOV KURIOU EPESTH KAI FWV ELAMQEN EN TW OIKHMATI PATAXAV DE THN PLEURAN TOU PETROU HGEIREN AUTON LEGWN ANASTA EN TACEI KAI EXEPESON AUTOU AI ALUSEIV EK TWN CEIRWN
05L-ACTS-12-08 EIPEN TE O AGGELOV PROV AUTON PERIZWSAI KAI UPODHSAI TA SANDALIA SOU EPOIHSEN DE OUTWV KAI LEGEI AUTW PERIBALOU TO IMATION SOU KAI AKOLOUYEI MOI
05L-ACTS-12-09 KAI EXELYWN HKOLOUYEI AUTW KAI OUK HDEI OTI ALHYEV ESTIN TO GINOMENON DIA TOU AGGELOU EDOKEI DE ORAMA BLEPEIN
05L-ACTS-12-10 DIELYONTEV DE PRWTHN FULAKHN KAI DEUTERAN HLYON EPI THN PULHN THN SIDHRAN THN FEROUSAN EIV THN POLIN HTIV AUTOMATH HNOICYH AUTOIV KAI EXELYONTEV PROHLYON RUMHN MIAN KAI EUYEWV APESTH O AGGELOV AP AUTOU
05L-ACTS-12-11 KAI O PETROV GENOMENOV EN EAUTW EIPEN NUN OIDA ALHYWV OTI EXAPESTEILEN KURIOV TON AGGELON AUTOU KAI EXEILETO ME EK CEIROV HRWDOU KAI PASHV THV PROSDOKIAV TOU LAOU TWN IOUDAIWN
05L-ACTS-12-12 SUNIDWN TE HLYEN EPI THN OIKIAN MARIAV THV MHTROV IWANNOU TOU EPIKALOUMENOU MARKOU OU HSAN IKANOI SUNHYROISMENOI KAI PROSEUCOMENOI
05L-ACTS-12-13 KROUSANTOV DE TOU PETROU THN YURAN TOU PULWNOV PROSHLYEN PAIDISKH UPAKOUSAI ONOMATI RODH
05L-ACTS-12-14 KAI EPIGNOUSA THN FWNHN TOU PETROU APO THV CARAV OUK HNOIXEN TON PULWNA EISDRAMOUSA DE APHGGEILEN ESTANAI TON PETRON PRO TOU PULWNOV
05L-ACTS-12-15 OI DE PROV AUTHN EIPON MAINH H DE DIISCURIZETO OUTWV ECEIN OI DE ELEGON O AGGELOV AUTOU ESTIN
05L-ACTS-12-16 O DE PETROV EPEMENEN KROUWN ANOIXANTEV DE EIDON AUTON KAI EXESTHSAN
05L-ACTS-12-17 KATASEISAV DE AUTOIV TH CEIRI SIGAN DIHGHSATO AUTOIV PWV O KURIOV AUTON EXHGAGEN EK THV FULAKHV EIPEN DE APAGGEILATE IAKWBW KAI TOIV ADELFOIV TAUTA KAI EXELYWN EPOREUYH EIV ETERON TOPON
05L-ACTS-12-18 GENOMENHV DE HMERAV HN TARACOV OUK OLIGOV EN TOIV STRATIWTAIV TI ARA O PETROV EGENETO
05L-ACTS-12-19 HRWDHV DE EPIZHTHSAV AUTON KAI MH EURWN ANAKRINAV TOUV FULAKAV EKELEUSEN APACYHNAI KAI KATELYWN APO THV IOUDAIAV EIV THN KAISAREIAN DIETRIBEN
05L-ACTS-12-20 HN DE O HRWDHV YUMOMACWN TURIOIV KAI SIDWNIOIV OMOYUMADON DE PARHSAN PROV AUTON KAI PEISANTEV BLASTON TON EPI TOU KOITWNOV TOU BASILEWV HTOUNTO EIRHNHN DIA TO TREFESYAI AUTWN THN CWRAN APO THV BASILIKHV
05L-ACTS-12-21 TAKTH DE HMERA O HRWDHV ENDUSAMENOV ESYHTA BASILIKHN KAI KAYISAV EPI TOU BHMATOV EDHMHGOREI PROV AUTOUV
05L-ACTS-12-22 O DE DHMOV EPEFWNEI FWNH YEOU KAI OUK ANYRWPOU
05L-ACTS-12-23 PARACRHMA DE EPATAXEN AUTON AGGELOV KURIOU ANY WN OUK EDWKEN DOXAN TW YEW KAI GENOMENOV SKWLHKOBRWTOV EXEQUXEN
05L-ACTS-12-24 O DE LOGOV TOU YEOU HUXANEN KAI EPLHYUNETO
05L-ACTS-12-25 BARNABAV DE KAI SAULOV UPESTREQAN EIV IEROUSALHM PLHRWSANTEV THN DIAKONIAN SUMPARALABONTEV KAI IWANNHN TON EPIKLHYENTA MARKON
05L-ACTS-13-01 HSAN DE TINEV EN ANTIOCEIA KATA THN OUSAN EKKLHSIAN PROFHTAI KAI DIDASKALOI O TE BARNABAV KAI SUMEWN O KALOUMENOV NIGER KAI LOUKIOV O KURHNAIOV MANAHN TE HRWDOU TOU TETRARCOU SUNTROFOV KAI SAULOV
05L-ACTS-13-02 LEITOURGOUNTWN DE AUTWN TW KURIW KAI NHSTEUONTWN EIPEN TO PNEUMA TO AGION AFORISATE DH MOI TON BARNABAN KAI TON SAULON EIV TO ERGON O PROSKEKLHMAI AUTOUV
05L-ACTS-13-03 TOTE NHSTEUSANTEV KAI PROSEUXAMENOI KAI EPIYENTEV TAV CEIRAV AUTOIV APELUSAN
05L-ACTS-13-04 OUTOI MEN OUN EKPEMFYENTEV UPO TOU PNEUMATOV TOU AGIOU KATHLYON EIV THN SELEUKEIAN EKEIYEN DE APEPLEUSAN EIV THN KUPRON
05L-ACTS-13-05 KAI GENOMENOI EN SALAMINI KATHGGELLON TON LOGON TOU YEOU EN TAIV SUNAGWGAIV TWN IOUDAIWN EICON DE KAI IWANNHN UPHRETHN
05L-ACTS-13-06 DIELYONTEV DE THN NHSON ACRI PAFOU EURON TINA MAGON QEUDOPROFHTHN IOUDAION W ONOMA BARIHSOUV
05L-ACTS-13-07 OV HN SUN TW ANYUPATW SERGIW PAULW ANDRI SUNETW OUTOV PROSKALESAMENOV BARNABAN KAI SAULON EPEZHTHSEN AKOUSAI TON LOGON TOU YEOU
05L-ACTS-13-08 ANYISTATO DE AUTOIV ELUMAV O MAGOV OUTWV GAR MEYERMHNEUETAI TO ONOMA AUTOU ZHTWN DIASTREQAI TON ANYUPATON APO THV PISTEWV
05L-ACTS-13-09 SAULOV DE O KAI PAULOV PLHSYEIV PNEUMATOV AGIOU KAI ATENISAV EIV AUTON
05L-ACTS-13-10 EIPEN W PLHRHV PANTOV DOLOU KAI PASHV RADIOURGIAV UIE DIABOLOU ECYRE PASHV DIKAIOSUNHV OU PAUSH DIASTREFWN TAV ODOUV KURIOU TAV EUYEIAV
05L-ACTS-13-11 KAI NUN IDOU CEIR KURIOU EPI SE KAI ESH TUFLOV MH BLEPWN TON HLION ACRI KAIROU PARACRHMA DE EPEPESEN EP AUTON ACLUV KAI SKOTOV KAI PERIAGWN EZHTEI CEIRAGWGOUV
05L-ACTS-13-12 TOTE IDWN O ANYUPATOV TO GEGONOV EPISTEUSEN EKPLHSSOMENOV EPI TH DIDACH TOU KURIOU
05L-ACTS-13-13 ANACYENTEV DE APO THV PAFOU OI PERI TON PAULON HLYON EIV PERGHN THV PAMFULIAV IWANNHV DE APOCWRHSAV AP AUTWN UPESTREQEN EIV IEROSOLUMA
05L-ACTS-13-14 AUTOI DE DIELYONTEV APO THV PERGHV PAREGENONTO EIV ANTIOCEIAN THV PISIDIAV KAI EISELYONTEV EIV THN SUNAGWGHN TH HMERA TWN SABBATWN EKAYISAN
05L-ACTS-13-15 META DE THN ANAGNWSIN TOU NOMOU KAI TWN PROFHTWN APESTEILAN OI ARCISUNAGWGOI PROV AUTOUV LEGONTEV ANDREV ADELFOI EI ESTIN LOGOV EN UMIN PARAKLHSEWV PROV TON LAON LEGETE
05L-ACTS-13-16 ANASTAV DE PAULOV KAI KATASEISAV TH CEIRI EIPEN ANDREV ISRAHLITAI KAI OI FOBOUMENOI TON YEON AKOUSATE
05L-ACTS-13-17 O YEOV TOU LAOU TOUTOU EXELEXATO TOUV PATERAV HMWN KAI TON LAON UQWSEN EN TH PAROIKIA EN GH AIGUPTW KAI META BRACIONOV UQHLOU EXHGAGEN AUTOUV EX AUTHV
05L-ACTS-13-18 KAI WV TESSARAKONTAETH CRONON ETROPOFORHSEN AUTOUV EN TH ERHMW
05L-ACTS-13-19 KAI KAYELWN EYNH EPTA EN GH CANAAN KATEKLHRONOMHSEN AUTOIV THN GHN AUTWN
05L-ACTS-13-20 KAI META TAUTA WV ETESIN TETRAKOSIOIV KAI PENTHKONTA EDWKEN KRITAV EWV SAMOUHL TOU PROFHTOU
05L-ACTS-13-21 KAKEIYEN HTHSANTO BASILEA KAI EDWKEN AUTOIV O YEOV TON SAOUL UION KIV ANDRA EK FULHV BENIAMIN ETH TESSARAKONTA
05L-ACTS-13-22 KAI METASTHSAV AUTON HGEIREN AUTOIV TON DAUID EIV BASILEA W KAI EIPEN MARTURHSAV EURON DAUID TON TOU IESSAI ANDRA KATA THN KARDIAN MOU OV POIHSEI PANTA TA YELHMATA MOU
05L-ACTS-13-23 TOUTOU O YEOV APO TOU SPERMATOV KAT EPAGGELIAN HGAGEN TW ISRAHL SWTHRIAN
05L-ACTS-13-24 PROKHRUXANTOV IWANNOU PRO PROSWPOU THV EISODOU AUTOU BAPTISMA METANOIAV TW ISRAHL
05L-ACTS-13-25 WV DE EPLHROU O IWANNHV TON DROMON ELEGEN TINA ME UPONOEITE EINAI OUK EIMI EGW ALL IDOU ERCETAI MET EME OU OUK EIMI AXIOV TO UPODHMA TWN PODWN LUSAI
05L-ACTS-13-26 ANDREV ADELFOI UIOI GENOUV ABRAAM KAI OI EN UMIN FOBOUMENOI TON YEON UMIN O LOGOV THV SWTHRIAV TAUTHV APESTALH

05L-ACTS-13-31 OV WFYH EPI HMERAV PLEIOUV TOIV SUNANABASIN AUTW APO THV GALILAIAV EIV IEROUSALHM OITINEV EISIN MARTUREV AUTOU PROV TON LAON
05L-ACTS-13-32 KAI HMEIV UMAV EUAGGELIZOMEYA THN PROV TOUV PATERAV EPAGGELIAN GENOMENHN OTI TAUTHN O YEOV EKPEPLHRWKEN TOIV TEKNOIV AUTWN HMIN ANASTHSAV IHSOUN
05L-ACTS-13-33 WV KAI EN TW QALMW TW DEUTERW GEGRAPTAI UIOV MOU EI SU EGW SHMERON GEGENNHKA SE

05L-ACTS-13-35 DIO KAI EN ETERW LEGEI OU DWSEIV TON OSION SOU IDEIN DIAFYORAN
05L-ACTS-13-36 DAUID MEN GAR IDIA GENEA UPHRETHSAV TH TOU YEOU BOULH EKOIMHYH KAI PROSETEYH PROV TOUV PATERAV AUTOU KAI EIDEN DIAFYORAN
05L-ACTS-13-37 ON DE O YEOV HGEIREN OUK EIDEN DIAFYORAN

05L-ACTS-13-41 IDETE OI KATAFRONHTAI KAI YAUMASATE KAI AFANISYHTE OTI ERGON EGW ERGAZOMAI EN TAIV HMERAIV UMWN O OU MH PISTEUSHTE EAN TIV EKDIHGHTAI UMIN

05L-ACTS-14-01 EGENETO DE EN IKONIW KATA TO AUTO EISELYEIN AUTOUV EIV THN SUNAGWGHN TWN IOUDAIWN KAI LALHSAI OUTWV WSTE PISTEUSAI IOUDAIWN TE KAI ELLHNWN POLU PLHYOV
05L-ACTS-14-02 OI DE APEIYOUNTEV IOUDAIOI EPHGEIRAN KAI EKAKWSAN TAV QUCAV TWN EYNWN KATA TWN ADELFWN
05L-ACTS-14-03 IKANON MEN OUN CRONON DIETRIQAN PARRHSIAZOMENOI EPI TW KURIW TW MARTUROUNTI TW LOGW THV CARITOV AUTOU DIDONTI SHMEIA KAI TERATA GINESYAI DIA TWN CEIRWN AUTWN
05L-ACTS-14-04 ESCISYH DE TO PLHYOV THV POLEWV KAI OI MEN HSAN SUN TOIV IOUDAIOIV OI DE SUN TOIV APOSTOLOIV

05L-ACTS-14-11 OI DE OCLOI IDONTEV O EPOIHSEN O PAULOV EPHRAN THN FWNHN AUTWN LUKAONISTI LEGONTEV OI YEOI OMOIWYENTEV ANYRWPOIV KATEBHSAN PROV HMAV

05L-ACTS-14-13 O DE IEREUV TOU DIOV TOU ONTOV PRO THV POLEWV AUTWN TAUROUV KAI STEMMATA EPI TOUV PULWNAV ENEGKAV SUN TOIV OCLOIV HYELEN YUEIN
05L-ACTS-14-14 AKOUSANTEV DE OI APOSTOLOI BARNABAV KAI PAULOV DIARRHXANTEV TA IMATIA AUTWN EISEPHDHSAN EIV TON OCLON KRAZONTEV

05L-ACTS-14-21 EUAGGELISAMENOI TE THN POLIN EKEINHN KAI MAYHTEUSANTEV IKANOUV UPESTREQAN EIV THN LUSTRAN KAI IKONION KAI ANTIOCEIAN

05L-ACTS-14-28 DIETRIBON DE EKEI CRONON OUK OLIGON SUN TOIV MAYHTAIV
05L-ACTS-15-01 KAI TINEV KATELYONTEV APO THV IOUDAIAV EDIDASKON TOUV ADELFOUV OTI EAN MH PERITEMNHSYE TW EYEI MWUSEWV OU DUNASYE SWYHNAI
05L-ACTS-15-02 GENOMENHV OUN STASEWV KAI ZHTHSEWV OUK OLIGHV TW PAULW KAI TW BARNABA PROV AUTOUV ETAXAN ANABAINEIN PAULON KAI BARNABAN KAI TINAV ALLOUV EX AUTWN PROV TOUV APOSTOLOUV KAI PRESBUTEROUV EIV IEROUSALHM PERI TOU ZHTHMATOV TOUTOU
05L-ACTS-15-03 OI MEN OUN PROPEMFYENTEV UPO THV EKKLHSIAV DIHRCONTO THN FOINIKHN KAI SAMAREIAN EKDIHGOUMENOI THN EPISTROFHN TWN EYNWN KAI EPOIOUN CARAN MEGALHN PASIN TOIV ADELFOIV
05L-ACTS-15-04 PARAGENOMENOI DE EIV IEROUSALHM APEDECYHSAN UPO THV EKKLHSIAV KAI TWN APOSTOLWN KAI TWN PRESBUTERWN ANHGGEILAN TE OSA O YEOV EPOIHSEN MET AUTWN
05L-ACTS-15-05 EXANESTHSAN DE TINEV TWN APO THV AIRESEWV TWN FARISAIWN PEPISTEUKOTEV LEGONTEV OTI DEI PERITEMNEIN AUTOUV PARAGGELLEIN TE THREIN TON NOMON MWUSEWV

05L-ACTS-15-07 POLLHV DE SUZHTHSEWV GENOMENHV ANASTAV PETROV EIPEN PROV AUTOUV ANDREV ADELFOI UMEIV EPISTASYE OTI AF HMERWN ARCAIWN O YEOV EN HMIN EXELEXATO DIA TOU STOMATOV MOU AKOUSAI TA EYNH TON LOGON TOU EUAGGELIOU KAI PISTEUSAI
05L-ACTS-15-08 KAI O KARDIOGNWSTHV YEOV EMARTURHSEN AUTOIV DOUV AUTOIV TO PNEUMA TO AGION KAYWV KAI HMIN
05L-ACTS-15-09 KAI OUDEN DIEKRINEN METAXU HMWN TE KAI AUTWN TH PISTEI KAYARISAV TAV KARDIAV AUTWN

05L-ACTS-15-21 MWUSHV GAR EK GENEWN ARCAIWN KATA POLIN TOUV KHRUSSONTAV AUTON ECEI EN TAIV SUNAGWGAIV KATA PAN SABBATON ANAGINWSKOMENOV
05L-ACTS-15-22 TOTE EDOXEN TOIV APOSTOLOIV KAI TOIV PRESBUTEROIV SUN OLH TH EKKLHSIA EKLEXAMENOUV ANDRAV EX AUTWN PEMQAI EIV ANTIOCEIAN SUN PAULW KAI BARNABA IOUDAN TON EPIKALOUMENON BARSABBAN KAI SILAN ANDRAV HGOUMENOUV EN TOIV ADELFOIV

05L-ACTS-15-24 EPEIDH HKOUSAMEN OTI TINEV EX HMWN EXELYONTEV ETARAXAN UMAV LOGOIV ANASKEUAZONTEV TAV QUCAV UMWN LEGONTEV PERITEMNESYAI KAI THREIN TON NOMON OIV OU DIESTEILAMEYA

05L-ACTS-16-01 KATHNTHSEN DE EIV DERBHN KAI LUSTRAN KAI IDOU MAYHTHV TIV HN EKEI ONOMATI TIMOYEOV UIOV GUNAIKOV TINOV IOUDAIAV PISTHV PATROV DE ELLHNOV
05L-ACTS-16-02 OV EMARTUREITO UPO TWN EN LUSTROIV KAI IKONIW ADELFWN
05L-ACTS-16-03 TOUTON HYELHSEN O PAULOV SUN AUTW EXELYEIN KAI LABWN PERIETEMEN AUTON DIA TOUV IOUDAIOUV TOUV ONTAV EN TOIV TOPOIV EKEINOIV HDEISAN GAR APANTEV TON PATERA AUTOU OTI ELLHN UPHRCEN
05L-ACTS-16-04 WV DE DIEPOREUONTO TAV POLEIV PAREDIDOUN AUTOIV FULASSEIN TA DOGMATA TA KEKRIMENA UPO TWN APOSTOLWN KAI TWN PRESBUTERWN TWN EN IEROUSALHM

05L-ACTS-16-08 PARELYONTEV DE THN MUSIAN KATEBHSAN EIV TRWADA
05L-ACTS-16-09 KAI ORAMA DIA THV NUKTOV WFYH TW PAULW ANHR TIV HN MAKEDWN ESTWV PARAKALWN AUTON KAI LEGWN DIABAV EIV MAKEDONIAN BOHYHSON HMIN
05L-ACTS-16-10 WV DE TO ORAMA EIDEN EUYEWV EZHTHSAMEN EXELYEIN EIV THN MAKEDONIAN SUMBIBAZONTEV OTI PROSKEKLHTAI HMAV O KURIOV EUAGGELISASYAI AUTOUV
05L-ACTS-16-11 ANACYENTEV OUN APO THV TRWADOV EUYUDROMHSAMEN EIV SAMOYRAKHN TH TE EPIOUSH EIV NEAPOLIN
05L-ACTS-16-12 EKEIYEN TE EIV FILIPPOUV HTIV ESTIN PRWTH THV MERIDOV THV MAKEDONIAV POLIV KOLWNEIA HMEN DE EN AUTH TH POLEI DIATRIBONTEV HMERAV TINAV
05L-ACTS-16-13 TH TE HMERA TWN SABBATWN EXHLYOMEN EXW THV POLEWV PARA POTAMON OU ENOMIZETO PROSEUCH EINAI KAI KAYISANTEV ELALOUMEN TAIV SUNELYOUSAIV GUNAIXIN
05L-ACTS-16-14 KAI TIV GUNH ONOMATI LUDIA PORFUROPWLIV POLEWV YUATEIRWN SEBOMENH TON YEON HKOUEN HV O KURIOV DIHNOIXEN THN KARDIAN PROSECEIN TOIV LALOUMENOIV UPO TOU PAULOU
05L-ACTS-16-15 WV DE EBAPTISYH KAI O OIKOV AUTHV PAREKALESEN LEGOUSA EI KEKRIKATE ME PISTHN TW KURIW EINAI EISELYONTEV EIV TON OIKON MOU MEINATE KAI PAREBIASATO HMAV
05L-ACTS-16-16 EGENETO DE POREUOMENWN HMWN EIV PROSEUCHN PAIDISKHN TINA ECOUSAN PNEUMA PUYWNOV APANTHSAI HMIN HTIV ERGASIAN POLLHN PAREICEN TOIV KURIOIV AUTHV MANTEUOMENH
05L-ACTS-16-17 AUTH KATAKOLOUYHSASA TW PAULW KAI HMIN EKRAZEN LEGOUSA OUTOI OI ANYRWPOI DOULOI TOU YEOU TOU UQISTOU EISIN OITINEV KATAGGELLOUSIN HMIN ODON SWTHRIAV
05L-ACTS-16-18 TOUTO DE EPOIEI EPI POLLAV HMERAV DIAPONHYEIV DE O PAULOV KAI EPISTREQAV TW PNEUMATI EIPEN PARAGGELLW SOI EN TW ONOMATI IHSOU CRISTOU EXELYEIN AP AUTHV KAI EXHLYEN AUTH TH WRA
05L-ACTS-16-19 IDONTEV DE OI KURIOI AUTHV OTI EXHLYEN H ELPIV THV ERGASIAV AUTWN EPILABOMENOI TON PAULON KAI TON SILAN EILKUSAN EIV THN AGORAN EPI TOUV ARCONTAV
05L-ACTS-16-20 KAI PROSAGAGONTEV AUTOUV TOIV STRATHGOIV EIPON OUTOI OI ANYRWPOI EKTARASSOUSIN HMWN THN POLIN IOUDAIOI UPARCONTEV
05L-ACTS-16-21 KAI KATAGGELLOUSIN EYH A OUK EXESTIN HMIN PARADECESYAI OUDE POIEIN RWMAIOIV OUSIN
05L-ACTS-16-22 KAI SUNEPESTH O OCLOV KAT AUTWN KAI OI STRATHGOI PERIRRHXANTEV AUTWN TA IMATIA EKELEUON RABDIZEIN
05L-ACTS-16-23 POLLAV TE EPIYENTEV AUTOIV PLHGAV EBALON EIV FULAKHN PARAGGEILANTEV TW DESMOFULAKI ASFALWV THREIN AUTOUV
05L-ACTS-16-24 OV PARAGGELIAN TOIAUTHN EILHFWV EBALEN AUTOUV EIV THN ESWTERAN FULAKHN KAI TOUV PODAV AUTWN HSFALISATO EIV TO XULON
05L-ACTS-16-25 KATA DE TO MESONUKTION PAULOV KAI SILAV PROSEUCOMENOI UMNOUN TON YEON EPHKROWNTO DE AUTWN OI DESMIOI
05L-ACTS-16-26 AFNW DE SEISMOV EGENETO MEGAV WSTE SALEUYHNAI TA YEMELIA TOU DESMWTHRIOU ANEWCYHSAN TE PARACRHMA AI YURAI PASAI KAI PANTWN TA DESMA ANEYH
05L-ACTS-16-27 EXUPNOV DE GENOMENOV O DESMOFULAX KAI IDWN ANEWGMENAV TAV YURAV THV FULAKHV SPASAMENOV MACAIRAN EMELLEN EAUTON ANAIREIN NOMIZWN EKPEFEUGENAI TOUV DESMIOUV
05L-ACTS-16-28 EFWNHSEN DE FWNH MEGALH O PAULOV LEGWN MHDEN PRAXHV SEAUTW KAKON APANTEV GAR ESMEN ENYADE
05L-ACTS-16-29 AITHSAV DE FWTA EISEPHDHSEN KAI ENTROMOV GENOMENOV PROSEPESEN TW PAULW KAI TW SILA
05L-ACTS-16-30 KAI PROAGAGWN AUTOUV EXW EFH KURIOI TI ME DEI POIEIN INA SWYW
05L-ACTS-16-31 OI DE EIPON PISTEUSON EPI TON KURION IHSOUN CRISTON KAI SWYHSH SU KAI O OIKOV SOU
05L-ACTS-16-32 KAI ELALHSAN AUTW TON LOGON TOU KURIOU KAI PASIN TOIV EN TH OIKIA AUTOU
05L-ACTS-16-33 KAI PARALABWN AUTOUV EN EKEINH TH WRA THV NUKTOV ELOUSEN APO TWN PLHGWN KAI EBAPTISYH AUTOV KAI OI AUTOU PANTEV PARACRHMA
05L-ACTS-16-34 ANAGAGWN TE AUTOUV EIV TON OIKON AUTOU PAREYHKEN TRAPEZAN KAI HGALLIATO PANOIKI PEPISTEUKWV TW YEW
05L-ACTS-16-35 HMERAV DE GENOMENHV APESTEILAN OI STRATHGOI TOUV RABDOUCOUV LEGONTEV APOLUSON TOUV ANYRWPOUV EKEINOUV
05L-ACTS-16-36 APHGGEILEN DE O DESMOFULAX TOUV LOGOUV TOUTOUV PROV TON PAULON OTI APESTALKASIN OI STRATHGOI INA APOLUYHTE NUN OUN EXELYONTEV POREUESYE EN EIRHNH
05L-ACTS-16-37 O DE PAULOV EFH PROV AUTOUV DEIRANTEV HMAV DHMOSIA AKATAKRITOUV ANYRWPOUV RWMAIOUV UPARCONTAV EBALON EIV FULAKHN KAI NUN LAYRA HMAV EKBALLOUSIN OU GAR ALLA ELYONTEV AUTOI EXAGAGETWSAN

05L-ACTS-16-40 EXELYONTEV DE EK THV FULAKHV EISHLYON PROV THN LUDIAN KAI IDONTEV TOUV ADELFOUV PAREKALESAN AUTOUV KAI EXHLYON
05L-ACTS-17-01 DIODEUSANTEV DE THN AMFIPOLIN KAI APOLLWNIAN HLYON EIV YESSALONIKHN OPOU HN H SUNAGWGH TWN IOUDAIWN
05L-ACTS-17-02 KATA DE TO EIWYOV TW PAULW EISHLYEN PROV AUTOUV KAI EPI SABBATA TRIA DIELEXATO AUTOIV APO TWN GRAFWN
05L-ACTS-17-03 DIANOIGWN KAI PARATIYEMENOV OTI TON CRISTON EDEI PAYEIN KAI ANASTHNAI EK NEKRWN KAI OTI OUTOV ESTIN O CRISTOV IHSOUV ON EGW KATAGGELLW UMIN
05L-ACTS-17-04 KAI TINEV EX AUTWN EPEISYHSAN KAI PROSEKLHRWYHSAN TW PAULW KAI TW SILA TWN TE SEBOMENWN ELLHNWN POLU PLHYOV GUNAIKWN TE TWN PRWTWN OUK OLIGAI
05L-ACTS-17-05 PROSLABOMENOI DE OI IOUDAIOI OI APEIYOUNTEV TWN AGORAIWN TINAV ANDRAV PONHROUV KAI OCLOPOIHSANTEV EYORUBOUN THN POLIN EPISTANTEV TE TH OIKIA IASONOV EZHTOUN AUTOUV AGAGEIN EIV TON DHMON
05L-ACTS-17-06 MH EURONTEV DE AUTOUV ESURON TON IASONA KAI TINAV ADELFOUV EPI TOUV POLITARCAV BOWNTEV OTI OI THN OIKOUMENHN ANASTATWSANTEV OUTOI KAI ENYADE PAREISIN
05L-ACTS-17-07 OUV UPODEDEKTAI IASWN KAI OUTOI PANTEV APENANTI TWN DOGMATWN KAISAROV PRASSOUSIN BASILEA LEGONTEV ETERON EINAI IHSOUN
05L-ACTS-17-08 ETARAXAN DE TON OCLON KAI TOUV POLITARCAV AKOUONTAV TAUTA
05L-ACTS-17-09 KAI LABONTEV TO IKANON PARA TOU IASONOV KAI TWN LOIPWN APELUSAN AUTOUV
05L-ACTS-17-10 OI DE ADELFOI EUYEWV DIA THV NUKTOV EXEPEMQAN TON TE PAULON KAI TON SILAN EIV BEROIAN OITINEV PARAGENOMENOI EIV THN SUNAGWGHN APHESAN TWN IOUDAIWN
05L-ACTS-17-11 OUTOI DE HSAN EUGENESTEROI TWN EN YESSALONIKH OITINEV EDEXANTO TON LOGON META PASHV PROYUMIAV TO KAY HMERAN ANAKRINONTEV TAV GRAFAV EI ECOI TAUTA OUTWV
05L-ACTS-17-12 POLLOI MEN OUN EX AUTWN EPISTEUSAN KAI TWN ELLHNIDWN GUNAIKWN TWN EUSCHMONWN KAI ANDRWN OUK OLIGOI
05L-ACTS-17-13 WV DE EGNWSAN OI APO THV YESSALONIKHV IOUDAIOI OTI KAI EN TH BEROIA KATHGGELH UPO TOU PAULOU O LOGOV TOU YEOU HLYON KAKEI SALEUONTEV TOUV OCLOUV
05L-ACTS-17-14 EUYEWV DE TOTE TON PAULON EXAPESTEILAN OI ADELFOI POREUESYAI WV EPI THN YALASSAN UPEMENON DE O TE SILAV KAI O TIMOYEOV EKEI
05L-ACTS-17-15 OI DE KAYISTWNTEV TON PAULON HGAGON AUTON EWV AYHNWN KAI LABONTEV ENTOLHN PROV TON SILAN KAI TIMOYEON INA WV TACISTA ELYWSIN PROV AUTON EXHESAN
05L-ACTS-17-16 EN DE TAIV AYHNAIV EKDECOMENOU AUTOUV TOU PAULOU PARWXUNETO TO PNEUMA AUTOU EN AUTW YEWROUNTI KATEIDWLON OUSAN THN POLIN
05L-ACTS-17-17 DIELEGETO MEN OUN EN TH SUNAGWGH TOIV IOUDAIOIV KAI TOIV SEBOMENOIV KAI EN TH AGORA KATA PASAN HMERAN PROV TOUV PARATUGCANONTAV
05L-ACTS-17-18 TINEV DE KAI TWN EPIKOUREIWN KAI TWN STOIKWN FILOSOFWN SUNEBALLON AUTW KAI TINEV ELEGON TI AN YELOI O SPERMOLOGOV OUTOV LEGEIN OI DE XENWN DAIMONIWN DOKEI KATAGGELEUV EINAI OTI TON IHSOUN KAI THN ANASTASIN EUHGGELIZETO
05L-ACTS-17-19 EPILABOMENOI TE AUTOU EPI TON AREION PAGON HGAGON LEGONTEV DUNAMEYA GNWNAI TIV H KAINH AUTH H UPO SOU LALOUMENH DIDACH
05L-ACTS-17-20 XENIZONTA GAR TINA EISFEREIV EIV TAV AKOAV HMWN BOULOMEYA OUN GNWNAI TI AN YELOI TAUTA EINAI
05L-ACTS-17-21 AYHNAIOI DE PANTEV KAI OI EPIDHMOUNTEV XENOI EIV OUDEN ETERON EUKAIROUN H LEGEIN TI KAI AKOUEIN KAINOTERON
05L-ACTS-17-22 STAYEIV DE O PAULOV EN MESW TOU AREIOU PAGOU EFH ANDREV AYHNAIOI KATA PANTA WV DEISIDAIMONESTEROUV UMAV YEWRW
05L-ACTS-17-23 DIERCOMENOV GAR KAI ANAYEWRWN TA SEBASMATA UMWN EURON KAI BWMON EN W EPEGEGRAPTO AGNWSTW YEW ON OUN AGNOOUNTEV EUSEBEITE TOUTON EGW KATAGGELLW UMIN
05L-ACTS-17-24 O YEOV O POIHSAV TON KOSMON KAI PANTA TA EN AUTW OUTOV OURANOU KAI GHV KURIOV UPARCWN OUK EN CEIROPOIHTOIV NAOIV KATOIKEI
05L-ACTS-17-25 OUDE UPO CEIRWN ANYRWPWN YERAPEUETAI PROSDEOMENOV TINOV AUTOV DIDOUV PASIN ZWHN KAI PNOHN KATA PANTA
05L-ACTS-17-26 EPOIHSEN TE EX ENOV AIMATOV PAN EYNOV ANYRWPWN KATOIKEIN EPI PAN TO PROSWPON THV GHV ORISAV PROSTETAGMENOUV KAIROUV KAI TAV OROYESIAV THV KATOIKIAV AUTWN
05L-ACTS-17-27 ZHTEIN TON KURION EI ARA GE QHLAFHSEIAN AUTON KAI EUROIEN KAI GE OU MAKRAN APO ENOV EKASTOU HMWN UPARCONTA

05L-ACTS-17-29 GENOV OUN UPARCONTEV TOU YEOU OUK OFEILOMEN NOMIZEIN CRUSW H ARGURW H LIYW CARAGMATI TECNHV KAI ENYUMHSEWV ANYRWPOU TO YEION EINAI OMOION
05L-ACTS-17-30 TOUV MEN OUN CRONOUV THV AGNOIAV UPERIDWN O YEOV TA NUN PARAGGELLEI TOIV ANYRWPOIV PASIN PANTACOU METANOEIN
05L-ACTS-17-31 DIOTI ESTHSEN HMERAN EN H MELLEI KRINEIN THN OIKOUMENHN EN DIKAIOSUNH EN ANDRI W WRISEN PISTIN PARASCWN PASIN ANASTHSAV AUTON EK NEKRWN
05L-ACTS-17-32 AKOUSANTEV DE ANASTASIN NEKRWN OI MEN ECLEUAZON OI DE EIPON AKOUSOMEYA SOU PALIN PERI TOUTOU

05L-ACTS-18-01 META DE TAUTA CWRISYEIV O PAULOV EK TWN AYHNWN HLYEN EIV KORINYON
05L-ACTS-18-02 KAI EURWN TINA IOUDAION ONOMATI AKULAN PONTIKON TW GENEI PROSFATWV ELHLUYOTA APO THV ITALIAV KAI PRISKILLAN GUNAIKA AUTOU DIA TO TETACENAI KLAUDION CWRIZESYAI PANTAV TOUV IOUDAIOUV EK THV RWMHV PROSHLYEN AUTOIV

05L-ACTS-18-05 WV DE KATHLYON APO THV MAKEDONIAV O TE SILAV KAI O TIMOYEOV SUNEICETO TW PNEUMATI O PAULOV DIAMARTUROMENOV TOIV IOUDAIOIV TON CRISTON IHSOUN
05L-ACTS-18-06 ANTITASSOMENWN DE AUTWN KAI BLASFHMOUNTWN EKTINAXAMENOV TA IMATIA EIPEN PROV AUTOUV TO AIMA UMWN EPI THN KEFALHN UMWN KAYAROV EGW APO TOU NUN EIV TA EYNH POREUSOMAI
05L-ACTS-18-07 KAI METABAV EKEIYEN HLYEN EIV OIKIAN TINOV ONOMATI IOUSTOU SEBOMENOU TON YEON OU H OIKIA HN SUNOMOROUSA TH SUNAGWGH

05L-ACTS-18-16 KAI APHLASEN AUTOUV APO TOU BHMATOV

05L-ACTS-18-25 OUTOV HN KATHCHMENOV THN ODON TOU KURIOU KAI ZEWN TW PNEUMATI ELALEI KAI EDIDASKEN AKRIBWV TA PERI TOU KURIOU EPISTAMENOV MONON TO BAPTISMA IWANNOU

05L-ACTS-19-10 TOUTO DE EGENETO EPI ETH DUO WSTE PANTAV TOUV KATOIKOUNTAV THN ASIAN AKOUSAI TON LOGON TOU KURIOU IHSOU IOUDAIOUV TE KAI ELLHNAV
05L-ACTS-19-11 DUNAMEIV TE OU TAV TUCOUSAV EPOIEI O YEOV DIA TWN CEIRWN PAULOU
05L-ACTS-19-12 WSTE KAI EPI TOUV ASYENOUNTAV EPIFERESYAI APO TOU CRWTOV AUTOU SOUDARIA H SIMIKINYIA KAI APALLASSESYAI AP AUTWN TAV NOSOUV TA TE PNEUMATA TA PONHRA EXERCESYAI AP AUTWN
05L-ACTS-19-13 EPECEIRHSAN DE TINEV APO TWN PERIERCOMENWN IOUDAIWN EXORKISTWN ONOMAZEIN EPI TOUV ECONTAV TA PNEUMATA TA PONHRA TO ONOMA TOU KURIOU IHSOU LEGONTEV ORKIZOMEN UMAV TON IHSOUN ON O PAULOV KHRUSSEI

05L-ACTS-19-41 KAI TAUTA EIPWN APELUSEN THN EKKLHSIAN
05L-ACTS-20-01 META DE TO PAUSASYAI TON YORUBON PROSKALESAMENOV O PAULOV TOUV MAYHTAV KAI ASPASAMENOV EXHLYEN POREUYHNAI EIV THN MAKEDONIAN
05L-ACTS-20-02 DIELYWN DE TA MERH EKEINA KAI PARAKALESAV AUTOUV LOGW POLLW HLYEN EIV THN ELLADA
05L-ACTS-20-03 POIHSAV TE MHNAV TREIV GENOMENHV AUTW EPIBOULHV UPO TWN IOUDAIWN MELLONTI ANAGESYAI EIV THN SURIAN EGENETO GNWMH TOU UPOSTREFEIN DIA MAKEDONIAV
05L-ACTS-20-04 SUNEIPETO DE AUTW ACRI THV ASIAV SWPATROV BEROIAIOV YESSALONIKEWN DE ARISTARCOV KAI SEKOUNDOV KAI GAIOV DERBAIOV KAI TIMOYEOV ASIANOI DE TUCIKOV KAI TROFIMOV
05L-ACTS-20-05 OUTOI PROSELYONTEV EMENON HMAV EN TRWADI
05L-ACTS-20-06 HMEIV DE EXEPLEUSAMEN META TAV HMERAV TWN AZUMWN APO FILIPPWN KAI HLYOMEN PROV AUTOUV EIV THN TRWADA ACRI HMERWN PENTE OU DIETRIQAMEN HMERAV EPTA
05L-ACTS-20-07 EN DE TH MIA TWN SABBATWN SUNHGMENWN TWN MAYHTWN KLASAI ARTON O PAULOV DIELEGETO AUTOIV MELLWN EXIENAI TH EPAURION PARETEINEN TE TON LOGON MECRI MESONUKTIOU
05L-ACTS-20-08 HSAN DE LAMPADEV IKANAI EN TW UPERWW OU HMEN SUNHGMENOI
05L-ACTS-20-09 KAYHMENOV DE TIV NEANIAV ONOMATI EUTUCOV EPI THV YURIDOV KATAFEROMENOV UPNW BAYEI DIALEGOMENOU TOU PAULOU EPI PLEION KATENECYEIV APO TOU UPNOU EPESEN APO TOU TRISTEGOU KATW KAI HRYH NEKROV

05L-ACTS-20-14 WV DE SUNEBALEN HMIN EIV THN ASSON ANALABONTEV AUTON HLYOMEN EIV MITULHNHN
05L-ACTS-20-15 KAKEIYEN APOPLEUSANTEV TH EPIOUSH KATHNTHSAMEN ANTIKRU CIOU TH DE ETERA PAREBALOMEN EIV SAMON KAI MEINANTEV EN TRWGULLIW TH ECOMENH HLYOMEN EIV MILHTON
05L-ACTS-20-16 EKRINEN GAR O PAULOV PARAPLEUSAI THN EFESON OPWV MH GENHTAI AUTW CRONOTRIBHSAI EN TH ASIA ESPEUDEN GAR EI DUNATON HN AUTW THN HMERAN THV PENTHKOSTHV GENESYAI EIV IEROSOLUMA
05L-ACTS-20-17 APO DE THV MILHTOU PEMQAV EIV EFESON METEKALESATO TOUV PRESBUTEROUV THV EKKLHSIAV
05L-ACTS-20-18 WV DE PAREGENONTO PROV AUTON EIPEN AUTOIV UMEIV EPISTASYE APO PRWTHV HMERAV AF HV EPEBHN EIV THN ASIAN PWV MEY UMWN TON PANTA CRONON EGENOMHN
05L-ACTS-20-19 DOULEUWN TW KURIW META PASHV TAPEINOFROSUNHV KAI POLLWN DAKRUWN KAI PEIRASMWN TWN SUMBANTWN MOI EN TAIV EPIBOULAIV TWN IOUDAIWN
05L-ACTS-20-20 WV OUDEN UPESTEILAMHN TWN SUMFERONTWN TOU MH ANAGGEILAI UMIN KAI DIDAXAI UMAV DHMOSIA KAI KAT OIKOUV

05L-ACTS-20-22 KAI NUN IDOU EGW DEDEMENOV TW PNEUMATI POREUOMAI EIV IEROUSALHM TA EN AUTH SUNANTHSONTA MOI MH EIDWV
05L-ACTS-20-23 PLHN OTI TO PNEUMA TO AGION KATA POLIN DIAMARTURETAI LEGON OTI DESMA ME KAI YLIQEIV MENOUSIN
05L-ACTS-20-24 ALL OUDENOV LOGON POIOUMAI OUDE ECW THN QUCHN MOU TIMIAN EMAUTW WV TELEIWSAI TON DROMON MOU META CARAV KAI THN DIAKONIAN HN ELABON PARA TOU KURIOU IHSOU DIAMARTURASYAI TO EUAGGELION THV CARITOV TOU YEOU
05L-ACTS-20-25 KAI NUN IDOU EGW OIDA OTI OUKETI OQESYE TO PROSWPON MOU UMEIV PANTEV EN OIV DIHLYON KHRUSSWN THN BASILEIAN TOU YEOU
05L-ACTS-20-26 DIOTI MARTUROMAI UMIN EN TH SHMERON HMERA OTI KAYAROV EGW APO TOU AIMATOV PANTWN
05L-ACTS-20-27 OU GAR UPESTEILAMHN TOU MH ANAGGEILAI UMIN PASAN THN BOULHN TOU YEOU
05L-ACTS-20-28 PROSECETE OUN EAUTOIV KAI PANTI TW POIMNIW EN W UMAV TO PNEUMA TO AGION EYETO EPISKOPOUV POIMAINEIN THN EKKLHSIAN TOU KURIOU KAI YEOU HN PERIEPOIHSATO DIA TOU IDIOU AIMATOV
05L-ACTS-20-29 EGW GAR OIDA TOUTO OTI EISELEUSONTAI META THN AFIXIN MOU LUKOI BAREIV EIV UMAV MH FEIDOMENOI TOU POIMNIOU
05L-ACTS-20-30 KAI EX UMWN AUTWN ANASTHSONTAI ANDREV LALOUNTEV DIESTRAMMENA TOU APOSPAN TOUV MAYHTAV OPISW AUTWN

05L-ACTS-20-33 ARGURIOU H CRUSIOU H IMATISMOU OUDENOV EPEYUMHSA

05L-ACTS-21-01 WV DE EGENETO ANACYHNAI HMAV APOSPASYENTAV AP AUTWN EUYUDROMHSANTEV HLYOMEN EIV THN KWN TH DE EXHV EIV THN RODON KAKEIYEN EIV PATARA
05L-ACTS-21-02 KAI EURONTEV PLOION DIAPERWN EIV FOINIKHN EPIBANTEV ANHCYHMEN
05L-ACTS-21-03 ANAFANENTEV DE THN KUPRON KAI KATALIPONTEV AUTHN EUWNUMON EPLEOMEN EIV SURIAN KAI KATHCYHMEN EIV TURON EKEISE GAR HN TO PLOION APOFORTIZOMENON TON GOMON
05L-ACTS-21-04 KAI ANEURONTEV MAYHTAV EPEMEINAMEN AUTOU HMERAV EPTA OITINEV TW PAULW ELEGON DIA TOU PNEUMATOV MH ANABAINEIN EIV IEROUSALHM
05L-ACTS-21-05 OTE DE EGENETO HMAV EXARTISAI TAV HMERAV EXELYONTEV EPOREUOMEYA PROPEMPONTWN HMAV PANTWN SUN GUNAIXIN KAI TEKNOIV EWV EXW THV POLEWV KAI YENTEV TA GONATA EPI TON AIGIALON PROSHUXAMEYA

05L-ACTS-21-08 TH DE EPAURION EXELYONTEV OI PERI TON PAULON HLYON EIV KAISAREIAN KAI EISELYONTEV EIV TON OIKON FILIPPOU TOU EUAGGELISTOU ONTOV EK TWN EPTA EMEINAMEN PAR AUTW
05L-ACTS-21-09 TOUTW DE HSAN YUGATEREV PARYENOI TESSAREV PROFHTEUOUSAI

05L-ACTS-21-11 KAI ELYWN PROV HMAV KAI ARAV THN ZWNHN TOU PAULOU DHSAV TE AUTOU TOUV PODAV KAI TAV CEIRAV EIPEN TADE LEGEI TO PNEUMA TO AGION TON ANDRA OU ESTIN H ZWNH AUTH OUTWV DHSOUSIN EN IEROUSALHM OI IOUDAIOI KAI PARADWSOUSIN EIV CEIRAV EYNWN
05L-ACTS-21-12 WV DE HKOUSAMEN TAUTA PAREKALOUMEN HMEIV TE KAI OI ENTOPIOI TOU MH ANABAINEIN AUTON EIV IEROUSALHM

05L-ACTS-21-14 MH PEIYOMENOU DE AUTOU HSUCASAMEN EIPONTEV TO YELHMA TOU KURIOU GENESYW

05L-ACTS-21-17 GENOMENWN DE HMWN EIV IEROSOLUMA ASMENWV EDEXANTO HMAV OI ADELFOI

05L-ACTS-21-21 KATHCHYHSAN DE PERI SOU OTI APOSTASIAN DIDASKEIV APO MWUSEWV TOUV KATA TA EYNH PANTAV IOUDAIOUV LEGWN MH PERITEMNEIN AUTOUV TA TEKNA MHDE TOIV EYESIN PERIPATEIN

05L-ACTS-21-25 PERI DE TWN PEPISTEUKOTWN EYNWN HMEIV EPESTEILAMEN KRINANTEV MHDEN TOIOUTON THREIN AUTOUV EI MH FULASSESYAI AUTOUV TO TE EIDWLOYUTON KAI TO AIMA KAI PNIKTON KAI PORNEIAN
05L-ACTS-21-26 TOTE O PAULOV PARALABWN TOUV ANDRAV TH ECOMENH HMERA SUN AUTOIV AGNISYEIV EISHEI EIV TO IERON DIAGGELLWN THN EKPLHRWSIN TWN HMERWN TOU AGNISMOU EWV OU PROSHNECYH UPER ENOV EKASTOU AUTWN H PROSFORA
05L-ACTS-21-27 WV DE EMELLON AI EPTA HMERAI SUNTELEISYAI OI APO THV ASIAV IOUDAIOI YEASAMENOI AUTON EN TW IERW SUNECEON PANTA TON OCLON KAI EPEBALON TAV CEIRAV EP AUTON
05L-ACTS-21-28 KRAZONTEV ANDREV ISRAHLITAI BOHYEITE OUTOV ESTIN O ANYRWPOV O KATA TOU LAOU KAI TOU NOMOU KAI TOU TOPOU TOUTOU PANTAV PANTACOU DIDASKWN ETI TE KAI ELLHNAV EISHGAGEN EIV TO IERON KAI KEKOINWKEN TON AGION TOPON TOUTON

05L-ACTS-21-34 ALLOI DE ALLO TI EBOWN EN TW OCLW MH DUNAMENOV DE GNWNAI TO ASFALEV DIA TON YORUBON EKELEUSEN AGESYAI AUTON EIV THN PAREMBOLHN

05L-ACTS-21-39 EIPEN DE O PAULOV EGW ANYRWPOV MEN EIMI IOUDAIOV TARSEUV THV KILIKIAV OUK ASHMOU POLEWV POLITHV DEOMAI DE SOU EPITREQON MOI LALHSAI PROV TON LAON

05L-ACTS-22-01 ANDREV ADELFOI KAI PATEREV AKOUSATE MOU THV PROV UMAV NUNI APOLOGIAV

05L-ACTS-22-30 TH DE EPAURION BOULOMENOV GNWNAI TO ASFALEV TO TI KATHGOREITAI PARA TWN IOUDAIWN ELUSEN AUTON APO TWN DESMWN KAI EKELEUSEN ELYEIN TOUV ARCIEREIV KAI OLON TO SUNEDRION AUTWN KAI KATAGAGWN TON PAULON ESTHSEN EIV AUTOUV
05L-ACTS-23-01 ATENISAV DE O PAULOV TW SUNEDRIW EIPEN ANDREV ADELFOI EGW PASH SUNEIDHSEI AGAYH PEPOLITEUMAI TW YEW ACRI TAUTHV THV HMERAV
05L-ACTS-23-02 O DE ARCIEREUV ANANIAV EPETAXEN TOIV PARESTWSIN AUTW TUPTEIN AUTOU TO STOMA
05L-ACTS-23-03 TOTE O PAULOV PROV AUTON EIPEN TUPTEIN SE MELLEI O YEOV TOICE KEKONIAMENE KAI SU KAYH KRINWN ME KATA TON NOMON KAI PARANOMWN KELEUEIV ME TUPTESYAI
05L-ACTS-23-04 OI DE PARESTWTEV EIPON TON ARCIEREA TOU YEOU LOIDOREIV
05L-ACTS-23-05 EFH TE O PAULOV OUK HDEIN ADELFOI OTI ESTIN ARCIEREUV GEGRAPTAI GAR ARCONTA TOU LAOU SOU OUK EREIV KAKWV
05L-ACTS-23-06 GNOUV DE O PAULOV OTI TO EN MEROV ESTIN SADDOUKAIWN TO DE ETERON FARISAIWN EKRAXEN EN TW SUNEDRIW ANDREV ADELFOI EGW FARISAIOV EIMI UIOV FARISAIOU PERI ELPIDOV KAI ANASTASEWV NEKRWN EGW KRINOMAI

05L-ACTS-23-09 EGENETO DE KRAUGH MEGALH KAI ANASTANTEV OI GRAMMATEIV TOU MEROUV TWN FARISAIWN DIEMACONTO LEGONTEV OUDEN KAKON EURISKOMEN EN TW ANYRWPW TOUTW EI DE PNEUMA ELALHSEN AUTW H AGGELOV MH YEOMACWMEN
05L-ACTS-23-10 POLLHV DE GENOMENHV STASEWV EULABHYEIV O CILIARCOV MH DIASPASYH O PAULOV UP AUTWN EKELEUSEN TO STRATEUMA KATABHNAI KAI ARPASAI AUTON EK MESOU AUTWN AGEIN TE EIV THN PAREMBOLHN
05L-ACTS-23-11 TH DE EPIOUSH NUKTI EPISTAV AUTW O KURIOV EIPEN YARSEI PAULE WV GAR DIEMARTURW TA PERI EMOU EIV IEROUSALHM OUTWV SE DEI KAI EIV RWMHN MARTURHSAI
05L-ACTS-23-12 GENOMENHV DE HMERAV POIHSANTEV TINEV TWN IOUDAIWN SUSTROFHN ANEYEMATISAN EAUTOUV LEGONTEV MHTE FAGEIN MHTE PIEIN EWV OU APOKTEINWSIN TON PAULON
05L-ACTS-23-13 HSAN DE PLEIOUV TESSARAKONTA OI TAUTHN THN SUNWMOSIAN PEPOIHKOTEV
05L-ACTS-23-14 OITINEV PROSELYONTEV TOIV ARCIEREUSIN KAI TOIV PRESBUTEROIV EIPON ANAYEMATI ANEYEMATISAMEN EAUTOUV MHDENOV GEUSASYAI EWV OU APOKTEINWMEN TON PAULON
05L-ACTS-23-15 NUN OUN UMEIV EMFANISATE TW CILIARCW SUN TW SUNEDRIW OPWV AURION AUTON KATAGAGH PROV UMAV WV MELLONTAV DIAGINWSKEIN AKRIBESTERON TA PERI AUTOU HMEIV DE PRO TOU EGGISAI AUTON ETOIMOI ESMEN TOU ANELEIN AUTON
05L-ACTS-23-16 AKOUSAV DE O UIOV THV ADELFHV PAULOU TO ENEDRON PARAGENOMENOV KAI EISELYWN EIV THN PAREMBOLHN APHGGEILEN TW PAULW
05L-ACTS-23-17 PROSKALESAMENOV DE O PAULOV ENA TWN EKATONTARCWN EFH TON NEANIAN TOUTON APAGAGE PROV TON CILIARCON ECEI GAR TI APAGGEILAI AUTW
05L-ACTS-23-18 O MEN OUN PARALABWN AUTON HGAGEN PROV TON CILIARCON KAI FHSIN O DESMIOV PAULOV PROSKALESAMENOV ME HRWTHSEN TOUTON TON NEANIAN AGAGEIN PROV SE ECONTA TI LALHSAI SOI
05L-ACTS-23-19 EPILABOMENOV DE THV CEIROV AUTOU O CILIARCOV KAI ANACWRHSAV KAT IDIAN EPUNYANETO TI ESTIN O ECEIV APAGGEILAI MOI
05L-ACTS-23-20 EIPEN DE OTI OI IOUDAIOI SUNEYENTO TOU ERWTHSAI SE OPWV AURION EIV TO SUNEDRION KATAGAGHV TON PAULON WV MELLONTA TI AKRIBESTERON PUNYANESYAI PERI AUTOU
05L-ACTS-23-21 SU OUN MH PEISYHV AUTOIV ENEDREUOUSIN GAR AUTON EX AUTWN ANDREV PLEIOUV TESSARAKONTA OITINEV ANEYEMATISAN EAUTOUV MHTE FAGEIN MHTE PIEIN EWV OU ANELWSIN AUTON KAI NUN ETOIMOI EISIN PROSDECOMENOI THN APO SOU EPAGGELIAN
05L-ACTS-23-22 O MEN OUN CILIARCOV APELUSEN TON NEANIAN PARAGGEILAV MHDENI EKLALHSAI OTI TAUTA ENEFANISAV PROV ME
05L-ACTS-23-23 KAI PROSKALESAMENOV DUO TINAV TWN EKATONTARCWN EIPEN ETOIMASATE STRATIWTAV DIAKOSIOUV OPWV POREUYWSIN EWV KAISAREIAV KAI IPPEIV EBDOMHKONTA KAI DEXIOLABOUV DIAKOSIOUV APO TRITHV WRAV THV NUKTOV
05L-ACTS-23-24 KTHNH TE PARASTHSAI INA EPIBIBASANTEV TON PAULON DIASWSWSIN PROV FHLIKA TON HGEMONA
05L-ACTS-23-25 GRAQAV EPISTOLHN PERIECOUSAN TON TUPON TOUTON
05L-ACTS-23-26 KLAUDIOV LUSIAV TW KRATISTW HGEMONI FHLIKI CAIREIN
05L-ACTS-23-27 TON ANDRA TOUTON SULLHFYENTA UPO TWN IOUDAIWN KAI MELLONTA ANAIREISYAI UP AUTWN EPISTAV SUN TW STRATEUMATI EXEILOMHN AUTON MAYWN OTI RWMAIOV ESTIN
05L-ACTS-23-28 BOULOMENOV DE GNWNAI THN AITIAN DI HN ENEKALOUN AUTW KATHGAGON AUTON EIV TO SUNEDRION AUTWN
05L-ACTS-23-29 ON EURON EGKALOUMENON PERI ZHTHMATWN TOU NOMOU AUTWN MHDEN AXION YANATOU H DESMWN EGKLHMA ECONTA
05L-ACTS-23-30 MHNUYEISHV DE MOI EPIBOULHV EIV TON ANDRA MELLEIN ESESYAI UPO TWN IOUDAIWN EXAUTHV EPEMQA PROV SE PARAGGEILAV KAI TOIV KATHGOROIV LEGEIN TA PROV AUTON EPI SOU ERRWSO
05L-ACTS-23-31 OI MEN OUN STRATIWTAI KATA TO DIATETAGMENON AUTOIV ANALABONTEV TON PAULON HGAGON DIA THV NUKTOV EIV THN ANTIPATRIDA
05L-ACTS-23-32 TH DE EPAURION EASANTEV TOUV IPPEIV POREUESYAI SUN AUTW UPESTREQAN EIV THN PAREMBOLHN
05L-ACTS-23-33 OITINEV EISELYONTEV EIV THN KAISAREIAN KAI ANADONTEV THN EPISTOLHN TW HGEMONI PARESTHSAN KAI TON PAULON AUTW
05L-ACTS-23-34 ANAGNOUV DE O HGEMWN KAI EPERWTHSAV EK POIAV EPARCIAV ESTIN KAI PUYOMENOV OTI APO KILIKIAV
05L-ACTS-23-35 DIAKOUSOMAI SOU EFH OTAN KAI OI KATHGOROI SOU PARAGENWNTAI EKELEUSEN TE AUTON EN TW PRAITWRIW HRWDOU FULASSESYAI
05L-ACTS-24-01 META DE PENTE HMERAV KATEBH O ARCIEREUV ANANIAV META TWN PRESBUTERWN KAI RHTOROV TERTULLOU TINOV OITINEV ENEFANISAN TW HGEMONI KATA TOU PAULOU
05L-ACTS-24-02 KLHYENTOV DE AUTOU HRXATO KATHGOREIN O TERTULLOV LEGWN POLLHV EIRHNHV TUGCANONTEV DIA SOU KAI KATORYWMATWN GINOMENWN TW EYNEI TOUTW DIA THV SHV PRONOIAV
05L-ACTS-24-03 PANTH TE KAI PANTACOU APODECOMEYA KRATISTE FHLIX META PASHV EUCARISTIAV
05L-ACTS-24-04 INA DE MH EPI PLEION SE EGKOPTW PARAKALW AKOUSAI SE HMWN SUNTOMWV TH SH EPIEIKEIA
05L-ACTS-24-05 EURONTEV GAR TON ANDRA TOUTON LOIMON KAI KINOUNTA STASIN PASIN TOIV IOUDAIOIV TOIV KATA THN OIKOUMENHN PRWTOSTATHN TE THV TWN NAZWRAIWN AIRESEWV
05L-ACTS-24-06 OV KAI TO IERON EPEIRASEN BEBHLWSAI ON KAI EKRATHSAMEN
05L-ACTS-24-07
05L-ACTS-24-08 PAR OU DUNHSH AUTOV ANAKRINAV PERI PANTWN TOUTWN EPIGNWNAI WN HMEIV KATHGOROUMEN AUTOU
05L-ACTS-24-09 SUNEPEYENTO DE KAI OI IOUDAIOI FASKONTEV TAUTA OUTWV ECEIN
05L-ACTS-24-10 APEKRIYH DE O PAULOV NEUSANTOV AUTW TOU HGEMONOV LEGEIN EK POLLWN ETWN ONTA SE KRITHN TW EYNEI TOUTW EPISTAMENOV EUYUMOTERON TA PERI EMAUTOU APOLOGOUMAI
05L-ACTS-24-11 DUNAMENOU SOU GNWNAI OTI OU PLEIOUV EISIN MOI HMERAI DEKADUO AF HV ANEBHN PROSKUNHSWN EN IEROUSALHM

05L-ACTS-24-13 OUTE PARASTHSAI ME DUNANTAI PERI WN NUN KATHGOROUSIN MOU
05L-ACTS-24-14 OMOLOGW DE TOUTO SOI OTI KATA THN ODON HN LEGOUSIN AIRESIN OUTWV LATREUW TW PATRWW YEW PISTEUWN PASIN TOIV KATA TON NOMON KAI TOIV PROFHTAIV GEGRAMMENOIV
05L-ACTS-24-15 ELPIDA ECWN EIV TON YEON HN KAI AUTOI OUTOI PROSDECONTAI ANASTASIN MELLEIN ESESYAI NEKRWN DIKAIWN TE KAI ADIKWN

05L-ACTS-24-17 DI ETWN DE PLEIONWN PAREGENOMHN ELEHMOSUNAV POIHSWN EIV TO EYNOV MOU KAI PROSFORAV
05L-ACTS-24-18 EN OIV EURON ME HGNISMENON EN TW IERW OU META OCLOU OUDE META YORUBOU TINEV APO THV ASIAV IOUDAIOI
05L-ACTS-24-19 OUV DEI EPI SOU PAREINAI KAI KATHGOREIN EI TI ECOIEN PROV ME
05L-ACTS-24-20 H AUTOI OUTOI EIPATWSAN TI EURON EN EMOI ADIKHMA STANTOV MOU EPI TOU SUNEDRIOU
05L-ACTS-24-21 H PERI MIAV TAUTHV FWNHV HV EKRAXA ESTWV EN AUTOIV OTI PERI ANASTASEWV NEKRWN EGW KRINOMAI SHMERON UF UMWN
05L-ACTS-24-22 AKOUSAV DE TAUTA O FHLIX ANEBALETO AUTOUV AKRIBESTERON EIDWV TA PERI THV ODOU EIPWN OTAN LUSIAV O CILIARCOV KATABH DIAGNWSOMAI TA KAY UMAV
05L-ACTS-24-23 DIATAXAMENOV TE TW EKATONTARCH THREISYAI TON PAULON ECEIN TE ANESIN KAI MHDENA KWLUEIN TWN IDIWN AUTOU UPHRETEIN H PROSERCESYAI AUTW
05L-ACTS-24-24 META DE HMERAV TINAV PARAGENOMENOV O FHLIX SUN DROUSILLH TH GUNAIKI OUSH IOUDAIA METEPEMQATO TON PAULON KAI HKOUSEN AUTOU PERI THV EIV CRISTON PISTEWV
05L-ACTS-24-25 DIALEGOMENOU DE AUTOU PERI DIKAIOSUNHV KAI EGKRATEIAV KAI TOU KRIMATOV TOU MELLONTOV ESESYAI EMFOBOV GENOMENOV O FHLIX APEKRIYH TO NUN ECON POREUOU KAIRON DE METALABWN METAKALESOMAI SE
05L-ACTS-24-26 AMA KAI ELPIZWN OTI CRHMATA DOYHSETAI AUTW UPO TOU PAULOU OPWV LUSH AUTON DIO KAI PUKNOTERON AUTON METAPEMPOMENOV WMILEI AUTW
05L-ACTS-24-27 DIETIAV DE PLHRWYEISHV ELABEN DIADOCON O FHLIX PORKION FHSTON YELWN TE CARITAV KATAYESYAI TOIV IOUDAIOIV O FHLIX KATELIPEN TON PAULON DEDEMENON
05L-ACTS-25-01 FHSTOV OUN EPIBAV TH EPARCIA META TREIV HMERAV ANEBH EIV IEROSOLUMA APO KAISAREIAV
05L-ACTS-25-02 ENEFANISAN DE AUTW O ARCIEREUV KAI OI PRWTOI TWN IOUDAIWN KATA TOU PAULOU KAI PAREKALOUN AUTON

05L-ACTS-25-04 O MEN OUN FHSTOV APEKRIYH THREISYAI TON PAULON EN KAISAREIA EAUTON DE MELLEIN EN TACEI EKPOREUESYAI
05L-ACTS-25-05 OI OUN DUNATOI EN UMIN FHSIN SUGKATABANTEV EI TI ESTIN EN TW ANDRI TOUTW KATHGOREITWSAN AUTOU
05L-ACTS-25-06 DIATRIQAV DE EN AUTOIV HMERAV PLEIOUV H DEKA KATABAV EIV KAISAREIAN TH EPAURION KAYISAV EPI TOU BHMATOV EKELEUSEN TON PAULON ACYHNAI
05L-ACTS-25-07 PARAGENOMENOU DE AUTOU PERIESTHSAN OI APO IEROSOLUMWN KATABEBHKOTEV IOUDAIOI POLLA KAI BAREA AITIWMATA FERONTEV KATA TOU PAULOU A OUK ISCUON APODEIXAI
05L-ACTS-25-08 APOLOGOUMENOU AUTOU OTI OUTE EIV TON NOMON TWN IOUDAIWN OUTE EIV TO IERON OUTE EIV KAISARA TI HMARTON
05L-ACTS-25-09 O FHSTOV DE TOIV IOUDAIOIV YELWN CARIN KATAYESYAI APOKRIYEIV TW PAULW EIPEN YELEIV EIV IEROSOLUMA ANABAV EKEI PERI TOUTWN KRINESYAI EP EMOU
05L-ACTS-25-10 EIPEN DE O PAULOV EPI TOU BHMATOV KAISAROV ESTWV EIMI OU ME DEI KRINESYAI IOUDAIOUV OUDEN HDIKHSA WV KAI SU KALLION EPIGINWSKEIV
05L-ACTS-25-11 EI MEN GAR ADIKW KAI AXION YANATOU PEPRACA TI OU PARAITOUMAI TO APOYANEIN EI DE OUDEN ESTIN WN OUTOI KATHGOROUSIN MOU OUDEIV ME DUNATAI AUTOIV CARISASYAI KAISARA EPIKALOUMAI
05L-ACTS-25-12 TOTE O FHSTOV SULLALHSAV META TOU SUMBOULIOU APEKRIYH KAISARA EPIKEKLHSAI EPI KAISARA POREUSH

05L-ACTS-25-14 WV DE PLEIOUV HMERAV DIETRIBEN EKEI O FHSTOV TW BASILEI ANEYETO TA KATA TON PAULON LEGWN ANHR TIV ESTIN KATALELEIMMENOV UPO FHLIKOV DESMIOV
05L-ACTS-25-15 PERI OU GENOMENOU MOU EIV IEROSOLUMA ENEFANISAN OI ARCIEREIV KAI OI PRESBUTEROI TWN IOUDAIWN AITOUMENOI KAT AUTOU DIKHN
05L-ACTS-25-16 PROV OUV APEKRIYHN OTI OUK ESTIN EYOV RWMAIOIV CARIZESYAI TINA ANYRWPON EIV APWLEIAN PRIN H O KATHGOROUMENOV KATA PROSWPON ECOI TOUV KATHGOROUV TOPON TE APOLOGIAV LABOI PERI TOU EGKLHMATOV
05L-ACTS-25-17 SUNELYONTWN OUN AUTWN ENYADE ANABOLHN MHDEMIAN POIHSAMENOV TH EXHV KAYISAV EPI TOU BHMATOV EKELEUSA ACYHNAI TON ANDRA
05L-ACTS-25-18 PERI OU STAYENTEV OI KATHGOROI OUDEMIAN AITIAN EPEFERON WN UPENOOUN EGW
05L-ACTS-25-19 ZHTHMATA DE TINA PERI THV IDIAV DEISIDAIMONIAV EICON PROV AUTON KAI PERI TINOV IHSOU TEYNHKOTOV ON EFASKEN O PAULOV ZHN
05L-ACTS-25-20 APOROUMENOV DE EGW THN PERI TOUTOU ZHTHSIN ELEGON EI BOULOITO POREUESYAI EIV IEROUSALHM KAKEI KRINESYAI PERI TOUTWN
05L-ACTS-25-21 TOU DE PAULOU EPIKALESAMENOU THRHYHNAI AUTON EIV THN TOU SEBASTOU DIAGNWSIN EKELEUSA THREISYAI AUTON EWV OU PEMQW AUTON PROV KAISARA
05L-ACTS-25-22 AGRIPPAV DE PROV TON FHSTON EFH EBOULOMHN KAI AUTOV TOU ANYRWPOU AKOUSAI O DE AURION FHSIN AKOUSH AUTOU
05L-ACTS-25-23 TH OUN EPAURION ELYONTOV TOU AGRIPPA KAI THV BERNIKHV META POLLHV FANTASIAV KAI EISELYONTWN EIV TO AKROATHRION SUN TE TOIV CILIARCOIV KAI ANDRASIN TOIV KAT EXOCHN OUSIN THV POLEWV KAI KELEUSANTOV TOU FHSTOU HCYH O PAULOV
05L-ACTS-25-24 KAI FHSIN O FHSTOV AGRIPPA BASILEU KAI PANTEV OI SUMPARONTEV HMIN ANDREV YEWREITE TOUTON PERI OU PAN TO PLHYOV TWN IOUDAIWN ENETUCON MOI EN TE IEROSOLUMOIV KAI ENYADE EPIBOWNTEV MH DEIN ZHN AUTON MHKETI
05L-ACTS-25-25 EGW DE KATALABOMENOV MHDEN AXION YANATOU AUTON PEPRACENAI KAI AUTOU DE TOUTOU EPIKALESAMENOU TON SEBASTON EKRINA PEMPEIN AUTON
05L-ACTS-25-26 PERI OU ASFALEV TI GRAQAI TW KURIW OUK ECW DIO PROHGAGON AUTON EF UMWN KAI MALISTA EPI SOU BASILEU AGRIPPA OPWV THV ANAKRISEWV GENOMENHV SCW TI GRAQAI

05L-ACTS-26-04 THN MEN OUN BIWSIN MOU THN EK NEOTHTOV THN AP ARCHV GENOMENHN EN TW EYNEI MOU EN IEROSOLUMOIV ISASIN PANTEV OI IOUDAIOI
05L-ACTS-26-05 PROGINWSKONTEV ME ANWYEN EAN YELWSIN MARTUREIN OTI KATA THN AKRIBESTATHN AIRESIN THV HMETERAV YRHSKEIAV EZHSA FARISAIOV
05L-ACTS-26-06 KAI NUN EP ELPIDI THV PROV TOUV PATERAV EPAGGELIAV GENOMENHV UPO TOU YEOU ESTHKA KRINOMENOV
05L-ACTS-26-07 EIV HN TO DWDEKAFULON HMWN EN EKTENEIA NUKTA KAI HMERAN LATREUON ELPIZEI KATANTHSAI PERI HV ELPIDOV EGKALOUMAI BASILEU AGRIPPA UPO IOUDAIWN
05L-ACTS-26-08 TI APISTON KRINETAI PAR UMIN EI O YEOV NEKROUV EGEIREI
05L-ACTS-26-09 EGW MEN OUN EDOXA EMAUTW PROV TO ONOMA IHSOU TOU NAZWRAIOU DEIN POLLA ENANTIA PRAXAI
05L-ACTS-26-10 O KAI EPOIHSA EN IEROSOLUMOIV KAI POLLOUV TWN AGIWN EGW FULAKAIV KATEKLEISA THN PARA TWN ARCIEREWN EXOUSIAN LABWN ANAIROUMENWN TE AUTWN KATHNEGKA QHFON
05L-ACTS-26-11 KAI KATA PASAV TAV SUNAGWGAV POLLAKIV TIMWRWN AUTOUV HNAGKAZON BLASFHMEIN PERISSWV TE EMMAINOMENOV AUTOIV EDIWKON EWV KAI EIV TAV EXW POLEIV
05L-ACTS-26-12 EN OIV KAI POREUOMENOV EIV THN DAMASKON MET EXOUSIAV KAI EPITROPHV THV PARA TWN ARCIEREWN
05L-ACTS-26-13 HMERAV MESHV KATA THN ODON EIDON BASILEU OURANOYEN UPER THN LAMPROTHTA TOU HLIOU PERILAMQAN ME FWV KAI TOUV SUN EMOI POREUOMENOUV
05L-ACTS-26-14 PANTWN DE KATAPESONTWN HMWN EIV THN GHN HKOUSA FWNHN LALOUSAN PROV ME KAI LEGOUSAN TH EBRAIDI DIALEKTW SAOUL SAOUL TI ME DIWKEIV SKLHRON SOI PROV KENTRA LAKTIZEIN

05L-ACTS-26-17 EXAIROUMENOV SE EK TOU LAOU KAI TWN EYNWN EIV OUV EGW SE APOSTELLW

05L-ACTS-26-20 ALLA TOIV EN DAMASKW PRWTON KAI IEROSOLUMOIV EIV PASAN TE THN CWRAN THV IOUDAIAV KAI TOIV EYNESIN APAGGELLWN METANOEIN KAI EPISTREFEIN EPI TON YEON AXIA THV METANOIAV ERGA PRASSONTAV
05L-ACTS-26-21 ENEKA TOUTWN OI IOUDAIOI ME SULLABOMENOI EN TW IERW EPEIRWNTO DIACEIRISASYAI

05L-ACTS-26-27 PISTEUEIV BASILEU AGRIPPA TOIV PROFHTAIV OIDA OTI PISTEUEIV

05L-ACTS-27-01 WV DE EKRIYH TOU APOPLEIN HMAV EIV THN ITALIAN PAREDIDOUN TON TE PAULON KAI TINAV ETEROUV DESMWTAV EKATONTARCH ONOMATI IOULIW SPEIRHV SEBASTHV
05L-ACTS-27-02 EPIBANTEV DE PLOIW ADRAMUTTHNW MELLONTEV PLEIN TOUV KATA THN ASIAN TOPOUV ANHCYHMEN ONTOV SUN HMIN ARISTARCOU MAKEDONOV YESSALONIKEWV
05L-ACTS-27-03 TH TE ETERA KATHCYHMEN EIV SIDWNA FILANYRWPWV TE O IOULIOV TW PAULW CRHSAMENOV EPETREQEN PROV TOUV FILOUV POREUYENTA EPIMELEIAV TUCEIN
05L-ACTS-27-04 KAKEIYEN ANACYENTEV UPEPLEUSAMEN THN KUPRON DIA TO TOUV ANEMOUV EINAI ENANTIOUV
05L-ACTS-27-05 TO TE PELAGOV TO KATA THN KILIKIAN KAI PAMFULIAN DIAPLEUSANTEV KATHLYOMEN EIV MURA THV LUKIAV
05L-ACTS-27-06 KAKEI EURWN O EKATONTARCOV PLOION ALEXANDRINON PLEON EIV THN ITALIAN ENEBIBASEN HMAV EIV AUTO
05L-ACTS-27-07 EN IKANAIV DE HMERAIV BRADUPLOOUNTEV KAI MOLIV GENOMENOI KATA THN KNIDON MH PROSEWNTOV HMAV TOU ANEMOU UPEPLEUSAMEN THN KRHTHN KATA SALMWNHN
05L-ACTS-27-08 MOLIV TE PARALEGOMENOI AUTHN HLYOMEN EIV TOPON TINA KALOUMENON KALOUV LIMENAV W EGGUV HN POLIV LASAIA
05L-ACTS-27-09 IKANOU DE CRONOU DIAGENOMENOU KAI ONTOV HDH EPISFALOUV TOU PLOOV DIA TO KAI THN NHSTEIAN HDH PARELHLUYENAI PARHNEI O PAULOV
05L-ACTS-27-10 LEGWN AUTOIV ANDREV YEWRW OTI META UBREWV KAI POLLHV ZHMIAV OU MONON TOU FORTIOU KAI TOU PLOIOU ALLA KAI TWN QUCWN HMWN MELLEIN ESESYAI TON PLOUN
05L-ACTS-27-11 O DE EKATONTARCHV TW KUBERNHTH KAI TW NAUKLHRW EPEIYETO MALLON H TOIV UPO TOU PAULOU LEGOMENOIV
05L-ACTS-27-12 ANEUYETOU DE TOU LIMENOV UPARCONTOV PROV PARACEIMASIAN OI PLEIOUV EYENTO BOULHN ANACYHNAI KAKEIYEN EI PWV DUNAINTO KATANTHSANTEV EIV FOINIKA PARACEIMASAI LIMENA THV KRHTHV BLEPONTA KATA LIBA KAI KATA CWRON
05L-ACTS-27-13 UPOPNEUSANTOV DE NOTOU DOXANTEV THV PROYESEWV KEKRATHKENAI ARANTEV ASSON PARELEGONTO THN KRHTHN
05L-ACTS-27-14 MET OU POLU DE EBALEN KAT AUTHV ANEMOV TUFWNIKOV O KALOUMENOV EUROKLUDWN
05L-ACTS-27-15 SUNARPASYENTOV DE TOU PLOIOU KAI MH DUNAMENOU ANTOFYALMEIN TW ANEMW EPIDONTEV EFEROMEYA
05L-ACTS-27-16 NHSION DE TI UPODRAMONTEV KALOUMENON KLAUDHN MOLIV ISCUSAMEN PERIKRATEIV GENESYAI THV SKAFHV
05L-ACTS-27-17 HN ARANTEV BOHYEIAIV ECRWNTO UPOZWNNUNTEV TO PLOION FOBOUMENOI TE MH EIV THN SURTHN EKPESWSIN CALASANTEV TO SKEUOV OUTWV EFERONTO
05L-ACTS-27-18 SFODRWV DE CEIMAZOMENWN HMWN TH EXHV EKBOLHN EPOIOUNTO
05L-ACTS-27-19 KAI TH TRITH AUTOCEIREV THN SKEUHN TOU PLOIOU ERRIQAMEN
05L-ACTS-27-20 MHTE DE HLIOU MHTE ASTRWN EPIFAINONTWN EPI PLEIONAV HMERAV CEIMWNOV TE OUK OLIGOU EPIKEIMENOU LOIPON PERIHREITO PASA ELPIV TOU SWZESYAI HMAV
05L-ACTS-27-21 POLLHV DE ASITIAV UPARCOUSHV TOTE STAYEIV O PAULOV EN MESW AUTWN EIPEN EDEI MEN W ANDREV PEIYARCHSANTAV MOI MH ANAGESYAI APO THV KRHTHV KERDHSAI TE THN UBRIN TAUTHN KAI THN ZHMIAN
05L-ACTS-27-22 KAI TA NUN PARAINW UMAV EUYUMEIN APOBOLH GAR QUCHV OUDEMIA ESTAI EX UMWN PLHN TOU PLOIOU

06P-ROMN-03-23 PANTEV GAR HMARTON KAI USTEROUNTAI THV DOXHV TOU YEOU
