06P-ROMN-03-25 ON PROEYETO O YEOV ILASTHRION DIA THV PISTEWV EN TW AUTOU AIMATI EIV ENDEIXIN THV DIKAIOSUNHV AUTOU DIA THN PARESIN TWN PROGEGONOTWN AMARTHMATWN
06P-ROMN-03-26 EN TH ANOCH TOU YEOU PROV ENDEIXIN THV DIKAIOSUNHV AUTOU EN TW NUN KAIRW EIV TO EINAI AUTON DIKAION KAI DIKAIOUNTA TON EK PISTEWV IHSOU
06P-ROMN-03-27 POU OUN H KAUCHSIV EXEKLEISYH DIA POIOU NOMOU TWN ERGWN OUCI ALLA DIA NOMOU PISTEWV
06P-ROMN-03-28 LOGIZOMEYA OUN PISTEI DIKAIOUSYAI ANYRWPON CWRIV ERGWN NOMOU
06P-ROMN-03-29 H IOUDAIWN O YEOV MONON OUCI DE KAI EYNWN NAI KAI EYNWN
06P-ROMN-03-30 EPEIPER EIV O YEOV OV DIKAIWSEI PERITOMHN EK PISTEWV KAI AKROBUSTIAN DIA THV PISTEWV
06P-ROMN-03-31 NOMON OUN KATARGOUMEN DIA THV PISTEWV MH GENOITO ALLA NOMON ISTWMEN
06P-ROMN-04-01 TI OUN EROUMEN ABRAAM TON PATERA HMWN EURHKENAI KATA SARKA
06P-ROMN-04-02 EI GAR ABRAAM EX ERGWN EDIKAIWYH ECEI KAUCHMA ALL OU PROV TON YEON
06P-ROMN-04-03 TI GAR H GRAFH LEGEI EPISTEUSEN DE ABRAAM TW YEW KAI ELOGISYH AUTW EIV DIKAIOSUNHN
06P-ROMN-04-04 TW DE ERGAZOMENW O MISYOV OU LOGIZETAI KATA CARIN ALLA KATA OFEILHMA
06P-ROMN-04-05 TW DE MH ERGAZOMENW PISTEUONTI DE EPI TON DIKAIOUNTA TON ASEBH LOGIZETAI H PISTIV AUTOU EIV DIKAIOSUNHN
06P-ROMN-04-06 KAYAPER KAI DAUID LEGEI TON MAKARISMON TOU ANYRWPOU W O YEOV LOGIZETAI DIKAIOSUNHN CWRIV ERGWN
06P-ROMN-04-07 MAKARIOI WN AFEYHSAN AI ANOMIAI KAI WN EPEKALUFYHSAN AI AMARTIAI
06P-ROMN-04-08 MAKARIOV ANHR W OU MH LOGISHTAI KURIOV AMARTIAN
06P-ROMN-04-09 O MAKARISMOV OUN OUTOV EPI THN PERITOMHN H KAI EPI THN AKROBUSTIAN LEGOMEN GAR OTI ELOGISYH TW ABRAAM H PISTIV EIV DIKAIOSUNHN
06P-ROMN-04-10 PWV OUN ELOGISYH EN PERITOMH ONTI H EN AKROBUSTIA OUK EN PERITOMH ALL EN AKROBUSTIA
06P-ROMN-04-11 KAI SHMEION ELABEN PERITOMHV SFRAGIDA THV DIKAIOSUNHV THV PISTEWV THV EN TH AKROBUSTIA EIV TO EINAI AUTON PATERA PANTWN TWN PISTEUONTWN DI AKROBUSTIAV EIV TO LOGISYHNAI KAI AUTOIV THN DIKAIOSUNHN
06P-ROMN-04-12 KAI PATERA PERITOMHV TOIV OUK EK PERITOMHV MONON ALLA KAI TOIV STOICOUSIN TOIV ICNESIN THV PISTEWV THV EN TH AKROBUSTIA TOU PATROV HMWN ABRAAM
06P-ROMN-04-13 OU GAR DIA NOMOU H EPAGGELIA TW ABRAAM H TW SPERMATI AUTOU TO KLHRONOMON AUTON EINAI TOU KOSMOU ALLA DIA DIKAIOSUNHV PISTEWV
06P-ROMN-04-14 EI GAR OI EK NOMOU KLHRONOMOI KEKENWTAI H PISTIV KAI KATHRGHTAI H EPAGGELIA
06P-ROMN-04-15 O GAR NOMOV ORGHN KATERGAZETAI OU GAR OUK ESTIN NOMOV OUDE PARABASIV
06P-ROMN-04-16 DIA TOUTO EK PISTEWV INA KATA CARIN EIV TO EINAI BEBAIAN THN EPAGGELIAN PANTI TW SPERMATI OU TW EK TOU NOMOU MONON ALLA KAI TW EK PISTEWV ABRAAM OV ESTIN PATHR PANTWN HMWN
06P-ROMN-04-17 KAYWV GEGRAPTAI OTI PATERA POLLWN EYNWN TEYEIKA SE KATENANTI OU EPISTEUSEN YEOU TOU ZWOPOIOUNTOV TOUV NEKROUV KAI KALOUNTOV TA MH ONTA WV ONTA
06P-ROMN-04-18 OV PAR ELPIDA EP ELPIDI EPISTEUSEN EIV TO GENESYAI AUTON PATERA POLLWN EYNWN KATA TO EIRHMENON OUTWV ESTAI TO SPERMA SOU
06P-ROMN-04-19 KAI MH ASYENHSAV TH PISTEI OU KATENOHSEN TO EAUTOU SWMA HDH NENEKRWMENON EKATONTAETHV POU UPARCWN KAI THN NEKRWSIN THV MHTRAV SARRAV
06P-ROMN-04-20 EIV DE THN EPAGGELIAN TOU YEOU OU DIEKRIYH TH APISTIA ALL ENEDUNAMWYH TH PISTEI DOUV DOXAN TW YEW
06P-ROMN-04-21 KAI PLHROFORHYEIV OTI O EPHGGELTAI DUNATOV ESTIN KAI POIHSAI
06P-ROMN-04-22 DIO KAI ELOGISYH AUTW EIV DIKAIOSUNHN
06P-ROMN-04-23 OUK EGRAFH DE DI AUTON MONON OTI ELOGISYH AUTW
06P-ROMN-04-24 ALLA KAI DI HMAV OIV MELLEI LOGIZESYAI TOIV PISTEUOUSIN EPI TON EGEIRANTA IHSOUN TON KURION HMWN EK NEKRWN
06P-ROMN-04-25 OV PAREDOYH DIA TA PARAPTWMATA HMWN KAI HGERYH DIA THN DIKAIWSIN HMWN 
06P-ROMN-05-01 DIKAIWYENTEV OUN EK PISTEWV EIRHNHN ECOMEN PROV TON YEON DIA TOU KURIOU HMWN IHSOU CRISTOU 
06P-ROMN-05-02 DI OU KAI THN PROSAGWGHN ESCHKAMEN TH PISTEI EIV THN CARIN TAUTHN EN H ESTHKAMEN KAI KAUCWMEYA EP ELPIDI THV DOXHV TOU YEOU
06P-ROMN-05-03 OU MONON DE ALLA KAI KAUCWMEYA EN TAIV YLIQESIN EIDOTEV OTI H YLIQIV UPOMONHN KATERGAZETAI
06P-ROMN-05-04 H DE UPOMONH DOKIMHN H DE DOKIMH ELPIDA
06P-ROMN-05-05 H DE ELPIV OU KATAISCUNEI OTI H AGAPH TOU YEOU EKKECUTAI EN TAIV KARDIAIV HMWN DIA PNEUMATOV AGIOU TOU DOYENTOV HMIN
06P-ROMN-05-06 ETI GAR CRISTOV ONTWN HMWN ASYENWN KATA KAIRON UPER ASEBWN APEYANEN
06P-ROMN-05-07 MOLIV GAR UPER DIKAIOU TIV APOYANEITAI UPER GAR TOU AGAYOU TACA TIV KAI TOLMA APOYANEIN
06P-ROMN-05-08 SUNISTHSIN DE THN EAUTOU AGAPHN EIV HMAV O YEOV OTI ETI AMARTWLWN ONTWN HMWN CRISTOV UPER HMWN APEYANEN
06P-ROMN-05-09 POLLW OUN MALLON DIKAIWYENTEV NUN EN TW AIMATI AUTOU SWYHSOMEYA DI AUTOU APO THV ORGHV
06P-ROMN-05-10 EI GAR ECYROI ONTEV KATHLLAGHMEN TW YEW DIA TOU YANATOU TOU UIOU AUTOU POLLW MALLON KATALLAGENTEV SWYHSOMEYA EN TH ZWH AUTOU
06P-ROMN-05-11 OU MONON DE ALLA KAI KAUCWMENOI EN TW YEW DIA TOU KURIOU HMWN IHSOU CRISTOU DI OU NUN THN KATALLAGHN ELABOMEN
06P-ROMN-05-12 DIA TOUTO WSPER DI ENOV ANYRWPOU H AMARTIA EIV TON KOSMON EISHLYEN KAI DIA THV AMARTIAV O YANATOV KAI OUTWV EIV PANTAV ANYRWPOUV O YANATOV DIHLYEN EF W PANTEV HMARTON
06P-ROMN-05-13 ACRI GAR NOMOU AMARTIA HN EN KOSMW AMARTIA DE OUK ELLOGEITAI MH ONTOV NOMOU
06P-ROMN-05-14 ALL EBASILEUSEN O YANATOV APO ADAM MECRI MWUSEWV KAI EPI TOUV MH AMARTHSANTAV EPI TW OMOIWMATI THV PARABASEWV ADAM OV ESTIN TUPOV TOU MELLONTOV
06P-ROMN-05-15 ALL OUC WV TO PARAPTWMA OUTWV KAI TO CARISMA EI GAR TW TOU ENOV PARAPTWMATI OI POLLOI APEYANON POLLW MALLON H CARIV TOU YEOU KAI H DWREA EN CARITI TH TOU ENOV ANYRWPOU IHSOU CRISTOU EIV TOUV POLLOUV EPERISSEUSEN
06P-ROMN-05-16 KAI OUC WV DI ENOV AMARTHSANTOV TO DWRHMA TO MEN GAR KRIMA EX ENOV EIV KATAKRIMA TO DE CARISMA EK POLLWN PARAPTWMATWN EIV DIKAIWMA
06P-ROMN-05-17 EI GAR TW TOU ENOV PARAPTWMATI O YANATOV EBASILEUSEN DIA TOU ENOV POLLW MALLON OI THN PERISSEIAN THV CARITOV KAI THV DWREAV THV DIKAIOSUNHV LAMBANONTEV EN ZWH BASILEUSOUSIN DIA TOU ENOV IHSOU CRISTOU
06P-ROMN-05-18 ARA OUN WV DI ENOV PARAPTWMATOV EIV PANTAV ANYRWPOUV EIV KATAKRIMA OUTWV KAI DI ENOV DIKAIWMATOV EIV PANTAV ANYRWPOUV EIV DIKAIWSIN ZWHV
06P-ROMN-05-19 WSPER GAR DIA THV PARAKOHV TOU ENOV ANYRWPOU AMARTWLOI KATESTAYHSAN OI POLLOI OUTWV KAI DIA THV UPAKOHV TOU ENOV DIKAIOI KATASTAYHSONTAI OI POLLOI
06P-ROMN-05-20 NOMOV DE PAREISHLYEN INA PLEONASH TO PARAPTWMA OU DE EPLEONASEN H AMARTIA UPEREPERISSEUSEN H CARIV
06P-ROMN-05-21 INA WSPER EBASILEUSEN H AMARTIA EN TW YANATW OUTWV KAI H CARIV BASILEUSH DIA DIKAIOSUNHV EIV ZWHN AIWNION DIA IHSOU CRISTOU TOU KURIOU HMWN
06P-ROMN-06-01 TI OUN EROUMEN EPIMENOMEN TH AMARTIA INA H CARIV PLEONASH
06P-ROMN-06-02 MH GENOITO OITINEV APEYANOMEN TH AMARTIA PWV ETI ZHSOMEN EN AUTH
06P-ROMN-06-03 H AGNOEITE OTI OSOI EBAPTISYHMEN EIV CRISTON IHSOUN EIV TON YANATON AUTOU EBAPTISYHMEN
06P-ROMN-06-04 SUNETAFHMEN OUN AUTW DIA TOU BAPTISMATOV EIV TON YANATON INA WSPER HGERYH CRISTOV EK NEKRWN DIA THV DOXHV TOU PATROV OUTWV KAI HMEIV EN KAINOTHTI ZWHV PERIPATHSWMEN
06P-ROMN-06-05 EI GAR SUMFUTOI GEGONAMEN TW OMOIWMATI TOU YANATOU AUTOU ALLA KAI THV ANASTASEWV ESOMEYA
06P-ROMN-06-06 TOUTO GINWSKONTEV OTI O PALAIOV HMWN ANYRWPOV SUNESTAURWYH INA KATARGHYH TO SWMA THV AMARTIAV TOU MHKETI DOULEUEIN HMAV TH AMARTIA
06P-ROMN-06-07 O GAR APOYANWN DEDIKAIWTAI APO THV AMARTIAV
06P-ROMN-06-08 EI DE APEYANOMEN SUN CRISTW PISTEUOMEN OTI KAI SUZHSOMEN AUTW
06P-ROMN-06-09 EIDOTEV OTI CRISTOV EGERYEIV EK NEKRWN OUKETI APOYNHSKEI YANATOV AUTOU OUKETI KURIEUEI
06P-ROMN-06-10 O GAR APEYANEN TH AMARTIA APEYANEN EFAPAX O DE ZH ZH TW YEW
06P-ROMN-06-11 OUTWV KAI UMEIV LOGIZESYE EAUTOUV NEKROUV MEN EINAI TH AMARTIA ZWNTAV DE TW YEW EN CRISTW IHSOU TW KURIW HMWN
06P-ROMN-06-12 MH OUN BASILEUETW H AMARTIA EN TW YNHTW UMWN SWMATI EIV TO UPAKOUEIN AUTH EN TAIV EPIYUMIAIV AUTOU
06P-ROMN-06-13 MHDE PARISTANETE TA MELH UMWN OPLA ADIKIAV TH AMARTIA ALLA PARASTHSATE EAUTOUV TW YEW WV EK NEKRWN ZWNTAV KAI TA MELH UMWN OPLA DIKAIOSUNHV TW YEW
06P-ROMN-06-14 AMARTIA GAR UMWN OU KURIEUSEI OU GAR ESTE UPO NOMON ALL UPO CARIN
06P-ROMN-06-15 TI OUN AMARTHSOMEN OTI OUK ESMEN UPO NOMON ALL UPO CARIN MH GENOITO
06P-ROMN-06-16 OUK OIDATE OTI W PARISTANETE EAUTOUV DOULOUV EIV UPAKOHN DOULOI ESTE W UPAKOUETE HTOI AMARTIAV EIV YANATON H UPAKOHV EIV DIKAIOSUNHN
06P-ROMN-06-17 CARIV DE TW YEW OTI HTE DOULOI THV AMARTIAV UPHKOUSATE DE EK KARDIAV EIV ON PAREDOYHTE TUPON DIDACHV
06P-ROMN-06-18 ELEUYERWYENTEV DE APO THV AMARTIAV EDOULWYHTE TH DIKAIOSUNH
06P-ROMN-06-19 ANYRWPINON LEGW DIA THN ASYENEIAN THV SARKOV UMWN WSPER GAR PARESTHSATE TA MELH UMWN DOULA TH AKAYARSIA KAI TH ANOMIA EIV THN ANOMIAN OUTWV NUN PARASTHSATE TA MELH UMWN DOULA TH DIKAIOSUNH EIV AGIASMON
06P-ROMN-06-20 OTE GAR DOULOI HTE THV AMARTIAV ELEUYEROI HTE TH DIKAIOSUNH
06P-ROMN-06-21 TINA OUN KARPON EICETE TOTE EF OIV NUN EPAISCUNESYE TO GAR TELOV EKEINWN YANATOV
06P-ROMN-06-22 NUNI DE ELEUYERWYENTEV APO THV AMARTIAV DOULWYENTEV DE TW YEW ECETE TON KARPON UMWN EIV AGIASMON TO DE TELOV ZWHN AIWNION
06P-ROMN-06-23 TA GAR OQWNIA THV AMARTIAV YANATOV TO DE CARISMA TOU YEOU ZWH AIWNIOV EN CRISTW IHSOU TW KURIW HMWN
06P-ROMN-07-01 H AGNOEITE ADELFOI GINWSKOUSIN GAR NOMON LALW OTI O NOMOV KURIEUEI TOU ANYRWPOU EF OSON CRONON ZH
06P-ROMN-07-02 H GAR UPANDROV GUNH TW ZWNTI ANDRI DEDETAI NOMW EAN DE APOYANH O ANHR KATHRGHTAI APO TOU NOMOU TOU ANDROV
06P-ROMN-07-03 ARA OUN ZWNTOV TOU ANDROV MOICALIV CRHMATISEI EAN GENHTAI ANDRI ETERW EAN DE APOYANH O ANHR ELEUYERA ESTIN APO TOU NOMOU TOU MH EINAI AUTHN MOICALIDA GENOMENHN ANDRI ETERW
06P-ROMN-07-04 WSTE ADELFOI MOU KAI UMEIV EYANATWYHTE TW NOMW DIA TOU SWMATOV TOU CRISTOU EIV TO GENESYAI UMAV ETERW TW EK NEKRWN EGERYENTI INA KARPOFORHSWMEN TW YEW
06P-ROMN-07-05 OTE GAR HMEN EN TH SARKI TA PAYHMATA TWN AMARTIWN TA DIA TOU NOMOU ENHRGEITO EN TOIV MELESIN HMWN EIV TO KARPOFORHSAI TW YANATW
06P-ROMN-07-06 NUNI DE KATHRGHYHMEN APO TOU NOMOU APOYANONTEV EN W KATEICOMEYA WSTE DOULEUEIN HMAV EN KAINOTHTI PNEUMATOV KAI OU PALAIOTHTI GRAMMATOV
06P-ROMN-07-07 TI OUN EROUMEN O NOMOV AMARTIA MH GENOITO ALLA THN AMARTIAN OUK EGNWN EI MH DIA NOMOU THN TE GAR EPIYUMIAN OUK HDEIN EI MH O NOMOV ELEGEN OUK EPIYUMHSEIV
06P-ROMN-07-08 AFORMHN DE LABOUSA H AMARTIA DIA THV ENTOLHV KATEIRGASATO EN EMOI PASAN EPIYUMIAN CWRIV GAR NOMOU AMARTIA NEKRA
06P-ROMN-07-09 EGW DE EZWN CWRIV NOMOU POTE ELYOUSHV DE THV ENTOLHV H AMARTIA ANEZHSEN EGW DE APEYANON
06P-ROMN-07-10 KAI EUREYH MOI H ENTOLH H EIV ZWHN AUTH EIV YANATON
06P-ROMN-07-11 H GAR AMARTIA AFORMHN LABOUSA DIA THV ENTOLHV EXHPATHSEN ME KAI DI AUTHV APEKTEINEN
06P-ROMN-07-12 WSTE O MEN NOMOV AGIOV KAI H ENTOLH AGIA KAI DIKAIA KAI AGAYH
06P-ROMN-07-13 TO OUN AGAYON EMOI GEGONEN YANATOV MH GENOITO ALLA H AMARTIA INA FANH AMARTIA DIA TOU AGAYOU MOI KATERGAZOMENH YANATON INA GENHTAI KAY UPERBOLHN AMARTWLOV H AMARTIA DIA THV ENTOLHV
06P-ROMN-07-14 OIDAMEN GAR OTI O NOMOV PNEUMATIKOV ESTIN EGW DE SARKIKOV EIMI PEPRAMENOV UPO THN AMARTIAN
06P-ROMN-07-15 O GAR KATERGAZOMAI OU GINWSKW OU GAR O YELW TOUTO PRASSW ALL O MISW TOUTO POIW
06P-ROMN-07-16 EI DE O OU YELW TOUTO POIW SUMFHMI TW NOMW OTI KALOV
06P-ROMN-07-17 NUNI DE OUKETI EGW KATERGAZOMAI AUTO ALL H OIKOUSA EN EMOI AMARTIA
06P-ROMN-07-18 OIDA GAR OTI OUK OIKEI EN EMOI TOUT ESTIN EN TH SARKI MOU AGAYON TO GAR YELEIN PARAKEITAI MOI TO DE KATERGAZESYAI TO KALON OUC EURISKW
06P-ROMN-07-19 OU GAR O YELW POIW AGAYON ALL O OU YELW KAKON TOUTO PRASSW
06P-ROMN-07-20 EI DE O OU YELW EGW TOUTO POIW OUKETI EGW KATERGAZOMAI AUTO ALL H OIKOUSA EN EMOI AMARTIA
06P-ROMN-07-21 EURISKW ARA TON NOMON TW YELONTI EMOI POIEIN TO KALON OTI EMOI TO KAKON PARAKEITAI
06P-ROMN-07-22 SUNHDOMAI GAR TW NOMW TOU YEOU KATA TON ESW ANYRWPON
06P-ROMN-07-23 BLEPW DE ETERON NOMON EN TOIV MELESIN MOU ANTISTRATEUOMENON TW NOMW TOU NOOV MOU KAI AICMALWTIZONTA ME TW NOMW THV AMARTIAV TW ONTI EN TOIV MELESIN MOU
06P-ROMN-07-24 TALAIPWROV EGW ANYRWPOV TIV ME RUSETAI EK TOU SWMATOV TOU YANATOU TOUTOU
06P-ROMN-07-25 EUCARISTW TW YEW DIA IHSOU CRISTOU TOU KURIOU HMWN ARA OUN AUTOV EGW TW MEN NOI DOULEUW NOMW YEOU TH DE SARKI NOMW AMARTIAV
06P-ROMN-08-01 OUDEN ARA NUN KATAKRIMA TOIV EN CRISTW IHSOU MH KATA SARKA PERIPATOUSIN ALLA KATA PNEUMA
06P-ROMN-08-02 O GAR NOMOV TOU PNEUMATOV THV ZWHV EN CRISTW IHSOU HLEUYERWSEN ME APO TOU NOMOU THV AMARTIAV KAI TOU YANATOU
06P-ROMN-08-03 TO GAR ADUNATON TOU NOMOU EN W HSYENEI DIA THV SARKOV O YEOV TON EAUTOU UION PEMQAV EN OMOIWMATI SARKOV AMARTIAV KAI PERI AMARTIAV KATEKRINEN THN AMARTIAN EN TH SARKI
06P-ROMN-08-04 INA TO DIKAIWMA TOU NOMOU PLHRWYH EN HMIN TOIV MH KATA SARKA PERIPATOUSIN ALLA KATA PNEUMA
06P-ROMN-08-05 OI GAR KATA SARKA ONTEV TA THV SARKOV FRONOUSIN OI DE KATA PNEUMA TA TOU PNEUMATOV
06P-ROMN-08-06 TO GAR FRONHMA THV SARKOV YANATOV TO DE FRONHMA TOU PNEUMATOV ZWH KAI EIRHNH
06P-ROMN-08-07 DIOTI TO FRONHMA THV SARKOV ECYRA EIV YEON TW GAR NOMW TOU YEOU OUC UPOTASSETAI OUDE GAR DUNATAI
06P-ROMN-08-08 OI DE EN SARKI ONTEV YEW ARESAI OU DUNANTAI
06P-ROMN-08-09 UMEIV DE OUK ESTE EN SARKI ALL EN PNEUMATI EIPER PNEUMA YEOU OIKEI EN UMIN EI DE TIV PNEUMA CRISTOU OUK ECEI OUTOV OUK ESTIN AUTOU
06P-ROMN-08-10 EI DE CRISTOV EN UMIN TO MEN SWMA NEKRON DIA AMARTIAN TO DE PNEUMA ZWH DIA DIKAIOSUNHN
06P-ROMN-08-11 EI DE TO PNEUMA TOU EGEIRANTOV IHSOUN EK NEKRWN OIKEI EN UMIN O EGEIRAV TON CRISTON EK NEKRWN ZWOPOIHSEI KAI TA YNHTA SWMATA UMWN DIA TO ENOIKOUN AUTOU PNEUMA EN UMIN
06P-ROMN-08-12 ARA OUN ADELFOI OFEILETAI ESMEN OU TH SARKI TOU KATA SARKA ZHN
06P-ROMN-08-13 EI GAR KATA SARKA ZHTE MELLETE APOYNHSKEIN EI DE PNEUMATI TAV PRAXEIV TOU SWMATOV YANATOUTE ZHSESYE
06P-ROMN-08-14 OSOI GAR PNEUMATI YEOU AGONTAI OUTOI EISIN UIOI YEOU
06P-ROMN-08-15 OU GAR ELABETE PNEUMA DOULEIAV PALIN EIV FOBON ALL ELABETE PNEUMA UIOYESIAV EN W KRAZOMEN ABBA O PATHR
06P-ROMN-08-16 AUTO TO PNEUMA SUMMARTUREI TW PNEUMATI HMWN OTI ESMEN TEKNA YEOU
06P-ROMN-08-17 EI DE TEKNA KAI KLHRONOMOI KLHRONOMOI MEN YEOU SUGKLHRONOMOI DE CRISTOU EIPER SUMPASCOMEN INA KAI SUNDOXASYWMEN
06P-ROMN-08-18 LOGIZOMAI GAR OTI OUK AXIA TA PAYHMATA TOU NUN KAIROU PROV THN MELLOUSAN DOXAN APOKALUFYHNAI EIV HMAV
06P-ROMN-08-19 H GAR APOKARADOKIA THV KTISEWV THN APOKALUQIN TWN UIWN TOU YEOU APEKDECETAI
06P-ROMN-08-20 TH GAR MATAIOTHTI H KTISIV UPETAGH OUC EKOUSA ALLA DIA TON UPOTAXANTA EP ELPIDI
06P-ROMN-08-21 OTI KAI AUTH H KTISIV ELEUYERWYHSETAI APO THV DOULEIAV THV FYORAV EIV THN ELEUYERIAN THV DOXHV TWN TEKNWN TOU YEOU
06P-ROMN-08-22 OIDAMEN GAR OTI PASA H KTISIV SUSTENAZEI KAI SUNWDINEI ACRI TOU NUN
06P-ROMN-08-23 OU MONON DE ALLA KAI AUTOI THN APARCHN TOU PNEUMATOV ECONTEV KAI HMEIV AUTOI EN EAUTOIV STENAZOMEN UIOYESIAN APEKDECOMENOI THN APOLUTRWSIN TOU SWMATOV HMWN
06P-ROMN-08-24 TH GAR ELPIDI ESWYHMEN ELPIV DE BLEPOMENH OUK ESTIN ELPIV O GAR BLEPEI TIV TI KAI ELPIZEI
06P-ROMN-08-25 EI DE O OU BLEPOMEN ELPIZOMEN DI UPOMONHV APEKDECOMEYA
06P-ROMN-08-26 WSAUTWV DE KAI TO PNEUMA SUNANTILAMBANETAI TAIV ASYENEIAIV HMWN TO GAR TI PROSEUXOMEYA KAYO DEI OUK OIDAMEN ALL AUTO TO PNEUMA UPERENTUGCANEI UPER HMWN STENAGMOIV ALALHTOIV
06P-ROMN-08-27 O DE EREUNWN TAV KARDIAV OIDEN TI TO FRONHMA TOU PNEUMATOV OTI KATA YEON ENTUGCANEI UPER AGIWN
06P-ROMN-08-28 OIDAMEN DE OTI TOIV AGAPWSIN TON YEON PANTA SUNERGEI EIV AGAYON TOIV KATA PROYESIN KLHTOIV OUSIN
06P-ROMN-08-29 OTI OUV PROEGNW KAI PROWRISEN SUMMORFOUV THV EIKONOV TOU UIOU AUTOU EIV TO EINAI AUTON PRWTOTOKON EN POLLOIV ADELFOIV
06P-ROMN-08-30 OUV DE PROWRISEN TOUTOUV KAI EKALESEN KAI OUV EKALESEN TOUTOUV KAI EDIKAIWSEN OUV DE EDIKAIWSEN TOUTOUV KAI EDOXASEN
06P-ROMN-08-31 TI OUN EROUMEN PROV TAUTA EI O YEOV UPER HMWN TIV KAY HMWN
06P-ROMN-08-32 OV GE TOU IDIOU UIOU OUK EFEISATO ALL UPER HMWN PANTWN PAREDWKEN AUTON PWV OUCI KAI SUN AUTW TA PANTA HMIN CARISETAI
06P-ROMN-08-33 TIV EGKALESEI KATA EKLEKTWN YEOU YEOV O DIKAIWN
06P-ROMN-08-34 TIV O KATAKRINWN CRISTOV O APOYANWN MALLON DE KAI EGERYEIV OV KAI ESTIN EN DEXIA TOU YEOU OV KAI ENTUGCANEI UPER HMWN
06P-ROMN-08-35 TIV HMAV CWRISEI APO THV AGAPHV TOU CRISTOU YLIQIV H STENOCWRIA H DIWGMOV H LIMOV H GUMNOTHV H KINDUNOV H MACAIRA
06P-ROMN-08-36 KAYWV GEGRAPTAI OTI ENEKEN SOU YANATOUMEYA OLHN THN HMERAN ELOGISYHMEN WV PROBATA SFAGHV

06P-ROMN-14-21 KALON TO MH FAGEIN KREA MHDE PIEIN OINON MHDE EN W O ADELFOV SOU PROSKOPTEI H SKANDALIZETAI H ASYENEI
06P-ROMN-14-22 SU PISTIN ECEIV KATA SEAUTON ECE ENWPION TOU YEOU MAKARIOV O MH KRINWN EAUTON EN W DOKIMAZEI
06P-ROMN-14-23 O DE DIAKRINOMENOV EAN FAGH KATAKEKRITAI OTI OUK EK PISTEWV PAN DE O OUK EK PISTEWV AMARTIA ESTIN
06P-ROMN-14-24 TW DE DUNAMENW UMAV STHRIXAI KATA TO EUAGGELION MOU KAI TO KHRUGMA IHSOU CRISTOU KATA APOKALUQIN MUSTHRIOU CRONOIV AIWNIOIV SESIGHMENOU
06P-ROMN-14-25 FANERWYENTOV DE NUN DIA TE GRAFWN PROFHTIKWN KAT EPITAGHN TOU AIWNIOU YEOU EIV UPAKOHN PISTEWV EIV PANTA TA EYNH GNWRISYENTOV
06P-ROMN-14-26 MONW SOFW YEW DIA IHSOU CRISTOU W H DOXA EIV TOUV AIWNAV AMHN
06P-ROMN-15-01 OFEILOMEN DE HMEIV OI DUNATOI TA ASYENHMATA TWN ADUNATWN BASTAZEIN KAI MH EAUTOIV ARESKEIN
06P-ROMN-15-02 EKASTOV HMWN TW PLHSION ARESKETW EIV TO AGAYON PROV OIKODOMHN
06P-ROMN-15-03 KAI GAR O CRISTOV OUC EAUTW HRESEN ALLA KAYWV GEGRAPTAI OI ONEIDISMOI TWN ONEIDIZONTWN SE EPEPESON EP EME
06P-ROMN-15-04 OSA GAR PROEGRAFH EIV THN HMETERAN DIDASKALIAN PROEGRAFH INA DIA THV UPOMONHV KAI DIA THV PARAKLHSEWV TWN GRAFWN THN ELPIDA ECWMEN
06P-ROMN-15-05 O DE YEOV THV UPOMONHV KAI THV PARAKLHSEWV DWH UMIN TO AUTO FRONEIN EN ALLHLOIV KATA CRISTON IHSOUN
06P-ROMN-15-06 INA OMOYUMADON EN ENI STOMATI DOXAZHTE TON YEON KAI PATERA TOU KURIOU HMWN IHSOU CRISTOU

06P-ROMN-15-09 TA DE EYNH UPER ELEOUV DOXASAI TON YEON KAYWV GEGRAPTAI DIA TOUTO EXOMOLOGHSOMAI SOI EN EYNESIN KAI TW ONOMATI SOU QALW
06P-ROMN-15-10 KAI PALIN LEGEI EUFRANYHTE EYNH META TOU LAOU AUTOU

06P-ROMN-15-14 PEPEISMAI DE ADELFOI MOU KAI AUTOV EGW PERI UMWN OTI KAI AUTOI MESTOI ESTE AGAYWSUNHV PEPLHRWMENOI PASHV GNWSEWV DUNAMENOI KAI ALLOUV NOUYETEIN

06P-ROMN-15-16 EIV TO EINAI ME LEITOURGON IHSOU CRISTOU EIV TA EYNH IEROURGOUNTA TO EUAGGELION TOU YEOU INA GENHTAI H PROSFORA TWN EYNWN EUPROSDEKTOV HGIASMENH EN PNEUMATI AGIW
06P-ROMN-15-17 ECW OUN KAUCHSIN EN CRISTW IHSOU TA PROV TON YEON
06P-ROMN-15-18 OU GAR TOLMHSW LALEIN TI WN OU KATEIRGASATO CRISTOV DI EMOU EIV UPAKOHN EYNWN LOGW KAI ERGW
06P-ROMN-15-19 EN DUNAMEI SHMEIWN KAI TERATWN EN DUNAMEI PNEUMATOV YEOU WSTE ME APO IEROUSALHM KAI KUKLW MECRI TOU ILLURIKOU PEPLHRWKENAI TO EUAGGELION TOU CRISTOU
06P-ROMN-15-20 OUTWV DE FILOTIMOUMENON EUAGGELIZESYAI OUC OPOU WNOMASYH CRISTOV INA MH EP ALLOTRION YEMELION OIKODOMW

06P-ROMN-15-22 DIO KAI ENEKOPTOMHN TA POLLA TOU ELYEIN PROV UMAV
06P-ROMN-15-23 NUNI DE MHKETI TOPON ECWN EN TOIV KLIMASIN TOUTOIV EPIPOYIAN DE ECWN TOU ELYEIN PROV UMAV APO POLLWN ETWN
06P-ROMN-15-24 WV EAN POREUWMAI EIV THN SPANIAN ELEUSOMAI PROV UMAV ELPIZW GAR DIAPOREUOMENOV YEASASYAI UMAV KAI UF UMWN PROPEMFYHNAI EKEI EAN UMWN PRWTON APO MEROUV EMPLHSYW
06P-ROMN-15-25 NUNI DE POREUOMAI EIV IEROUSALHM DIAKONWN TOIV AGIOIV

06P-ROMN-15-27 EUDOKHSAN GAR KAI OFEILETAI AUTWN EISIN EI GAR TOIV PNEUMATIKOIV AUTWN EKOINWNHSAN TA EYNH OFEILOUSIN KAI EN TOIV SARKIKOIV LEITOURGHSAI AUTOIV

06P-ROMN-15-30 PARAKALW DE UMAV ADELFOI DIA TOU KURIOU HMWN IHSOU CRISTOU KAI DIA THV AGAPHV TOU PNEUMATOV SUNAGWNISASYAI MOI EN TAIV PROSEUCAIV UPER EMOU PROV TON YEON
06P-ROMN-15-31 INA RUSYW APO TWN APEIYOUNTWN EN TH IOUDAIA KAI INA H DIAKONIA MOU H EIV IEROUSALHM EUPROSDEKTOV GENHTAI TOIV AGIOIV
06P-ROMN-15-32 INA EN CARA ELYW PROV UMAV DIA YELHMATOV YEOU KAI SUNANAPAUSWMAI UMIN

06P-ROMN-16-01 SUNISTHMI DE UMIN FOIBHN THN ADELFHN HMWN OUSAN DIAKONON THV EKKLHSIAV THV EN KEGCREAIV

06P-ROMN-16-03 ASPASASYE PRISKAN KAI AKULAN TOUV SUNERGOUV MOU EN CRISTW IHSOU

06P-ROMN-16-07 ASPASASYE ANDRONIKON KAI IOUNIAN TOUV SUGGENEIV MOU KAI SUNAICMALWTOUV MOU OITINEV EISIN EPISHMOI EN TOIV APOSTOLOIV OI KAI PRO EMOU GEGONASIN EN CRISTW
06P-ROMN-16-08 ASPASASYE AMPLIAN TON AGAPHTON MOU EN KURIW

06P-ROMN-16-13 ASPASASYE ROUFON TON EKLEKTON EN KURIW KAI THN MHTERA AUTOU KAI EMOU

06P-ROMN-16-17 PARAKALW DE UMAV ADELFOI SKOPEIN TOUV TAV DICOSTASIAV KAI TA SKANDALA PARA THN DIDACHN HN UMEIV EMAYETE POIOUNTAV KAI EKKLINATE AP AUTWN
06P-ROMN-16-18 OI GAR TOIOUTOI TW KURIW HMWN IHSOU CRISTW OU DOULEUOUSIN ALLA TH EAUTWN KOILIA KAI DIA THV CRHSTOLOGIAV KAI EULOGIAV EXAPATWSIN TAV KARDIAV TWN AKAKWN
06P-ROMN-16-19 H GAR UMWN UPAKOH EIV PANTAV AFIKETO CAIRW OUN TO EF UMIN YELW DE UMAV SOFOUV MEN EINAI EIV TO AGAYON AKERAIOUV DE EIV TO KAKON
06P-ROMN-16-20 O DE YEOV THV EIRHNHV SUNTRIQEI TON SATANAN UPO TOUV PODAV UMWN EN TACEI H CARIV TOU KURIOU HMWN IHSOU CRISTOU MEY UMWN
06P-ROMN-16-21 ASPAZONTAI UMAV TIMOYEOV O SUNERGOV MOU KAI LOUKIOV KAI IASWN KAI SWSIPATROV OI SUGGENEIV MOU

06P-ROMN-16-23 ASPAZETAI UMAV GAIOV O XENOV MOU KAI THV EKKLHSIAV OLHV ASPAZETAI UMAV ERASTOV O OIKONOMOV THV POLEWV KAI KOUARTOV O ADELFOV
06P-ROMN-16-24 H CARIV TOU KURIOU HMWN IHSOU CRISTOU META PANTWN UMWN AMHN
07P-1COR-01-01 PAULOV KLHTOV APOSTOLOV IHSOU CRISTOU DIA YELHMATOV YEOU KAI SWSYENHV O ADELFOV
07P-1COR-01-02 TH EKKLHSIA TOU YEOU TH OUSH EN KORINYW HGIASMENOIV EN CRISTW IHSOU KLHTOIV AGIOIV SUN PASIN TOIV EPIKALOUMENOIV TO ONOMA TOU KURIOU HMWN IHSOU CRISTOU EN PANTI TOPW AUTWN TE KAI HMWN
07P-1COR-01-03 CARIV UMIN KAI EIRHNH APO YEOU PATROV HMWN KAI KURIOU IHSOU CRISTOU
07P-1COR-01-04 EUCARISTW TW YEW MOU PANTOTE PERI UMWN EPI TH CARITI TOU YEOU TH DOYEISH UMIN EN CRISTW IHSOU
07P-1COR-01-05 OTI EN PANTI EPLOUTISYHTE EN AUTW EN PANTI LOGW KAI PASH GNWSEI
07P-1COR-01-06 KAYWV TO MARTURION TOU CRISTOU EBEBAIWYH EN UMIN
07P-1COR-01-07 WSTE UMAV MH USTEREISYAI EN MHDENI CARISMATI APEKDECOMENOUV THN APOKALUQIN TOU KURIOU HMWN IHSOU CRISTOU
07P-1COR-01-08 OV KAI BEBAIWSEI UMAV EWV TELOUV ANEGKLHTOUV EN TH HMERA TOU KURIOU HMWN IHSOU CRISTOU
07P-1COR-01-09 PISTOV O YEOV DI OU EKLHYHTE EIV KOINWNIAN TOU UIOU AUTOU IHSOU CRISTOU TOU KURIOU HMWN
07P-1COR-01-10 PARAKALW DE UMAV ADELFOI DIA TOU ONOMATOV TOU KURIOU HMWN IHSOU CRISTOU INA TO AUTO LEGHTE PANTEV KAI MH H EN UMIN SCISMATA HTE DE KATHRTISMENOI EN TW AUTW NOI KAI EN TH AUTH GNWMH
07P-1COR-01-11 EDHLWYH GAR MOI PERI UMWN ADELFOI MOU UPO TWN CLOHV OTI ERIDEV EN UMIN EISIN
07P-1COR-01-12 LEGW DE TOUTO OTI EKASTOV UMWN LEGEI EGW MEN EIMI PAULOU EGW DE APOLLW EGW DE KHFA EGW DE CRISTOU
07P-1COR-01-13 MEMERISTAI O CRISTOV MH PAULOV ESTAURWYH UPER UMWN H EIV TO ONOMA PAULOU EBAPTISYHTE
07P-1COR-01-14 EUCARISTW TW YEW OTI OUDENA UMWN EBAPTISA EI MH KRISPON KAI GAION
07P-1COR-01-15 INA MH TIV EIPH OTI EIV TO EMON ONOMA EBAPTISA
07P-1COR-01-16 EBAPTISA DE KAI TON STEFANA OIKON LOIPON OUK OIDA EI TINA ALLON EBAPTISA
07P-1COR-01-17 OU GAR APESTEILEN ME CRISTOV BAPTIZEIN ALL EUAGGELIZESYAI OUK EN SOFIA LOGOU INA MH KENWYH O STAUROV TOU CRISTOU
07P-1COR-01-18 O LOGOV GAR O TOU STAUROU TOIV MEN APOLLUMENOIV MWRIA ESTIN TOIV DE SWZOMENOIV HMIN DUNAMIV YEOU ESTIN
07P-1COR-01-19 GEGRAPTAI GAR APOLW THN SOFIAN TWN SOFWN KAI THN SUNESIN TWN SUNETWN AYETHSW
07P-1COR-01-20 POU SOFOV POU GRAMMATEUV POU SUZHTHTHV TOU AIWNOV TOUTOU OUCI EMWRANEN O YEOV THN SOFIAN TOU KOSMOU TOUTOU
07P-1COR-01-21 EPEIDH GAR EN TH SOFIA TOU YEOU OUK EGNW O KOSMOV DIA THV SOFIAV TON YEON EUDOKHSEN O YEOV DIA THV MWRIAV TOU KHRUGMATOV SWSAI TOUV PISTEUONTAV
07P-1COR-01-22 EPEIDH KAI IOUDAIOI SHMEION AITOUSIN KAI ELLHNEV SOFIAN ZHTOUSIN
07P-1COR-01-23 HMEIV DE KHRUSSOMEN CRISTON ESTAURWMENON IOUDAIOIV MEN SKANDALON ELLHSIN DE MWRIAN
07P-1COR-01-24 AUTOIV DE TOIV KLHTOIV IOUDAIOIV TE KAI ELLHSIN CRISTON YEOU DUNAMIN KAI YEOU SOFIAN
07P-1COR-01-25 OTI TO MWRON TOU YEOU SOFWTERON TWN ANYRWPWN ESTIN KAI TO ASYENEV TOU YEOU ISCUROTERON TWN ANYRWPWN ESTIN
07P-1COR-01-26 BLEPETE GAR THN KLHSIN UMWN ADELFOI OTI OU POLLOI SOFOI KATA SARKA OU POLLOI DUNATOI OU POLLOI EUGENEIV
07P-1COR-01-27 ALLA TA MWRA TOU KOSMOU EXELEXATO O YEOV INA TOUV SOFOUV KATAISCUNH KAI TA ASYENH TOU KOSMOU EXELEXATO O YEOV INA KATAISCUNH TA ISCURA
07P-1COR-01-28 KAI TA AGENH TOU KOSMOU KAI TA EXOUYENHMENA EXELEXATO O YEOV KAI TA MH ONTA INA TA ONTA KATARGHSH

07P-1COR-01-31 INA KAYWV GEGRAPTAI O KAUCWMENOV EN KURIW KAUCASYW
07P-1COR-02-01 KAGW ELYWN PROV UMAV ADELFOI HLYON OU KAY UPEROCHN LOGOU H SOFIAV KATAGGELLWN UMIN TO MARTURION TOU YEOU
07P-1COR-02-02 OU GAR EKRINA TOU EIDENAI TI EN UMIN EI MH IHSOUN CRISTON KAI TOUTON ESTAURWMENON
07P-1COR-02-03 KAI EGW EN ASYENEIA KAI EN FOBW KAI EN TROMW POLLW EGENOMHN PROV UMAV

07P-1COR-02-10 HMIN DE O YEOV APEKALUQEN DIA TOU PNEUMATOV AUTOU TO GAR PNEUMA PANTA EREUNA KAI TA BAYH TOU YEOU
07P-1COR-02-11 TIV GAR OIDEN ANYRWPWN TA TOU ANYRWPOU EI MH TO PNEUMA TOU ANYRWPOU TO EN AUTW OUTWV KAI TA TOU YEOU OUDEIV OIDEN EI MH TO PNEUMA TOU YEOU
07P-1COR-02-12 HMEIV DE OU TO PNEUMA TOU KOSMOU ELABOMEN ALLA TO PNEUMA TO EK TOU YEOU INA EIDWMEN TA UPO TOU YEOU CARISYENTA HMIN
07P-1COR-02-13 A KAI LALOUMEN OUK EN DIDAKTOIV ANYRWPINHV SOFIAV LOGOIV ALL EN DIDAKTOIV PNEUMATOV AGIOU PNEUMATIKOIV PNEUMATIKA SUGKRINONTEV
07P-1COR-02-14 QUCIKOV DE ANYRWPOV OU DECETAI TA TOU PNEUMATOV TOU YEOU MWRIA GAR AUTW ESTIN KAI OU DUNATAI GNWNAI OTI PNEUMATIKWV ANAKRINETAI

07P-1COR-03-20 KAI PALIN KURIOV GINWSKEI TOUV DIALOGISMOUV TWN SOFWN OTI EISIN MATAIOI

07P-1COR-03-23 UMEIV DE CRISTOU CRISTOV DE YEOU
07P-1COR-04-01 OUTWV HMAV LOGIZESYW ANYRWPOV WV UPHRETAV CRISTOU KAI OIKONOMOUV MUSTHRIWN YEOU
07P-1COR-04-02 O DE LOIPON ZHTEITAI EN TOIV OIKONOMOIV INA PISTOV TIV EUREYH
07P-1COR-04-03 EMOI DE EIV ELACISTON ESTIN INA UF UMWN ANAKRIYW H UPO ANYRWPINHV HMERAV ALL OUDE EMAUTON ANAKRINW
07P-1COR-04-04 OUDEN GAR EMAUTW SUNOIDA ALL OUK EN TOUTW DEDIKAIWMAI O DE ANAKRINWN ME KURIOV ESTIN
07P-1COR-04-05 WSTE MH PRO KAIROU TI KRINETE EWV AN ELYH O KURIOV OV KAI FWTISEI TA KRUPTA TOU SKOTOUV KAI FANERWSEI TAV BOULAV TWN KARDIWN KAI TOTE O EPAINOV GENHSETAI EKASTW APO TOU YEOU
07P-1COR-04-06 TAUTA DE ADELFOI METESCHMATISA EIV EMAUTON KAI APOLLW DI UMAV INA EN HMIN MAYHTE TO MH UPER O GEGRAPTAI FRONEIN INA MH EIV UPER TOU ENOV FUSIOUSYE KATA TOU ETEROU
07P-1COR-04-07 TIV GAR SE DIAKRINEI TI DE ECEIV O OUK ELABEV EI DE KAI ELABEV TI KAUCASAI WV MH LABWN

13P-1THS-03-04 KAI GAR OTE PROV UMAV HMEN PROELEGOMEN UMIN OTI MELLOMEN YLIBESYAI KAYWV KAI EGENETO KAI OIDATE
13P-1THS-03-05 DIA TOUTO KAGW MHKETI STEGWN EPEMQA EIV TO GNWNAI THN PISTIN UMWN MHPWV EPEIRASEN UMAV O PEIRAZWN KAI EIV KENON GENHTAI O KOPOV HMWN
13P-1THS-03-06 ARTI DE ELYONTOV TIMOYEOU PROV HMAV AF UMWN KAI EUAGGELISAMENOU HMIN THN PISTIN KAI THN AGAPHN UMWN KAI OTI ECETE MNEIAN HMWN AGAYHN PANTOTE EPIPOYOUNTEV HMAV IDEIN KAYAPER KAI HMEIV UMAV
13P-1THS-03-07 DIA TOUTO PAREKLHYHMEN ADELFOI EF UMIN EPI PASH TH YLIQEI KAI ANAGKH HMWN DIA THV UMWN PISTEWV
13P-1THS-03-08 OTI NUN ZWMEN EAN UMEIV STHKETE EN KURIW
13P-1THS-03-09 TINA GAR EUCARISTIAN DUNAMEYA TW YEW ANTAPODOUNAI PERI UMWN EPI PASH TH CARA H CAIROMEN DI UMAV EMPROSYEN TOU YEOU HMWN

13P-1THS-03-13 EIV TO STHRIXAI UMWN TAV KARDIAV AMEMPTOUV EN AGIWSUNH EMPROSYEN TOU YEOU KAI PATROV HMWN EN TH PAROUSIA TOU KURIOU HMWN IHSOU CRISTOU META PANTWN TWN AGIWN AUTOU
13P-1THS-04-01 LOIPON OUN ADELFOI ERWTWMEN UMAV KAI PARAKALOUMEN EN KURIW IHSOU KAYWV PARELABETE PAR HMWN TO PWV DEI UMAV PERIPATEIN KAI ARESKEIN YEW INA PERISSEUHTE MALLON
13P-1THS-04-02 OIDATE GAR TINAV PARAGGELIAV EDWKAMEN UMIN DIA TOU KURIOU IHSOU

13P-1THS-04-06 TO MH UPERBAINEIN KAI PLEONEKTEIN EN TW PRAGMATI TON ADELFON AUTOU DIOTI EKDIKOV O KURIOV PERI PANTWN TOUTWN KAYWV KAI PROEIPOMEN UMIN KAI DIEMARTURAMEYA
13P-1THS-04-07 OU GAR EKALESEN HMAV O YEOV EPI AKAYARSIA ALL EN AGIASMW
13P-1THS-04-08 TOIGAROUN O AYETWN OUK ANYRWPON AYETEI ALLA TON YEON TON KAI DONTA TO PNEUMA AUTOU TO AGION EIV UMAV
13P-1THS-04-09 PERI DE THV FILADELFIAV OU CREIAN ECETE GRAFEIN UMIN AUTOI GAR UMEIV YEODIDAKTOI ESTE EIV TO AGAPAN ALLHLOUV
13P-1THS-04-10 KAI GAR POIEITE AUTO EIV PANTAV TOUV ADELFOUV TOUV EN OLH TH MAKEDONIA PARAKALOUMEN DE UMAV ADELFOI PERISSEUEIN MALLON
13P-1THS-04-11 KAI FILOTIMEISYAI HSUCAZEIN KAI PRASSEIN TA IDIA KAI ERGAZESYAI TAIV IDIAIV CERSIN UMWN KAYWV UMIN PARHGGEILAMEN

13P-1THS-04-13 OU YELOMEN DE UMAV AGNOEIN ADELFOI PERI TWN KEKOIMHMENWN INA MH LUPHSYE KAYWV KAI OI LOIPOI OI MH ECONTEV ELPIDA
13P-1THS-04-14 EI GAR PISTEUOMEN OTI IHSOUV APEYANEN KAI ANESTH OUTWV KAI O YEOV TOUV KOIMHYENTAV DIA TOU IHSOU AXEI SUN AUTW
13P-1THS-04-15 TOUTO GAR UMIN LEGOMEN EN LOGW KURIOU OTI HMEIV OI ZWNTEV OI PERILEIPOMENOI EIV THN PAROUSIAN TOU KURIOU OU MH FYASWMEN TOUV KOIMHYENTAV
13P-1THS-04-16 OTI AUTOV O KURIOV EN KELEUSMATI EN FWNH ARCAGGELOU KAI EN SALPIGGI YEOU KATABHSETAI AP OURANOU KAI OI NEKROI EN CRISTW ANASTHSONTAI PRWTON
13P-1THS-04-17 EPEITA HMEIV OI ZWNTEV OI PERILEIPOMENOI AMA SUN AUTOIV ARPAGHSOMEYA EN NEFELAIV EIV APANTHSIN TOU KURIOU EIV AERA KAI OUTWV PANTOTE SUN KURIW ESOMEYA
